unicode_script = "devanagari"
+++
**_Manuśāstravivaraṇam_**

---
## 06
**ṣaṣṭho 'dhyāyaḥ**

	**vaitānikāñ ca juhuyād agnihotraṃ yathāvidhi |**

**	darśam askandayan parva paurṇamāsaṃ ca yogataḥ || 6.9 ||**

homasādhanapradarśanārtham **agnihotra**grahaṇam || 6.9 ||

	**ṛkṣeṣṭyāgrayaṇaṃ caiva cāturmāsyāni cāharet |**

**	turāyaṇaṃ ca kramaśodākṣasyāyanam eva ca || 6.10 ||**

vaitānikam iti śloke smārtānām eva pravṛttir darśapaurṇamāsādiśabde stutyartham ucyate | śrautānāṃ tu nityānāṃ carupuroḍāśādīnāṃ vrīhyādiniyatatvād asāmarthyasmṛtir vrīhyādinirvartane || 6.10 ||

	**vāsantaśāradair medhyair munyannaiḥ svayamāhṛtaiḥ |**

**	puroḍāśāṃś carūṃś caiva vidhivan nirvapet pṛthak || 6.11 ||**

vaikhānasoktā evaite carupuroḍāśāḥ smārtā veditavyāḥ || 6.11||

	**devatābhyas tu tad dhutvā vanyaṃ medhyataraṃ haviḥ |**

**	śeṣaṃ samupayuñjīta lavaṇaṃ ca svayaṃkṛtam || 6.12 ||**

taccheṣavṛttitāsya niyamyate || 6.12 ||

	**sthalajaudakaśākāni puṣpamūlaphalāni ca |**

**	medhyavṛkṣodbhavāny adyāt snehāṃś ca phalasaṃbhavān || 6.13 ||**

āraṇyāny evaitāni śyāmākādīni gṛhyante || 6.13 ||

	**varjayen madhumāṃsāni bhaumāni kavakāni ca |**

**	bhūstrṛṇaṃ śigrukaṃ caiva śleṣmātakaphalāni ca || 6.14 ||**

**bhauma**śabdo gojihvikāviṣayo pṛthaguktatvāt | **kavaka**śabdas tu prasiddārtha eva | apare tu kavakaviśeṣaṇaṃ **bhauma**śabdam icchanti | teṣām abhojyatvaṃ prāpnoti | pūrvasminn abhakṣyaprakaraṇe cāviśeṣeṇa pratiṣedhaḥ sarvacchatrākāṇm. atha tu tatpadārthaviśiṣṭapratiṣedhāt ekajātiviṣaya eva | **śigruka**śabdaś ca bhūstṛṇasāhacaryān na saubhañjanakaviṣayaḥ, kiṃ tarhi tatsvarūpatṛṇajātiviṣayaḥ |

	ayaṃ pratiṣedho 'narthaka iti, yataḥ kavakagrahaṇam anarthakam iti <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecit</span>. 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ahaṃ tu bruve</span>, nānarthakyaṃ śāstre veditavyaṃ prasiddhānām avadhānatvād ṛṣeḥ | yato 'nuvādo 'yaṃ pratiṣiddhānāṃ bhūstṛṣādīnāṃ sāhacaryāt tatsamapratyavāyaprajñāpanārtho, tatbhojanaṃ ca prāyaścittasāmyam |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">aparas</span> tu śutāpasapratiṣedhārtham idam āha |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">tat punar</span> vicāryam |kavakānāṃ punarvidhānena tatsahopadiṣṭānāṃ laśunādīnāṃ vikatthaś śakyo vaktum, samācāra . . . punargrahaṇavat |

	**tyajed āśvayuje māsi munyannaṃ pūrvasaṃcitam |**

**	jīrṇāni caiva vāsāṃsi śākamūlaphalāni ca || 6.15 ||**

"ṣaṇmāsanicayaḥ" (MDh 6.18) iti vaikalpikāni vakṣyati || 6.15 ||

	**na phālakṛṣṭam aśnīyād utsṛṣṭaṃ pūrvasaṃcitam |**

**	jīrṇāni caiva vāsāṃsi śākamūlaphalāni ca || 6.16 ||**

ayaṃ pratiṣedho **phālakṛṣṭānāṃ** tathāphālakṛṣṭānām api grāmajātānām āraṇyānām || 6.16 ||

	**agnipakvāśano vā syāt kālapakvabhug eva vā |**

**	aśmakuṭṭo bhaved vāpi dantolūkhaliko 'pi vā || 6.17 ||**

agnipakvabhik kālapakvabhug aśmakuttabhug ity ete dantolūkhalikāḥ || 6.17 ||

	**sadyaḥ prakṣālako vā syān māsasaṃcayiko 'pi vā |**

**	ṣaṇmāsanicayo vā syāt samānicaya eva vā || 6.18 ||**

. . . samānicyasyāpavādaḥ || 6.18 ||

	**naktaṃ vānnaṃ samaśnīyād divā vāhṛtya śaktataḥ|**

**	caturthakāliko vā syāt syād vāpy aṣṭamakālikaḥ || 6.19 ||**

[The commentary is illegible here.]

	**cāndrāyaṇavidhānair vā śuklakṛṣṇe ca vartayet |**

**	pakṣāntayor vāpy aśnīyād yavāgūṃ kvathitāṃ sakṛt || 6.20 ||**

[The commentary is illegible here.]

	**puṣpamūlaphalair vāpi kevalair vartayet sadā |**

**	kālapakvaiḥ svayaṃ śīrṇair vaikhānasamate sthitaḥ || 6.21 ||**

**The commentary and the mūla texts from 6.21–38 were illegible to Derrett. This is something that we may want to revisit by reading the original Malayalam manuscript. The readable commentary ends thus:

punar brāhmaḥ etasmāl liṅgād agniparityāgāt . . . yotsannaśākhāstham anutsannaśākhāsthaṃ vā caturtham āśramāntaraṃ prasādayitayaṃ śrutyavirodenha, yat kāraṇaṃ na hy akasmāt sarvakarmasūtrakartano 'sti |

	**yo gattvā darvabhūtebhyaḥ pravrajaty abhayaṃ gṛhāt |**

**	tasya tejomayā lokāḥ**

tejasvino brahmalokasthānaviśeṣā apunarāvartino 'sya nityaprakāśalakṣaṇā vā paramātmaprāptilakṣaṇā vā

		**bhavanti brahmavādinaḥ || 6.39 ||**

paramātmajñasya na kevalaṃ pravrajitasyeti || 6.39 ||

	**yasmād aṇv api bhūtānāṃ dvijān notpadyate bhayam |**

**	tasya dehād vimuktasya bhayaṃ nāsti kutaścana || 6.40 ||**

**	agānād abhiniṣkrāntaḥ pavitropacito muniḥ |**

**	samupoḍheṣu kāmeṣu nirapekṣaḥ parivrajet || 6.41 ||**

anena ślokatrayeṇa sarvabhūtābhayapradānaṃ pravrajitasya vidhīyate | ekārāmatā cānena || 6.40–41 ||

	**eka eva caren nityaṃ siddhyartham asahāyavān |**

**	siddhim ekasya saṃpaśyan na jahāti na hīyate || 6.42 ||**

siddhe śāstrāgnityāge laukikāgnityāgārtham idam ucyate || 6.42 ||

	**anagnir aniketaḥ syād grāmam annārtham āśrayet |**

**	upekṣako 'saṃcayiko munir bhāvasamāśritaḥ || 6.43 ||**

**anagniḥ syāt** | so 'yam agnīndhanatatsaṃparigrahapratiṣedhaḥ | **aniketaś** ca **syāt** | grāmaikarātrikanyāyena **grāmam annārtham āśrayet** | arthāc cheṣaṃ kālam araṇye tiṣṭhet | **upekṣakaḥ** svaśarīrādiṣu | **asaṃcayikaḥ** apratiṣiddhāsv api kamaṇḍalvādimātrāsu | **munir bhāvasamāśritaḥ** | cittasaṃyamopadeśaparam idaṃ dhyānātmānuṣṭhānam || 6.43 ||

	**kapālaṃ vṛkṣamūlāni kucelam asahāyatā |**

**	samatā caiva sarvasminn etan muktasya lakṣaṇam || 6.44 ||**

**samatā**diguṇavidhānārtham idaṃ bhikṣoḥ || 6.44 ||

	**nābhinandeta maraṇam**

anena kleśābhighātodvegena kārtsne

		**nābhinandeta jīvitam |**

vijñānāvigamasaṅgaprītyā,

	**kālam eva pratīkṣeta nirveśaṃ bhṛtako yathā || 6.45 ||**

	**dṛṣṭipūtaṃ nyaset pādaṃ vastrapūtaṃ jalaṃ pibet |**

**	manaḥpūtāṃ vaded vācaṃ satyapūtaṃ samācaret || 6.46 ||**

prasiddhārthaślokaḥ || 6.46 ||

	**ativādāṃs titikṣeta**

kṣamopadeśo 'yam |

		**nāvamanyeta kaṃcana |**

iti parāvamānaṃ vārayati |

	**na cemaṃ deham āśritya vairaṃ kūrvīta kenacit || 6.47 ||**

evaṃ ca sati kṣamāyogā

	**krudhyantaṃ na pratikrudhyed ākruṣṭaḥ kuśalaṃ vadet |**

śivena manasā dhyāyed ākroṣṭāraṃ na kevalaṃ na krudhyet |

	**saptadvārāvakīrṇāṃ ca na vācam anṛtāṃ vadet || 6.48 ||**

**vācas saptadvārāṇi** dharmo 'rthaḥ kāmo dharmārthāv arthakāmau dharmakāmau dharmārthakāmā iti | tatra mokṣāśritām eva **vācaṃ** vaden, na **saptadvārāśritām** **anṛtāṃ** trivargāśrayām |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">apare</span> tu sapta śirasi prāṇāḥ, tadāśritāṃ ity āhuḥ | 

	saptavibhaktyāśritām ity <span style="text-decoration:underline;">apare</span> || 6.48 ||

	**adhyātmaratir āsīno nirapekṣo nirāmiṣaḥ |**

**	ātmanaiva sahāyena sukhārthī vicared iha || 6.49 ||**

**	na cotpātanimittābhyāṃ na nakṣatrāṅgavidyayā |**

**	nānuśāsanavādābhyāṃ bhikṣāṃ lipseta karhicit || 6.50 ||**

**	na tāpasair brāhmaṇair vā vayobhir api vā śvabhiḥ |**

**	ākīrṇaṃ bhikṣukair vānyair agāram upasaṃviśet || 6.51 ||**

**	kḷptakeśanakhaśmaśruḥ pātrī daṇḍī kusumbhavān |**

**	vicaren niyato nityaṃ sarvabhūtāny apīḍayan || 6.52 ||**

**	ataijasāni pātrāṇi tasya syur nirvraṇāni ca |**

**	teṣām adbhiḥ smṛtaṃ śaucaṃ camasānām ivādhvare || 6.53 ||**

**	alābuṃ dārupātraṃ ca mṛnmayaṃ vaidalaṃ tathā |**

**	catvāri yatipātrāṇi manuḥ svāyambhuvo 'bravīt || 6.54 ||**

**	ekakālaṃ cared bhaikṣe na prasajjeta vistare |**

**	bhaikṣe prasakto hi yatir viṣayeṣv api sajjati || 6.55 ||**

sāyaṃ bhojanasya pratiṣedhaḥ, gārhasthye dvibhojanasya prāptasya || 6.55 ||

	**vidhūme sannamusale vyaṅgāre bhuktavajjane |**

**	vṛtte śarāvasaṃpāte bhikṣāṃ nityaṃ yatiś caret || 6.56 ||**

**	alābhe na viṣādī syāl lābhaś cāinaṃ na harṣayet |**

**	prāṇayātrikamātraḥ syān mātrāsaṅgād vinirgataḥ || 6.57 ||**

arthaprāpta . . . m asminn api || 6.57 ||

	**abhipūjitalābhāṃs tu jugupsetaiva sarvaśaḥ |**

**	abhipūjitalābhais tu yatir mukto 'pi badhyate || 6.58 ||**

**	alpānnābhyavahāreṇa rahaḥsthānāsanena ca |**

**	hriyamāṇāni viṣayair indriyāṇi nivartayet || 6.59 ||**

indriyajayopāyadvayopadeśo 'yam | kasya punar hetore yau...

	**indriyāṇāṃ nirodhena rāgadveṣakṣayeṇa ca |**

**	ahiṃsayā ca bhūtānām amṛtatvāya kalpate || 6.60 ||**

saṃsārasvabhāvāvalokanena ca nityam indriyajayam ātiṣṭhet | tac ca punar idam || 6.60 ||

	**avekṣeta gatir nṝṇāṃ karmadoṣasamudbhavāḥ |**

**	niraye caiva patanaṃ yātanāś ca yamakṣaye || 6.61 ||**

**	viprayogaṃ priyaiś caiva saṃprayogaṃ tathāpriyaiḥ |**

**	jarayā cābhibhavanaṃ vyādhibhiś caiva pīḍanam || 6.62 ||**

**	dehād utkramaṇaṃ cāsmāt punar garbhe ca saṃbhavam |**

**	yonikoṭisahasreṣu sṛtīś cāsyāntarātmanaḥ || 6.63 ||**

**	adharmaprabhavaṃ caiva duḥkhayogaṃ śarīriṇām |**

**	dharmārthaprabhavaṃ caiva sukhasaṃyogam akṣayam || 6.64 ||**

**	sūkṣmatāṃ cānvavekṣeta yogena paramātmanaḥ |**

**	deheṣu caivopapattim uttameṣv adhameṣu ca || 6.65 ||**

**	dūṣito 'pi cared dharmaṃ yatra tatrāśrame rataḥ|**

**	samaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu na liṅgaṃ dharmakāraṇam || 6.66 ||**

prasaṃkhyānadyānātmānuṣṭhānastutir iyaṃ samatvadarśanasya, na tu liṅgapratiṣedho, vihitatvāt |

	**phalaṃ katakavṛkṣasya yady apy ambuprasādakam |**

**	na nāmagrahaṇād eva tasya vāri prasīdati || 6.67 ||**

kriyātaḥ phalam, na vijñānamātrād ity anuṣṭhānastutir iyam || 6.67 ||

	**saṃrakṣaṇārthaṃ jantūnāṃ rātrāv ahani vā sadā |**

**	śarīrasyātyaye caiva samīkṣya vasudhāṃ caret || 6.68 ||**

apratyayād dharmotpattir eva yatnavato 'pi, yasmād **samīkṣya vasudhāṃ cared** iti | tasya ca prāyaścittam aprakaraṇe 'py ādarārtham || 6.68 ||

	**ahnā rātryā ca yāñ jantūn hinasty ajñānato yatiḥ |**

**	teṣāṃ snātvā viśuddhyarthaṃ prāṇāyāmān ṣaḍ ācaret || 6.69 ||**

**	prāṇāyāmā brāhmaṇasya trayo 'pi vidhivat kṛtāḥ |**

**	vyāhṛtipraṇavair yuktā vijñeyaṃ paramaṃ tapaḥ || 6.70 ||**

**	dahyante dhmāyamānānāṃ dhātūnāṃ hi yathā malāḥ |**

**	tathendriyāṇāṃ dahyante doṣāḥ prāṇasya nigrahāt || 6.71 ||**

evaṃ ca sati |

	**prāṇāyāmair dahed doṣān dhāraṇābhiś ca kilbiṣam |**

**	pratyāhāreṇa saṃsargān dhyānenānīśvarān guṇān || 6.72 ||**

**prāṇāyāmair dahed doṣān** rāgādīn saviṣayān tatkāraṇaṃ vā 'kuśalakarmarāśi | tathā ca prāṇāyāmān śuddhihetūn vakṣyati prāyaścittaprakaraṇe | tathā ca prāṇāyāmān śuddhihetūn vakṣyati prāyaścittaprakaraṇe | prāṇāyāmasya doṣāṇāṃ ca vināśyavināśakasaṃbandhaḥ | śāstralakṣaṇatvāc chraddadhānīyaḥ, vidhipakṣam āśritya | yato nāyaṃ prāṇāyāmastutyartho 'rthavādaḥ | stutyarthatve 'pi ca sati na hy akasmāt stutiḥ prāṇāyāmānāmupapadyate iti stutyā vidhir anumātavyaḥ | **dhāraṇāḥ** punar avadhārayaty ātmānam upasṛṣṭo yatir yogasamādhyavasthāyāṃ kāmakrodhamohalobhasnehādibhiḥ pravartyamānam akuśaleṣu, tabhiś ca paramārthadarśanaprasaṃkhyānabhāvanākhyābhiḥ kāmādipratipakṣabhūtābhir **dhāraṇābhiḥ kilbiṣam** anutpattyā **dahet** | evaṃ ca prāṇāyāmaiḥ saṃcitavirodhaḥ dhāraṇābhir snāgatānutpattir akuśalasyety uktaṃ bhavati | apare tv āhur viśiṣṭāni śarīrātmapradeśāni manasaḥ prajñāprayatnakṛtāny ātmano yathābalaṃ **dhāraṇāh** |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye</span> dhāraṇā maitryādyāḥ saṃcakṣate |

	maitrīkṛpāmudopekṣāḥ sarvaprāṇiṣv avasthitāḥ |

	brahmalokaṃ nayanty āśu dhyātāraṃ dhāraṇās tv iha || 

**pratyāhāreṇa** manasa indriyāṇāṃ ca **saṃsargān** viṣayasaṃparkākhyāñ chabdādyupalabdhihetūn | teṣu hy evam upahetuṣu antaḥkaraṇapratyāhāreṇa manasaḥ samādhānayogaḥ pratyanīkaḥ | pratilabdhasamādhānasya pratibandhakaraṇatvāc chabdādyupalabdhikaṇṭakāni dhyānādīny āhur ācāryāḥ | paramātmakarmakeṇa ca praṇava**dhyānenānīśvarā**n **guṇān** yogarddhipratyanīkabhūtānaiśvaryādīn pratilabdhasamādhānasya dahamānasya yoginaḥ sarvopasargasthānam atikrāntasya paramārthadarśanaprasaṃkhyānabhāvanābhir iti || 6.72 ||

_kiṃ cānyat_ |

	**uccāvaceṣu bhūteṣu durjñānām akṛtātmabhiḥ |**

**	jñānayogena saṃpaśyed gatim asyāntarātmanaḥ || 6.73 ||**

**uccāvaceṣu** gatiṣūtkṛṣṭāpakṛṣṭeṣu vā bhūtānām utpattisthāneṣu gatisaṃbhavam **asyāntarātmanaḥ** karmādhikārapuruṣasya **jñānayogena**, **jñānaṃ** śastraṃ jñāyate 'neneti kṛtvā, tadadhyayanavijñānasaṃbandhenābhyāsayogena vā | tasya **durjñānām akṛtātmabhir** anadhītāśrutaśāstraiḥ | evaṃ hi prasaṃkhyānavān nityam adhyātmaratir utkṛṣyate || 6.73 ||

_kasya punar hetor etad evam, yasmād āha |_

	**samyagdarśanasaṃpannaḥ karmabhir na nibadhyate |**

**	darśanena vihīnas tu saṃsāraṃ pratipadyate || 6.74 ||**

**samyagdarśanaṃ** nāma paramātmadarśanam | saṃsāryātmano 'saṃsāryātmano vā dehendriyamanobuddhyādivyatiriktasya saṃsāryātmano 'dhikārīpuruṣasya vā pradhānapuruṣayor vā nānātvakasya karmāṅgadevatāyā vā saṃsārasvabhāvasya ca vā "avekṣeta gatīr nṝṇām" (MDh 6.61) ity evamādy uktaṃ prasaṃkhyānavijñānaṃ vā śarīragataṃ śuklaśoṇitādyutpannam iti viṣayagataṃ ca **saṃyagdarśana**śabdenocyate | tathā ca vakṣyaty "asthisthūṇam" (MDh 6.76) ity evamādi | sarvaṃ caitad yathāviṣayaṃ **saṃyagdarśana**śabdenocyate | sāmarthyād evaṃ jñānakarmasamuccayam upadekṣyaty anantaraśloka evam | ataś caitad evam ataḥ, **darśanena vihīnas tu** kevalakarmakṛt **saṃsāram** āvṛttim **pratipadyate** pitṛlokadvāreṇa | saiṣā jñānakarmasamuccyastutir vijñānamātrastutir vā || 6.74 ||

_tathā ca darśayati |_

	**ahiṃsayendriyāsaṅgair vaidikaiś caiva karmabhiḥ |**

**	tapasaś caraṇaiś cograiḥ sādhayantīha tatpadam || 6.75 ||**

**ahiṃsayeti** sāmānyam apīdaṃ pravrajitasya viśeṣasādhanam | tad dharmānām api viśeṣāṇāṃ nidarśanārtham | evam **indriyasaṅgaiḥ** brahmacāriṇaḥ, **vaidikaiś** cāgnihotrādikarmabhiḥ gṛhasthasya, **tapasaś caraṇair** iti tāpasasya | tadaivaṃ sarvāśrameṣv ayaṃ jñānakarmasamuccayo brahmatvaprāptihetur vijñeyaḥ, samuccayavikalpapakṣayor āśramāṇām, na tu bādhāpakṣe | prakaraṇād vāyaṃ pravrajitasya vijñānakarmasmuccayaḥ | evaṃ ca sati **vaidikaiś caiva karmabhir** ity atra vedāntacoditā paramātmopāsanā gṛhyate, nāgnihotrādīni karmāṇi | **tapasaś caraṇair** ity atrāpi tad dharmā evānūdyante | tathā copaniṣatsv evāha: "tasmād evaṃvic chānto dānta uparatas titikṣuḥ samāhito bhūtvātmany evātmānaṃ paśyati" iti | na vānaprasthadharmāḥ || 6.75 ||

evaṃ ca saty ayam anena samyagvijñānasamānabhāvanākarameṇa prasannatattvajñāno vairāgyaprakarṣāt prasaṃkhyāyemaṃ kāyam eva,

	**asthisthūṇaṃ snāyubaddhaṃ māṃsaśoṇitalepanam |**

**	carmāvanaddhaṃ durgandhiṃ pūrṇaṃ mūtrapurīṣayoḥ || 6.76 ||**

**	jarāśokasamāviṣṭaṃ rogāyatam āturam |**

**	rajasvalam anityaṃ ca bhūtāvāsam imaṃ tyajet || 6.77 ||**

_tasya ca tyāgasyopāyabhedād dvitvaṃ dṛṣṭāntadvayena pradarśayati |_

	**nadīkūlaṃ yathā vṛkṣo vṛkṣaṃ vā śakunir yathā |**

**	tathā tyajann imaṃ dehaṃ duḥkhagrāhād vimucyate || 6.78 ||**

yas tāvad ghaṭamānakas tasya karmakṣayāt aparādhino dehatyāgaḥ, yathā vṛkṣasyābuddhipūrvaḥ pātaḥ | yaḥ punar abhyāsasāmarthyāt prāṇamanonigrahas tasya nistīrṇopadhasya paśyaprakṛter dharmaviśeṣopaṣkṛtātmano mahāyogayuktadīkasya buddhipūrvo dehatyāgaḥ śakunivad jijñeyaḥ sāṃkhyayogayor āśayo dehapātadvayopadeśo dṛṣṭāntadvayena pradarśyate || 6.78 ||

_idānīṃ kṣamāsādhanastutyarthaṃ madhyasthyapradarśanārthaṃ vā prasaṃkhyānam idam atrocyate |_

	**priyeṣu sveṣu sukṛtam apriyeṣu ca duṣkṛtam |**

**	visṛjya dhyānayogena brahmābhyeti sanātanam || 6.79 ||**

**priyeṣu sveṣu** dharmaviruddheṣv ātmīyeṣu svādubhaikṣalābhādiṣu ca nipatatsu kāraṇatvenātmīyam eva **sukṛtaṃ** visṛjya, dhyānayogena paramārthadarśanena viniyujya, tam kāraṇatayā svadharmaṃ vyudasya ca tatsaṃpādayitāraṃ puruṣam, evam **apriyeṣu duṣkṛtaṃ visṛjya dhyānayogena** paraṃ **brahmābhyeti**.

_kṣamayānayā vigatarāgadveṣatayā ca madhyastho bhūtvā, evaṃ ca ayam_,

	**yadā bhāvena bhavati sarvabhāveṣu niḥspṛhaḥ |**

**	tadā sukham avāpnoti pretya ceha ca śāśvatam || 6.80 ||**

**iha** śamasukhaṃ **pretya ca** brahmalokaprāptisukham | śāśvatam itīyaṃ stutiḥ bhūtārthānuvādo vā || 6.80 ||

_adhunā sarvasaṅgatyāgopayopadeśasya prayojanam idam ācaṣṭe |_

	**anena vidhinā sarvāṃs tyaktvā saṅgāñ chanaiḥ śanaiḥ |**

**	sarvadvandvair vipramuito brahmaṇy evāvatiṣṭhate || 6.81 ||**

ubhāv api cemau ślokau "priyeṣu sveṣu sukṛtam" (MDh 6.79) ity etasya ślokasya śeṣayor vacanīyau || 6.81 ||

_tathā ca saty etad atra yat paramārthadarśanaṃ rāgadveṣaprahāṇāyoktaṃ "visṛjya dhyānayogena" iti tatstutim adhikṛtya sarvavijñānastutyarthaṃ vedam ārabhyate |_

	**dhyānikaṃ sarvam evaitad yad etad abhiśabditam |**

prakaraṇāt pravrajyākhyaṃ karma sarvāśramakara vā, kāryasāmānyāt | **dyāna**śabdena ca yāvat kiṃcid atra pravrajyāprakaraṇe śāstre vā paramārthadarśanam uktaṃ tat sarvam abhidhīyate | tasmin dhyāne paramārthadarśane yat karma tad dhyānikam | evaṃ ca sati paramārthadarśanastitur iyam, jñānakarmasamuccayastutir vā | tathā coktam: "samyagdarśanasaṃpannaḥ karmabhir na nibadhyate" (MDh 6.74) iti | asya vā hetur ayaṃ vijñeyaḥ | kasmāt punar etad evaṃ bhavati, yasmāt,

	**na hy anadhyātmavit kaścit kriyāphalam upāśnute || 6.82 ||**

ātmani tad ity adhyātmaṃ buddhyādi tad vettīty **adhyātmavic** ca | punar yathāviṣayaṃ vyākaraṇīyam | asya nidarśanārtham idaṃ rahasyabrāhmaṇaṃ bhavati "yo vā etad akṣaraṃ gārgy aviditvā 'smiṃl loke juhoti yajate tapas tapyate bahūni varṣasahasrāṇy antavad evāsya tad bhavati" iti śruteḥ | tathā ca samuccaye praśasyate: "tad ya ittam etad vidur ye ceme 'raṇye śraddhā tapa ity upāsate, te 'rciṣam abhisaṃbhavanti" ity evamādiḥ | adhunā ṣaḍaṅgavedādhyayanopadeśāt pūrvatra brahmacāriprakaraṇe niyamārthaṃ pravrajitasyedam ārabhyate, viśeṣārthaṃ vā || 6.82 ||

_adhyātmaniṣṭhatvopadeśe vā sati tannivṛttyāśaṅkayānuvṛttyartham idam ucyate |_

	**[adhiyajñaṃ brahma japed] adhidaivikam eva ca |**

**	ādhyātmikaṃ ca satataṃ vedāntābhihitaṃ ca yat || 6.83 ||**

yajñe tad ity **adhiyajñaṃ** karmopadeśaḥ | **brahma** vidhyarthavādanāmadheyākhyam | **ādhidaivikaṃ** mantrāḥ | ādhyātmikaṃ ca brahmamantraikadeśaḥ | prakaraṇāt puruṣasūktādi sukriyā vā | **vedāntābhihitam** upaniṣadaḥ | sāmarthyāt soyaṃ mantrabrāhmaṇākhyo vedaḥ, ślokasamāptyartham evaṃ caturdhoktaḥ | tathā ca sati yathaiva pravrajitasyādhyātmānuṣṭhānam utkarṣāya, evaṃ vedābhyāso 'pīty etad api sāmarthyād avagamyate | tathā ca smṛtiḥ:

	śabdabrahmaṇi niṣṇātaḥ

tasyādhyayanavijñānatadarthānuṣṭhānena,

		paraṃ brahmādhigacchati ||

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">aparas</span> tv āha: samarthasyedam adhyātmānuṣṭhāne śrautasya vā tatrārater vā |

_asyedānīṃ sarvavidher vā yathāyogaṃ stutyartham idam ārabhyate |_

	**idaṃ śaraṇam ajñānām idam eva vijānatām |**

**	idam anvicchatāṃ svargam idam ānantyam icchatām || 6.84 ||**

ānantaryād brahmaṇo japakarmedam ucyate yathā sāṃkhyena | atha vā parivrajyāpraśaṃseyam, tadupasaṃhāradarśanāt cāturāśramidharmakrameṇa śāstrasyānupasaṃhārāt tasya | tathā ca śāstropasaṃhāraśāstrastutir vakṣyate || 6.84 ||

	**anena kramayogena parivrajati yo dvijaḥ |**

**	sa vidhūyeha pāpmānaṃ paraṃ brahmādhigacchati || 6.85 ||**

ayaṃ ślokaḥ paravrajyādhikārastutyarthaḥ, āśramasamuccayastutyartho vā || 6.85 ||

	**eṣa dharmo 'nuśiṣṭo vo yatīnāṃ niyatātmanām |**

**	vedasaṃnyāsikānāṃtu karmayogaṃ nibodhata || 6.86 ||**

pūrvottarayoḥ prakaraṇayor upasaṃhārārthopanyāsārthaḥ ślokaḥ | vedasya saṃnyāso vedasaṃnyāsaḥ | tatra bhavo **vedasaṃnyāsikam** | na hi vedasya saṃnyāso 'sti śāstravirodhāt, yataḥ sāmarthyād ayam asyārtha ucyate | vedasya hi granthārthābhyāsanimittaḥ, tadarthānuṣṭhānāya ca pratigrahādīnāṃ vṛttikarmaṇāṃ saṃnyāso yasya sa vedasaṃnyāsiko gṛhasta eva kṛtakaraṇīyo 'bhidhīyate sāmarthyāt | tathā ca taṃ vakṣyaty anantaram eva | kṛtasaṃpattividhāno vā āsannamṛtyūpadarśakenāriṣṭadarśanena | tathā ca vājasaneyakaṃ rahasyabrāhmaṇam idamarthaṃ bhavati | "athātaḥ saṃprattiḥ | yadā praiṣyan manyate 'tha putram āha" ity evamādi | sa hi kṛtakaraṇīyaḥ tathāvasannaśarīro vā jarasā kṛtasaṃpattividhāno putropahṛtavṛttir asyām avasthāyāṃ nirutsukaḥ paramasaṃyamavān paramātmadhyānaikālambanaḥ sukham āsīta | na tu nityānām agnihotrādīnāṃ saṃnyāso 'sti, nityatvād eva, śāstravirodhāc ca, na ca vedasyety uktam | yato 'yam eva śāstrārtha iti, vikalpārthaś cāyam asyehopadeśaḥ pārivrājyenākrame 'pi katham | yas tāvat samartho gṛhāt pravrajyāyāṃ tasya yathāśāstraṃ saṃbhavati, asamarthasya punar utsṛṣṭāgneḥ śāstrād arthād veyam avasthocyate | pravrajyā vaikalpikī | evaṃ ca kṛtvā pravrajyānantaraṃ (?) tadupadeśo yujyata iti || 6.86 ||

_ukta āśramāṇāṃ samuccayas, teṣāṃ punar adhunā bādhāvikalpau vaktavyāv iti | yatas tatprasiddhaya idam ārabhyate |_

	**brahmacārī gṛhasthaś ca vānaprastho 'tha bhikṣukaḥ |**

**	ete gṛhasthaprabhavāś catvāraḥ pṛthag āśramāḥ || 6.87 ||**

evaṃ ca na pāṣaṇḍotpannāḥ santaḥ svakarmaṇā saṃbadhyante | sarvāśramāṇāṃ ca gārhasthyasya śraiṣṭhyam | bādhāpakṣam āśritya yad vakṣyati tatstutyartham idaṃ veditavyam | vikalpārthaṃ punar idam eṣām || 6.87 ||

	**sarve 'pi kramaśas tv ete yathāśāstraṃ niṣevitāḥ |**

**	yathoktakāriṇaṃ vipraṃ nayanti paramāṃ gatim || 6.88 ||**

**api**śabdāt sarve 'pi trayo 'pi dvāv api eko 'pīty ayam eva vikalpaḥ pradarśanīyaḥ, samuccayavat teṣām | tathā ca smṛtyantaram: "tasyāśramavikalpam eke" (GDh 3.1) iti | sarvasamuccayavac ca dvitrisamuccayo 'py **api**śabdasāmarthyād upadiṣṭo mantavyaḥ || 6.88 ||

_bādhāpakṣas tu |_

	**sarveṣām api tv eteṣāṃ vedaśrutividhānataḥ |**

**	gṛhastha ucyate śreṣṭhaḥ sa trīn etān bibharti hi || 6.89 ||**

**vedaśrutyā** gārhasth(y)asyādhānāt prabhṛty āśmaśānakaraṇāt sarvam abhidhīyate, na smṛtyā | ataḥ "pratyakṣavidhānād gārhasthyasya" (GDh 3.36) tadanuṣṭhānapuruṣo 'pi **śreṣṭha** ucyate yataś ca **sa trīn etān bibharty** annādibhiḥ | ataś ca gṛhasthāśramasya **vedaśrutividhānataḥ** śraiṣṭhyavacanāt tadvirodhenāśramāntarapratipattir arthād gamyate | evaṃ ca saty āśramāṇāṃ na samo vikalpaḥ, kiṃ tarḥi viṣamaḥ || 6.89 ||

_asmin bādhāpakṣe smārtatvād āśramāṇām asya stutuḥ |_

	**yathā nadī nadāḥ sarve sāgare yānti saṃsthitam |**

**	tathaivāśramiṇaḥ sarve gṛhasthe yānti saṃsthitam || 6.90 ||**

yathā ca gautamaḥ: "aikāśramyaṃ tv ācāryāḥ" ity evamādi | trayo 'pi caite, āśramāṇāṃ vikalpād asmin pakṣe vedasmṛtiśāstrāvirodhena yathādhikāraṃ vyākhyeyāḥ | ekāntagrahaṇas tv ācāryaḥ śāstravirodhād vijñeyaḥ || 6.90 ||

	**caturbhir api tūpetair nityam āśramibhir dvijaiḥ |**

**	daśalakṣaṇako dharmaḥ sevitavyaḥ prayatnataḥ || 6.91 ||**

tatra tatra śāstre vikṣepeṇoktānāṃ vṛttyādīnāṃ samāhṛtyehopadeśaḥ punar asaṃmohārthaḥ, atha vā sādhāraṇatvapradarśanārthaḥ, viśeṣaṇārtho vā || 6.91 ||

	**dhṛtiḥ kṣamā damo 'steyaṃ śaucam indriyasaṃyamaḥ |**

**	dhīr vidyā satyam akrodho daśakaṃ dharmalakṣaṇam || 6.92 ||**

**dhṛtir** nāma yathāśāstram avasthānam ātmagunād yato bhavati sā **dhṛtiḥ** | **kṣamā** cittasaṃkṣobhahetuṣv apratikriyāparādhamarṣanena | **damas** tu dvandvābhimukhyam, śāstravihitābhyāsaṃ **damaṃ** manyante ca | paradravyeṣv ātmasaṃyamo **'steyam** | āhārādiśuddhiḥ **śaucam** | **indriyasaṃyamo** nāma indriyaviṣayeṣv aviruddheṣv aprasaṅgaṃ yathāviṣayam | vijñānaṃ śastrāt saṃśayādipratipakṣarahitaṃ **dhīḥ** | **vidyā** vedābhyāsaḥ | **satyam** prasiddham | **akrodhaḥ** satsv api saṃkṣobhahetuṣu cittasyāvikāraḥ | pūrvatrotpannasya krodhasya kāryānāraṃbhaḥ **kṣamety** uktaḥ, iha tv anutpattir eva krodhasyeti viśeṣaḥ | sarvaṃ caitac chāstravihitam api sat sukhāvabhodhanārthaṃ punaḥ saṃkṣipyoktam || 6.92 ||

_paricintyamānaś ca sarvo 'yaṃ yamaniyamādhīneti tatphalavivakṣayedam āha |_

	**daśa lakṣaṇāni darmasya ye viprāḥ samadhīyate |**

**	adhītya cānuvartante te yānti paramāṃ gatim || 6.93 ||**

_saṃnyāsakramārtham adhunedam ucyate |_

	**daśalakṣaṇakaṃ dharmam anutiṣṭhan samāhitaḥ |**

**	vadāntān vidhivac chrutvā saṃnyased anṛṇo dvijaḥ || 6.94 ||**

prakaraṇāc ca vedanyāsikasyocyate | anye tu pravrajiṣyato 'py āhuḥ | evaṃ ca sati parityaktasarvabāhyavyāpāraḥ || 6.94 ||

	**saṃnyasya sarvakarmāṇi karmadoṣān apānudan |**

**	niyato vedam abhyasya putraiśvarye sukhaṃ vaset || 6.95 ||**

_saṃnyāsaprayojam idānīṃ tadanuṣṭhānaprarocanārtham āha |_

	**evaṃ saṃnyāsya karmāṇi svakāryaparamo 'spṛhaḥ |**

**	saṃyāsenāpahatyainaḥ prāpnoti paramāṃ gatim || 6.96 ||**

phalārthavādo 'yam, phalavidhir vā || 6.96 ||

	**eṣa vo 'bhihito dharmo brāhmaṇasya caturvidhaḥ |**

**	puṇyo 'kṣayaphalaḥ pretya rājñāṃ dharmaṃ nibodhata || 6.97 ||**

āgamaḥ saty api dvijātitve | tathā ca vājasaneyakaṃ rahasyabrāhmaṇam idamarthaṃ bhavati: "brāhmaṇāḥ pravrajanti" evamādy ukto varṇāśramadharmaḥ | tadvyatikramanimittas tv idānīṃ prāyaścittalakṣaṇo vaktavyo 'pi sa nocyate, tatsaṃrakṣaṇahetoḥ pārtivadharmasyānabhidhānāt | evaṃ ca sati yaḥ śraddadhānatayā yathāśastraṃ gurum upasthāsyate tasya vyatikarmābhāvāt prāyaścittānadhikāra eva, itarasya tu rājadaṇḍabhayāt | yaḥ punar anayoḥ rājācāryayoḥ śāsanātigo bhaviṣyati taṃ praty upadeśaḥ prāyaścittasya yujyate | yato 'rthakramād evaitasmāt prāyaścittāni protsārya rājadharmā eva tāvac chiṣyanta iti || 6.97 ||

**ṛjuvimalasya kṛtau manuśāstravivaraṇe ṣaṣṭho 'dhyāyaḥ |**


## 07
**saptamo 'dhyāyaḥ**

evam ekāśramyaṃ cāturāśramyaṃ ca savikalpaṃ prasādhya tatsaṃrakṣaṇārtham idānīm |

	**rājadharmān pravakṣyāmi yathā vṛtto bhaven nṛpaḥ |**

**	saṃbhavaś ca yathā tasya siddhiś ca paramā yathā || 7.1 ||**

**siddhis** tu **paramā** rājñaḥ svīkṛtasarvarājamaṇḍalasyānantaraṃ sakalamahīmaṇḍalādhipatye sati niratiśayā dharmārthasukhatrivargābhyudayaprāptir aparāmātyādiprakṛtisampat || 7.1 ||

_tatra siddhim avekṣyedam ucyate |_

	**brāhmaṃ prāptena saṃskāraṃ kṣatriyeṇa yathāvidhi |**

**	sarvasyāsya yathānyāyaṃ kartavyaṃ parirakṣaṇam || 7.2 ||**

brahmaṇe brahmaṇo vā saṃskāro **brāhmam** upanayanādiḥ snānāntas, taṃ **prāptena kṣatriyeṇa**, nānyavarṇena | **yathāvidhi** yathāśastram | **sarvasyāsyety** anenābhinayena varṇāśramau nirdiśati | **yathānyāyaṃ** yathopadeśaṃ **kartavyaṃ parirakṣaṇam** iti anyavṛttiparisaṃkhyeyaṃ niyamo vā |

	eke tu dṛṣṭārthatvād upadeśaṃ vṛttyarthaṃ manyante | tathā ca sati pitrye dhane nidhyadhigame 'nyathā prāptau na niyogataḥ kṣatriyo rājyam ātiṣṭhed iti | 

	tad ayuktam, "vedābhyāso brāhmaṇasya kṣatriyasya tu rakṣaṇam, vārtākarmaiva vaiśyasya viśiṣṭāni svakarmasu" ity uktatvād viśiṣṭatvaṃ caiṣāṃ dṛṣṭādṛṣṭasaṃbandhena yuktam | niyamāśrayaś cādṛṣṭasaṃbandhaḥ | vṛttidāś cānāthā dīnāś ca rājñā rakṣyante, yato na dṛṣṭārtham eva rakṣaṇam || 7.2 ||

_arājño 'pi ca kṣatriyasya grāmādisaṃrakṣaṇe 'py etadarthavanniyamaśāstrastutyāsya bhayo dhāraṇam adhunocyate |_

	**arājake hi loke 'smin sarvato vidrute bhayāt |**

**	rakṣārtham asya sarvasya rājānam asṛjat prabhuḥ || 7.3 ||**

hiraṇyagarbhaḥ mātsyanyāyo mā bhūt | prajānām iti [rakṣāya] rājotpattir anena pradarśyate | pūrvavidhistutir iyam || 7.3 ||

	**indrānilayamārkāṇām agneś ca varuṇasya ca |**

**	candravitteśayoś caiva mātrā nirhṛtya śāśvatīḥ|| 7.4 ||**

"bālo 'pi nāvamantavyaḥ" (MDh 7.8) ity asya vidher vakṣyamāṇasyeme daśa ślokāḥ śeṣatayā vijñeyāḥ | evam inrādīnāṃ svaviṣaye yena ceṣṭāḥ karoti tena teṣāṃ mātrābhyo nirmita ity ucyate || 7.4 ||

	**yasmād ēṣāṃ surendrāṇāṃ mātrābhyo nirmito nṛpaḥ |**

**	tasmād abhibhavaty eṣa sarvabhūtāni tejasā || 7.5 ||**

kāryeṇaitad arthaṃ darśayati | yasmād ādhipatyaiśvaryāt **sarvabhūtāny abhibhavati** svena **tejasā** ata indrādidevatā**mātrābhyo** **nirmita** iti stūyate || 7.5 ||

_yataś ca |_

	**tapaty ādityavac caiva cakṣūṃṣi ca manāṃsi ca |**

**	na cainaṃ bhuvi śaknoti kaścid apy abhivīkṣitum || 7.6 ||**

mahārājaliṅgena cāmaracchatrabhṛṅgādinā yukto dīptimattvāc **cakṣūṃṣy ādityavat** **tāpayati**, **manāṃsi** daṇḍapātanād | yasmād ato **na kaścid enaṃ śaknoty abhivīkṣitum** api, kiṃ punar apakartum | pūrvavad ayam api stutyai || 7.6 ||

_evaṃ ca sati tāsu tāsv avasthāsu kāryārtham |_

	**so 'gnir bhavati vāyuś ca so 'rkaḥ somaḥ sa dharmarāṭ |**

**	sa kuberaḥ sa varuṇaḥ sa mahendraḥ prabhāvataḥ || 7.7 ||**

evaṃ ceme lokapālā yair ayaṃ rājā tathaiva vyapadiśyate || 7.7 ||

_yataś caitad evam ataḥ |_

	**bālo 'pi nāvamantavyo manuṣya iti bhūmipaḥ |**

**	mahatī devatā hy eṣā nararūpeṇa tiṣṭhati || 7.8 ||**

śaknoti hy ayaṃ bālo 'py amātyādibhir akāryakāriṇo nivartayitum || 7.8 ||

_kiṃ cānyat |_

	**ekam eva dahaty agnir naraṃ durupasarpiṇam |**

**	kulaṃ dahati rājāgniḥ sapaśudravyasaṃcayam || 7.9 ||**

yasmād akāryakāriṇāṃ tatsahāyānāṃ tadaparādhasaṃbandhānāṃ ca **kulaṃ dahati** | ato 'py asau nāvamantavyaḥ || 7.9||

_yataś ca:_

	**kāryaṃ sa 'vekṣya śaktiṃ ca deśakālau ca tattvataḥ |**

**	kurute dharmasiddhyarthaṃ viśvarūpaṃ punaḥ punaḥ || 7.10 ||**

ataś cāsau vāllabhyān maitryāt svājanyadvāreṇa vā nāvamantavyaḥ || 7.10 ||

_yataś ca tasya samyag upacaritasya:_

	**[yasya] prasāde padmā śrīr vijayaś ca parākrame |**

**	mṛtyuś ca vasati krodhe sarvatejomayo hi saḥ || 7.11 ||**

ato na kevalam asau bhayāt pratyavāyaparihārārtham ārādhyaḥ, abhyudayo 'pi hi tasmāt samyag upacaritād viśiṣṭo bhavati || 7.11 ||

_ataś caivaṃ ca sati:_

	**taṃ yas tu dveṣṭi saṃmohāt sa vinaśyaty asaṃśayam |**

yathoktam upadeśam aparigaṇayya paunahpunyana | yatas taṃ na dviṣyād anyārthāparādham, yena:

	**tasya hy āśu vināśāya rājā prakurute manaḥ || 7.12 ||**

anayas tu dviṣyamāṇaḥ kadācid dharmāpekṣayāśaktyā vā saheta, rājñaḥ punaḥ sahamānasya svatantravirodo yato 'śaktaś cāsau nigrahaṇaṃ kartum iti | ataḥ sadānuvartitavyo nirupadhais sadbhiḥ || 7.12 ||

	**tasmāt dharmaṃ yam iṣṭeṣu vyavasyati narādhipaḥ |**

**	aniṣṭaṃ cāpy aniṣṭeṣu taddharmaṃ na vicārayet || 7.13 ||**

na hi rājā varṇāśramadharmapravṛttau hetuḥ, śāstralakṣaṇatvād dharmādharmayoḥ | avyavasthā caivaṃ syāt | vyavasthākāriṇā ca śāstreṇa bhavitavyam | tathā ca bahukṛtvas taduktiḥ, tadvirodhaś cānyāyyaḥ | yataḥ prakaraṇād rājastutiparam etat pratyavagantavyam | laukikadharmāpekṣayā vedaṃ vijñeyaṃ śāstram | samāptā rājotpattiḥ || 7.13 ||

_adhunā tatsahakārī daṇḍo vyākriyate:_

	**tasyārthe sarvabhūtānāṃ goptāraṃ dharmam ātmajam |**

**	brahmatejomayaṃ daṇḍam asṛjat pūrvam īśvaraḥ || 7.14 ||**

idam ārabhya dvādaśaślokāḥ daṇḍotpattyarthāḥ | daṇḍanāmānaṃ **tejomayaṃ sarvabhūtagoptāraṃ dharmam ātmajam asṛjat pūrvaṃ** rājotpatteḥ | etad uktaṃ bhavati "daṇḍād ṛte rājasatvaṃ nābhivartate tasmān naiva daṇḍotsarjanena rājā prajā rakṣiṣyati" iti || 7.14 ||

_yataś ca:_

	**tasya sarvāṇi bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca |**

**	bhayād bhogāya kalpante svadharmān na calanti ca || 7.15 ||**

jātaś cāsau yukto rājasāhāyye yasya bhayāt **sthāvarāṇi** phalacchāyādibhir **bhogāya kalpante**, kiṃ punar anye | yo hi sthāvaro vṛkṣo na **bhogāya** kalpate niyataṃ tasya pariśodhanādy ārabhate, yataś ca na pariśuddhyate hitvāsāv aṅgārīkriyate, yaś ca pratikūlaṃ vartate tasya chedanamūlotpāṭanādibhir daṇḍaḥ praṇīyate eva | yathā rājamārgādijātasya bīraṇastaṃbādeḥ|| 7.15 ||

	**taṃ deśakālau śaktiṃ ca vidyāṃ cāvekṣya tattvataḥ |**

**	yathārhataḥ saṃpraṇayen nareṣv anyāyavṛttiṣu || 7.16 ||**

grāmāraṇyabāhyābhyantararathyādir **deśaḥ** | divā naktaṃ bālo yuvā sthavira iti **kālaḥ** | **śaktiḥ** śarīragatārthagatā ca | **vidyā** trayī śāṅgopāṅgā | etadapekṣayā daṇḍaḥ praṇeyaḥ | anyathā praṇīto 'nartham utpādayati, arthaṃ ca na karotīti daṇḍastutyartho 'yam anuvādaḥ | daṇḍapātanavidhiṃ tūpariṣṭād vakṣyaty aparādhaṃ pratijñāyeti || 7.16 ||

	**sa rājā puruṣo daṇḍaḥ sa netā śāsitā ca saḥ |**

**	caturṇām āśramāṇāṃ ca dharmasya pratibhūḥ smṛtaḥ || 7.17 ||**

**daṇḍa** eva **rājā**, tannimittatvād rājatvasya | sa eva **puruṣaḥ**, yena balīyaso 'pi puruṣān strīvan nyakkrtvā vaśam ānayati | sa netā yasmāt tadbhayād eva kāryāṇi samyāṅ nīyante | sa eva **śāsitā** yena tadapekṣayaiva vāsanā śāsanībhavati | sa eva **patibhūr** varṇāśramavyatikrame pratibhūr iva pratibhūḥ || 7.17 ||

_yataś caivam ataḥ:_

	**daṇḍaḥ śāsti prajāḥ sarvā daṇḍa evābhirakṣati |**

**	daṇḍaḥ supteṣu jāgarti daṇḍaṃ dharmaṃ vidur budhāḥ || 7.18 ||**

na śāstraṃ rājā vā śāsti | saty api ca śāstre rājani ca **daṇḍa**bhayād eva śāsanam anuvartante varṇāśramiṇaḥ | evaṃ ca sa **evābhirakṣati**, akāryakāribhya itarān | supteṣv api rājapuruṣeṣv aihikabhayāt paralokabhayād vā na yathākāmaṃ pravartate lokaḥ || 7.18 ||

	**samīkṣya sa dhṛtaḥ samyak sarvā rañjayati prajāḥ |**

**	asamīkṣya praṇītas tu vināśayati sarvataḥ || 7.19 ||**

naitāvatā mucyāmahe, asamyagdhṛtaḥ kāryaṃ na karotīti | yathaiva samyagdhṛto **rañjayati prajāḥ**, evam asamyagdhṛtaḥ sarvam eva **vināśayati** || 7.19 ||

	**yadi na praṇayed rājā daṇḍaṃ daṇḍyeṣv atandritaḥ |**

**	śūle matyān evāpakṣyan durbalān balavattarāḥ || 7.20 ||**

na kevalaṃ daṇḍapraṇītau guṇāvāptiḥ, apraṇītau matsyasya nyāyaḥ pravartate || 7.20 ||

	**adyāt kākaḥ puroṣāśaṃ śvāvalihyād dhavis tathā |**

**	svāmyaṃ ca na syāt kasmiṃścit pravartetādharottaram || 7.21 ||**

sarvā dharmāṇ (?) | kākaśvādayaḥ ṛddhimadbhiḥ sarvottamair api devair daṇḍād ṛte na śakyante prativārayitum | kiṃ punar anyaḥ | suhṛnmitrasvajanavacanād iti || 7.21 ||

_evaṃ ca sati:_

	**sarvo daṇḍajito loko durlabho hi śucir naraḥ |**

**	daṇḍasya hi bhayāt sarvaṃ jagad bhogāya kalpate || 7.22 ||**

prāyaṇa **sarvo daṇḍajita** eva **lokaḥ**, yena **durlabhaḥ** svabhāvaśuddhaḥ, śāsanānuvartī | tad etad daṇḍapātanaṃ yady api duḥkhotpādanaṃ tathāpi prakalpyate śāstreṇa, yenānya upāyo dharmasthiter nāstīti || 7.22 ||

	**devadānavagandharvā rakṣāṃsi patagoragāḥ |**

**	te 'pi bhogāya kalpante daṇḍenaiva nipīḍitāḥ || 7.23 ||**

evam īśvarā api santo devādayo 'nugrahopaghātābhyām | daṇḍabhayād evānugrāhyān anugṛhṇanti, upaghātyāṃś copaghnanti | yadi ca daṇḍān na bibhur aiśvaryād yathākāmam abhipravarteran, na ca pravartante | ato manyāmahe devādayo 'pi daṇḍabhayād eva saty apy aiśvarye yathā karmānugrahopaghātābhyāṃ vartante na yathākāmam iti atiśayavacanenaiṣā daṇḍastutiḥ || 7.23 ||

_tathā ca:_

	**duṣyeyuḥ sarvavarṇāś ca bhidyeran sarvasetavaḥ |**

**	sarvalokaprakopaś ca bhaved daṇḍasya vibhramāt || 7.24 ||**

adhāryamāṇe nyāyan daṇḍe varṇanimittā dharmā **duṣyeyuḥ** | ye ca dharmārthakāma**setavaḥ** te ca **bhudyeran** | kiṃ bahunā, kaḥ śaknoti bhagavantaṃ daṇḍaṃ dharmanāmānaṃ vyavasthākāriṇaṃ bahuguṇatvāt stotum || 7.24 ||

	**yatra śyāmo lohitākṣo daṇḍaś carati pāpahā |**

**	prajās tatra na muhyante metā cet sādhu paśyati || 7.25 ||**

etadrūpaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ praśastam abhīṣṭaṃ cātas tenāsatā rūpakaṃ kṛtvā stauti | atha vā dvirūpo daṇḍaḥ kuḥkhado bhayadaś ceti | yatas tasya dvābhyāṃ rūpābhyāṃ stūyate bhayahetutvaṃ śyāmatayā duḥkhahetutvaṃ ca lohitākṣatveneti, devatārūpaṃ vedaṃ śāstrapratyakṣaṃ yathābhūtam anenānūdyate | samāptā daṇḍastutiḥ || 7.25 ||

	**tasyāhuḥ saṃpraṇetāraṃ rājānaṃ satyavādinam |**

**	samīkṣya kāriṇaṃ prājñaṃ dharmakāmārthakovidam || 7.26 ||**

**tasya** daṇḍasya praṇetā jātyā kṣatriyo 'bhiṣekād ādhipatyaprabhāvaguṇayuktaḥ | **satyavādi** nānavasthitaṃ daṇḍaṃ prītyā prāpayati, dveṣeṇa vā vardhayati | **samīkṣya kārī** daṇḍāvadhāreṇa deśādhyapekṣayā **prājño** deśādīnām utsargāpavādadarśane | **dharmakāmārtheṣu** ca paṇḍitaḥ teṣām avasthāviśeṣajñaḥ samacittaḥ | tam evaṃvidhaṃ daṇḍasya preṇetāram āhuḥ || 7.26 ||

_evaṃvidhaś ca:_

	**taṃ rājā praṇayan samyak trivargeṇābhivardhate |**

**	kāmātmā viṣamaḥ kṣudro daṇḍenaiva nihanyate || 7.27 ||**

adṛṣṭam utsṛjya dṛṣṭena cainaṃ praguṇīkaroti | yena **samyak** praṇīta eṣa trivargeṇa praṇetāraṃ vardhayati | kāmādidiṣaiś ca **daṇḍenaiva nihanyate** || 7.27 ||

_yasmād:_

	**daṇḍo hi sumahattejo durdharaś cākṛtātmabhiḥ |**

**	dharmād dhi calitaṃ hanti nṛpam eva sabāndhavam || 7.28 ||**

yeṣāṃ svābhāviko vidyopanītaś ca vinayas te kṛtātmānaḥ | tair ayam śako dhārayitum | vparītaṃ tasmāc **calitaṃ daṇda eva sabāndhavaṃ hanti** || 7.28 ||

	**tato durgaṃ ca rāṣṭraṃ ca lokaṃ ca sacarācaram |**

**	antarikṣagatāṃś caiva munīn devāṃś ca pīḍayet || 7.29 ||**

yadi nṛpaṃ sabāndhavaṃ hatvāvatiṣṭheta daṇḍaḥ kiṃ na labdhaṃ bhavet | yena tu naitāvatāvatiṣṭheta daṇḍaḥ kiṃ na labdhaṃ bhavet | yena tu naitāvatāvatiṣṭhate durgādīn api hanti | **antarikṣagatān** dyulokagatāṃś ca devādīn api hanti | yasmād itaḥ pradānajīvanā devā munayaś caitasmād asamyakpraṇayanād deśādiviplave tadijyāvicchedena hatā eva devādayo bhavanti, yebhyo na pradīyate | tathā ca paurāṇikāḥ:

	varṇāśramebhyas tv ijyā tu loke 'smin yā pravartate |

	sarvāsāṃ devayonīnāṃ sthitihetuḥ sa vai smṛtaḥ || iti |

	**so 'sahāyen mūḍhena lubdhenākṛtabuddhinā |**

**	na śakyo nyāyato netuṃ saktena viṣayeṣu ca || 7.30 ||**

yasmād daṇḍo duṣpraṇīto dṛṣṭam adṛṣṭaṃ ca hanti, ato **'sahāyena mūḍhena lubdhenākṛtabuddhinā** viṣayātisevineti pañcabhir etair doṣair yukten**āśakyo netum** | || 7.30 ||

_etad viparītaiś ca pañcabhir guṇair yuktenāsau śakyo netum, yatas tatpradarśanāyedam ucyate:_

	**śucinā satyasaṃdhena yathāśāstrānusāriṇā |**

**	daṇḍaḥ praṇayituṃ śakyas susahāyena dhīmatā || 7.31 ||**

**śucinā** jitendriyeṇa, **satyasaṃdhena** prakaraṇād alubdhena, **yathāśastrānusāriṇā** amūḍhena, **susahāyena** nāsahāyena mūrkhasahāyena vā, **dhīmatā** kṛtaśāstraprajñena smṛtimatā vā || 7.31 ||

_evaṃvidhaś ca san rājā:_

	**svarāṣṭre nyāyavṛttaḥ syād bhṛśadaṇḍaś ca śatruṣu |**

**	suhṛtsv ajihmaḥ snigdheṣu brāhmaṇeṣu kṣamānvitaḥ || 7.32 ||**

pararāṣṭre tīkṣṇadaṇḍatocyate, śauryaprajñāpanārtham | samānābhyudayapratyavāyaḥ **suhṛd**, yasya kāryānapekṣaṃ suhṛttvaṃ sa **snigdhaḥ** | tasmin na kuṭilavṛttir, anyasmiṃs tu kāryāpekṣayā kuṭilavṛttir api syāt | **brāhmaṇeṣu kṣamānvitaḥ** niyacchann api daṇḍena brāhmaṇān akāryakāriṇaḥ kṣamāpūrvaṃ niyacchen na tu krodhena sahasaiva ca || 7.32 ||

	**evaṃvṛttasya nṛpateḥ śilocchenāpi (?) jīvataḥ |**

**	vistīryate yaśo loke tailabindur ivāmbhasi || 7.33 ||**

**evaṃvṛttasya** rājño 'ntareṇāpi kośaṃ kevalenaiva samyagdaṇḍapraṇayanena **vistīryate** rājayaśaḥ, yena śaknoti pararāṣṭrāṇy apy ātmīkartuṃ paripālayituṃ ca || 7.33 ||

	**atas tu viparītasya nṛpater ajitātmanaḥ |**

**	saṃkṣipyate yaśo loke ghṛtabindur ivāmbhasi || 7.34 ||**

**ato viparītasya** rāṣṭram api saṃkucati nirguṇatvāt, kuto 'nyad bhaviṣyati | saiṣā daṇḍapraṇayanastutiḥ samāptā || 7.34 ||

_kasmāt punar etad evam | yadmād evaṃguṇa eva:_

	**sve sve dharme niviṣṭānāṃ sarveṣām anupūrvaśaḥ |**

**	varṇānām āśramāṇāṃ ca rājā sṛṣṭo 'bhirakṣitā || 7.35 ||**

upanyāsārtham uttaravivakṣārthaṃ cedam uktam ap sad ucyate || 7.35 ||

	**tena yad yat sabhṛtyena kartavyaṃ rakṣatā prajāḥ |**

**	tat tad vo 'haṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ || 7.36 ||**

śrotṝṇām avadhānārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 7.36 ||

	**brāhmaṇān paryupāsīta prātar utthāya pārthivaḥ |**

**	traividyavṛddhān viduṣas tiṣṭhet teṣāṃ ca śāsane || 7.37 ||**

trayo 'vayavā asyeti trayī | tasyāṃ granthārthayor vṛddhās te **traividyavṛddhāḥ**, tān | atha vā traividyādhyāyinas traividyavṛddhāś ca vayasthaprajñayā ca traividyavṛddhā, ye ānvīkṣikyāṃ daṇḍanītyāṃ ca svabhivinītās te vidvāṃsaḥ tān **viduṣaḥ prātar utthāyopāsītā**nanyacittaḥ | yac ca te brūyus tac cāviśaṅkitaṃ kuryān na hi te kiṃcid ahitaṃ rājño vakṣyanti paramadhārmikatvāt || 7.37 ||

	**vṛddhāṃś ca nityaṃ seveta viprān vedavidaḥ śucīn |**

**	vṛddhasevī hi satataṃ rakṣobhir api pūjyate || 7.38 ||**

imān aparān vidyāvṛddhān brāhmaṇān dharmāyaiva kevalāya seveta | yena **vṛddhasevī** na kevalaṃ dharmeṇa yujyate, loke 'pi ca viśvasanīyatamo bhavati | ataś ca **rakṣobhir api pūjyate** ity ucyate || 7.38 ||

	**tebhyo 'dhigacched vinayaṃ vinītātmāpi nityaśaḥ |**

**	vinītātmā hi nṛpatir na vinaśyati karhicit || 7.39 ||**

vinayo hi dvividhaḥ: vābhāvikaḥ ādheyaś ca | śuśrūṣādiguṇayuktaṃ ca vidyā vinayati | ato yady api svabhāvato vinītātmā bhavet, tathāpy abhyāsena pāṭavaṃ janayet | kasmāt | punar iyān vinayādhāne yatna āsthīyate || 7.39 ||

_yena:_

	**bahavo 'vinayān naṣṭā rājānaḥ suparigrahāḥ |**

**	vanasthāś caiva rājyāni vinayāt pratipedire || 7.40 ||**

ubhayatopadeśo hi vinayādhānādarārthaḥ || 7.40 ||

_tānidānīṃ (?) darśayati:_

	**veno vinaṣṭo 'vinayān nahuṣaś caiva parthivaḥ |**

**	sudāḥ paijavanaś caiva sumukhi nimir eva ca || 7.41 ||**

**	pṛthus tu vinayād rājyaṃ prāptavān manur eva ca |**

**	kuberaś ca dhanaiśvaryaṃ brāhmaṇyaṃ caiva gādhijaḥ || 7.42 ||**

tribhiḥ śḷokair vinayasya pratyakṣaphalatāṃ venādidṛṣṭāntair darśayati vinayādhānaprarocanāya || 7.42 ||

_evaṃ ca saty āhitavinayo rājā:_

	**traividyebhyas trayīṃ vidyāṃ daṇḍanītiṃ ca śāsvatīm |**

**	ānvīkṣikīṃ cātmavidyāṃ vārtāraṃbhāṃś ca lokataḥ || 7.43 ||**

adhigacched iti vartate | **traividyebhyo** vedādhigamasyoktatvād brahmacāryavasthāyām eva tadarthādhigamārtho 'yaṃ punar ārambhaḥ sāmarthyād veditavyaḥ | anadhigatādhigamārtho vā vratasnātakapakṣe daṇḍanītyupadidikṣayā vā punar asyopadeśo dṛṣṭāntārthavādārthaḥ | evaṃ daṇḍanītividbhyo **daṇḍanītim** adhigacchet | **śāśvatīm** iti stutiparam etat | danḍanīter vedavad [ānantyaṃ nāsti] | yady api ca daṇḍanītyāśrayaṃ sarvaṃ śakyate lokato grahītum, dṛṣṭopāyasādhyatvāt tasya, tathāpy abuddhā na pratipadyeran, buddhāś ca daṇḍapātane niyamena varteran | lobhān parityajyādṛṣṭam asyāṅkanam asya vivāsanam | iyāṃś ca punar ayam asya daṇḍa itīṣyate ca niyamo, dṛṣṭaprayojanatvān niyamasmṛteḥ | ato rājñā **daṇḍanītir** avaśyam adhyetavyā | **ānvīkṣikīṃ cātmavidāṃ** tadvidbhyaḥ | evaṃ ca saty ayaṃ tayāhitatattvavijñāno 'bhyudayopanipātāpakramakāleṣu harṣaviṣādavikāropaśamaprayojanam adhyātmaprasaṃkhyānam avāpya na rājyatantraṃ parihāpayiṣyati | prajñāvākyakriyāvaiśāradyaṃ cāsyā jāyate, ānvīkṣikyadhigame tac cāsyāgamike vidhau sāmantadūtasaṃvādādiṣu saprayojanaṃ bhavati | **vārtāraṃbhāṃś ca** kośopacayahetūn **lokato** **'dhigacched** iti vartate || 7.43 ||

_āhitavidyāvinayaś cāyaṃ rājā prayatnataḥ,_

	**indriyāṇāṃ jaye yogaṃ samātiṣṭhed divāniśam |**

**	jitendriyas tu śaknoti vaśe sthāpayituṃ prajāḥ || 7.44 ||**

śrotrādīnāṃ śabdādiṣu yathāśāstraṃ pravṛttir indriyajayaḥ | sa ca varṇadharmeṣūkto [mukhyo vinaya iti punar ihopadiṣṭaḥ] || 7.44 ||

_kathaṃ nāmāyaṃ jitendriyaḥ |_

	**daśa kāmasamuttāni tathāṣṭau krodhajāni ca |**

**	vyasanāni durantāni prayatnena vivarjayet || 7.45 ||**

kāmakrodhasamutthayor duḥkhayor upanyāsas tyāgārthaḥ, kāmakrodhaparityāgena | tattyāgaś cendriyajayenety uktam | balābalam adhunā vyasanavargasyocyate, ādarārtham | kathaṃ nāmāyaṃ gurutaraṃ vyasanavargam ādareṇa jahyāt || 7.45 ||

	**kāmajeṣu prasaktas tu vyasaneṣu mahīpatiḥ |**

**	viyujyate 'rthadharmābhyāṃ krodhajeṣv ātmanaiva tu || 7.46 ||**

anayos tu vargayoḥ **kāmajeṣu prasaktaḥ** pānadyūtagītanṛttavāditrādiṣu **arthadharmābhyāṃ viyujyate**, yenārthadharmābhyām avirodena naiṣā pravṛttiḥ saṃbhavati | **krodhajeṣa** tu paiśunasāhasādau vartamāno dveṣyabhāvam upagato niyatam ucchidyate || 7.46 ||

	**mṛgayākṣo divāsvapnaḥ parivādaḥ striyo madaḥ|**

**	tauryatriko vṛthāṭyā ca kāmajo daśako gaṇaḥ || 7.47 ||**

**kāmaja** it kāmād icchāto jāto viśiṣṭakāmārtho vā | sa ca yaḥ sukhopabhogārtho jāyate | pūrvānubhūtaviṣayānucintanasukhād vā kāmaparāṇāṃ jāyate | yenātaḥ kāmaja ity ucyate **daśako gaṇaḥ** | kāmajavyasanavargasvarūpanirdeśo mṛgayādiḥ | yānaṃ **mṛgayā** | **divāsvapnaḥ** karmānuṣṭhānakāle karmasv avyāpāraḥ | **parivādas** tv amātyādīnāṃ kriyamāṇaḥ svatantravirodhī saṃpadyeta,sarvo hi pṛṣṭamāṃsabhakṣaṇe kriyamāṇe rājakāryaṣu na samyag vartate, praśithilamānatayā | aparivādyānāṃ ca parivāde prasiddho darmavirodhaḥ | **striyo mada** ity etad dvayaṃ pratītam | **tauryatriko** nṛttagītavāditrāṇi | **vṛthāṭyā** aprayojanam aṭanam | dharmārthasukharahitam īṣatprayojanaṃ vā | evaṃ ca sati sarvam etad rājño 'rthavirodhena vartate | ato 'sya kāmajavyasanavargasya parihartavyatayopadeśo yuktataraḥ || 7.47 ||

	**paiśunaṃ sāhasaṃ droha īrṣyāsūyārthadūṣaṇam | **

**	vāgdaṇḍajaṃ ca pāruṣyaṃ krodhajo 'pi gaṇo 'ṣṭakaḥ || 7.48 ||**

**paiśunaṃ** heḍakatvaṃ tac ca krodhāt kriyate | evaṃ **sāhasaṃ** ca | tac ca sādhor nīce karmaṇi niyogaḥ, karmoparodho vā niṣkāraṇam | **droha** upāṃśuvadhaḥ, tantroparodho vā jīvata eva | **īrṣyā** viṣayasādhāraṇatvavyāvṛttīcchā | **asūyā** paratuṇopaghātārthā vākpravṛttiś ceṣṭā vā, jihvikādharavikṣepahastābhinayaiḥ | **arthadūṣaṇam** adānam apaharaṇaṃ vā | **vāgdaṇḍajapāruṣyaṃ** prasiddhārtham | evaṃ **krodhajo 'pi gaṇo 'ṣṭakaḥ** || 7.48 ||

	**dvayor apy etayor mūlaṃ yaṃ sarve kavayo viduḥ |**

**	taṃ yatnena yajel lobhaṃ tajjau hy etau gaṇāv ubhau || 7.49 ||**

stryādiṣu lubdhaḥ kāmajaṃ gaṇaṃ sevate | pratihatasya ca tatra krodha iti | sa evam ayaṃ **lobhaḥ** kāmakrodhayoḥ vyasanavargayoḥ mūlam ucyate | upadeśaprayojanaṃ tu tattyāge vyasanavargadvayābhāvaḥ pradarśito yathā syāt kāraṇābhāvāt | atha vānyāyena paradravyādānaṃ lobhāt kriyate, mṛgayāyāṃ ca vartamānaḥ svatantrāvasādād avaśyam anyāyena paradravyāṇy ādatte | yaś ca mṛgayāparityāge vartate, avaśyam asau svatantrasiddhyarthaṃ kośopacayahetvanuṣṭhāne yateta, tatra ca vyāpṛtasya mṛgayāyām apravṛttiḥ | evaṃ divāsvapnādiṣu api vyākhyeyam | akṣeṣu tu prasiddaiva lobhāt pravṛttiḥ | evaṃ krodhajeṣv api paiśunādiṣu vartamāno lubdha evāntaṃ gacchati | kevalena tu krodhena pravartamānaḥ svalpake vā viāśe 'vatiṣṭhate, upaśamaṃ vā gacchati | vyasanavargadvayāsevinaḥ kāryasāmānyād vā lobhasya dvayor apy etayor vyasanavargayor mūlaṃ lobha ucyate | yathāśrutārthāsaṃbhavād itaratra ca sāmarthyāt so 'yam atra nindātiśayaḥ, parityāgādarārtho rājyatantrasiddhaya iti || 7.49 ||

	**pānam akṣāḥ striyaś caiva mṛgayā ca yathākramam |**

**	etat kaṣṭataraṃ vidyāc catuṣkaṃ kāmaje gaṇe || 7.50 ||**

divāsvapnādibhyo 'yaṃ catuṣko kaṣṭatara iti prasiddham itīdaṃ vyākhyeyam || 7.50 ||

	**daṇḍasya pātanaṃ caiva vākpāruṣyārthadūṣaṇe |**

**	krodhaje 'pi gaṇe vidyāt kaṣṭam etat trikaṃ sadā || 7.51 ||**

ayam api triko gaṇaḥ paiśunādibhyaḥ pāpīyān iti supratītam || 7.51 ||

	**saptakasyāsya vargasya sarvatraivānuṣaṅgiṇaḥ |**

**	pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ gurutaraṃ vidyād vyasanam ātmavān || 7.52 ||**

pānadyūtayoḥ pānaṃ garīyaḥ | tatra hi saṃjñāpraṇāśaḥ, anumattasyonmattatvam apretasya pretatvaṃ [kaupīnadarśanaṃ] śrutaprañāprahāṇaṃ mitrahāniḥ sadbhir viyogaḥ, asadbhiś ca prayogaḥ, gītādiṣu cārthaghneṣu prasaṅgaḥ, rahasyamantraprakāśaṃ madavegeneti pānadoṣāḥ | dyūte tu jitam evākṣaviduṣā anakṣajñasyāpi pākṣikaḥ parājayaḥ | dyūtastrīvyasanayoś ca dyūtaṃ garīyaḥ | yena tad eva jitadravyaṃ tasyāpy [āmiṣaṃ] bhavati, tathā tannimitto vairānubandhaḥ | jayaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ kevalaḥ parājayo 'nubhaktanāśaḥ | mūtrapurīṣavegadhāraṇāc ca śarīratantraśaithilyaṃ vyādhinidānam āsevanena kṣudrādibhiś ca pīḍātiśayena | mātary api ca mṛtāyāṃ dīvyaty eva kitavaḥ, kṛcchreṣu ca pṛcchyamānaḥ suhṛdbhir api kupyatīti dyūtadoṣāḥ | strīvyasane tv apatyotpattiḥ, pratikarmabhojanabhūyiṣṭgam (?) anusavanaṃ dharmārthaparigrahaḥ | śakyā ca strī rājahite niyoktum apavāhayituṃ vā | strīmṛgayāvyasanayoḥ strīvyasanaṃ garīyaḥ | adarśanaṃ kāryāṇām, strīvyasanāsaṅgeṣu rājakāryeṣu nirvedaḥ | kālātipātanam | dharmalopaḥ | pānadoṣānubandhaḥ | arthagheṣu ca nṛttādiṣu prasaṅga iti | mṛgāyāṃ tu vyāyāmaḥ pittaśleṣamedhaḥsvedādināśaḥ | cale sthire ca kāle lakṣaparicayaḥ | praharaṇavaiśāradyopajananaṃ grāmyajanaparicayaś ceti | evaṃ kāmajasya catuṣkasya svavarge pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ pāpīyaḥ | tatas teṣāṃ pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ yatnataḥ pariharet | krodhajasya tu trikasya daṇḍapātanavākpāruṣyayor daṇḍapātanaṃ garīyaḥ | daṇḍapātane hi śarīravināśād aśakyaṃ pratisandhānam, vākpāruṣye tv amarṣajaḥ krodhāgniḥ śakyate dānamānāmbhobhiḥ śamayitum | vākpāruṣyārthadūṣaṇayor vākpāruṣyaṃ garīyaḥ | tejasvino hi paruṣavacanasya cittasaṃkṣobhe bheṣajaṃ nāsādayanti | tathā ca pravādaḥ:

	sthiraṃ svādhim itaṃ gāḍhaṃ bhittvāstisaṃpraveśita 

	niḥśalyam aṅgān kṛntanti na vāco hṛdayād api ||

	saṃrohati śarair viddhaṃ vanaṃ paraśunā hatam

	vācā duruktaṃ bībhatsaṃ na rohati parikṣatam ||

bhāgyāyattatvād arthasya ca tejasvino 'rthadūṣaṇaṃ na gaṇayanti | evam evāsyāpi krodhajasya trikasya pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ garīya iti vyākhyātam || 7.52 ||

	**vyasanasya ca mṛtyoś ca vyasanaṃ kaṣṭam ucyate |**

**	vyasany adho hi vrajati svaryāty avyasanī mṛtaḥ || 7.53 ||**

vyasananindeyaṃ sāmānyatas tatparihārārtham | yady api mṛtyuvyasane sarvahare, tathāpy ayam anayor viśeṣaḥ: mṛtyur asminn eva loke sarvaharaḥ, vyasanaṃ punar ubhayor api lokayor iti | atha vā yathāśruta evāsya ślokasyārtho vacanīyaḥ | evaṃ ca bruvatā kāmakrodhajānāṃ puruṣadharmāṇāṃ vyasanībhūtānāṃ pratiṣedha ukto bhavati, na tv īṣad āsevanena | yenābhyasyāmānā hy ete vyasanībhūtā dharmārthaprāṇaharā bhavanti rājyatantraśaithilyan | api cātyantāsevanam apy uktam, rājña śakyaṃ ceti | yato vyasanākhyānām eṣāṃ pratiṣedhaḥ | evam avyasanasya rājño guṇavatsahāyasaṃpadartham amātyalakṣaṇam idam adhunocyate || 7.53 ||

	**maulāñ chāstravidaḥ śūrāṃl labdhalakṣān kulodgatān |**

**	sacivān sapta vāṣṭau vā prakurvīta parīkṣitān || 7.54 ||**

[mūlam] anvayam, anvayāgatā jānapadāś ca **maulāḥ** | **śāstravid**grahaṇena tu sarve 'mātyaguṇā gṛhyante, sāmarthyāt | tad yathā prājñaḥ svavagrahaḥ dhārayiṣṇur dakṣo vāgmī pragalbhaḥ pratipattimān utsāhaprabhāvayuktaḥ kleśasahaḥ śucir maitraḥ śīlabalāryoga[sattva]yuktaḥ stambhacāpalahīnas [saṃpriyo] vairā[ṇām akartety amātyasaṃpat | **śūra**śabdena rājakā]ryeṣu śarīrakalatrāpatyadhanādiṣv api nirapekṣo gamyate | atha vā prasiddhyapekṣa evāsyārthaḥ | **labdhalakṣa**grahaṇena ca paridṛṣṭābhyastatatkarmā gṛhyate | [kulodgatā hi sāmānyato 'kā]ryeṣu na pravartante | **saciva**śabdaḥ sahāyaparyāyaḥ | **saptāṣṭa**grahaṇaṃ niyamārtham | yenālpānām ekacittatādoṣaḥ, bahūnāṃ mantrabhedaḥ pakṣavi[bhāgat [?] | **suparīkṣitān** iti dharmārthakāmabhayopadhābhiḥ | seyaṃ parī]kṣocyate | purohitaḥ svalpe kārye rājñā vyājenākṣipto 'mṛṣyamāṇaḥ saśapatham ekaikam amātyam upajapet | "adhārmiko 'yaṃ rā[jā] | sādhu dhārmikam ekaṃ kulīnam avaruddham ekapragrahaṃ sāmantam āṭavikaṃ vā pratipādayāmaḥ | anyabhyaś ca mantribhya etad rocate | bhavatas tu katham" iti | pratyākhyāne dharmopadhāśuddhaḥ | senāpatir asatpratigraheṇāvakṣipto rājñā sarvapratyakṣaṃ bahunārthasaṃpradānenāptapuruṣair ekaikam amātyam upajaped rājavināśāya | "etac ca sarvamantribhyo rocate, atha kathaṃ bhavataḥ" iti | pratyākhyāne 'rthopadhāśuddhaḥ | parivrājikāntaḥpure labdhaviśvāsā ekaikam amātyam upajaped "rājamahiṣī bhavantaṃ kāmayate tatkṛtasamāgamopāyā ca" [iti pratyākhyāna (?) kāmopadhāśuddhaḥ | rājaprayuktā eva kecit puruṣāḥ pravādam āviṣkuryuḥ, "kṛtasamayair amātyāi rājā hanyate" iti | upalabdhapravāda] āptapuruṣaḥ kaścid amātyeṣu mantram avaśrāvayed "imaṃ pravādam upaśrutya bhavatāṃ nigraho rājñāvadhṛtaḥ" iti | teṣām eva cānyatamaḥ kṛtasaṃvitkaḥ pratyekaṃ tān rājāmātyeṣūtsāhayet | tatra ye pratyācakṣate te bhayopadhāśuddhāḥ |

	atha vā **maulāṃs** tāvat kuryād arthasamāhartṝn saṃnidhātṝn arthavyavahāriṇaḥ | **śāstravidaḥ** kuryāt prajñāsacivān | **śūrāṃs** tu daṇḍātiśayavyavahāriṇaḥ kuryāt | sarvāṃś caitān **labdhalakṣān** dṛṣṭaśaucānurāgasāmarthyān ity arthaḥ | **kulodgatān** iti caitat sarveṣāṃ pūrvaviśeṣaṇam | **sacivān sapta vāṣṭau veti** yathā saṃbhavaṃ rājakāryeṣu prasamīkṣya kuryāt | **suparīkṣitān** iti caitat sarvāmātyaviśeṣaṇam | katham | praṇidhibhiḥ sarvopadhāśuddhān ity arthaḥ| iyaṃ parīkṣā rājaviṣayād anyatra, na tu pūrvavat | itarathā hy etad eva śuddhibhede hetuḥ syāt | amātyānāṃ vyutpattāv amātyā nānākarmaprayojanā rājñā parigṛhyante || 7.54 || 

_yasmāt_,

	**api yat sukaraṃ karma tad apy ekena duṣkaram |**

**	viśeṣato 'sahāyena kim u rājyaṃ mahodayam || 7.55 ||**

evaṃ ca sati mantriṇām avidhānād anyatraita eva yathāsaṃbhavaṃ rājño mantriṇaḥ syuḥ | tathā ca kṛtvoktam eveti || 7.55

_tatra ye teṣāṃ mantrisacivaḥ,_

	**taiḥ sārdhaṃ cintayen nityaṃ sāmānyaṃ saṃdhivigraham |**

**	sthānaṃ samudayaṃ guptiṃ labdhapraśamanāni ca || 7.56 ||**

taiḥ saha saṃdhivgrahādau ṣāḍguṇye sāmānyaṃ guṇadoṣabalābalaṃ vicārayet | sa nātirahasyam | yat tv idaṃ kartavyāvadhāraṇaṃ paramarahasyaṃ tat svacittenaiva vyavasyet | evam asya rājñaḥ parapraṇeyatā na bhavati | kiṃ cānyat **sthānaṃ tais sārdhaṃ cintayed** iti vartate | tat punaś caturvidham: daṇḍakośapurarāṣṭrāṇi | tatra daṇḍo hastyaśvarathapadātayaḥ | teṣāṃ pratikarmapoṣaṇarakṣaṇādi cintyam | tathā kośasya hemarūpyabāhulyam āyavyayarakṣaṇāni ca cintyāni | tathā rāṣṭrasya deśaprayāyasya svājīva ātmasaṃdhāraṇaḥ parasaṃdhāraṇo, āpadi svārakṣyaḥ, paśavyaḥ śatrudveṣi sītāprāyo guptagocaraḥ, paśumān adevamātṛkaḥ, āpadi ca daṇḍakarasaha ity evamādi cintyam | purasya vakṣyati: tat syād āyudhasaṃpanna ity evamādi |

	atha vā **sthānaṃ** svadeśād apracyavanam | evaṃ samudayāś cintyāḥ | te ca kṛṣir vrajo gulmasthānaṃ vaṇikpathaḥ śulkadaṇḍa ity evamādayaḥ | **guptiṃ** svarāṣṭragatāṃ vakṣyati | **labdhapraśamanāni** devatāśramavidvyāvatāṃ dhārmikāṇāṃ ca śūrāṇāṃ ca dānamānatyāgāyogaḥ | ucitānāṃ cābhyanujñānam | sarvabandhanamokṣaḥ | anugraho dīnānāthavyādhitānām | utsavānāṃ cāpūrvāṇāṃ prava[rtanaṃ, pravṛttānām anuvṛttiḥ | yac ca kośa]daṇḍopaghātakam adhārmikaṃ vā cāritraṃ tad apanīya dharmavyavahāraṃ sthāpayet | āha ca: "cāritram [akṛtaṃ dharmyaṃ kṛtaṃ cānyaiḥ pravartayet, pravartayen na cādharmyaṃ kṛtaṃ cānyair nivartayet" iti | evaṃ] sthānādīni cintyāni || 7.56 ||

	**teṣāṃ svaṃ svam abhiprāyam upalabhya pṛthak pṛthak |**

**	smastānāṃ ca kāryeṣu vidadhyād dhitam ātmanaḥ || 7.57 ||**

parataḥ prajñām upāditsamānas tān mantri[ṇa ekaikaśaḥ pṛcchet] samastāṃś ca | yatkāraṇaṃ kaścid dhi puruṣaḥ pariṣady apratibhānavān bhavati, rahasi ca pragalbhaḥ pariṣadi ca ghaṭṭitaprajño bhavati | yatas tān apakṣyobhayathā pṛcchet | te yad uktavantas tad vyavasyet, tadanyatamopadiṣṭaṃ yāvad apratyanīkaṃ nirdoṣaṃ ca || 7.57 ||

	**sarveṣāṃ tu viśiṣṭena brāhmaṇena vipaścitā |**

**	mantrayeta paraṃ mantraṃ rājā ṣāṅguṇyasaṃyutam [?] || 7.58 ||**

adhikataraprajño hi brāhmaṇo dhārmikatvāc ca nirdoṣatayā viśvasanīyaḥ || 7.58 ||

_evaṃ ca sati,_

	**nityaṃ tasmin samāśvastaḥ sarvakāryāṇi nikṣipet |**

**	tena sārdhaṃ viniścitya tataḥ karma samācaret || 7.59 ||**

**	anyān api prakurvīta śucīn prājñān avasthitān |**

**	samyag arthasamāhartṝn amātyān suparīkṣitān || 7.60 ||**

mantriguṇayuktān etān api kuryāt sarvopadhābhidṛṣṭatayā ca **suparīkṣitān** | **arthasaamāhartṝn** saṃnidhātṝn [saptāṣṭau] vā saṃkhyāniyamāpavādo 'yaṃ rājasahāyānām ucyate || 7.60 ||

	**nivartetāsya yāvadbhir itikartavyatā nṛbhiḥ |**

**	tāvato 'tandritān dakṣān prakurvīta vicakṣaṇān || 7.61 ||**

kāryaparimāṇenāiṣāṃ rājñaḥ sacivānāṃ saṃgrahaḥ syāt | yatkāraṇaṃ kāryasamāveśād anyenopayogena hi kaścid viṣādaṃ gacchet, samartho 'pi ca pramādyati || 7.61 ||

	**teṣām arthe niyuñjīta śūrān dakṣān kulodgatān |**

**	śucīn ākarakarmānte bhīrūn antarniveśane || 7.62 ||**

**teṣām arthe** śucayo 'rthasyāyavyayayoḥ sthāpyāḥ | dṛṣṭakarmatayāviṣādinaḥ **śūrā** balādhyakṣā bhīravas tu bhojanādau niyoktavyāḥ | sarve caite **dakṣāḥ** karyāḥ, te hi dvandvopanipātān aparigaṇayyotthānaśīlatayā svāminaḥ kāryakālaṃ nātipātayanti || 7.62 ||

	**dūtaṃ caiva prakurvīta sarvaśāstraviśāradam |**

**	iṅgitākāraceṣṭajñaṃ śuciṃ dakṣaṃ kulodgatam || 7.63 ||**

**dūto** 'mātyaguṇasaṃpadupetaḥ kāryaḥ, **sarvaśāstraviśārado**padeśāt | imāś **ceṅgitākāraceṣṭā** dūtenāvaśyaṃ veditavyāḥ | paraviṣaye rājñaḥ | tatra saṃdhitsata imānīṅgitāni dūtasyādareṇa samp[arigrahaḥ, viśvasanam, muhuḥ saṃpūjanam, tadvākyasya cānasūyābhinandanam | etāny eva viparyastāni vijighṛkṣataḥ | **ākāraḥ** khalu śarīragataḥ, mlānamukhatā varṇaviparyayaḥ | tūṣṇīṃbhāvo dīrghoṣṇaniśvāsādiḥ śarīravikāro dainyaṃ sūcayati | prasannamukhatā vākyavaiśāradyaṃ śarīrasaṃskāra ity evamādi harṣam sūcayati | ceṣṭāsu karmasv anabhyutthānaṃ dainyam āviṣkaroti kāryavyāpadviṣādānugatam, abhyutthānaṃ punar harṣaṃ viparyaye | **śucitvam** asya dūtasya strīgate 'rthagate [ca] | sa ca viśeṣeṇopadiśyate | strīsaṃbandhe mantrabhedaḥ paribhavaś cārthagrahaṇe kāryahāniḥ | **kulodgata**prayojanam uktam || 7.63 ||

_kasya punar hetor ādareṇa dūtalakṣaṇam idaṃ kathyate, yasmāt |_

	**anuraktaḥ śucir dakṣaḥ smṛtimān deśakālavit |**

**	vapuṣmān vītabhīr vāgmī dūto rājñaḥ praśasyate || 7.64 ||**

**anurakto** 'hāryo bhavati | **śucir** arthe strīṣu cābhedyo bhavati | **dakṣo** deśakālau nātikrāmati | **smṛtimān** svāmisaṃdeśam aparimuṣitasmṛtiprasaṅgena kathayati | **deśakālavit** sarvatra kāryasādhakaḥ | **vapuṣmān** anādhṛṣyo bhavati, priyadarśanatvāc ca grāhyavāk | **vītabhīḥ** svāmisaṃdeśaṃ paruṣam apy avitatham ācaṣṭe | paunaḥ punyena | **vāgmī** saṃdeśasyottaraprativacanasamartho bhavati | kimartham ayaṃ dūtalakṣaṇādaropadeśa evaṃ kriyate || 7.64 ||

	**amātye daṇḍa āyatto daṇḍe vainayikī kriyā |**

**	nṛpatau kośarāṣṭre tu dūte saṃdhiviparyayau || 7.65 ||**

yathā balādhikṛte hastyaśvādibalam **ā[yattam** . . . rājasamudyamena rāṣṭram a]bhiprāyeṇa vardhate, tad upekṣayā ca kṣīyate | evaṃ **dūte** saṃdhivigrahāv āyattāv it bhūtārthasaṃbandhenaiṣā dūtastutiḥ | yataś caitad eva matam || 7.65 ||

	**dūta eva [hi saṃdhatte bhinatty eva ca saṃhatān |**

**	dūtas tat kurute] karma yena bhidyeta mānavāḥ || 7.66 ||**

mantrasya hi bhedena saṃvaraṇena cedam ubhayaṃ karotīty ucyata iti || 7.66 ||

	**sa vidyād asya kṛtyeṣu nigūḍheṅgitaceṣṭitaiḥ |**

**	[ākāram iṅgit]taṃ ceṣṭāṃ bhṛtyeṣu ca rājaśatruṣu || 7.67 ||**

**	buddhvā ca sarvaṃ tattvena pararājacikīrṣitam |**

sādhvasādhu vā sabhṛtyavargasya

	**tathā prayatnam ātiṣṭhed yathātmānaṃ na pīḍayet || 7.68 ||**

svāmino 'pīḍayā saṃdhivigrahādi pratipattavyaṃ dūtena | tathā rājadhānīm anujñātaḥ praviśet | āṭavikāntapālaiḥ saha saṃdadhyāt | yuddhoparodhabhūmim avekṣeta | durgarāṣṭrapramāṇaṃ sāraṃ copalebheta | prāṇābādhe 'pi ca śāsanaṃ yathoktaṃ brūyāt | pūjayā notsiktaḥ syāt | vākyam aniṣṭaṃ saheta | pānaṃ varjayet | kṛtyapkṣān upajapet | anurāgāparāgau ca yātavyaprakṛtīnāṃ vidyāt | svabalaparimāṇaṃ ca nācakṣīta, kenacid ajñānavikṣepādinā vyājena | yac cānyad api yātavyārambhasahakāri tat sarvaṃ bandhuratnāpaharaṇaṃ cārajñānādi cānutiṣṭhet || 7.68 ||

	**jāṅgalaṃ sasyasaṃpannam āryaprāyam anāvilam |**

**	ramyam ānatasāmantaṃ svājīvyaṃ deśam āvaset || 7.69 ||**

jāṅlgalaṃ nānāvidhadhānyamūlaphalapuṣpatṛṇendhanahetum | **sasyasaṃpannaṃ** durbhikṣarahitam | **āryaprāyaṃ** brāhmaṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ dharmādiparipālananimittam | **anāvilaṃ** śvāpadasarīsṛpataskaradaṃśamaśakādibhir anākulam | **ramyaṃ** sarvartukusumasamṛddhapādapodyānādibhiḥ | **ānatasāmantaṃ** prahvībhūtavinatasāmantam | **svājīvyaṃ** prasannasalilajalāśayam ativiśaṃkaṭagṛhaprāsādamālinam | ebhiś ca jāṅgalādibhir anyaiś ca deśaguṇaiḥ saṃpannaṃ **deśam āvaset** || 7.69 ||

	**dhanvadurgaṃ mahīdurgam abdurgaṃ vārkṣam eva vā |**

**	nṛdurgaṃ giridurgaṃ vā samāśrityāvaset puram || 7.70 ||**

prākāreṇa veṣṭitaṃ viṣkambhadviguṇotsedhenaiṣṭikena śailena vā dvādaśahast[ād ūrdhvam u]cchritena tālamūlena kapiśīrṣacitāgreṇa . . . dṛḍhavapreṇa pariṣkṛtaṃ **mahīdurgam** | agādhenānāsrāvaṇīyena codakena pariveṣṭitam **abdurgam** | samantato 'rdhayojanamātraṃ ghanamahāvṛkṣacitaṃ **vārkṣadurgam** | caturaṅgabalādhiṣṭhitaṃ pravarāyudhīyapuruṣaprāyaṃ **nṛdurgam** | giripṛṣṭaṃ durāroham ekamārgānugatam [antar]nadīprasravaṇodamaṃ **giridurgam** || 7.70 ||

	**sarveṇa tu prayatnena giridurgaṃ samāśrayet |**

**	eṣāṃ hi bāhuguṇyena giridurgaṃ viśiṣyate || 7.71 ||**

**eṣāṃ** durgāṇām anādhṛṣyatamatvād giridurgaṃ śreṣṭham || 7.71 ||

	**trīṇyādyāny āśritās tv eṣāṃ mṛgagartāśrayāpcarāḥ |**

**	trīṇy uttarāṇi kramaśaḥ plavaṅgamanarāmarāḥ || 7.72 ||**

**	yathā durgāśritān etān nopahiṃsanti śatravaḥ |**

**	tathārayo na hiṃsanti nṛpaṃ durgasamāśrayam || 7.73 ||**

dṛṣṭānatślokāv ādarapratipattyarthau || 7.72–73 ||

	**ekaḥ śataṃ yodhayati prākārastho dhanurdharaḥ |**

**	śataṃ daśasahasrāṇi tasmād durgaṃ vidhīyate || 7.74 ||**

pratyakṣaphalatvaṃ mahīdurgasya darśayati | evaṃ ca tasmin tasmin durge guṇo veditavyaḥ || 7.74 ||

	**tat syād āyudhasaṃpannaṃ dhanadhānyena vāhanaiḥ |**

**	brāḥmaṇaiḥ śilpibhir yantrair yavasenodakena ca || 7.75 ||**

durgoparodhakālaprayojanavatāṃ pradarśanārthaḥ ślokaḥ | evaṃ ca saty anyad api yat kālaprayojanaṃ vadhaśalyaviṣavaidyamauhūrtikādi tad api grāhyam || 7.75 ||

	**tasya madhye suparyāptaṃ kārayed gṛham ātmanaḥ |**

**	guptaṃ sarvartukaṃ śubhraṃ jalavṛkṣasamanvitam || 7.76 ||**

ātmatantrānurūpam asaṃbādhaṃ yathartusthānaṃ suruṅgādiyuktaṃ ca **gṛhaṃ kārayet** || 7.76 ||

	**tad adhyāsyodvahed bhāryāṃ savarṇāṃ lakṣaṇānvitām |**

**	kule mahati saṃbhūtāṃ hṛdyāṃ rūpaguṇānvitām || 7.77 ||**

rājyatantrasahāyārthaṃ mahataḥ kulād ity etatsaṃbandhena savarṇādīnām uktānām anuvādaḥ || 7.77 ||

	**purohitaṃ ca kurvīta vṛṇuyād eva cartvijaḥ |**

**	te 'sya gṛhyāṇi karmāṇi kuryur vaitānikāni ca || 7.78 ||**

amātyaguṇair brāhmaṇaguṇaiś ca yuktaḥ puro[hitaḥ s]yāt | ṛtvijas tu brāhmaṇaguṇayuktā eva || 7.78 ||

	**yajeta rājā kratubhir vividhair āptadakṣiṇaiḥ |**

**	dharmārthaṃ caiva viprebhyo dadyād bhogān dhanāni ca || 7.79 ||**

ime adhike yāgadāne rājño vidhīyete | nityavad evānayor apy akaraṇe pratyavāya eva || 7.79 ||

	**sāṃvatsarikam āptaiś ca rāṣṭrād āhārayed balim |**

**	syāc cāmnāyaparo loke varteta pitṛvan nṛṣu || 7.80 ||**

yathoktebhya āyasthānebhya āmnāyaprāmāṇyena ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamabhāgagrahaṇādinā **balim āhārayet** | [karadeṣv anyeṣu ca **pitṛvat**] syāt |

	**adhyakṣān vividhān kuryāt tatra tatra vipaścitaḥ |**

**	te 'sya sarvāṇy avekṣeran nṝṇāṃ kāryāṇi kurvatām || 7.81 ||**

suvarṇakoṣṭhāgārapṇyakupyāyudhatulāśulkanauhastyaśvarathapadāty**adhyakṣā**dīn **vividhān vipaścitaḥ** sthāpayet | sarva ete amātyaguṇasaṃpadyuktā vijñeyāḥ || 7.81 ||

	**āvṛttānāṃ gurukulād viprāṇāṃ pūjako bhavet |**

**	nṛpāṇām akṣayo hy eṣa nidhir brāhmo vidhīyate || 7.82 ||**

idam api snātakebhyo niyamadānaṃ rājño **vidhīyate** | etebhyo 'pi hy adadataḥ pratyavāyaḥ | tathā coktam "aditsaṃs tyāgam arhati" (MDh 10.113) iti || 7.82 ||

	**na taṃ stenā na cāmitrā haranti na ca naśyati |**

**	tasmād rājñā nidhātavyo brāhmaṇeṣv akṣayo nidhiḥ || 7.83 ||**

yathā stenā āṭavikā amitrā nṛpadravyāpahāriṇaḥ na tathā brāhmaṇādibhyo hiraṇyādidānena nidheḥ kutaścid vināśa ity arthavādo 'yaṃ niyatadānastutyarthaḥ || 7.84 ||

_ayaṃ cānyaḥ |_

	**na skandate na vyathate na ca naśyti karhicit |**

**	variṣṭham agnihotrebhyo brāhmaṇasya mukhe hutam || 7.84 ||**

yathā skannā āhutir doṣāya pātrabhedāc ca vyathitā, avijñātadevatā ca yathā yathānaśyati | tathā ca brāhmaṇam "ardhā ha vā eṣāhutir yā devatām avijñāya hutā" | evaṃ ca sati yā āhuter doṣatrayeṇa nindā sā prakṛtabrāhmaṇadānastutyarthā | tathā coktam "variṣṭham agnihotrebhyaḥ" iti | agnihotrebhyo 'gnihotrādibhya ity arthaḥ | sarvaṃ nityakarmopasaṃgrahārtham etad evaṃ vijñeyam | **mukha**grahaṇāc cānnadānam iti kecid āhuḥ | tad ayuktam | "pāṇyāsyo hi dvijaḥ smṛtaḥ" (MDh 4.117) iti vacanāt, sarvapratigrahaviṣayam etad vijñeyam || 7.84 ||

_idaṃ cānyat |_

	**samam abrāḥmaṇe dānaṃ dviguṇaṃ brāhmaṇabruve |**

**	sahasraguṇam ācārye tv anantaṃ vedapārage || 7.85 ||**

itaś caitebhyo deyam | guṇavatsnātakabrāhmaṇaniyamadānastutiprakaraṇād **abrāhmaṇā**digrahaṇam idaṃ vidvaddānapraśaṃsārthaṃ veditavyam | kathaṃ kṛtvā | abrāhmaṇabrāhmaṇabruvor nopapadyate | uktaṃ ca:

	vedavidyāvratasnātāñ śrotriyān gṛham āgatān |

	pūjayed dhavyakavyābhyāṃ viparītāṃs tu varjayet || iti | (MDh 8.63)

na cāyaṃ phalavidhiḥ, phalavidhau hi kāmyadānasya syād | evaṃ ca yathoktārthasāmarthyān nāyaṃ phalavidhiḥ kalpopadeśārthaḥ ślokaḥ | anyathā hi prakaraṇam uparudhyeteti | atha vā yathokte dīnānātanimitte abrāhmaṇādidāne pātraviśeṣāt phalaviśeṣapradarśanārthaḥ syād ayaṃ rājñāṃ viśeṣadharmaḥ | yatkāraṇaṃ na hy akasmāt praśaṃsā syād iti || 7.85 ||

_tathā cottaraślokaḥ|_

	**pātrasya hi viśeṣeṇa śraddadhānatayaiva ca |**

**	alpaṃ vā bahu vā pretya dānasyāvāpyate phalam || 7.86 ||**

evaṃ ca sati yathā pātraviśeṣāt phalaviśeṣaḥ, evaṃ dāne samānebhyo 'pi brāhmaṇebhya iti pātraviśeṣāpavādo 'yaṃ vijñeyaḥ | pūrvaślokārthasya tu dvitīyasyedam adhunā vivaraṇaṃ kriyate | na ca deyadravyasya phalena jātitaḥ sāmyam, na ca parimāṇato yujyate, śāśtravirodhān nyāyavirodhāc ca | kathaṃ tarhi idaṃ samaṃ vyākaraṇīyam | lokaprasiddhyā notkṛṣṭaṃ na ca nikṛṣṭam | yat tatsamaṃ tathā ca lokaprasiddhamevāvadhiṃ kṛtvā dvaiguṇyādayo vaktavyāḥ | anye tu manyante na deyadravyasya samaṃ phalaṃ ghaṭate | tasmād dātṛgataṃ sāmyaṃ pratyetavyam | abrāhmaṇāya datvā bhikṣādy api mānuṣaśarīreṇaiva taddānopaphalopabhogaṃ prāpnoti, notkṛṣṭapātradānāt | tad etad vicāraṇīyam | abrāhmaṇau ca kṣatriyavaiśyau | tathā ca gautamīye bhikṣādānaprakaraṇa etad uktam | brāhmaṇavarṇād anantarau ca tau | prayogaś ca "abrāhmaṇād vidyopayogaḥ" (GDh 7.1) iti | na ca śūdrād abrāhmaṇād vidyopayogaḥ | arthalobhāc chāstrapratiṣedhāc ca | brāhmaṇajāte . . . niteneti | kṣatriyavaiśyayos tu brahmacaāriṇor iṣyata eva bhaikṣādipratigrahopadeśasāmarthyād evaṃ cābrāhmaṇaśabdena tāv api yukta[taraṃ vijñeyau] || 7.86 ||

	**samottamādhamai rājā tv āhūtaḥ pālayan prajāḥ |**

**	na nivarteta saṃgrāmāt kṣatradharmam anusmaran || 7.87 ||**

āhūtasya [yena] kenāpi saṃgrāmād anivṛttiḥ syāt, yatkāraṇam eṣa hi rājñāṃ viśiṣṭo dharmaḥ || 7.87 ||

_yat_ |

	**saṃgrāmeṣv anivartitvaṃ prajānāṃ caiva pālanam |**

**	śuśrūṣā brāhmaṇānāṃ ca rājñāṃ śreyaskaraṃ param || 7.88 ||**

yathā prajāpālanabrāhmaṇaśuśrūṣaṇe rājñāṃ viśiṣṭo dharma, evaṃ saṃgrāmeṣv anivartitvam ity anivṛttistutiḥ || 7.88 ||

_tathā cāha |_

	**āhaveṣu mitho 'nyonyaṃ jighāṃsanto mahīkṣitaḥ |**

**	yudhyamānāḥ paraṃ śaktyā svargaṃ yānty aparāṅmukhāḥ || 7.89 ||**

ataś ca saṃgrāmād anivartitvaṃ rājñāṃ viśeṣadharmaḥ | tasya ca yudhyato niyamaḥ śiṣyate ca || 7.89 ||

	**na kūṭair āyudhair hanyād yudhyamāno raṇe ripūn |**

**	na karṇibhir nāpi dagdhair nāgnijvalitatejanaiḥ || 7.90 ||**

**	na ca hanyāt sthalārūḍhaṃ na klībaṃ na kṛtāñjalim |**

**	na muktakeśaṃ nāsīnaṃ na tavāsmīti vādinam || 7.91 ||**

**	na suptaṃ na visannāhaṃ na nagnaṃ na nirāyudham |**

**	nāyudhyamānaṃ paśyantaṃ na pareṇa samāgatam || 7.92 ||**

**	nāyudhavyasanaprāptaṃ nārtaṃ nātiparīkṣitam |**

**	na bhītaṃ na parāvṛttaṃ satāṃ dharmam anusmaran || 7.93 ||**

saṃgrāmaniyamavidhir ayam, teṣāṃ hatipratyavāyārtham || 7.90–93 ||

	**yas tu bhītaḥ parāvṛttaḥ saṃgrāme hanyate paraiḥ |**

**	bhartur yad duṣkṛtaṃ kiṃcit tat sarvaṃ pratipadyate || 7.94 ||**

**	yac cāsya sukṛtaṃ kiṃcid amutrārtham upārjitam |**

**	bhartā tat sarvam ādatte parāvṛttahatasya tu || 7.95 ||**

rājño 'nyasyāpi daṇḍapuruṣasya parāvṛttasy nindā ślokadvayenoktā, yuktā ca tannindā | yadartham asau hriyate tad akurvan pratyavety eva || 7.94–95 ||

	**rathāśvaṃ hastinaṃ chatraṃ dhanadhānyaṃ paśūn striyaḥ |**

**	sarvadravyāṇi kupyaṃ ca yo yaṃ jayati tasya tat || 7.96 ||**

svāmitvād rājagrahaṇanivṛttyartho niyamaḥ || 7.96 ||

	**rājñas tu dadyād uddhāram ity eṣā vaidikī śrutiḥ |**

**	rājñā ca sarvayodhebhyo dātavyam apṛthagjitam || 7.97 ||**

uddhāropariṣṭhadravyaṃ **sarvayodhebhyo** rājñā ādeyam | vaidikī śrutir "mahendram uddhāram udaharat vṛtraṃ hatvā" ityādi | apṛthagjitaṃ samūhajitaṃ yat, tataḥ sarvayodhebhyo yuddhavyāyāmakleśānurūpaṃ deyam || 7.97 ||

	**eṣo 'nupaskṛtaḥ prokto yaudhadharmaḥ sanātanaḥ |**

**	asmād dharmān na cyaveta kṣatriyo ghnan raṇe ripūn || 7.98 ||**

anupaskṛtaḥ akṛtaḥ svabhāvasiddhaguṇa ity arthaḥ | viguṇam upaskriyate guṇādhānārtham | upasaṃhārārthaślokaḥ || 7.98 ||

	**alabdhaṃ caiva lipseta labdhaṃ rakṣec ca yatnataḥ |**

**	rakṣitaṃ vardhayec cainaṃ vṛddhaṃ pātreṣu nikṣipet || 7.99 ||**

[**lipsetā**]lipsamānaḥ saṃtuṣṭaḥ san rājā sapatnair mahadbhir dāyādair vardhamānair ucchidyetālpatantratvād, arjitaṃ cārakṣan kevalenārjitakleśena phalarahitena saṃkṣipyate, **rakṣitaṃ** ca samyag avardhayan kṣīyate | tadupayuñjāno 'nyasyābhāvāt tadārjitaṃ rakṣitaṃ vardhitaṃ ca yan mahatā yatnatrayeṇa tadaprayacchan pātrebhyaḥ paralokād dhīyate | niṣkā[matayāsyaiva yatna]trayasādhyaṃ kleśatrayam āpadyate || 7.99 ||

	**etac caturvidhaṃ vidyāt puruṣārthaprayojanam |**

**	asya nityam anuṣṭhānaṃ samyak kuryād atandritaḥ || 7.100||**

**	alabdham icched daṇḍena labdhaṃ rakṣed avikṣayā |**

**	rakṣitaṃ vardhayed vṛddhyā vṛddhaṃ pātreṣu nikṣipet || 7.101 ||**

atra vṛddhyartham upāyo vṛddhiśabdenocyate, prakaraṇasāmarthyāt | **[caturvidha]nirdeśaḥ ** dānena **pātreṣu nikṣipet** | [**caturvidha**]nirdeśaḥ **puruṣārtha**siddhaye rājñaḥ || 7.100–01 ||

_yata etad evam, ataḥ |_

	**nityam udyatadaṇḍaḥ syān nityaṃ vivṛtapauruṣaḥ |**

**	nityaṃ saṃvṛtasaṃcāro nityaṃ chidrānusāry areḥ || 7.102 ||**

hastyādibalaṃ yogyādibhir nityam abhivinayet, śastrāvaraṇe ca saṃskuryāt | satatam evam asyodyatdaṇḍatā rājamaṇḍale prakāśībhavati | saṃdhipālāṭavīsthānādiṣu cāptapuruṣopagṛhītaiḥ saṃnaddhaiḥ kavacibhiḥ satataṃ jāgaritavyam | evam asya **vivṛtapauruṣa**tāvirbhavati | kṛtyapakṣasya ca rakṣaṇopagrahābhyāṃ [**saṃvṛtasaṃcāro**] bavat | parakṛtyadūṣaṇena carichidrānusārī syāt || 7.102 ||

	**nityam udyatadaṇḍasya kṛtsnam udvijate jagat |**

**	tasmāt sarvāṇi bhūtāni daṇḍenaiva prasādhayet || 7.103 ||**

**udyatadaṇḍasyā**yatnenaiva śatrūpa[natir bhavati] || 7.103 ||

	**amāyayaiva varteta na kathaṃcana māyayā |**

**	buddhyetāriprayuktāṃ tu māyāṃ nityaṃ susaṃvṛtaḥ || 7.104 ||**

kruddhalubdhabhītamāninām anyarājaprakṛtīnām upajāpaṃ pūrvaṃ na kuryāt | ātmīy[aviṣaye paraviṣaye ca pravṛtta]dharmasya dhārmikatvāt sarvaṃ praty anurāgaḥ sulabhaḥ | tatra vipralabdhas tulyakāriṇaḥ śilpe copakāre ca vimānito vallabhāvaruddhaḥ pravāsitabandhuḥ m[ithyācāravāri]taḥ sakulyair antarhitaḥ sarvasvam āhārita ity evamādiḥ kruddhavargaḥ | pāpakarmā tulyadoṣadaṇdodvigno 'nantarabhūmir daṇḍopanataḥ sarvādhikaraṇasthaḥ sahasopacitārtha ity evamādir bhnāsya chidraṃ ītavargaḥ | [parikṣīnaḥ] kadaryo vyasanīty evamādir lubdhavargaḥ | ātmasaṃbhāvitaḥ śatrupūjāmarṣito nīcair upahatas tīkṣṇaḥ sāhasiko bhogenāsantuṣṭa ity evamādir mānivargaḥ | etān parasyātmanaś ca buddhvā saṃrakṣed upajapec ca || 7.104 ||

	**nāsya chidraṃ paro vidyād vidyāc chidraṃ parasya tu |**

**	gūhet kūrma ivāṅgāni rakṣed vivaram ātmanaḥ || 7.105 ||**

abhiyogātiśayena svachidragūhanaṃ parachidradarśanaṃ ca śakyate kartum | tac ca svaviṣaye gūḍhapuruṣāṇāṃ kāpaṭikādīnāṃ saṃcāreṇa vijānīyāt paraviṣaye ceti || 7.105 ||

	**bakavac cintayed arthān śaśavac ca viniṣpatet |**

**	vṛkavac cāvalumpeta siṃhavac ca parākramet || 7.106 ||**

yathā apdurgāśrayaṃ matsyabalaṃ svabhāvatas tadgrahaṇārthaṃ **bakaḥ** paryupāsanayā tadgrahaṇopāyaṃ dhyānayogād āsādayati, evam arthacintābhiyogātiśayena suduṣprāpā apy arthā āsādyanta iti matvā na nirvedaṃ gacchet | yathā **śaśo** 'lpakāyatvāc chaknoti viniṣpatitum arigaṅghād api, tathaiko 'py asahāyaḥ sarvataḥ samutthitasāmantaprakopo 'śakto 'vasthātum, durgaparisaṃgrahaṃ kṛtvā tasmān niṣpatet guṇavatisaṃśrayārthī | yathā ca vṛkaḥ paśugrahaṇābhiyogāt pālapramādam āsādyāvaluṃpate, evaṃ svārakṣāpara it kṛtvā tadgrahaṇābhhiyogo na moktavyo, bhaviṣyati sa kālaḥ, yatrāyaṃ vṛkavad alalumpiṣyate | yathā ca **siṃho** mahākāyān api hatyādīn parākramyotsāhaśaktyāyogād dhanti, evaṃ mahad aribalam iti kṛtvā na bhettavyam | mahad apy alpaprāṇam alpena mahāprāṇena hanyata iti || 7.106 ||

	**evaṃ vijayamānasya ye 'sya syuḥ paripanthinaḥ |**

**	tān ānayed vaśaṃ sarvān sāmādibhir upakramaiḥ || 7.107 ||**

evaṃ vijaye sthitasya rājño ye pratāpena nopanameran tān paścāt sāmādibhir vaśīkuryāt || 7.107 ||

	**yadi te tu na tiṣṭheyur upāyaiḥ prathamaiś tribhiḥ |**

**	daṇḍena tu prasahyaitāṃś chanakair vaśam ānayet || 7.108 ||**

sāmādhyupāyatrayaparikṣaye daṇḍasya prayoganiyamaḥ || 7.108 ||

	**sāmādīnām upāyānāṃ caturṇām api paṇḍitāḥ |**

**	sāmadaṇḍau praśaṃsanti nityaṃ rāṣṭrābhivṛddhaye || 7.109 ||**

sāmaprayoge kṣayavyayāyāsā na bhavanti, daṇḍe tu sarvasiddhir eva tatpratāpād, atas tāv atra praśastau || 7.110 ||

_asya dṛṣṭāntaḥ |_

	**yathā hanti ca nirdātā kakṣaṃ dhānyaṃ ca rakṣati |**

**	tathā rakṣen nṛpo rāṣṭraṃ hanyāc ca paripanthinaḥ || 7.110 ||**

**	mohād rājā ca rāṣṭraṃ yaḥ karśayaty anapakṣayā |**

**	so 'cirād bhraśyate rāṣṭrāj jīvitāc ca sabāndhavaḥ || 7.111 |||**

**	śarīrakarśanāt prāṇāḥ kṣīyante prāṇināṃ yathā |**

**	tathā rājñām api prāṇāḥ kṣīyante rāṣṭrakarśanāt || 7 112 ||**

rāṣṭraṃ hi tasya śarīram iti | yataś caitad evam atas taddoṣaparyudāsāya || 7.11012 ||

	**rāṣṭrasya saṃgrahe nityaṃ vidhānam idam ācaret |**

**	susaṃgṛhītarāṣṭro hi pārthivaḥ sukham edhate || 7.113 ||**

**	dvayos trayāṇāṃ pañcānāṃ madhye gulmam adhiṣṭhitam |**

**	tathā grāmaśatānāṃ ca kuryād rāṣṭrasya guptaye || 7.114 ||**

rājabhāvyasaṃgrahārthaṃ rakṣārthaṃ ca || 7.113–14 ||

	**grāmasyādhipatiṃ kuryād daśagrāmapatiṃ tathā |**

**	viṃśatīśaṃ śateśaṃ ca sahasrapatim eva ca || 7.115 ||**

**	grāme doṣān smutpannān grāmikaḥ śanakaiḥ svayam |**

**	śaṃsed grāmadaśeśāya daśeśo viṃśatīśine || 7.116 ||**

**	viṃśatīśas tu tatsarvaṃ śateśāya nivedayet |**

**	śaṃsed grāmaśateśas tu sahasrapataye svayam || 7.117 ||**

āsannakāryajñāpanārthaṃ grāmādiṣv adhipatikriyās tribhiḥ ślokaiḥ || 7.115–17 ||

	**yāni rājñaḥ pradeyāni [pratyahaṃ grāmavāsibhiḥ |**

**	annapānedndhanādī]ni grāmikas tāny avāpnuyāt || 7.118 ||**

**	daśī kulaṃ tu bhuñjīta viṃśī pañcakulāni tu |**

**	grāmaṃ grāmaśatādhyakṣaḥ sahasrādhipatiḥ puram || 7.119 ||**

adhipatīnām iyaṃ vṛttikalpanā śloka[dvayena] || 7.118–19 ||

	**teṣāṃ grāmyāni kāryāṇi pṛthakkāryāṇi caiva ha |**

**	rājño 'nyaḥ sacivaḥ snigdhas tāni paśyed atandritaḥ || 7.120 ||**

adhipatīnāṃ kartā kṛtitas tatkṛtākṛtam anupaśyet || 7.120 ||

	**nagare nagare [caikaṃ kuryāt sarvarthacintakam |**

**	uccaiḥ sthānaṃ] ghorarūpaṃ nakṣatrāṇām iva graham || 7.121 ||**

hastyaśvādi[bala]saṃpannaṃ pratinagaraṃ nāgarikaṃ sthāpayet || 7.121 ||

	**sa tān anuparikrāmet sarvān eva sadā svayam |**

**	teṣāṃ vṛttaṃ pariṇayet [samyag rāṣṭreṣu taccaraiḥ] || 7.122 ||**

ayam adhipatīn sadā parikrāmet parirakṣaṇāya, teṣāṃ ca vṛttaṃ rāja[caraiḥ] kāpaṭikādibhyā āgamayet || 7.122 ||

_yatkāraṇam |_

	**rājño hi rakṣādhikṛtāḥ parasvādāyinaḥ śaṭhāḥ |**

**	bhṛtyā bhavanti prāyeṇa tebhyo rakṣed imāḥ prajāḥ || 7.123 ||**

śucayo 'py adhikṛtā bhakṣayanti vittānīty arthatvān manuṣyāṇām | ato na śucyanumānopekṣaṇīyās ta iti || 7.123 ||

	**ye kāryakebhyo 'rtham eva gṛhṇīyuḥ pāpacetasaḥ |**

**	teṣāṃ sarvasvam ādāya rājā kuryāt pravāsanam || 7.124 ||**

jñātavyatikramāṇāṃ rājādhikṛtānāṃ sarvasvādānapravāsane kāreyet, janapadarakṣārthīty arthaḥ || 7.124 ||

	**rājakarmasu yuktānāṃ strīṇāṃ preṣyajanasya ca |**

**	pratyahaṃ kalpayed vṛttiṃ sthānakarmānurūpataḥ || 7.125 ||**

vastrasaṃskārādyupalepanabhojanādilakṣaṇety arthaḥ|| 7.125 ||

	**paṇo deyo 'vakṛṣṭasya ṣaḍ utkṛṣṭasya bhaktakam |**

**	ṣaṇmāsikas tathācchādo dhānyaṃ droṇaś ca māsikaḥ || 7.126 ||**

bhaktaparkḷptiḥ ślokadvayena | paṇadroṇayoḥ parimāṇaṃ vakṣyati || 7.126 ||

	**krayavikrayam adhvānaṃ bhaktāñ ca saparivyayam |**

**	yogakṣemaṃ ca saṃprekṣya vaṇijo dāpayet karān || 7.127 ||**

tasyedaṃ sāmānyena lakṣaṇam || 7.127 ||

	**yathā phalena yujyeta rājā kartā ca karmaṇām |**

**	tathāvekṣya nṛpo rāṣṭre kalpayet satataṃ karān || 7.128 ||**

_asya dṛṣṭāntaḥ |_

	**yathālpālpam adanty ādyaṃ vatsavāryokaṣaṭpadāḥ |**

**	tathālpo 'lpo gṛhītavyo rāṣṭrād rājñābdikaḥ karaḥ || 7.129 ||**

karādānavidhistutyartho dṛṣṭāntaślokaḥ || 7.129 ||

	**pañcāśadbhāga ādeyo rājñā paśuhiraṇyayoḥ |**

**	dhānyānām aṣṭamo bhāgaḥ ṣaṣṭho dvādaśa eva vā|| 7.130 ||**

mūlyādhikayoḥ paśuhiraṇyayoḥ **pañcāśadbhāgo** grāhyaḥ | dhānyānāṃ bhāgaviśeṣaḥ sukarāpakṣayā kalpyaḥ || 7.130 ||

	**ādadītātha ṣaḍbhāgaṃ drumāṇāṃ madhusarpiṣām |**

**	gandhauṣadhirasānāṃ ca puṣpamūlaphalasya ca || 7.131 ||**

**	patraśākatṛṇānāṃ ca carmaṇāṃ vaiṇavasya ca |**

**	mṛṇmayānāṃ ca bhāṇḍānāṃ sarvasyāśmamayasya ca || 7.132 ||**

yathoktānāṃ drumādīnāṃ lābhāt ṣaḍbhāgādānam || 7.131–32 ||

	**mriyamāṇo 'py ādadīta na rājā śrotriyāt karam |**

**	na ca kṣudhāsya saṃsīdec chrotriyo viṣaye vasan || 7.133 ||**

asya nindārthavādaḥ || 7.133 ||

	**yasya rājñas tu viṣaye (?) śrotriyaḥ sīdati kṣudhā|**

**	tasyāpi tat kṣudhā rāṣṭram acirād eva sīdati || 7.134 ||**

**	śrutavṛtte viditvāsya vṛttiṃ dharmyāṃ prakalpayet |**

**	saṃrakṣet sarvataś cainaṃ pitā putram ivaurasam || 7.135 ||**

**	saṃrakṣyamāṇo rājñā yaṃ kurute dharmam anvaham |**

**	tenāyur vardhate rājño draviṇaṃ rāṣṭram eva ca || 7.136 ||**

śrotriyasyādhikakṣemaprayojanārthās trayaḥ ślokāḥ || 7.134–36 ||

	**yatkiṃcid api varṣasya dāpayet karasaṃjñitam |**

**	vyavahāreṇa jīvantaṃ rāṣṭre rājā pṛthagjanam || 7.137 ||**

brāhmaṇād anyaḥ **pṛthagjanaḥ** | svalpenāpi vyavahāreṇa jīvan dāpayitavyaḥ karaḥ || 7.137 ||

	**kārukāñ chilpinaś caiva śūdrāṃś cātmopajīvinaḥ |**

**	ekaikaṃ kārayet karma māse māse mahīpatiḥ || 7.138 ||**

ye śilpamātropajīvinas tān māsānumāsikam **ekaikam** ahaḥ karma kārayet, **ātmopajīvinaś** ca || 7.138 ||

	**nocchindyād ātmano mūlaṃ pareṣāṃ cātitṛṣṇayā |**

**	ucchindan hy ātmano mūlam ātmānaṃ tāṃś ca pīḍayet || 7.139 ||**

tad eva pratiṣedhād ātmanaḥ pareṣāṃ ca tantraṃ nocchindyāt || 7.139 ||

	**tīkṣāaś caiva mṛduś caiva syāt kāryaṃ vīkṣya mahīpatiḥ |**

**	tīkṣṇaś caiva mṛduś caiva rājā bhavati saṃmataḥ || 7.140 ||**

saṃsata etadrājavṛttaṃ nityam abhyasasīyaṃ || 7.140 ||

	**amātyamukhyaṃ dharmajñaṃ prājñaṃ dāntaṃ kulodgatam |**

**	sthāpayed āsane tasmin khinnaḥ kāryekṣaṇe nṛpaḥ || 7.141 ||**

kāryadarśane **khinnaḥ** sarvotkṛṣṭam amātyaṃ darśanasthāne sthāpayet || 7.141 ||

	**evaṃ sarvaṃ vidhāyedam itikartavyam ātmanaḥ |**

**	uktaś caivāpramattaś ca parirakṣed imāḥ prajāḥ || 7.142 ||**

**	vikrośantyo yasya rāṣṭrād dhriyante dasyubhiḥ prajāḥ |**

**	saṃpaśyataḥ sabhṛtyasya mṛtaḥ sa na sa jīvati || 7.143 ||**

**	kṣatriyasya paro dharmaḥ prajānām eva pālanam |**

**	nirdiṣṭaphalabhoktā hi rājā dharmeṇa yujyate || 7.144 ||**

**yuktaś caivāpramattaś** cā[skhalitabuddhir] yasya | prajārakṣaṇavidhyarthavādārthās trayaḥ ślokāḥ || 7.142–44 ||

	**utthāya paścime yāme kṛtaśaucaḥ samāhitaḥ |**

**	hutvāgnīn brāhmaṇān arcya praviśet tu sabhāṃ śubhām || 7.145 ||**

**	tatra sthitaḥ prajāḥ sarvāḥ pratinandya vi[sarjayet |**

**	visṛjya ca prajāḥ sarvā mantrayet saha mantribhiḥ || 7.146 ||**

**mantri]bhiḥ saha** | nityavṛttaṃ rājñaḥ ślokadvayenocyate || 7.145–46 ||

	**giripṛṣṭaṃ samāruhya prāsādaṃ vā rahogataḥ |**

**	araṇye niḥśalāke vā mantrayed [avibhāvitaḥ|| 7.147 ||**

mantra]pañcāṅgaṃ mantryet | tad yathā karmaṇām ārambhopāyaḥ puruṣadravyasampad deśakālavibhāgaḥ vinipātapratīkāraḥ kāryasiddhir iti | tān ekaikaśaḥ pṛcchet samastāṃś ca | hetubhiḥ sarveṣāṃ matipravivekaṃ vidyāt | avāptārthaḥ kālaṃ nātipātayen, na ca dīrghamantraḥ syāt | na ca teṣāṃ pakṣīyair mantraṃ mantrayet yeṣām apakuryāt | guptamantraś ca syāt || 7.147 ||

_yena |_

	**yasya mantraṃ na jānanti samāgamya pṛthagjanāḥ |**

**	sa kṛtsnāṃ pṛthivīṃ bhuṅkte kośahīno 'pi pārthivaḥ || 7.148 ||**

_evaṃ ca sati saṃrakṣaṇārtham |_

	**jaḍāndhamūkabadhirāṃs tairyagyonān vayotigān |**

**	strīmlecchavyādhitavyaṅgān mantre tu pratiṣedhayet || 7.149 ||**

_yasmāt |_

	**bhindanty avamatā mantraṃ tairyagyonās tathaiva ca |**

**	striyaś caiva viśeṣeṇa tasmāt tatrādṛto bhavet || 7.150 ||**

**	madhyaṃdine 'rdharātre vā viśrānto vigataklamaḥ |**

**	cintayed dharmakāmārthān sārdhaṃ tair eka eva vā || 7.151 ||**

dharmārthakāmānāṃ vṛddhiṃ **cintayet** | parasparavirodhināṃ rājñām anyatamavivṛddhau teṣām ucchittir jāyate || 7.150–51 ||

	**parasparaviruddhānāṃ teṣāṃ ca samupārjanam |**

**	kanyānāṃ sampradānaṃ ca kumārāṇāṃ ca rakṣaṇam || 7.152 ||**

mantriṇāṃ dharmārthakāmānāṃ vā, parasparavirodhe teṣāṃ balābalavyapekṣā | **kanyānāṃ saṃpradānaṃ** svakāryasiddhivaśena cintyam | **kumārāṇāṃ rakṣaṇam**, tava vayam ity evaṃ vādibhiḥ sattribhiḥ darmam arthaṃ ca grāhayitavyam | navaṃ hi dravyaṃ yena yenārthajātenopadihyate tad tad evācūṣati | evam ayaṃ navabuddhir yad yad ucyate tat tat pratipadyate | vyasanebhyaś cainam upāyato nivartayeyur iti nityānuśāsanāc ca kālena guṇasaṃpannaṃ yauvarājye sthāpayet, nirguṇān anyān pratyanteṣy nikṣipet: ity evamādinābhiyogātiśayena rājñā putrarakṣaṇaṃ pratyahaṃ cintyam || 7.152 ||

	**dūtasaṃpreṣaṇaṃ caiva kāryaśeṣaṃ tathaiva ca |**

**	antaḥpurapracāraṃ ca praṇidhīnāṃ ca ceṣṭitam || 7.153 ||**

yena saha sandhānaṃ vigraho vā cikīrṣyate tatra **dūtasaṃpreṣaṇaṃ** cintyam | ārabdha**kāryaśeṣa**tvaṃ ca cintayet, āsthāpanāya | kakṣyāntareṣv antarvaṃśikasainyādhiṣṭhito 'ntaḥpuraṃ praviśet | tatra sthavirastrīpariśuddhāṃ devīṃ paśyen nāpariśuddhām | devyā gṛhanilīno hi bhrātā bhadrasenam jaghāna, mātuḥ śayanāntargataś ca putraḥ kārūṣam, viṣadigdhena nūpureṇa vairantyaṃ [devī] jaghāna, mekhalāmaṇinā sauviram, veṇyāṃ nigūḍhena śastreṇa vidūratham | tasmād etāny āspadasthānāni yatnataḥ parīkṣeta | muṇḍajaṭilakuhakapartisaṃsargaṃ bāhyābhiś ca dāsībhir antaḥpuradāsīnāṃ pratiṣedhayet | **praṇidhīnāṃ** ca kāpaṭikādīnāṃ cāraparamparābhiś **ceṣṭitaṃ** cintayet || 7.153 ||

	**kṛtsnaṃ cāṣṭavidhaṃ karma pañcavaraṃ ca tattvataḥ |**

**	anurāgāparāgau ca pracāraṃ maṇḍalasya ca || 7.154 ||**

akṛtārambham ārabdhasyānuṣṭhānam anuṣṭhitaviśeṣaṇaṃ karmaphalasaṃgrahaḥ, tathā sāmabhedadānadaṇḍāh, etad **aṣṭavidhaṃ karma** | atha vā kṛṣir vaṇikpatha udake setubandhanaṃ [durgakaraṇaṃ] kṛtasya vā tatsaṃskāro hastibandhanaṃ khanikhananaṃ śūnyaveśanaṃ dāruvanachedanaṃ ceti |_ <span style="text-decoration:underline;">apare</span>_ tv āhuḥ |

	ādāne ca visarge ca tathā praiṣaniṣedhayoḥ |

	pañcame cārthavacane vyavahārasya cekṣaṇe ||

	daṇḍaśuddhyoḥ sadā yuktas tenāṣṭagatiko nṛpaḥ |

	aṣṭakarmā divaṃ yāti rājā śakrābhipūjitaḥ ||

ity auśanasau ślokau | tadvivaraṇam: **ādānaṃ** balinā | bhṛtyebhyo dhana**visargaḥ** | **praiṣo** dūṣṭatyāgaḥ | arthādhikṛtānām atipravṛttinirodho **niṣedhaḥ** | asaṃpravṛtter **arthavacanam** | varṇāśramiṇāṃ svakarmasaṃśraye vyavahārekṣaṇam | parasparābhiyoge **daṇḍa**nipātanaṃ parājitānām | **śuddhir** ātmane (?), pramādaskhalite tu [prā]yaścittam ity etad aṣṭavi[dhaṃ karma |
