**anubandhaṃ parijñāyeti** | kecit atra vyatikramānuṣṭhānasya paunaḥpunyaṃ kriyānuṣṭhānābhyāsalakṣaṇam āhuḥ | vayaṃ punar **anubandham** aparādhakāraṇam ācakṣmahe | katham anubadhyate 'nenety **anubandho**, lobhādipadārthaḥ | kiṃ tat, aparādhaś cauryādiḥ | taṃ parijñāya kim ayaṃ cauryādir aparādho 'sy kāmāt uta krodhāt atha lobhān mohād vā | athātmakuṭumbasthityai dharmatantrānugrahāya vety evam | asya cāparādhahetor anubandhasva vijñāne prayojanam, tadbhedād daṇḍaviśeṣo yathā syād iti | deśakālau ca tattvataḥ parijñāyeti vartate | tatra gṛharathyākhalakṣetrasvaviṣayaparaviṣayādinirdeśo 'parādhe 'pekṣitavyaḥ | kvāyam aparādhaḥ tathā kālaḥ, subhikṣadurbhikṣākulānākulavayo'vasthādiḥ | sāraṃ cāparādhasya dravyādbhijanādiḥ, tadviparyayaṃ cāsāraṃ nidarśanārthatvāt sāragrahaṇasya | aparādhaṃ cāvekṣya gurulaghutvena jñānājñānakṛtaṃ vastrahiraṇyādikṛtaṃ vā daṇḍaṃ daṇḍyeṣu pātayet deśādīn avekṣya, yasmād anyathā hi tasya — || 8.127 ||

	**adharmadaṇḍanaṃ like yaśoghanaṃ kīrtināśanam |**

**	asvargyaṃ ca paratrāpi tasmāt tat parivarjayet || 8.128 ||**

deśādyapekṣayā daṇḍaṃ vidadhyād yatnataḥ | evaṃ ca sati tasyāyaṃ prayogakramavidhiḥ śiṣyate || 8.128 ||

	**vāgdaṇḍaṃ prathamaṃ kuryād dhigdaṇḍaṃ tadanantaram |**

**	tṛtīyaṃ dhanadaṇḍaṃ tu vadhadaṇḍam ataḥ param || 8.129 ||**

aparādhāpekṣaiṣā daṇḍaprakḷptiḥ krameṇa syāt | vadhaś cātra tāḍane na tu māraṇe, sāmarthyāt | tathā ca darśayati — || 8.129 ||

	**vadhenāpi yadā tv etān nigrahītuṃ na śaknuyāt |**

avineyatvād eteṣām —

	**tadaiṣu sarvam apy etat prayuñjīta catuṣṭayam || 8.130 ||**

kṛte 'pi śārīre daṇḍe yadi nopatiṣṭhetāparādhāt, tato 'sya vāgdaṇḍādicatuṣṭayaṃ samastaṃ kriyate, na punar aparādhī kṛtanigraha ity utsṛjyet vyavasthārthaṃ lokasya | itarathā mātsyanyāyaḥ syāt | dhanadaṇḍarthaś cāyaṃ punarārambhaḥ | vāgdaṇḍadighdaṇḍau tu mṛdutvāt kaḥ prayacchatīti | tathā ca prakaraṇāntare imam eva kramaṃ vakṣayti | "aṅgulīr granthibhedasya chedayen prathame grahe dvitīye hastacaraṇau tṛtīye vadham arhati" || 8.130 ||

	**lokasaṃvyavahārārthaṃ yāḥ saṃjñāḥ prathitā bhuvi |**

**	tāmrarūpyasuvarṇānāṃ tāḥ pravakṣyāmy aśeṣataḥ || 8.131 ||**

viśiṣṭajātiparimāṇasya dravyasya saṃjñārtha upadeśo daṇḍaviśeṣārthaḥ || 8.131 ||

	**trasareṇavo 'ṣṭau vijñeyā likṣaikā parimāṇataḥ |**

**	tā rājasarṣapas tisras te trayo gaurasarṣapaḥ || 8.132 ||**

**	sarṣapāḥ ṣaṭ yavo madhyas triyavaṃ tv ekakṛṣṇalam |**

**	pañcakṛṣṇaliko māṣas te suvarṇas tu ṣoḍaśa || 8.133 ||**

**	palaṃ suvarṇāś catvāraḥ palāni dharaṇaṃ daśa |**

**	[dve kṛṣṇale sa]madhṛte vijñeyo rūpyamāṣakaḥ || 8.134 ||**

**	te ṣoṣaśa syād dharaṇaṃ purāṇaś caiva rājataḥ |**

**	kārṣāpaṇas tu vijñeyas tāmrikaḥ kārṣikaḥ paṇaḥ || 8.135 ||**

**	dharaṇāni daśa jñeyaḥ śatamānas tu rājataḥ |**

**	catuḥ sau[varṇiko niṣko vijñeyas tu pramāṇataḥ || 8.136 ||**

**	paṇānāṃ] dve śate sārdhe prathamaḥ sāhasaḥ smṛtaḥ |**

**	madhyamaḥ pañca vijñeyaḥ sahasraṃ tv eva cottamaḥ || 8.137 ||**

sarvasaṃjñārthāḥ ślokāḥ | tatra ya eteṣu saṃchanneṣu kūṭīmaṭheṣv [ādityakaradṛṣṭās re]ṇavas te trayas trasareṇavaḥ || 8.132–127 ||

	**ṛṇe deye pratijñāte pañcakaṃ śatam arhati |**

**	apahanave taddviguṇaṃ tan manor anuśāsanam || 8.138 ||**

ṛṇavyavahāre svayaṃ pratipanno viṃśa[tibhāgam, pratipādi]taḥ sākṣyādibhir daśabhāgam | asamartho daṇḍaleśaṃ yat kiṃcid iti | tac coktaṃ purastād "daṇḍaleśaṃ ca śaktitaḥ" iti | ete trayo 'dharmarṇasya daṇḍāḥ | ye tūttamarṇaṃ daśabhāgaṃ dāpayanti adhamarṇaṃ cānyaṃ daṇḍaṃ smṛtyantarāt te dāpayanti | idaṃ tu mānavaṃ darśanam || 8.138 ||

	**vasiṣṭhavihitāṃ vṛ[ddhiṃ] sṛjed vittavivardhinīm |**

**	aśītibhāgaṃ gṛhṇīyān māsād vārdhu[ṣikaḥ] śate || 8.139 ||**

aśītabhāgaḥ prathamaḥ kalpaḥ prayuktasyārthasya vṛddhiḥ || 8.139 ||

	**dvikaṃ śataṃ vā gṛhṇīta satāṃ dharmam anusmaran |**

**	dvikaṃ śataṃ hi gṛhṇāno na bhavaty arthakilbiṣī || 8.140 ||**

pañcāśadbhāgo 'nukalpaḥ || 8.140 ||

	**dvikam trikaṃ catuṣkaṃ ca [pañcakaṃ ca} śataṃ samam |**

**	māsasya vṛddhiṃ gṛhṇīyād varṇānām sanupūrvaśaḥ || 8.141 ||**

ayaṃ ca varṇānupūrvyāt tṛtīyaḥ kalpaḥ | eṣāṃ tu pūrvaḥ pūrvo jyāyān | anye 'pi tu samām iti paṭhanti | samāgrahaṇād atreyaṃ vṛddhir na saṃvatsarāt parataḥ | pūrvātaḥ syāt | parato 'pi alpatvād vṛddheḥ | prayogaś ca dvividho bhavati | gṛhītvā cādhim anyathā ca | tatrādhigrahaṇapakṣe viśeṣārtham idam ucyate — || 8.141 ||

	**na tv evādhau sopakāre kausīdīṃ vṛddhim āpnuyāt |**

**	na cādheḥ kālasaṃrodhān nisargo 'sti na vikrayaḥ || 8.142 ||**

bhuñjānasya hi prayoktur ādhiṃ kṣetrādikaṃ vṛddhir na syāt | arthāc cānupakāriṇyādhau sopakāre 'pi ca samayād abhujyamāne syād vṛddhiḥ | na cādher abhogyasya kālasaṃrodhād dviguṇībhūte 'rthe kāle 'dhigacchati nisargo 'syānyatrādhamanam ananujñātasya gṛhītrā | kiṃ tu yāvad dhanaṃ na prayacched dviguṇībhūtaṃ tāvad ādhiṃ bhuñjītaiva sāmarthyād vijñāyate, prayuktārthasādhanāya | vikrayasādharmyāc cānyatrādhamanaṃ nisargo vijñāyate | evaṃ vikrayo 'pi vijñeyaḥ | tathā ca saty arthaprayogakāla eva pratiṣiddhena prayoktrā — || 8.142 ||

	**na bhoktavyo balād ādhir bhuñjāno vṛddhim utsṛjet |**

idaṃ tāvat pūrvaślokam evoktam uttarārtham | tac cedam ucyate —

	**mūlyena toṣayed vainam**

ādhamayitāraṃ divasabhogavṛddhyā dravyasya, tāmrakaṭāhādyupakṣayaṃ parijñāya tadvidbhyaḥ | rahasyaṃ tu prayuñjāno dṛṣṭenāpi doṣeṇa yujyate | yad ayam āha —

		**ādhisteno 'nyathā bhavet || 8.143 ||**

vijñātāraś ca | rājñā daṇḍaḥ syāt | idaṃ śāstraṃ bhogakṣaya evādhau samarthaṃ bhavati nānyatra | anyas tv āha: dviguṇībhūte 'rthe svāminānujñātam ādhiṃ bhuñjāno mūlahiraṇyenaiva bhuñjīta | mūlahiraṇyam eva vā parigaṇayyāpratipadyamānamūlyena paritoṣayet | evaṃ ca dviguṇībhūte hiraṇye 'yam ādhibhogapratiṣedhaḥ, pūrvasmiṃś cārtha ādāv eva || 8.143 ||

	**ādhiś copanidhiś cobhau na kālātyayam arhataḥ |**

**	avahāryau bhavetāṃ tau dīrghakālam avasthitau || 8.144 ||**

ādhisādṛśyenopanidher api samānavidhitvād atropadeśaḥ | na cādheḥ kālasaṃrodhe 'pi nisargavikrayau sta iti kṛtvā tasmād ādhātrā tanmokṣaṇe yatitavyam | kālātyayena hi tau jalāgnicorādibhir vināśaṃ gaccheyātām | atha vā daśavarṣabhogena | tathā ca vakṣyati "yati kiṃcid daśavarṣāṇi" iti | athādhyupanidhyoḥ ko viśeṣaḥ | ādhir hiraṇyabhogyaḥ; prītibhogya upanidhiḥ | tathā ca vakṣyati "nikṣiptasya dhanasyāivaṃ prītyopanihitasya ca" iti || 8.144 ||

	**saṃprītyā bhujyamānāni na naśyanti kadācana |**

**	dhenuś coṣṭro vahann aśvo yaś ca damyaḥ prayujyate || 8.145 ||**

ādhyupanidhyoḥ prakaraṇād etad grahaṇam | uktaṃ hi "ādhiś copanidhiś cobhau na kālātyayam arhataḥ" | atha vā saṃprītibhogavacanād upanidhir ayam, nādhiḥ | tathā ca prītyopanihitasya cety evaṃvidham upanidhiṃ vakṣyati | saṃprītyā bhujyamāno dhenūṣṭrāḥ vahantaś cāśvādayaḥ svaṃ svam arthaṃ prayacchanti | yaś ca damyaḥ prayujyate avahann api | ete na naśyanti kadācid atibhogena | atha vā saṃprītyā bhujyamānāni gṛhādīny ucyante | ebhyas tv anye dhenvādayo 'pi prītibhogyā[ḥ naśyanti || 8.145 ||

	**yat kiṃcid daś varṣāṇi saṃnidhau] prekṣyate dhanī |**

**	bhujyamānaṃ parais tūṣṇīṃ na sa tal labdhum arhati || 8.146 ||**

prītirahitaṃ yati kiṃcid || 8.146 ||

	**[ajaḍaś ced apogaṇḍo] viṣaye cāsya bhujyate |**

**	bhagnaṃ tad vyavahāreṇa bhoktā taddhanam arhati || 8.147 ||**

ajaḍaś ced apo[gaṇḍa iti e]tau svadhanānveṣaṇāya paryāptau, na tu jaḍaḥ, pogaṇḍo vā, śaktivikalpatvāt | viṣaye cānyasya bhujyate cakṣuṣaḥ nāprakāśam | atha vā svaviṣaye nānya[viṣaye], na proṣītasya | evaṃ ca sati paśyataḥ samarthasya [sa]to bhujyamānaṃ svadravyam upakṣayā yuktas tadapahāro daśavarṣabhogena | ajaḍāpogaṇḍagrahaṇena cānyad api {svadha]nānveṣaṇavyāsaṅgakāraṇam apāṭavādi gṛhyate | satradīkṣādivyāsaṅgakāraṇam abhihitaṃ vijñeyam | daśavarṣabhogena svīkaraṇāpavādārtham idam ārabhyate || 8.147 ||

	**ādhiḥ sīmā bāladhanaṃ nikṣepopanidhiḥ striyaḥ |**

**	rājasvaṃ śrotriyasvaṃ ca na bhogena praṇaśyati || 8.148 ||**

striyaḥ paricārikāḥ noḍhāh śāstravirodhāt | anye tv āhuḥ: ūḍhā api pratyāharaṇīyāḥ prāyaścittena | yato na yuktam āsām āpady apahṛtānāṃ parityāgaḥ | rājasvaśrotriyasvayoś ca labdhakrītayor api bhogenāpraṇāśaḥ | tatra śrotriyadharmasyācārāsaṅgāt | rājñaś ca svatantrānuṣṭhānasaṅgena | anyadīyayos tu labdhakrītayor anya eva syāt || 8.148 ||

	**yaḥ svāminānanujñātam ādhiṃ bhuṅkte 'vicakṣaṇaḥ |**

**	tenārdhavṛddhir moktavyā tasya bhogasya niṣkrayaḥ || 8.149 ||**

svāmī ca gṛhe vyavaharati | tatprayuktaś ca bhṛtyaḥ | tathā ca vakṣyati "kuṭumbārtha 'dhyadhīnaḥ" [iti] | tenānanujñātaś ca svāminā ya ādhiṃ bhuṅkte 'vicakṣaṇaḥ tenārdhavṛddhir arthā upakṣyanta ity evaṃ na jānāti | etasmāt kāraṇād anena tasyārdhavṛddhir moktavyā bhoganiṣkṛtyartham | evaṃ ca grahaṇādhamanayoḥ pramāṇam adhyadhīnaḥ pṛthaktantutvat (?) tu nopabhogānujñāne dāne | etac ca yo veda sa vicakṣaṇaḥ | tathā cāyam eva yuktaḥ pāṭhaḥ: na vicakṣaṇaḥ svāmyupasarjanatvād adhyadhīnasyeti | anyas tv āha pūrvo dviguṇībhūte vidhir uktaḥ, "na bhoktavyo balād ādhir bhuñjāno vṛddhim utsṛjet" ity eṣaḥ | ayaṃ punar ādāv evocyate || 8.149 ||

	**kusīdavṛddhir dvaiguṇyaṃ nātyeti sakṛdāhitā |**

**	dhānye śade lave vāhye nātikrāmati pañcatām || 8.150 ||**

**vṛddhir dvaiguṇyaṃ nātyeti** | kālamahattve 'pi sati | **sakṛd āhitā** puruṣāntaram asaṃkrāntā, saṃkramite tu dhane prayoktrānyatra punarvardhata eva, gṛhītṛdoṣād apratipādanena pūrvaṃ prayoktur dhanasya | hiraṇye tāvad evam | **dhānye** tu phalakāle **śada**kāle prativarṣaṃ bhāgaśo vardhamānaṃ tat prayuktaṃ dhānyaṃ **nātikrāmati pañcatām** | hiraṇyavad dvaiguṇe prāpte idaṃ tatpratiṣedhārthaṃ pañcaguṇatvam ārabhyate | evaṃ **śade** pañcatāṃ parivartamāno **nātikrāmati** | evaṃ **lave** prayukta 'vyādyūrṇājānāṃ lavakāle lavakāle bhāgaśo vardhate tatprayuktam | **vāhye** tu balīvardādāv eṣa eva nyāyaḥ || 8.150 ||

	**kṛtānusārād adhikā vyatiriktā na sidhyati |**

**	kusīdapatham āhus taṃ pañcakaṃ śatam arhati || 8.151 ||**

yo hi kāryavarttāṃ vijñāya gṛhītuḥ pañcakāc chatād adhikaṃ vṛddhiṃ kārayet prayoktā na tasya sākāryasiddhiṃ gacchet | śāstravyatirekād dhetoḥ | yataḥ **pañcakam** eva **śataṃ** dātum **arhati** | atha vā **kṛtā** tu vṛddhir aviśeṣyā grahaṇakāle viśeṣyā vā alpān na kiṃcanāsya gṛhītuḥ pūrvam, paścād dhanavyavahāreṇaiva prāptaiśvaryasya, anyathā vā, puruṣakārāt saṃpallakṣaṇād adhikā, yathā mandīkṛtā tatprayoktṛlobhād uttarakālaṃ gṛhītuḥ saṃpadapekṣayā, na sidhyati, śāstravyatirekād dhetoḥ | tatra hi sarvamahatī vṛddhiḥ pañcakaṃ śatam | tad api śūdraviṣayam | kāmam aśūdrasyāpi tāvatī syād vṛddhiḥ, nāto vyatiriktā | tathā ca nindyate, kusīdapatham āhus tam iti || 8.151 ||

	**nātisāṃvatsarīṃ vṛddhiṃ**

**nātisāṃvatsarīṃ vṛddhiṃ** gṛhṇīyāt, yadi vṛddhimahattvāt saṃvatsara eva taddhanaṃ dviguṇībhavati | anyathā tu parastād api saṃvatsarasya gṛhṇīyāt yāvat taddvaiguṇyam | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "cirasthāne dvaiguṇyaṃ prayogasya" iti | anye tu labdhīm api vṛddhim aśītipañcāśadbhāgalakṣaṇāṃ nātivatsarīṃ manyante, dharma[virodhāt ta]syāḥ |

		**na cādṛṣṭām [punar] **

śāstraiḥ svayaṃkalpitāṃ dvikādivṛddhibhyo 'nyām

		**haret |**

atha vādṛṣṭām anupacitām ity arthaḥ | pratimāsaṃ na gṛhṇīyāt, pratimāsopajātāṃs tu tāvat gṛhṇīyāt yāvad dvaiguṇyam |

	**[cakravṛddhiḥ kālavṛddhiḥ kāritā kāyikā ca yā] || 8.152 ||**

parasparopakārāpekṣayā svayaṃ kṛtā vṛddhikalpābhyanujñāyate cakravad yānasaṃyuktā vṛddhiś **cakravṛddhiḥ** | atha vā cakravad āvartate | pratimāsaṃ yā [vardhate sā | kālavṛddhiḥ] kāl[āntare 's]yaitad dhanaṃ vardhate, na saṃpratyeva | etac ca prītyā kalpyate, svayam anugrāhyatayā parasya | atha vā asmin kāle aprayacchatas tathaiva [vardhate yathāniścitaṃ] svayam eva prayoktrā gṛhītrā ca deśakālakāryāvasthāpekṣayā | iyaṃ cābhihitāpavādakṛtānusārād adhiketi | **kāyikā** kāyikakarmasaṃśodhyā || 8.152 ||

	**ṛṇaṃ dātum aśakto yaḥ kartum icchet punaḥ kriyām |**

**	sa datvā nirjitāṃ vṛddhiṃ karaṇaṃ parivartayet || 8.153 ||**

mūlahiraṇyasya punaḥ kriyā na vṛddheḥ | katham | yo hi gṛhītā mūlaṃ vṛddhiṃ ca dātum aśaktaḥ karaṇaṃ sākṣyādi parivartayitum icchet, sa pūrva**nirjitāṃ** **vṛddhiṃ** datvā mūlamātrasya **karaṇaṃ parivartayet** | na tatra vṛddhim āropayet | yac ca dadyāt tad vṛddhitaḥ śodhayet, na tu mūlataḥ | ayaṃ ca rājña upadeśaḥ | pīḍitasya vṛddhyā rājñaivākārayitavyam || 8.153 ||

	**adarśayitvā tatraiva hiraṇyaṃ parivartayet |**

**	yāvatī saṃbhaved vṛddhis tāvatīṃ dātum arhati || 8.154 ||**

aśaktasya kākiṇim api dātuṃ saha vṛddhyā punaḥ kriyā || 8.154 ||

	**cakravṛddhiṃ samārūḍho deśakālavyavasthitaḥ |**

**	atikrāman deśakālau na tatphalam avāpnuyāt || 8.155 ||**

uttamarṇo 'dharmarṇād deśakālātikrameṇa svadoṣād eva | idānīṃ kāritā viṛddhiviṣayo 'yam apara ucyate || 8.155 ||

	**samudrayānakuśalā deśakālārthadarśinaḥ |**

**	sthāpayanti tu yāṃ vṛddhiṃ sā tatrādhigamaṃ prati || 8.156 ||**

tatra te vaṇijo yāṃ vṛddhiṃ sthāpayeyuḥ, sā pratīyeta, ye hi tatra kṣayavyayādhvalābhadravyasārajñāḥ | ṛṇasaṃbandhena, ayam aparaḥ pratibhuvo dharmaḥ śiṣyate || 8.156 ||

	**yo yasya pratibhūs tiṣṭhed darśanāyeha mānavaḥ |**

**	adarśayan sa taṃ tasya prayacchet svadhanād ṛṇam || 8.157 ||**

nigadavyākhyāta evāyaṃ ślokaḥ | idānīm asya darśanapratibhuvo 'dhamarṇam uttamarṇasyādarśayataḥ svadhanād ṛṇadānaprāptau satyām mṛtasya "rikthabhāja ṛṇaṃ pratikuryuḥ" ity anena śāstreṇārthataś ca tatputradānaṃ prāptaṃ sat pratiṣidhyate || 8.157 ||

	**prātibhāvyaṃ vṛthādānam ākṣikaṃ saurikaṃ ca yat |**

**	daṇḍaśulkāvaśeṣaṃ ca na putro dātum arhati || 8.158 ||**

eteṣu putrasyāsaṃbandhaḥ śāstrasāmarthyād vijñeyaḥ | śulkāvaśeṣam iti vacanāt kṛtsne śulke 'sti putrasya saṃbandhaḥ | daṇḍāvaśeṣasyāpy enaṃ vidhim icchanti kecit | prātibhāvyasaṃbandhena ca samānavidhitvāt vṛthādānādiṣu pitryeṣu na putrāḥ saṃbadhyante | idānīṃ dviprakārasya pratibhuvo na **putro dātum arhatī**ty etasmin prāpta idam ārabhyate — || 8.158 ||

	**darśanaprātibhāvye tu vidhiḥ syāt pūrvacoditaḥ |**

**	dānapratibhuvi prete dāyādān api dāpayet || 8.159 ||**

evaṃ ca sati dānapratibhuvaḥ putrasyāsti saṃbandhaḥ || 8.159 ||

	**adātari punar dātā vijñātaprakṛtāv ṛṇam |**

**	paścāt pratibhuvi prete parīpset kena hetunā || 8.160 ||**

samānavibhaktīni padāny ekārthatayā vyākhyeyāni | **adātari pratibhuvi prete vijñātaprakṛtau** vijñātaṃ kāraṇaṃ lagnakatve yasya, so 'yaṃ vijñātaprakṛtiḥ | kiṃ punas tatsaṃbandhakārpaṇam | evaṃ ca dhanāvaṣṭambhenāyam asyādhamarṇasya, yasmān na kiṃbhūtaḥ | tata ittaṃbhūte 'smin **pratibhuvi prete** paścād **dātā** prayuktam ṛṇaṃ **parīpset kena hetunā** saṃdihya pṛcchati | kathaṃ ca saṃdihyate yataḥ tatkāraṇam ucyate | yena tāvad dānapratibhuvaḥ putrasyāsti saṃbandha ity uktam, na darśanapratibhuvaḥ | ataḥ saty apitṛrikthasaṃbandhe śāstrasāmarthyān na yukto dāpayitum, yataś ca gṛhītadhane [pratibhuvi] prete darśanalagnakaputro 'pi san dāpayitum iti evam ubhayathā darśanāt saṃdehe satīdam āha — || 8.160 ||

	**nirādiṣṭadhanaś cet tu pratibhūḥ syād alaṃdhanaḥ |**

**	sva[dhanād eva tad dadyān nirādiṣṭa iti sthitiḥ || 8.161 ||**

**nirādiṣṭadhano**] pratibhūḥ samarpitadhanaḥ, na vāṅmātreṇa | **alaṃdhanaś** ca **syāt** paryāptadhanaḥ | yāvatā saṃbadhyate lagnakatvena | atha vā nirādiṣṭadhano vā[ṅmātrena pa]ścād alaṃdhanas samarpitadhanaḥ paryāptadhanaś ca bhavati, tatraitasmād dhetoḥ **svadhanād eva tad** dātum arhati | adhamarṇalagnakaputra uttamarṇāyeti | ayaṃ ca dānagrahaṇavidhiḥ [siddhi]kāraṇena || 8.161 ||

_anyaś ca_ |

	**mattonmattārtādhyadhīnair bālena sthaviraṇa vā |**

**	asaṃbandhakṛtaś caiva vyavahāro na sidhyati || 8.162 ||**

dharmavyavahārā eva mattādibhiḥ kṛtā na sidhyanti | na kevalaṃ prakaraṇād ṛṇavyavahāraḥ | amattādibhir api prayujyamānāḥ sarvavyavahāreṣu || 8.162 ||

	**satyā na bhāṣā bhavati yady api syāt pratiṣṭhitā |**

**	bahiś ced bhāṣyate dharmān niyatād vyāvahārikāt || 8.163 ||**

dharmaviruddhaś ca vyavahāro 'patyabhāryāvikrayādir na sidhyati | yenāsau [dharmaṃ] vārayati | vṛddhiḥ sā prayogakāle dviguṇībhūtāpi punar vardhata eva pratimāsam: evaṃ grāmapuñjagrahaṇādivṛddhayo 'pi pratiṣiddhā boddhavyāḥ | ṛṇasaṃbandhād idam aparaṃ tadgatam evocyate || 8.163 ||

	**yogādhamanavikrītaṃ yogadānapratigraham |**

**	yatra cāpy upadhiṃ paśyet tat sarvaṃ vinivartayet || 8.164 ||**

**yogādhamanaṃ** nāma lokayātrāyāṃ yan na sphuṭam ucyate | "tvaṃ tāvat anena kāryaṃ kuru, ahaṃ punar anena kāryaṃ kariṣyāmi" iti | vikrayo 'py evaṃlakṣaṇaḥ | **yogadānaṃ** ca yad yātrotsavavyapadeśena sopadhaṃ dīyate 'dhamarṇādibhir uttamarṇaprabhṛtīnām | amumūrṣuś cānapatyo jñātibhyo bibhyan nairāśyād dadāti, evamādinā yogena | dānapra[ti]grahayor viśeṣaḥ: dānaṃ maitryā pratigraho dharmeṇa | **yatra cāpy upadhiṃ paśyed** dānapratigrahagatam anyagataṃ vā **tat sarvaṃ vinivartayet**, rājā vyāvahārān paśyan anayatra vā | ṛṇasaṃbandhāc cedam anyam aparaṃ tadgatam evocyate || 8.164 ||

	**gṛhītā yadi naṣṭaḥ syāt kuṭumbārthe kṛto vyayaḥ |**

**	dātavyaṃ bāndhavaiś tat syāt pravibhaktair api svataḥ || 8.165 ||**

pratītārtha eva ślokaḥ || 8.165 ||

	**kuṭumbārthe 'dhyadhīno 'pi vyavahāraṃ yam ācaret |**

kuṭumbasthityai svāmyasaṃnidhāne —

	**svadeśe vā videśe vā taṃ jyāyān**

adhyadhīnasvāmī

		**na vicārayet || 8.166 ||**

"mama parokṣe 'py etad adhyadhīnena tvayā karma kasmāt krtam" iti na vicārayet | evam avicārya taddhanaṃ pratikuryāt | atha vā pūrvaślokaśeṣārtho 'yaṃ varṇanīyaḥ | kathaṃ kṛtvā | **kuṭumbārthe** 'py adhīno 'pi tāvad **vyavahāraṃ yam ācaret** pramāṇībhavet jyāyasaḥ, kiṃ punar bāndhavānām | evaṃ ca sati mattonmattādhyadhīnakṛto vyavahāro na sidhyatīty uktam | atha tv "asaṃbandhakṛto vyavahāro na sidhyati" ity etasmāc chakyate kathaṃcid adhyadhīnasya jyāyasi parokṣe gṛhārthe svātantryaṃ kalpayitum | tataḥ sārtha evāyaṃ śloko yathainam avocāma sāmartham | kuṭumbārthaṃ punar adhyadhīnasya dhanaṃ prayuktam — || 8.166 ||

	**balād dattaṃ balād bhuktaṃ balād yac cāpi lekhitam |**

**	sarvān balakṛtān arthān akṛtān manur abravīt || 8.167 ||**

**balāt** tāvad **dattaṃ** vṛddhikāmena dhanaṃ kṣetrādhyādhibhogakāmena ca tan nivartyaṃ rājñā | **balāc** ca **bhuktam** ādhidravyaṃ pratiṣiddhena satā tad ādhibhogānveṣaṇena nivartyam | atha vā nādhidrvyam api gṛhādi balād bhuktaṃ daśavarṣabhogenaitad apahartiṣyāmīty anayā bhuddhyā | **balād yac cāpi lekhitaṃ** patre sarvāṃś caivaṃ prakārān anyān apy arthān sākṣitvapratibhūkulagrahaṇakālāvadhidvaiguṇyakaraṇāna nirvartyam **manur** āha || 8.167 ||

_ye[na] —_

	**trayaḥ parārthe kliśyanti sākṣiṇaḥ pratibhūḥ kulam |**

**	catvāras tūpacīyante vipra āḍhyo vaṇiṅ nṛpaḥ || 8.168 ||**

yasmāt parasyārthaṃ kurvanti dṛṣṭāni sākṣipratibhūkulāni, ato nānicchātas tāni kārayet sākṣyādīni | **catvāras tūpacīyante** viprādayaḥ parārtham eva kurvantaḥ, **vipras** tāvan nāditsantaṃ dāpayet dātāram, **āḍhyaś** ca vṛddhyartham ajighṛkṣantaṃ na grāhayet, **vaṇik** ca nācikīrṣantaṃ kārayet lābhārthī | evaṃ nṛpo 'pi nāvyavajihīrṣantaṃ vyavahārayet | evaṃ ca saty ayaṃ śloko 'rthasya balāt kṛtasya padārthasya nivṛttipradarśanārtho 'pi vijñeyaḥ | yataś caitad evam ato balavān api san rājā, vyavahārād anyatra — || 8.168 ||

	**anādeyaṃ nādadīta parikṣīṇo 'pi pārthivaḥ |**

**	na cādeyaṃ [samṛddho 'pi sūkṣmam apy artham utsṛjet] || 8.169 ||**

_yena | _

	**anādeyasya cādānād ādeyasya ca varjanāt |**

**	daurbalyaṃ khyāpyate rājñaḥ sa pretyeha ca naśyati || 8.170 ||**

atra cādeyāparivarjananiyamaḥ śāstrasāmarthyāt | ato varja[nīyavarjayituḥ || 8.170 ||

	**svādānād varṇ]āsaṃsargād durbalānāṃ ca rakṣaṇāt |**

**	balaṃ saṃjāyate rājñaḥ sa pretyeha ca vardhate || 8.171 ||**

yathāśāstraṃ punar asya vartamānasya, vyavahārebhyo 'nyataś ca paurajānapadebhyas taddravyādānād, durbalānāṃ ca balavadbhyo rakṣaṇād, varṇānām asargaḥ paraspareṇāsaṅkaraḥ prajāsu bhavati | tataś ca rājā **pretyeha vardhata** iti | adhikṛtavidhistutimātram idam || 8.171 ||

_yasmāc caitad evam |_

	**tasmād yama iva svāmī svayaṃ hitvā priyāpriye |**

**	varteta yāmyayā vṛttyā jitakrodho jitendriyaḥ || 8.172 ||**

samaḥ prajāsu syād ity asya rājño 'yam upamārthaḥ | tathā ca vaiṣamyahetuvyākhyānam āha jitakrodho jitendriya iti || 8.172 ||

_ajitakāmakrodhaś ca punaḥ pārthivaḥ |_

	**yas tv adharmeṇa kāryāṇi mohāt kuryān narādhipaḥ |**

**	acirāt taṃ durātmānaṃ vaśe kurvanti śatravaḥ || 8.173 ||**

aparaktaprakṛtim, bahukṛtyavantaṃ vṛddhaparyavasānādibhiḥ | punar āhitavijñānanirṇayaḥ san rājā — || 8.173 ||

	**kāmakrodhau tu saṃyamya yo 'rthān dharmeṇa paśyati |**

**	prajās tam anuvartante samudram iva sindhavaḥ || 8.174 ||**

yathā hi sindhavo gamyaṃ samudraṃ gatvā na nivartante kiṃ tarhi tanmayyo bhavanti, evam itthaṃbhūtasya rājño nāparādhyante prakṛtayo 'mātyādayaḥ, kiṃ tarhi tanmayyo bhavantīty ayam upamārthaḥ || 8.174 ||

	**yaḥ sādhayantaṃ chandena vedayan dhanikaṃ nṛpe |**

**	sa rājñā taccaturbhāgaṃ dāpyas tasya ca taddhanam || 8.175 ||**

rājavāllabhyād abibhyan yo rājapuruṣas tasmai dhanikam āvedaye tasya tathopadeśaṃ daṇḍanaṃ dhanadānaṃ ca rājā kuryāt | aparaḥ pāṛhaḥ: "yo 'sādhyaṃ manyamānas tu vedayed dhanikaṃ naraḥ, sa rājñarṇacaturbhāgaṃ dāpyas tasya ca taddhanam" | atrāpi sa evārthaḥ | īṣad anyathā bhinnaḥ| aśaktasya dhanadāna etat | dhanadānāyedam upāyāntaram abhidhīyate dhanābhāvato vaikalpikaḥ || 8.175 ||

	**karmaṇāpi samaṃ kuryād dhanikāyādharmarṇikaḥ |**

**	samo 'pakṛṣṭajātiś ca dadyāc chreyāṃs tu tacchanaiḥ || 8.176 ||**

śreyaso mānyatvāt soḍhavyam eva tasyāpradānāt | akṣāntyā tu na kadācid apy asau samahīnavat karmakārayitavyaḥ | ēṇāpādānārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 8.176 ||

	**anena vidhinā rājā mitho vivadatāṃ nṛṇām |**

**	sākṣipratyayasiddhāni kāryāṇi samatām nayet || 8.177 ||**

**pratyayasiddhāni** hetusiddhānīty arthaḥ | ṛṇavyavahāropasaṃhārārthaḥ ślokaḥ | nikṣepavidhyartham idam adhunocyate || 8.177 ||

	**kulaje vṛttasaṃpanne dharmajñe satyavādini |**

**	mahāpakṣe dhaniny ārye nikṣepaṃ nikṣiped budhaḥ || 8.178 ||**

nikṣepilakṣaṇavidhyarthaḥ ślokaḥ | **kulaje** prakṛṣṭābhijane | [**vṛttasaṃpanne**] ācāravati | prakaraṇād arthavyavahāre, itaratra vā | evaṃ cārthavyavahāre śucir bhavati yadi dharmajñatayā **satyavādī** bhavati | tathā ca sati vṛttaviśeṣaṇam idaṃ vijñeyam | evaṃvṛtto yadi bhavati tato 'yaṃ nikṣepayogyaḥ saṃpadyate | **mahāpakṣaś** cāgamyaś cāṭavikādīnāṃ bhavati, svapakṣaparābhavabhayāc ca na vikāraṃ yāti | evaṃ ca dhanitvopadeśo vyākhyeyaḥ | **āryaś** caivaṃvṛttaḥ śūdro 'pi vijñeyaḥ, avikriyātmakatvād iti | anye tu dvijātim ācakṣate, tasya cādṛṣṭārthaṃ grahaṇam āhur iti || 8.178 ||

	**yo yathā nikṣiped dhaste yam arthaṃ yasya mānavaḥ |**

**	sa tathaiva gṛhītavyo yathā dāyas tathā grahaḥ || 8.179 ||**

yasmād ubhayathā nikṣepo dṛṣṭaḥ samudro vimudraś ca, asākṣitas susākṣitaś ca, saṃkhyāto 'saṃkhyātaś ca, tasmād idam ucyate: **yathā dāyas tathā grahaḥ** | **mānava**grahaṇāc ceha vijñāyate: pūrvaśloke **ārya**grahaṇaṃ sarvavarṇārtham, na tu dvijātiviṣayam | evaṃ ca sati dānapratidānayos tulyakriyayor nikṣepadhārakasyābhiyogo na jāyate || 8.179 ||

	**yo nikṣepaṃ yācyamāno nikṣeptur na prayacchati |**

**	sa yācyaḥ prāṅvivākena tannikṣeptur asaṃnidhau || 8.180 ||**

'sākṣyabhāve" ity upariṣṭād vakṣyati | tenāsya sāmarthyāt saṃbandho draṣṭavyaḥ | sākṣyabhāve **yo nikṣepaṃ yācyamāno na prayacchati** tato nikṣeptrā prāṅvivāko vijñāpi[taḥ imaṃ] kuryāt: pūrvanikṣiptasya parimāṇavayorūpasādṛśyena kaiścid apadeśaiḥ kenacid hiraṇyādi tasminn eva nikṣepaṃ pūrvanikṣepadhāriṇi nikṣipet | tataḥ kasmiṃścit kāle gate pūrvanikṣe[ptu]r **asaṃnidhau** prāṅvivāko dvitīyena nikṣeptrā dvitīyaṃ nikṣepaṃ yācayet || 8.180 ||

	**sa yadi pratipadyeta yathānyastaṃ yathā kṛtam |**

**	na tatra vidyate kiṃcid yat parair abhiyujyate || 8.181 ||**

yadi taṃ dvitīyaṃ nikṣepaṃ yathā [nyastaṃ pratipadyet tadā **na**] **kiṃcid** asti **yat parair abhiyujyate** || 8.181 ||

	**teṣāṃ na dadyād yadi tu taddhiraṇyaṃ yathāvidhi |**

**	ubhau nigṛhya dāpyaḥ syād iti dharmasya dhāraṇā || 8.182 ||**

atha prāḍvivākavijñātaṃ paścān niyo[jitaṃ na dadyāt] tata ubhayaṃ nigṛhya pūrvaṃ dvitīyaṃ ca dāpyaḥ || 8.182 ||

	**sākṣyabhāve pratinidhiṃ vayorūpasamanvitam |**

**	apadeśaiś ca saṃnyasya hiraṇyaṃ tasya tattvataḥ || 8.183 ||**

pūrveṇāsya saṃbandhaḥ | tathā coktaṃ "yo nikṣepaṃ yācyamānaḥ" ity evamādi || 8.183 ||

	**nikṣepopanidhī nityaṃ na deyau pratyantare |**

**	naśyetāṃ vinipāte tāv anipāte tv anāśinau || 8.184 ||**

nikṣeptari jīvati tat**pratyanantare** putre bhrātari vā tadīyadhanārhe **nikṣepopanidhī na deyau**, prārthayamānāya | yena na pratyanantarasyāvināśe 'sti gatiḥ | pratyanantarasya vināśe tu nikṣepadhārī nikṣeptrā yācitaḥ kim uttaraṃ dāsyati tasya | yato na tasya pratyanantaradānaṃ yuktam || 8.184 ||

	**svayam eva tu yo dadyān mṛtasya pratyanantare |**

**	na sa rājñābhiyoktavyo na nikṣeptuś ca bandhubhiḥ || 8.185 ||**

aviditanikṣepaṃ svayaṃ prayacchato nāsty abhiyogaḥ | atha tūdbhāvakaḥ kaścid atrārthaṃ darṣayed (?) adhikam, tataḥ— || 8.185 ||

	**acchalenaiva cānvicchet tam arthaṃ prītipūrvakam |**

**	vicārya tasya vā vṛttiṃ sāmnaiva parisādhayet || 8.186 ||**

aviditaṃ svayaṃ prayacchato yadi tadgataḥ kaścit karṇejapāt saṃśayaḥ syāt, tata **acchalenaiva** tasya **vṛttiṃ vicārya**, tadadhigamo vijñeyaḥ, nikṣepadhāriṇā prajñāya || 8.186 ||

	**[nikṣepśv eṣu sarveṣu vidhiḥ syāt parisādhane |**

**	samudre nāpnuyāt kiṃcid yadi tasmān na saṃharet ] || 8.187 ||**

tadīyaṃ dravyaṃ rūpataḥ parimāṇataś ca **samudra** eva nikṣepo dhārayitavyaḥ | na ca samudro nikṣepaḥ pratyarpita ity etāvatā nikṣepadhārī mucyate, yadi tasmān na kiṃcit saṃharati pra[ti]mudrākaraṇenāpasrāvaṇādinā vān[yen]opāyena | apare 'pi varṇayanti samudrayānarūḍhānāṃ nikṣepadhārī yānavyāpattau sati yadi kiṃcid ātmīyaṃ na saṃharaty arthaṃ nābhiyojyo bhavati nikṣeptuḥ | etad uktaṃ bhavati | parityajyātmīyaṃ nikṣeparakṣaṇe yatnaḥ karaṇīya iti || 8.187 ||

	**corair hṛtaṃ jalenoḍham agninā dagdham eva ca |**

**	na dadyād yadi tasmāt tu na saṃharati kiṃcana || 8.188 ||**

corādibhyo 'pi nāśe 'yam eva samudrayānavidhir vyākhyāta iti | yataḥ pūrva eva ślokārtho jyāyān || 8.188 ||

	**nikṣepasyāpahartāram anikṣeptāram eva ca |**

**	sarvair upāyair anvicchec chapathaiś caiva vaidikaiḥ || 8.189 ||**

yas tv apadeśād vinā nikṣiptaṃ yācyamāno nikṣeptre na dadyāt: asākṣike nikṣepa etad ucyate | nikṣeptā vā gṛhītvā punar yāceta, adatvā vā | sa rājñā prāṅvivākena vā sāmādibhiḥ sarvopāyair anveṣya, tadasaṃbhave tu **śapathaiś caiva vaidikaiḥ** agniharaṇādibhiḥ | **ca**śabdāl laukikā api kośapānādayo 'trānurudhyante | kāryasāmānyāc ca nikṣepavidher anyatrāpy eṣām apratiṣedhaḥ || 8.189 ||

	**yo nikṣepaṃ narpayati yaś cānikṣipya yācate |**

**	tāv ubhau coravac chāsyau dāpyau vā tatsamaṃ damam || 8.190 ||**

pūrvavyatikramakāriṇo daṇḍārtho 'yam ārambhaḥ vikalpena | tathā brāhmaṇaṃ tu — || 8.190 ||

	**nikṣepasyāpahartāraṃ tatsamaṃ dāpayed damam |**

coradaṇḍanivṛttyarthaṃ brāhmaṇasyedaṃ punarvacanaṃ dhanadāpanasya —

	**tathopanidhihartāram aviśeṣeṇa pārthivaḥ || 8.191 ||**

aupariṣṭaślokārdhasyopanidhyartha ārambhaḥ | coravacchiṣṭir adhikārād upanidhāv api syād brāhmaṇavarjam || 8.191 ||

	**upadhābhis tu yaḥ kaścit paradravyaṃ haren naraḥ |**

**	sasahāyaḥ sa hantavyaḥ prakāśaṃ vividhair vadhaiḥ || 8.192 ||**

pavitrāsanenāśādānena svakalatrasaṃ[bhoga]nyāsenāgāmikālopakārapradarśanenety evamādibhir upadhābhiḥ paradravyāpahārī sasahāyo vividhair vadhiḥ prakāśam anuśāsanīyaḥ, yena kaṣṭa[taras tadīyanigrahas sa]rvadravyāpahāreṇeti || 8.192 ||

	**nikṣepo yaḥ kṛto yena yāvāṃś ca kulasaṃnidhau |**

**	tāvān eva sa vijñeyo vibruvan daṇḍam arhati || 8.193 ||**

sasākṣike sati nikṣepe sā[kṣiṇām grāmyādīnām eva] pramāṇaṃ syād arthasaṃkhyāparimāṇe || 8.193 ||

	**mitho dāyaḥ kṛto yena gṛhīto mitha eva vā |**

**`	mitha eva pradātavyo yathā dāyas tathā grahaḥ || 8.194 ||**

upanidhyartho 'yaṃ punarārambhaḥ | "yo yathā nikṣipe[d dhaste" iti] pūrvaśloke nikṣepaprakaraṇoktaṃ tadartha eva | ayaṃ punar upanidhyarthatvāt punaruktas tenaiva vijñeyaḥ | sāmānyaviśeṣaprakḷptyā vānayoḥ slokayor apunaruktatā varṇayitavyā || 8.194 ||

	**nikṣiptasya dhanasyaivaṃ prītyopanihitasya ca |**

**	kuryād vinirṇayaṃ rājākṣiṇvan nyāsadhāriṇam || 8.195 ||**

samudro vimudro vā nikṣepaḥ | vimudra eva tu prītivimuktabhoga upanidhiḥ | tayor anveṣaṇavidhir ayaṃ vijñeyaḥ | asvāmivikraya idānīm ucyate || 8.195 ||

	**vikrīṇīte parasya svaṃ yo 'svāmī svāmyasaṃmataḥ |**

**	na taṃ nayeta sākṣyaṃ tu stenam astenamāninam || 8.196 ||**

na taṃ nayeta sākṣyam ity asya pradarśanārthatvāt sarvāprāmāṇyād eva taṃ nivartayati || 8.196 ||

	**avahāryo bhaved eṣa sānvayaḥ ṣaṭśataṃ damam |**

**	niranvayo 'napasaraḥ prāptaḥ syāc corakilbiṣam || 8.197 ||**

**avahāryo** daṇḍyaḥ **sānvayaḥ** saniḥsaraḥ ṣaṭśataṃ damam | **niranvayas** tad **anapasaraḥ prāptaḥ syāc corakilbiṣam** ity anenāparādhamahattvād daṇḍamahattvaṃ darśayati pūrvasmāt | anyas tv āha: **apasaraḥ** krayād anyo dhanāgamaḥ | evaṃ ca sati — || 8.197 ||

	**asvāminā kṛto yas tu dāyo vikraya eva vā |**

**	akṛtaḥ sa tu vijñeyo vyavahāre yathā sthitiḥ || 8.198 ||**

krayavikrayāv asvāmikṛtau nipātyāv eva | tathā ca svāmy eva dhanabhāk syāt | na tu kretā vikretā vā dhane svāmī paritoṣaṇīyaḥ | idānīm asvāmisakāśāt krītasya daśa[varṣa]bhogābhigamena mā bhūt svatvam iti, yata idam āha — || 8.198 ||

	**saṃbhogo yatra dṛśyeta na dṛśyetāgamaḥ kvacit | **

**	āgamaḥ kāraṇaṃ tatra na saṃbhoga iti sthitiḥ || 8.199 ||**

evaṃ cāgamād aśuddhadravyasya daśavarṣabhogenāpi na svāmitvam | yataś caitad evam ataḥ — || 8.199 ||

	**vikrayād yo dhanaṃ kiṃcid gṛhṇīyāt kulasaṃnidhau |**

**	krayeṇa sa viśuddhas tu nyāyato labhate dhanam || 8.200 ||**

nyāyatas tu krayaḥ kulasaṃnidhāv ucitena mūlyena saṃbhāvyāc ca puruṣāt | etac ca tasyānabhiyogaṃ dhanalābhaś ca yuktaḥ | evaṃ buddhipūrvavyavahārayitāya nyāyakāriṇaḥ || 8.200 ||

	**atha mūlyam anāhāryaṃ prakāśakrayaśodhitam |**

**	adaṇḍyo mucyate rājñā nāṣṭiko labhate dhanam || 8.201 ||**

abhiyogakāle ca tasya yadi mūlyam āhartuṃ śakyaṃ [na] syāt vikretur abhāvāt, atas tasya prakāśakrayeṇa śuddhasyādaṇḍatvaṃ yuktam | api ca deśāntarād āgataiḥ pāpakāribhiḥ niḥśaṅkaṃ rājasaṃnidhāv apravikāśaṃ vikriyate dravyam, tatra ca yadi mūlyasyānāhāryatvāt prakāśakrayaśuddhe vikraye kretur doṣaḥ syāt, evaṃ ca sati rājñaḥ sarvadikko vyavahāraḥ sādhūnām api vicchidyeta | na caitad iṣṭam | ataḥ kreturn atra nāsti doṣaḥ | nāṣṭikas tu kāraṇataḥ svam arthaṃ prajñāpayan katham iva na labhate svadhanam: atas tasya dhanalābho yuktaḥ | itarasya cādoṣatvād adaṇḍyatvaṃ yuktam | asvāmivikrayavyavahārasādharmyāt tatprakaraṇam evāyam ucyate || 8.201 ||

	**nānyad anyena saṃsṛṣṭaṃ rūpaṃ vikrayam arhati |**

**	na sāvadyaṃ na ca nyūnaṃ na dūre na tirohitam || 8.202 ||**

**anyat** kuṅumādidravyam **anyena** kusumbhādinā dravyeṇa **saṃsṛṣṭaṃ vikrayaṃ** nārhati | evaṃ ca pratiṣedhād asyaivam akāryam anumīyate | evaṃ **sāvadyam** asaṃsṛṣṭam api yad bhāṇḍaṃ pūtikaṃ cirantanaṃ jīrṇavastrādi | **na ca nyūnaṃ** yat tulyāntareṇa paścād dhīyate palasaṃkhyayā | na dūre 'pratyakṣatvāt | etena **tirohitaṃ** vyākhyātam: adravyaṃ vā dravyābhāsaṃ yat kriyate bhāṇḍarāgādinā karmaṇā tat **tirohitam** | evaṃ ca sati, īdṛśam evaṃ vikrīṇānasya doṣatvād asya daṇḍārhatā | na kevalam aśuddhatā vikretuḥ | tathā ca sati, kretrā ūrdhvam api daśāhād etad vikretuḥ pratyarpaṇīyam eva | yenāsyāitat pratiṣedhaśāstram asadvikrayeṇāpoditam, "pareṇa tu daśāhasya na dadyān nāpi dāpayet" iti | vikrayasaṃbandhenaivāyam aparaḥ kānyavyavahāraḥ śulkāśrayaḥ prastūyate — || 8.202 ||

	**anyāṃ ced darśayitvānyā voḍhuḥ kanyā pradīyate |**

**	ubhe ta ekaśulkena vahed ity abravīn manuḥ || 8.203 ||**

niravadyāṃ kanyāṃ darśayitvā yaḥ sā[vadyāṃ dadā]ti tasya ubhe api **te ekaśulkena**iva vahanīye || 8.203 ||

	**nonmattāyā na kuṣṭhinyā na ca yā spṛṣṭamaithunā |**

**	pūrvaṃ doṣān abhikhyāpya pradātā daṇḍam arhati || 8.204 ||**

evaṃ ca sati doṣavatyās taddoṣākathane vipa[ryayaṇa dātā daṇḍyaḥ, pūrvam ā]vedane ūḍhāyāś ca doṣavatyā api parityāgo nāsti | kramaprāptaṃ saṃbhūyasamutthānam adhunocyate, yataḥ tadarthaṃ śrautam udāharaṇaṃ darśayati || 8.204 ||

	**ṛtvig yadi vṛto yajñe [svakarma parihāpayet |**

**	tasya karmānurūpyeṇa deyo 'ṃśaḥ saha ka]rtṛbhiḥ || 8.205 ||**

pradhānartvik prakrāntakarmā yadi **parihāpayet svakarma** deśāntaragamanāpāṭavādibhir arthalakṣaṇaiḥ **tasya karmānurūpyeṇa** dakṣiṇāṃśaḥ syāt | katham | karmaṇa[ś caturthe kṛte dakṣiṇā]yā api caturbhāgaḥ | evaṃ tribhāgādiṣv api yojyam | saha kartṛbhir iti [prati]prasthātṛprabhṛtīṃs tatputuṣān āha | asyāpavādaḥ — || 8.205 ||

	**dakṣiṇāsu tu dattāsu svakarma parihāpayan |**

**	kṛtsnam eva labhetāṃśam anyenaiva ca kārayet || 8.206 ||**

dakṣinādānād ūrdhvaṃ teṣāṃ svakarmākurvatāṃ kāraṇāntarato na pratyāharaṇīyā dakṣiṇās tebhyaḥ | akurva[tāṃ yān]y aupartiṣṭāni karmāṇi anyenaiva ca kārayet tāni tatpuruṣeṇa vānyena vā, pariśiṣṭakarmānurūpaṃ yat kiṃcid dattvā, itarathā hy aparijitaṃ dakṣiṇayā tatkarmayajamānārthaṃ na syāt | idam eva śāstraṃ pariśiṣṭakarmānuṣṭhātur dakṣiṇādāne vijñeyam | anena ca prasaṅgenedam aparaṃ tadgatam evocyate || 8.206 ||

	**yasmin karmaṇi yās tu syur uktāḥ pratyaṅgadakṣiṇāḥ |**

**	sa eva tā ādadīta bhajeran sarva eva vā || 8.207 ||**

pratyaṅgadakṣiṇāḥ sarvadā saṃśayyante | kim amīṣām ṛtvijāṃ pratigrahaniyamaś cāturvidyaviniyuktapādikabrāhmaṇavat, uta padārthasvarūpasvābhāvyāt tadartheneti nyāyavikalpo 'nūdyate | tādarthyapakṣaṃ cāśrityaitad adhunocyate || 8.207 ||

	**rathaṃ hareta cādhvaryur brahmādhāne ca vājinam |**

**	hotā vāpi hared aśvam udgātā cāpy anaḥ kraye || 8.208 ||**

kratau nānāśākhāsv avasthitānām aṅgadakṣiṇānāṃ bahvīnāṃ pradarśanārthaḥ ślokaḥ | evaṃ tāvad ādhāne pradhānartvigdakṣiṇā anaḥ somikeṣv api || 8.208 ||

	**sarveṣām ardhino mukhyās tad ardhenārdhino 'pare |**

**	tṛtīyinas tṛtīyāṃśāś caturthāṃśās tu pādinaḥ || 8.209 ||**

"tāñ chatena dākṣayanti" iti vacanād aṣṭacatvāriṃśad bhavantīti | evaṃ tadardhād iva saṃkhyānirdeśa uttaratra samartho bhavati | ten**ārdhino** 'dhvaryubrahmodgātṛhotāro **mukhyā** ṛtvijo bhavanti | tadardhena caturviṃśatyā **ardhino 'pare** uktebhyo dvitīyasthānaṃ pratiprasthātṛmaitrāvaruṇabrāhmaṇācchaṃsiprastotāraḥ | evaṃ ca kātyāyanaḥ "ṣat ṣat dvitīyebhyaḥ" vakti | **tṛtīyinaḥ** tṛtīyaṃ sthānaṃ yeṣāṃ ta ime tṛtiyinaḥ, tṛtīyāṃśāḥ | samudāyena ṣoḍaśa paśubhājaḥ | kātyāyano 'pi caivam eva vakti: "catasraś catasras tṛtīyebhyaḥ" iti | pratyekaṃ caturtha aṃśo yeṣāṃ ta ime **caturthāṃśāḥ** samudāyato dvādaśapaśubhājaḥ **pādino** bhavanti | kātyāyano 'pi "tisras tisra itarebhyaḥ" | ādyasaṃkhyāpekṣayā pāda eṣām astīti **pādinaḥ** | caturthasthānā ucyante | sthāne sthānināṃ vyapadeśo 'yam | **caturthāṃśa**śabdas tu bhāgakalpakaḥ samāsapadena | tathā coktam, viparyayeṇa vaitad vyākhyeyam | ubhavanirdeśaś cātra pādapūraṇārtho vijñeyaḥ | yady apy anyatarasmād ubhayārthapratītiḥ ayaṃ sarvo vidhir nyāyaśrutisiddho dṛṣṭāntatvenehopādīyate | yathā saṃbhūyaikaṃ karma sahakurvatāṃ dṛṣṭā gurulaghutām avakṣyānavekṣya vā vacanasāmarthyād viṣamāṃśaprakḷptiḥ | evam — || 8.209 ||

	**saṃbhūya svāni karmāṇi kurvadbhir iha mānavaiḥ |**

**	anena vidhiyogena kartavyāṃśaprakalpanā || 8.210 ||**

ekasmin gṛhakaraṇādau sūtrakāravadhakisthapatyādīnāṃ gurulaghutām avakṣyānavekṣya vā yathāsmaraṇaṃ **kartavyāṃśaprakalpanā** | na hy aśilpeṣu vyavahāreṣu vā manuṣyāṇāṃ tulyatā śakyā grahītum | adattānapakarma[var]ṇārtham idam āha — || 8.210 ||

	**dharmārthaṃ yena dattaṃ syāt kasmaicid yācate dhanam |**

**	paścāc ca na tathā tat syān na deyaṃ tasya tad bhavet || 8.211 ||**

svanigadopavarṇitaḥ ślokaḥ || 8.211 ||

	**yadi saṃsādayet tat tu darpāl lobhena vā punaḥ |**

**	rā[jñā dāpyaḥ suvarṇaṃ syāt tasya steyasya niṣkṛtiḥ] || 8.212 ||**

yena dharmārthaṃ kiṃcit pratiśrutaṃ na tu dattam | taṃ ced dharmam akurvan pratiśrutam iti kṛtvā sādhayed adātāram, tato **rājñā suvarṇaṃ** sa **dāpyaḥ** | sopadhaṃ [yācitāraḥ na steyakāriṇaḥ, anyāyakāritvād u]ddhṛtadaṇḍās tv iti || 8.212 ||

	**dattasyaiṣoditā dharmyā yathāvad anapakriyā |**

**	ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi vetanasyānapakriyām || 8.213 ||**

upasaṃhāropanyāsārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 8.214 ||

	**bhṛ[to 'nārto na kuryād yo darpāt] karma yathoditam |**

**	sa daṇḍyaḥ kṛṣṇalāny aṣṭau na deyaṃ cāsya vetanam || 8.214 ||**

utpanne vetane kiṃcitkṛtakarmāpi daṇḍayitavyaḥ vetanaṃ ca [na] labheta, yena darpāt karmaṇaḥ prakrāntasyākṛtsnakārī || 8.214 ||

	**ārtas tu kuryāt svasthaḥ san yathā bhāṣitam āditaḥ |**

**	sudīrghasyāpi kālasya tal labhetaiva vetanam || 8.215 ||**

pratītārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 8.215 ||

	**yathoktam ārtaḥ svastho vā yas tatkarma na kārayet |**

**	na tasya vetanaṃ deyam alponasyāpi karmaṇaḥ || 8.216 ||**

ārtaḥ svastho vā yathoditaṃ karma na kurvan, na kārayan vā, alponasyāpi vetanaṃ na labheta || 8.216 ||

	**eṣa dharmo 'khilenokto vetanādānakarmaṇaḥ |**

**	ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi dharmaṃ samayabhedinām || 8.217 ||**

upasaṃhāropanyāsārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 8.217 ||

	**yo grāmadeśasaṅghānāṃ kṛtvā satyena saṃvidam |**

**	visaṃvaden naro lobhāt taṃ rāṣṭrād vpravāsayet || 8.218 ||**

dharmārthayukteṣu prayojaneṣu rājakāryāvirodhiṣu gopracārodakarakṣaṇadevatāyatanapratisaṃskaraṇādiṣu grāmādīnāṃ yā saṃvid utpadyate, tatra vyabhicāriṇaṃ tasmād deśād rājā nirvāsayet || 8.218 ||

	**nigṛhya dāpayec cainaṃ samayavyabhicāriṇam |**

**	catus suvarṇān ṣaṇniṣkāñ chatamānaṃ ca rājatam || 8.219 ||**

**catuḥ suvarṇādi** ca daṇḍaṃ ca dāpyaḥ, tato nirvāsyaḥ | "nigṛhya dāpayed vainam" ity aparo daṇḍavikalpapāṭhaḥ | evaṃ ca sati nirvāsanaṃ daṇḍo vā || 8.219 ||

	**etad daṇḍavidhiṃ kuryād dhārmikaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ |**

**	grāmajātisamūheṣu samayavyabhicāriṇām || 8.220 ||**

upasaṃhārārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 8.220 ||

	**krītvā vikrīya vā kiṃcid yasyehānuśayo bhavet |**

**	so 'yaṃ daśāhāt taddravyaṃ dadyāc caivādadīta ca || 8.221 ||**

antardaśāham ādānapratyarpaṇe sāmnety ayam apāṭhaḥ | yenordhvam api daśāhāt kaḥ śaktas sāmnā dānādāne pratiṣeddhum | labdhimeṣv api dravyeṣu sāmāśakyaṃ pratiṣeddhum, kiṃ punaḥ kṛtrimeṣu, yatra kaścid dharmagatir nāsti | dharmyeṣu tu pratigraheṣu tadanantaranirvṛttatvād dharmasya sāmnāpy aśkyaṃ kṛtam akṛtaṃ kartum | tatra pratyarpaṇe punardānaṃ vā kṛtaṃ bhavet parityāgo vā | yataś caitad evam | ata evaṃ paṭhitavya uttaraślokārdhaḥ: "so 'yaṃ daśāhāt taddravyaṃ dadyāc caivādadīta ca" iti | atraivārtha uttaraślokārdhapāṭho 'nyo bhavati: "dānādāne daśāhaṃ tu syātām api nipātini" iti | atha vā sāmagrahaṇaṃ daśāhe daṇḍanivṛttyartham | antardaśāhānuśaye kathaṃcid vivadatāṃ rājādhigame daṇḍanivṛttir yathā syād rājatas tayoḥ | tathā ca daśāhasyottaratra tadvivāde daṇḍaḥ śrūyate || 8.221 ||

	**pareṇa tu daśāhasya na dadyān nāpi dāpayet |**

**	ādadāno dadac caiva rājñā dāpyaḥ śatāni ṣaṭ || 8.222 ||**

nāyaṃ śloko daśāhād ūrdhvaṃ sāmapratiṣedhārtha ārabhyate, sāmnāpy ūrdhvaṃ daśāhān **na dadyān nāpi dāpayed** iti | na hi sāma pratiṣeddhuṃ śakyam ity uktam | yatra tu sāmnāpi pratyarpaṇaṃ nāsti, tatra niyamayaty eva, yathā "sakṛd aṃśo nipatati" iti; atrāpi tv aṃśapātane sāmnāiva pratiṣeddhuṃ śakyaṃ niyamābhāvād, vyavasthārthatvāc ca | kanyādāne tu niṣkramavisargābhyām iti viśeṣaniyamāt sāma na vidyate || 8.222 ||

_anuśayaprasaṅgād idam anyad atrocyate |_

	**yas tu doṣavatīṃ kanyām anākhyāya prayacchati |**

**	tasya kuryān nṛpo daṇḍaṃ svayaṃ ṣaṇṇavatiṃ paṇān || 8.223 ||**

dharmaprajānirodhinā rogeṇa gṛhītā spṛṣṭamaithunā vā doṣavatī | tām **anākhyāya doṣavatīṃ** prayacchato daṇḍaḥ, "nonmattāyā" iti pūrvoktaślokenaiva gatārtho, yataḥ vayam atra nādhīyāmahe | atha vānuvādapakṣaḥ kenacit kāraṇena tasyāsya ca śakyate darśayitum, yato yuktam adhyayanam [ihāpi || 8.223 ||

	**akanyeti tu yaḥ kanyāṃ brūyād dve]ṣeṇa mānavaḥ |**

**	sa śataṃ prāpnuyād daṇḍaṃ tasyā doṣam adarśayan || 8.224 ||**

svaśabdavyākhyātaḥ ślokaḥ | kasya punar hetor ayaṃ daṇḍo mahān vidhīyate, yena — || 8.224 ||

	**pāṇigrāhaṇikā mantrāḥ kanyāsv eva [pratiṣṭhitāḥ |**

**	nākanyāsu kvacin nṛṇāṃ luptadharmakriyā hi tāḥ] || 8.225 ||**

tathā vaivāhiko mantraḥ "aryamaṇaṃ devaṃ kanyāgnimayakṣata | sa no aryamā devaḥ preto muñcatu mā pateḥ svāhā" ityādinā **kanyāsv** ity atra [mantrārthaḥ, tāsv eva pratiṣṭhi]tā vivāhādibhir ity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca sati pūrvaṃ pāṇigrahaṇāt pratigṛhītāpi spṛṣṭamaithunā parityaktavyeti || 8.225 ||

_yaś ca |_

	**pāṇigrāhaṇikā mantrā niyataṃ dāralakṣa[ṇam |**

**	teṣāṃ niṣṭhā tu vijñeyā vidvadbhiḥ saptame pade || 8.226 ||**

vivāh]ārthe saṃskāre [pāṇigra]halakṣaṇe bhavāh pāṇigrāhaṇikāḥ, tatkarmasādhanabhūtā mantrāḥ | niyataṃ dāralakṣaṇaṃ dāropasaṃgrahalakṣaṇam, kanyānām eva gṛhyaśāstrato nākanyānām | tathā ca darśayati: "vivāhe udagayana āpūryamāṇapakṣe puṇyāhe, kumāryāḥ pāṇiṃ gṛhṇīyāt | triṣu triṣūttarādiṣu | svātau mṛgaśirasi rohiṇyāṃ vā" iti | punaś caitam evārthaṃ saṃdarśayati: "kumāryā bhrātā śamipalāśamiśrāl lājān añjalināñjalāv āvapati | tāñ juhoti sarṭ hatena (?) tiṣṭhati" iti | yataś caitad eva | atas **teṣāṃ niṣṭhā tu vujñeyā vidvadbhiḥ saptame pade | teṣāṃ** mantrāṇāṃ pāṇigrahaṇaprayojanānāṃ **saptame pade** niṣṭhā parisamāptiḥ | pretya tasya kāryataḥ prāptavyasya saptalokasaṃsthasya jagataḥ iyatparimāṇatvāt | sapta hi lokā bhūrādayaḥ satyāntāḥ; tān asau padasaṃkhyā saṃmitāṃs tayā saha śrautasmārtaiḥ karmabhir yātum icchati | tathā ca mantraḥ etadarthānuvādy eva bhavati: "sakhā saptapadī bhava" iti | evaṃ ca sati, āsaptabhyaḥ padebhyaḥ spṛṣṭamaithunatvena vijñātā heyā bhavati | ūrdhvaṃ tu saptamāt padāt spṛṣṭamaithunāpi satī na parityājyā | tasmān niṣṭhāvacanaliṅgād bhavati | tathā ca sati sahoḍhakānīnayoḥ śāstropadeśaḥ samartho bhavati | yā tu rogiṇī satī dharmaprajananayor anyatrasamarthā bhavati, tāṃ pratigṛhya notsṛjeta | na ha tasyā dharmāvirodhe prajāvirodhe vā sati puṃsā kartavyatānyāsti | athāpy asyādṛṣṭārthaḥ saprayogaḥ, tathāpy asau prāg agnyādheyād anyām udvāhayiṣyati | yā tūbhayor api dharmaprajananayor samarthā sā vidyamānayātulyeti parityājyaiva | ayaṃ ca kanyāvyavahāraḥ krayavikrayānuśayasādṛśyād etasminn avadhāv ucyata iti || 8.226 ||

	**yasmin yasmin kṛte kārye yasyehānuśayo bhavet |**

**	tam anena vidhānena dharme pathi niveśayet || 8.227 ||**

ādhivetanasamayādyanuśayeṣu daśāha eva niṣṭhā syāt || 8.227 ||

	**paśuṣu svāmināṃ caiva pālānāṃ ca vyatikrame |**

**	vivādaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi yathāvad dharmatattvataḥ || 8.228 ||**

upanyāsārthaślokaḥ || 8.228 ||

	**divā vaktavyatā pāle rātrau svāmini tadgṛhe |**

**	yogakṣeme 'nyathā cet tu pālo vaktavyatām iyāt || 8.229 ||**

partītārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 8.229 ||

	**gopaḥ kṣīrabhṛto yas tu sa duhed daśato varām |**

**	gosvāmy anumatāṃ bhṛtyaḥ sā syāt pāle 'bhṛte bhṛtiḥ || 8.230 ||**

**kṣīrabhṛto** [na] bhktācchādanabhṛto, dvividho yasmād gopaḥ | ata idaṃ viśeṣyate | **kṣīrabhṛto yas tu gopaḥ** **sa duhed daśataḥ** daśabhyo dhenubhya ekāṃ **varāṃ** śreṣṭhām ity arthaḥ | tām api ca **gosvāmy** anumataḥ, na svecchayā, **sā syāt pāle** bhṛtyantareṇ**ābhṛte bhṛtiḥ **| evaṃ ca sati pañcāvasthāsu goṣu bahvavasthāsu vā gosvāmibhir gopaiś ca tribhāgaḥ kṣīrasya kalpitaḥ parikalpya bhogyābhogyarūpāṇy anenaiva śāstreṇa, yenāitasmād eva ca darśanāt kṣīrabhṛtiḥ paśūnāṃ saṃrakaṇe na doṣāyāpratiṣedhāt tasyā iti | evaṃ ca sati — || 8.230 ||

	**naṣṭaṃ vinaṣṭaṃ kṛmibhiś śvahataṃ viṣame mṛtam |**

**	hīnaṃ puruṣakāreṇa [pradadyāt pāla eva tu] || 8.231 ||**

gopapramādena || 8.231 ||

_asyāpavādaḥ_ |

	**vighuṣya tu hṛtaṃ corair na pālo dātum arhati |**

**	vadi deśe ca kāle ca svāminaḥ svasya śaṃsati || 8.232 ||**

haraṇa**deśe** haraṇa**kāle** ca vighuṣya anantaraṃ **svāmina** ākhyāte **pālo** na dadyāt | svayaṃ mṛtyunāpi ca mṛteṣu prayatnavato gopasya sa idaṃ kuryāt || 8.232 ||

	**karṇau ca carma vālāṃś ca bastisnāyūni rocanām |**

**	paśusvāmiṣu dadyāt tu mṛteṣv aṅkāṃś ca darśa[yet || 8.233 ||**

vidhir ayaṃ] cāviśeṣaḥ || 8.233 ||

_[ajā]vikārtham idam āha |_

	**ajāvike tu saṃruddhe vṛkaiḥ pāle tv anāyati |**

**	yāṃ prasahya vṛko hanyāt pāle tatkilbiṣaṃ bhavet || 8.234 ||**

paśurakṣakasya satas tadasaṃni[dhāne vā vṛko hanyāt sa eva] dadyāt | yasmād avaruddhānāṃ saṃnihito na bhavati | vṛkagrahaṇaṃ cānyeṣām api pradarśanārtham || 8.234 ||

	**tāsāṃ ced avaruddhānāṃ carantīnāṃ mitho vane |**

**	yām utplutya vṛko hanyān na pāla[s tatra kilbiṣī] || 8.235 ||**

aśakyatvād aṭavyāṃ bahuvṛkṣakṣupagartāyāṃ tatsaṃrakṣaṇasya mithaś carantīnāṃ na pālāparādhaḥ | etena gomahiṣyādi vyākhyātam | ukto gosaṃrakṣaṇavidhiḥ | paśupīḍāpaśusaṃhārārtham idam ucya[te] || 8.235 ||

	**dhanuḥ śataṃ parīhāro grāmasya syāt samantataḥ |**

**	śamyāpātās trayo vāpi triguṇo nagarasya tu || 8.236 ||**

yo deśo grāmanagarayoḥ samantato gavāṃ sukhapracārasthānāsanārtham anuptasasyakāryaḥ || 8.236 ||

	**tatrāparivṛtaṃ dhānyaṃ vihiṃsyuḥ paśavo yadi |**

**	na tatra praṇayed daṇḍaṃ nṛpatiḥ paśurakṣiṇām || 8.237 ||**

yadi tu tatra bhūlopāt samupyate na kenacit parivṛtaṃ ca bhavet, tatas tadbhakṣaṇe gobhir na doṣaḥ syāt paśurakṣiṇām || 8.237 ||

	**vṛtiṃ tatra tu kurvīta yām uṣṭro nāvalokayet |**

**	chidraṃ cāvārayet sarvaṃ śvasūkaramukhānugam | 8.238 ||**

paśuvāraṇasamarthāyām tu vṛtau kṛtāyāṃ sasyopaghāte pālasya doṣaḥ syāt || 8.238 ||

	**pathi kṣetre 'parivṛte grāmāntīye 'tha vā punaḥ |**

**	sa pālaḥ śatadaṇḍārho vipālaṃ vārayet paśum || 8.239 ||**

yaṣṭipātena khādayan pālaḥ śatadaṇḍārhaḥ syāt, **vipālaṃ** ca **paśuṃ vārayet** | adaṇḍaś ca syāt paśupālaḥ tadasaṃnidhānāt | anyas tv atrārthaḥ saha pālena **sapālaḥ** kṣetrikaḥ na paśur atrocyate | pūrvavacchatadaṇḍārhaḥ syāt | ubhayāparādhāt, kṣetrikeṇa tāvat kim iti kṣetraṃ svam anāvṛtam iti, tasmād ubhayāparādhād ubhayor daṇḍaḥ | gautamīye 'pi coktam "pathi kṣetre 'nāvṛte pālakṣetrikayoḥ" iti || 8.239 ||

	**kṣetreṣv anyeṣu tu paśuḥ sapādaṃ paṇam arhati |**

**	sarvatra tu śado deyaḥ kṣetrikasyeti dhāraṇā || 8.240 ||**

anyakṣetrāṇi pūrvoktād avadher yāni bahiḥ tāny ucyante | goś ca sapādasya paṇasyopadeśād, upaghātānurūpeṇa mahiṣyādīnāṃ syād rājabhāvyo daṇḍaḥ | **śadaḥ kṣetrikasya** **sarvatra**śabdāc ca vipāle 'pi śado deyat iti || 8.240 ||

	**anirdaśāhāṃ gāṃ sūtāṃ vṛṣān devapaśūṃs tathā |**

**	sapālān vāpy apālān vā na daṇḍyān manur abravīt || 8.241 ||**

pūrvāpavādaḥ | vṛṣāḥ sektāraḥ prati tān | devapaśavaś cotsṛṣṭā vṛṣotsarganyāyena, anye ca mṛgā āpy ajādayo devāyatanamaṇḍanā adaṇḍyāḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca niṣparigrahatvād devapaśuṣv etad ayuktaṃ, saparigrahānugamād eṣāṃ tadvatprāptau satyām apavādaḥ | atha vā dṛṣṭāntārtham eva paśava upādīyante | yathā devapaśavo 'daṇḍyāḥ, evam anirdaśāhā gauḥ sūtā vṛṣāś ca sektāra iti parigrahavad vā | devāyataneṣv etad daṇḍaṃ na yuktam | evaṃ ca sati yo 'nyeṣāṃ parigrahavatāṃ darmaḥ sa eva teṣām api syāt | na caitad iṣṭam || 8.241 ||

	**kṣetrikasyātyaye daṇḍo bhāgād daśaguṇo bhavet |**

**	tato 'rdhadaṇḍo bhṛtyānām ajñānāt kṣetrikasya tu || 8.242 ||**

yasmāt sasyāt kṣetriko yad apaharet tasya bhāgakalpanayā daśaguṇo daṇḍaḥ prakalpyaḥ | **ardhadaṇḍā** bhṛtyāḥ syuḥ | **ajñānāt kṣetrikasya tu** prayogād eva bhṛtyānām asāv eva daṇḍaḥ syāt | sasyasambandhaprasaṅgāc cāyaṃ kṣetrikasya vyatikrama ucyate, asteyābhimatatvāc ca || 8.242 ||

	**etad vidhānam ātiṣṭhed dhārmikaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ |**

**	svāmināṃ ca paśūnāṃ ca pālānāṃ ca vyatikrame || 8.243 ||**

upasaṃhārāthaḥ ślokaḥ || 8.243 ||

	**sīmāṃ prati samutpanne vivāde grāmayor dvayoḥ |**

**	jyeṣṭhamāse nayet sīmāṃ suprakāśeṣu setuṣu || 8.244 ||**

upanyāsaś cittapraṇidhānārthaḥ | **jyeṣṭhamāse** setavaḥ, sīmāvyavacchedahetavaḥ, suvijñātā bhavanti || 8.244 ||

	**sīmāvṛkṣāṃs tu kurvīta nyagrodhāśvatthakiṃśukān |**

**	śālmalīn śālatālāṃś ca kṣīriṇaś caiva pādapān || 8.245 ||**

**	gulmān veṇūṃś ca vividhāñ chamīvallīsthalāni ca |**

**	śarān kubjakagulmāṃś ca tathā sīmā na naśyati || 8.246 ||**

**	taṭākāny udapānāni vāpīḥ prasravaṇāni ca |**

**	sīmāsaṃdhiṣu kāryāṇi devatāyatanāni ca || 8.247 ||**

**	upacchannāni cānyāni sīmāliṅgāni kārayet |**

**	sīmā[jñāne] nṛṇāṃ vīkṣya loke nityaṃ viparyayam || 8.248 ||**

**	aśmano 'sthīni govālāṃs tuṣān bhasma kapālikāḥ |**

**	karīṣam iṣṭakāṅgārāṃś charkarā vālukās tathā || 8.249 ||**

**	yāni caivaṃ prakārāṇi kālād bhūmir na bhakṣayet |**

**	tāni saṃdhiṣu [sīmāyām aprakāśaṃ] nidhāpayet || 8.250 ||**

ṣaṭ cchlokāḥ sīmāsetuprakāradarśanārthāḥ || 8.245–250 ||

	**etair liṅgair nayet sīmāṃ rājā vivadamānayoḥ |**

**	pūrvabhuktyā ca satatam udakasyāgamena ca || 8.251 ||**

yatra nibaddhāni liṅgā[ni naṣṭāni] na cānyatarasya śūnyatā smaryate, tatra pūrvabhuktiḥ pramāṇam | anyataraśūnyatve tu 'na bhogena praṇaśyati" iti pūrvabhuktir nāśriyate | vidyate hi bhogasya nimitta[tvam yasmāt aśūnye 'va]cchedaḥ kriyate | kim atra liṅgakaraṇena srota eva hi nityam abhipravṛttaṃ sīmāsthāpakaṃ bhaviṣyati | na hi pūrvabhuktau satyām udakāgamo nirhetuko vikalpena vā bādha[ko yuktaḥ kalpa]yitum | tasmāc chūnyaviṣaya eva sukhapratipattyartha āyatyupetayor udakāgamaḥ kalpyate | atha vā mahāsroto [aśūnya]viṣaya eva draṣṭavyaḥ | srotāṃsi hi mahānti kadācit [apathena] pravartante, tatra pūrvabhuktim atītyāpi srota eva nirṇayāya syād iti || 8.251 ||

	**yadi saṃśaya eva syāl liṅgānām api darśane |**

**	sākṣipratyaya eva syāt sīmāvāde vinirṇayaḥ || 8.252 ||**

[na kutaścil liṅg]otpattāv ubhayathā liṅgānusmṛtau ca sākṣipratyayaḥ || 8.252 ||

	**grāmeyakakulānāṃ tu samakṣaṃ sīmasākṣiṇaḥ |**

**	praṣṭavyāḥ sīmaliṅgāni tayoś caiva vivādinoḥ || 8.253 ||**

praśnavidhiḥ || 8.253 ||

	**te pṛṣṭās tu yathā brūyuḥ samastāḥ sīmni niścayam |**

**	nibadhnīyāt tathā sīmāṃ sarvāṃs tāṃś caiva nāmataḥ || 8.254 ||**

nibandhanaṃ lekhyam api smaraṇārthaṃ tal likhet || 8.254 ||

	**śirobhis te gṛhītvorvīṃ sragviṇo raktavāsasaḥ |**

**	sukṛtaiḥ śāpitāḥ svaiḥ svair nayeyus te samañjasam || 8.255 ||**

nayanavidhiḥ || 8.255 ||

	**yathoktena nayantas te pūyante satyasākṣiṇaḥ |**

**	viparītaṃ nayantas te dāpyāḥ syur dviśataṃ damam || 8.256 ||**

stutiḥ prarocanārthā | daṇḍaś ca yathoktaḥ | viparītanayanaṃ tv anyena vyavahārāntareṇa jñātavyam || 8.256 ||

	**sākṣyabhāve tu catvāro grāmyāḥ sāmantavāsinaḥ |**

**	sīmno vinirṇayaṃ kuryuḥ prayatā rājasaṃnidhau || 8.257 ||**

pūrve 'nubhāvinaḥ | ime tu sāmantāḥ karṇaparaṃparayā śrutavantaḥ || 8.257 ||

	**sāmantānām abhāve tu maulānāṃ sīmni sākṣiṇām |**

**	imān apy anuyuñjīta puruṣān vanagocarān || 8.258 ||**

tadabhāve tu vanagocarāḥ pramāṇaṃ syuḥ || 8.258 ||

	**vyādhāñ chākunikān gopān kaivartān mūlakhanakān |**

**	vyālagrāhān uñchavṛttīn anyāṃś ca vanagocarān || 8.259 ||**

**	te pṛṣṭās tu yathā brūyuḥ sīmāsaṃdhiṣu lakṣaṇam |**

**	tat tathā sthāpayed rājā dharmeṇa grāmayor dvayoḥ || 8.260 ||**

upasaṃhārārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 8.260 ||

	**kṣetrakūpataṭākānām ārāmasya gṛhasya ca |**

**	sāmantapratyayo jñeyaḥ sīmāsetuvinirṇayaḥ || 8.261 ||**

sīmni gurutvād arthasya kadācid daśavarṣāṇi nābhiyogaṃ kuryuḥ | atas tatra 'na bhogena praṇaśyati" ity uktam | kṣetrādiṣu [tv] atyalpatvād arthasya "yat kiṃcid daśavarṣāni" ity ayam eva pakṣa āśrīyate | ata eṣāṃ **sāmantapratyayo** nirṇaya ucyate | yathaivānyeṣāṃ dravyāṇāṃ sākṣipratyayo nirṇayaḥ, evam amīṣām apīti || 8.261 ||

	**sāmantāś cen mṛṣā brūyuḥ setau vivadatāṃ nṛṇām |**

**	sarve pṛthak pṛthag daṇḍyā rājñā madhyamasāhasam || 8.262 ||**

sīmsākṣiṇām ayaṃ viśeṣadaṇḍaḥ || 8.262 ||

	**gṛhaṃ taṭākam ārāmaṃ kṣetraṃ vā bhīṣayā haran |**

**	śatāni pañca daṇḍyas syād ajñānād dviśato damaḥ || 8.263 ||**

jñānājñānaharaṇe 'yaṃ daṇḍaḥ || 8.263 ||

	**sīmāyām aviṣahyāyāṃ svayaṃ rājaiva dharmavit |**

**	pradiśed bhūmim eteṣām upakārād iti sthitiḥ || 8.264 ||**

dūratvād aśakyopabhogāyāṃ rājā dṛṣṭopakārasaṃbandhenaikatra prayacchet bhūmim | na ca rājño grahaṇe tatra doṣaḥ | evamarthaś cāyam upadeśaḥ; ato 'pradāne 'pi na doṣaḥ || 8.264 ||

	**eṣo 'khilenābhihito dharmaḥ sīmāvinirṇaye |**

**	ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi vākpāruṣyasya nirṇayam || 8.265 ||**

upasaṃhāropanyāsārthaḥ ślokaḥ | nanu caivaṃ kramabhedaḥ, "pāruṣye daṇḍavācike" ity abhidhānād vyavahārāspandānukraṇyām | [śabdakram]āt tatra pūrvaṃ daṇḍapāruṣyagrahaṇam | ayaṃ tv arthakramam aśrityātra vākpāruṣyasya pūrvam upanyāsaḥ | sa ca śabdakramād garīyān | yato nāsti kramabhedaḥ, alpāctaratvād (?) [asmin dvan]dve || 8.265 ||

	**śataṃ brāhmaṇam ākruśya kṣatriyo daṇḍam arhati |**

**	vaiśyo 'dhyardhaśataṃ dve vā śūdras tu vadham arhati || 8.266 ||**

avacanīyād ākrośād ṛte anyasminn ākrośe ete yathārhaṃ daṇḍavi[dhayaḥ brāḥmaṇākrośane yo] vaiśyasya daṇḍa uktaḥ tato 'rdhaṃ kṣatriyam ākruśya vaiśyasya nyāyād āpnoti daṇḍam | śūdrasya tv ekajātidaṇḍaḥ "ekajātir dvijātim" iti dvijātimātr[ākrośane tadvidhānāt || 8.266 ||

	**pañcāśad brāhmaṇo daṇḍyaḥ kṣatri]yasyābhiśaṃsane |**

**	vaiśye syād ardhapañcāśac chūdre dvādaśako damaḥ || 8.267 ||**

gadavyākhyātaḥ ślokaḥ | atrāpi nyāyaprakḷptyā kṣatriyo vaiśyam ākru[śya brāhmaṇadaṇḍād dviguṇaṃ] daṇḍyaḥ syāt, vaiśyas tu śūdram ākruśya brāhmaṇadaṇḍāt triguṇaṃ dadyāt || 8.267 ||

	**samavarṇe dvijātīnāṃ dvādaśaiva vyatikrame |**

**	vādeṣv avacanīyeṣu tad eva dviguṇaṃ bhavet || 8.268 ||**

[brāhmaṇasya] brāhmaṇa (?) | evam itarayor api | śūdre 'pi kāryasāmānyād etad eva syāt | evaṃ ca dvijātigrahaṇasyāvivakṣitatvād ekajātipradarśanārtham apy etad atra syāt | **avacanīyeṣu** tu vādeṣu "śataṃ brāhmaṇam ākruṣya" iti evamādiṣu yad yad uktaṃ tat tad dviguṇaṃ tatra syāt || 8.268 ||

	**ekajātir dvijātiṃ tu vācā dāruṇayā kṣipan |**

**	jihvāhāḥ prāpnuyāc chedaṃ jaghanyaprabhavo hi saḥ || 8.269 ||**

brāhmaṇākrośe vadha uktaḥ śūdrasya | yato 'yaṃ kṣatriyavaiśyākrośe tasya daṇḍavidhir jñeyaḥ | yataḥ jihvācchedaś cāprāṇoparodhī sāmārthyād asya vijñāyate || 8.269 ||

	**nāmajātigrahaṃ caiṣām abhidroheṇa kurvataḥ |**

**	nikheyo 'yomayaḥ śaṅkur jvalann āsye daśāṅgulaḥ || 8.270 ||**

avacanīyair abhidroheṇākrośataḥ śūdrasyānena prakāreṇa vadha upadiśyate || 8.270 ||

	**dharmopadeśaṃ darpeṇa viprāṇām asya kurvataḥ |**

**	taptam āsecayet tailaṃ vaktre śrotre ca pārthivaḥ || 8.271 ||**

dharmopadeśasāmarthyaṃ caitacchūdrasyārthād vijñeyam | evaṃ ca sati nedaṃ liṅgaṃ śūdrasya śāstraprāpter bhavati || 8.271 ||

	**śrutaṃ deśaṃ ca jātiṃ ca karma śārīram eva ca |**

**	vitathena bruvan darpād dāpyaḥ syād dviśataṃ damam || 8.272 ||**

saty api śūdraprakaraṇe sarveṣāṃ brāhmaṇādīnām ayaṃ vidhir jñeyaḥ sāmarthāt || 8.272 ||

	**kāṇaṃ vāpy atha vā khañjam anyaṃ vāpi tathāvidham |**

**	tathyenāpi bruvan dāpyo (?) daṇḍaṃ kārṣāpaṇāvaram || 8.273 ||**

kārṣāpaṇāvaratvaṃ cāparādhaṃ parijñāya sthāpyam | tathā ca vihitadaṇḍāpavādaḥ śāstrokta evānubandhaṃ parijñāyety evamādi || 8.273 ||

	**mātaraṃ pitaraṃ jāyāṃ bhrātaraṃ tanayaṃ gurum |**

**	ākṣārayañ chataṃ dāpyaḥ panthānaṃ cādadad guroḥ || 8.274 ||**

atra śloke jāyātanayagrahaṇam arthavādartham | kathaṃ kṛtvā | bhāryāputrayor eva tāvad ākṣāraṇe 'yam asya daṇḍo bhavitum arhati, prāg eva mātrādīnām | yasmān mātrādibh[ir nyū]natvaṃ bhāryāputrayoḥ | etasmāt sāmarthyād idam evaṃ vyākaraṇīyam | bhrātā ca yadi kanīyān tata eṣaivātra (?) vyākhyā | ata tu jyeṣṭhasya grahaṇam, tato gurutvād asya vidhyarthataiva nyāyyā | evaṃ ca sati gurugrahaṇaṃ vidyāguruprabhṛtīnām avarodhārtham | gurugrahaṇād eva ca mātrādigrahaṇe siddhe pṛthag upadeśas teṣām ādarārtho vijñeyaḥ | idaṃ cānyad arthāntaraviṣayaṃ vākyāntaraṃ samānadaṇḍatvād asminn evāvadhāv ucyate | **panthānaṃ cādadad guroḥ** sarvaprakārasyānākṣārayann apy ayam eva daṇḍa ekaḥ kāryaḥ syāt | etasmād eva ca gurugrahaṇāt pūrvatra bhāryāputragrahaṇam arthavādārthaṃ sutarāṃ vijñāyate | yena samānadaṇḍa eva vyabhicārāntarau śrūyete | ākṣāraṇaṃ ca prataradvākpāruṣyaviśeṣa ākrośādiḥ | anyas tv āha: anṛtena bhedanam ākṣāraṇam | anṛtābhiśaṃsanaṃ tv aparaḥ | tat tv etad ubhayaṃ prakaraṇavirodhād vicāraṇīyaṃ yuktāyuktatvena || 8.274 ||

	**brāhmaṇakṣatriyābhyāṃ tu daṇḍau kāryau vijānatā |**

**	brāhmaṇe sāhasaḥ pūrvaḥ kṣatriya tv eva madhyamaḥ || 8.275 ||**

**	viṭśūdrayor evam eva svajātiṃ prati tattvataḥ |**

**	chedavarjaṃ praṇayanaṃ daṇḍasyeti viniścayaḥ || 8.276 ||**

ayam apara upadeśasāmarthyād vikalpārtho vidhir ucyate | yadā brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyam ākrośati tadā tasya pūrvasāhasaḥ | yadā ca kṣatriyo brāhmaṇaṃ tadā tatra madhyamaḥ sāhasaḥ | evaṃ kṣatriyavaiśyayos tathā vaiśyaśūdrayoḥ | evaṃ ca sati śūdrasya jihvāchedanavarjaṃ daṇḍanipātanam uktaṃ bhavati || 8.275–76 ||

	**eṣa daṇḍavidhiḥ prokto vākpāruṣyasya tattvataḥ |**

**	ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi daṇḍapāruṣyanirṇayam || 8.277 ||**

**	yena kenacid aṅgena hiṃsyāc chreyāṃsam antyajaḥ |**

**	chettavyaṃ tat tad evāsya tan manor anuśāsanam || 8.278 ||**

ayam uktasya viśeṣaprapañcasya sāmānyanirdeśaḥ | śreṣṭhaṃ dvijātim[ātram iti] nidarśanāc ca pūrvavarṇasya hiṃsāyām uttareṇāpy etad vijñeyam | na kevalaṃ śūdrasya pūrvāparādhe | asya sāmānyaślokasya catvāro vakṣyamāṇāḥ ślokāḥ prapañcāḥ || 8.277–78 ||

	**pāṇim udyamya daṇḍaṃ vā pāṇi cchedanam arhati |**

**	[pādena praharan kopāt pāda cchedanam arhati] || 8.279 ||**

**	sahā]sanam abhiprepsur utkṛṣṭasyāpakṛṣṭajaḥ |**

**	kaṭyāṃ kṛtaṅko nirvāsyaḥ sphicaṃ vāsyāvakartayet || 8.280 ||**

**	avaniṣṭhīvato darpād dvāv oṣṭhau chedayen nṛpaḥ |**

**	avamūtrayato [meḍhram avaśardhayato gudam || 8.281 ||**

**	keśeṣu gṛhato hastau] chedayed avicārayan |**

**	pādayor nāsikāyām ca grīvāyāṃ vṛṣaṇe tathā || 8.282 ||**

evaṃ ca sati na māraṇam eva hiṃsā, kiṃ tarhi anekopāyasādhyaṃ ca paraduḥkh[otpādanam, dvi]jātīnām evānyonyavyatikrame dhanadaṇḍa ucyate, pūrvadaṇḍasya vaikalpikaḥ, eteṣām apratyayāparādhāpekṣayā || 8.282 ||

	**tvagbhedakaḥ śataṃ daṇḍyo lohitasya ca darśakaḥ |**

**	māṃsabhedī tu ṣaṇniṣkān pravāsyas tv asthibhedakṛt || 8.283 ||**

yas tvaco vikāraṃ darśayaty alohitaṃ sa vijñeyas tvagbhedakaḥ | ṛjv anyat | asya tu viśeṣaḥ | manuṣyānāṃ paśūnāṃ ceti || 8.283 ||

	**vanaspatīnāṃ sarveṣām upabhogo yathā yathā |**

**	tathā tathā damaḥ kāryo hiṃsāyām iti dhāraṇā || 8.284 ||**

atra vanaspatiśabdena vṛkṣāṇām api grahaṇam | "anubandhaṃ parijñāya" ity anenaivāyaṃ ślokaḥ uktārtha iti kaścid āha | tad ayuktam | asmin hiṃsati daṇḍavidhyartho 'yaṃ śloka upapadyate || 8.284 ||

	**manuṣyāṇām paśūnāṃ ca duḥkhāya prakṛte sati |**

**	yathā yathā mahad duḥkhaṃ daṇḍaṃ kuryāt tathā tathā|| 8.285 ||**

evaṃ ca saty ayaṃ pūrvasya hiṃsādaṇdasya viśeṣārtho vijñeyaḥ | katham | "tvagbhedaka" iti hi yo daṇḍavidhir uktaḥ, tasyāparādhānurūpeṇonādhikatā prāṅvivākena kalpanīyety evamarthaḥ ślokaḥ || 8.285 ||

	**aṅgāvapīḍanāyāṃ ca prāṇaśoṇitayos tathā |**

**	samutthānavyayaṃ dāpyaḥ sarvadaṇḍam athāpi vā || 8.286 ||**

samutthānaṃ punaḥ pratyāpattiḥ tadgataṃ vyayaṃ tasmai rājñā dāpyo 'vapīḍayitā | atha tv asau na gṛhṇīyād avapīḍitaḥ samutthānavyayam avapīḍakāt, tato rājaivobhayataḥ piṇḍīkṛtya gṛhṇīyāt || 8.286 ||

	**dravyāṇi hiṃsyād yo yasya jñānato 'jñānato 'pi vā |**

**	sa tasyotpādayet tuṣṭiṃ rājñe dadyāc ca tatsamam || 8.287 ||**

jānann ajānan vā hiṃsayan vināśayan daṇḍyaḥ | na tv ajñānata iti pramoktavyaḥ | tuṣṭyutpattiś ca tatpratisaṃskāreṇa niranvayavināśe vā tathāvidhasyānyasya pratipādanena || 8.287 ||

	**carmacārmikabhāṇḍeṣu kāṣṭhaloṣṭamayeṣu ca |**

**	mūlyāt pañcaguṇo daṇḍaḥ puṣpamūlaphaleṣu ca || 8.288 ||**

eteṣāṃ vināśe pañcaguṇo daṇḍaḥ, na tu tatsamaḥ | evaṃ caibhyo 'nyatra pūrvaślokavidhis tatsamo vijñeyaḥ | tuṣṭyutpattiś ca vyavasthita eva || 8.288 ||

	**yānasya caiva yātuś ca yānasvāmina eva ca |**

**	daśātivartanāny āhuḥ (?) śeṣe daṇḍo vidhīyate || 8.289 ||**

vakṣyamāṇeṣu daśasu nimitteṣu dravyavināśe prāṇivadhe vā daṇḍo nāstīty etad ativartanaṃ daṇḍasya | apare tu tasya na daśatvam [vivakṣitam] āhuḥ || 8.289 ||

	**chinnanāsye bhagnayuge tiryak pratimukhāgate |**

**	akṣabhaṅge ca yānasya cakrabhaṅge tathaiva ca || 8.290 ||**

**	chedane caiva yantrāṇāṃ yoktraraśmyos tathaiva ca |**

**	ākrande cāpy apaihīti na daṇḍyān manur abravīt || 8.291 ||**

chinnanāsya balīvarde yugye bhagnayuge ca tasminn eva tiryagāgate pratimukhāgate ca yāne akṣabhaṅgacakrabhaṅgayoś ca | evaṃ yoktraraśmyoḥ, ākrande cāpy apaihīti, eṣu daśasu nimitteṣu na daṇḍaḥ kāryo rājñā yānasvāmiprabhṛtīnām | ebhyas tv anyatraiṣām aparādhahetur ucyate, manuṣyādihiṃsāyāṃ vakṣyamāṇadaṇḍārthaḥ || 8.290–91 ||

	**yatrāpavartate yugyaṃ vaiguṇyāt prājakasya tu |**

**	tatra svāmī bhaved daṇḍyo hiṃsāyāṃ dviśataṃ damam || 8.292 ||**

akuśale prājake svāmino 'parādhaḥ, tatprayuktatvāt prājakasya | dviśatagrahaṇaṃ cātra na vivakṣitam | yena daṇḍahetor aparādhasya prakaraṇam idam | manuṣyādihiṃsādaṇḍasya vakṣyamāṇasya taṃ hi prāṇaviśeṣāśrayaṃ tadhiṃsāyāṃ vakṣyati, "manuṣyamāraṇe kṣipraṃ coravat kilbiṣaṃ bhavet" iti | tathā cedaṃ kṣudrapaśvāśrayaṃ tatraiva prakaraṇe viśeṣadaṇḍaṃ vakṣyati "kṣudrakāṇāṃ paśūnāṃ tu hiṃsāyāṃ dviśato damaḥ" iti | yata evam avivakṣitvaitad uktaṃ dviśatagrahaṇam || 8.292 ||

	**prājakaś ced bhave āptaḥ prājako daṇḍam arhati |**

**	yugyasthāḥ prājake 'nāpte sarve daṇḍyāḥ śataṃ śatam || 8.293 ||**

kuśale prājake prā[jaka eva daṇḍyaḥ | yugyasthā]s tu yugyasvāmiprabhṛtir, yānāsvāmino 'pi santaḥ, akuśale sati pratyekaṃ śataṃ śataṃ daṇḍyā bhaveyuḥ | yena [prājako] 'nāptaḥ yugyasvāmināṃ deśāntarā[digamanāya pra]yuktaḥ, nānyathā | śataṃ daṇḍatvaṃ cāvivakṣitam iti kṛtavyākhyānam etat || 8.293 ||

	**sa cet tu pathi saṃruddhaḥ paśubhir vā rathena vā |**

**	pramā[payet prāṇabhṛtas tatra daṇḍo vicāritaḥ || 8.294 ||**

anā]ptād vājñānāt saṃrodhādidoṣāt paśubhir vā saṃmukhīnarathayuktaiḥ saṃroddhṛbhiḥ rathena vā jaghanopasarpiṇā saṃruddhayugyas saṃni[hi]taś cāmut[aś ca paripāt]ādibhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ tatra daṇḍanimitto 'prādho daṇḍa ity ucyate | guṇataḥ sa vicārito 'nantaram eva | yānasvāmyādīnāṃ "yatrāpavartate yugyam" ity evamādinā vākye[ṣv a]tra daṇḍo vicāritaḥ | vakṣyamāṇaślokeṣu yānasvāmyādīnām anantarokteśv aparādheṣu yugyāvartanādibhiḥ kāraṇair manuṣyādimāraṇe vakṣyamāṇo "manuṣyamāraṇe kṣipram" ity evamādiḥ | na tv aviśeṣeṇa manuṣyādiprāṇihiṃsāyā daṇḍaḥ | kiṃ tarhi vicāritaḥ nānāprakāra upadiṣṭaḥ manuṣyādihiṃsāviśeṣākhyaḥ | atha vā paśurathagrahaṇaṃ naiva svayānasaṃruddhviśeṣaṇaṃ yathā vyākhyātam asmābhiḥ, kiṃ tarhi paśubhir vā balīvardhākhyair ātmīyarathayuktaiḥ rathena vā ātmīyan kvacit saṅkule itaś cāmutaś ca mārgāt paripataṃs tatsaṅkaṭatvād yadi 'pramāpayet prāṇabhṛtaḥ tatra daṇḍo vicāritaḥ" ity etad uktārtham | idānīṃ pūrvāparādheṣu prājakādīnāṃ daṇḍavikalpa ucyate || 8.294 ||

	**manuṣyamāraṇe kṣipraṃ coravat kilbiṣaṃ bhavet |**

**	prāṇabhṛtsu mahatsv ardhaṃ gogajoṣṭrahayādiṣu || 8.295 ||**

saty apy aviśeṣābhidāne **coravat** kilbiṣe na vadhaḥ, kiṃ tarhi uttamasāhaso dhanadaṇḍaḥ | tathā ca **prāṇabhṛtsu mahatsu** prabhāvataḥ gavādiṣu parimāṇataś ca hastyādiṣv ardhadaṇḍam āha, coravatkilbiṣadaṇḍāt | sa cārdhadaṇḍo dhanadaṇḍa evottamasāhase yujyate pūrvābhihite, na vadhe | tathā ca kṣudrakāṇāṃ paśūnāṃ tu **hiṃsāyāṃ** tṛtīyasthāne **dviśato dama** ucyamāna uttaraśloke, prathame sthāne uttamasāhasa (?) dhanadaṇḍaṃ darśayaty atra | evaṃ ca sati **coravat kilbiṣa** uttamasāhasa eva dhanadaṇḍaḥ, na vadho yujyate | yadi caitad evaṃ bhavati tato "rājā stenena gantavyaḥ" ity atra rājābhigamane stenasyobhayaṃ yuktam idam "śāsanād vā vimokṣād vā" iti | sa ca mokṣo dhanadaṇḍenaiva yuktaḥ | tathā ca kṛtvottaro daṇḍavidhir arthavān bhavati | **ādi**grahaṇaṃ ca hayādiṣv ity etat mahiṣādiviṣayaṃ vijñeyam || 8.295 ||

	**kṣudrakāṇāṃ paśūdāṃ tu hiṃsāyāṃ dviśato damaḥ |**

**	pañcāśat tu bhaved daṇḍaḥ śubheṣu mṛgapakṣiṣu || 8.296 ||**

ajāvikasya pṛthaggrahaṇāt kṣudrapaśugrahaṇam atrānyārtham | evaṃ cātrālpaprayojanānāṃ gavādīnāṃ dṛṣṭāt kāraṇāt grahaṇam | vikalpārthaṃ vā syāt punar ajāvikādīnām uttaraśloke grahaṇam | **śubhāś** ca **mṛgapakṣiṇo** devatāyatanabhūṣaṇā rurumayūraprabhṛtayaḥ anyaparigrahā vā || 8.296 ||

	**gardabhājāvikānāṃ tu daṇḍaḥ syāt pañcamāṣikaḥ |**

**	māṣikaś tu bhaved daṇḍaḥ śvasūkaranipātane || 8.297 ||**

**māṣika**grahaṇena cātra dravyagrahaṇaṃ puruṣaśaktyaparādhānubandhasāmarthyād vijñeyam | viśeṣataḥ saparigrahaprāṇihiṃsāviṣayaś cāyaṃ daṇḍa ucyamāno yānopaghātād anyatrāpi kāryasāmānyād vijñāyate || 8.297 ||

	**bhāryā putraś ca dāsās ca śiṣyo bhrātā ca sodaraḥ |**

**	prāptāparādhās tāḍyāḥ syū rajjvā venudalena vā || 8.298 ||**

daṇḍapratiṣedhartho 'yam ārambhaḥ, tāḍanāsādananiyamārthaś ca || 8.298 ||

	**pṛṣṭhatas tu śarīrasya nottamāṅge kathaṃcana |**

ayaṃ tu tāḍyadeśaniyamārthaḥ ślokārdhaḥ |

	**ato 'nyathā tu praharan prāptaḥ syāc corakilbiṣam || 8.299 ||**

ity ayaṃ niyamasya vyatikrame tāḍayituṃ vijñeyaḥ | na cāvaśyatāḍanam eteṣām aparādhināṃ putrādīnām, niyamārthatvād upadeśasya | **prāptaḥ syāc corakilbiṣam** ity ayaṃ niyamavyatikrame nindārthavādo nivṛttyarthaḥ | evaṃ ca saty **ato 'nyathā** tāḍane niyamātikramamātram, na tu coravad daṇḍyaḥ | dhigdaṇḍavāgdaṇḍamātraṃ vā, tatra tatsāmānyāt || 8.299 ||

	**eṣo 'khilenābhihito daṇḍapāruṣyanirṇayaḥ |**

**	[stenasyātaḥ pravakṣyāmi vidhiṃ daṇḍavinirṇaye || 8.300 ||**

upasaṃhā]ropanyāsārthaḥ ślokaḥ | mā bhūc ca pūrvair aparādhasya tulyatvam ity ato gurutvād asya tannigrahādarārtham idam āha || 8.300 ||

	**paramaṃ yatnam ātiṣṭhet stenā[nāṃ nigrahe nṛpaḥ |**

**	stenānāṃ nigrahādasya ya]śo rāṣṭraṃ ca vardhate || 8.301 ||**

katham | jānapadānāṃ hi karmaṇāṃ vṛttyarthānām adṛṣṭaprayojanānāṃ ca sukṛtaparipanthinigrahaṇam | evaṃ ca sati, iti || 8.301 ||

	**abhayasya his yo [dātā sa pūjyaḥ satataṃ nṛpaḥ |**

**	sattraṃ hi vardhate tasya sadaivābhayadakṣiṇam || 8.302 ||**

yena sattraṃ hi vardhate tasya tasya na nigraharūpaṃ sadaiva yāvajjīvam ity arthaḥ | na tu yathā vaitāne niyatakālam | tac āsya bhavati abhayadakṣiṇam: sattre dakṣiṇā[bhāvāt tadvailakṣyaṇyam asya sattrasya || 8.302 ||

	**sarvato] dharmaṣaḍbhāgo rājño bhavati rakṣataḥ |**

**sarvata** ity ādeya vṛttibhyo 'pi saparigrahebhyaḥ, kiṃ punar itarebhyaḥ, yato vṛttigandho 'pi nāsti | atha vā smārtatvād asyopadeśasya smṛtikarma[viṣaye] ṣaḍbhāge prāptam idaṃ **sarva**grahaṇaṃ karoti śrutikarmebhyaḥ — tathā cānantaraśloke vakṣyati, "yad adhīte yad yajate" ity evamādi | **rakṣataś** ced **rājño** dharmaṣaḍbhāgagrahaṇam | tena hetuviparyaya iti kṛtvedam ucyate:

	**adharmād api ṣaḍbhāgo bhavaty asya hy arakṣataḥ || 8.303 ||**

atha vā rakṣāyām adhikṛtasy svayaṃbhuvā, yogyatāśāstreṇa vā tasyānanuṣṭhānād yuktam adharmaṣaḍbhāgavacanam idaṃ śiṣṭasyākriyāyāḥ, abhiṣekakāle vā prajāsaṃrakṣaṇamatākriyāyāḥ, anyārthapratijñāhānivat || 8.304 ||

_adhunā **sarvato dharmaṣaḍbhāga** ity etat sūtrasthānaṃ vivṛnoti |_

	**yad adhīte yad yajate yad dadāti yad arcati |**

**	tasya ṣaḍbhāgabhāg rājā samyag bhavati rakṣaṇāt || 8.304 ||**

sarvakriyānidarśanārthatvāc cāsāṃ nirdiṣṭābhyo netarāḥ parisaṃkhyāyeran | vedasmṛtiśāstranyāyavirodhāś ca mā bhūvann iti | ata etaṃ yathāśrutaparikalpanāṃ parityajya, **dharmaṣaḍbhāga**grahaṇaṃ pranāḍikayārthavādo niyamadharmāpekṣaḥ bhavati, guṇavatpuruṣasaṃrakṣaṇāpekṣo vā, tad apekṣam etad dharmaṣaḍbhāgagrahaṇaṃ pranāḍikayārthavādārtham | na tu vṛttiparikrītatvād rājño nirbījam idaṃ prarocanārthamātrārthaṃ bhavitum arhati, asati dharmasaṃbhandha iti | itaś ca dharmaṣaḍbhāgagrahaṇaṃ rājñaḥ prajāsaṃrakṣaṇāpekṣam || 8.304 ||

_yad āha |_

	**rakṣan dharmeṇa bhūtāni rājā vadhyāṃś ca ghātayan |**

**	yajate 'harahar yajñaiḥ sahasraśatadakṣiṇaiḥ || 8.305 ||**

na hy akasmāt stutiḥ pravartate, yenātaḥ prajāsaṃrakṣaṇād yathoktena śāstranyāyena rājño dharmeṇa bhavitavyam | **vadhya**nigrahaś ca praṇāḍikayā saṃrakṣaṇārthaḥ | tathā ca tasmāt saṃrakṣaṇaṃ pṛthag eva darśayati "rakṣan dharmeṇa" | varṇāśramiṇo yathāśāstraṃ svakarmaṇy avasthāpayati, śāstrārthapradarśanena | katham | "yūyam evaṃ bhavata, śāstraśiṣṭaṃ kuruta" ity arthaḥ; "yūyaṃ punar maivaṃ bhūta, pratiṣiddhaṃ varjayata" ity arthaḥ | etadanuśāsanātikramād yathāśāstradaṇḍena vā tān rakṣati | tathā ca saty anyad rakṣaṇaṃ **vadhya**vadhakriyato vijñāyate | etadanuśāsanātikramād yathāśāstradaṇḍena vā tān rakṣati | tathā ca saty anyad rakṣaṇaṃ **vadhya**vadhakriyato vijñāyate | evaṃ ca sati vakṣyati "rakṣaṇād āryavṛttānāṃ kaṇṭakānāṃ ca śodhanāt", tathā "nigraheṇa ca pāpānāṃ sādhūnāṃ saṃgraheṇa ca" ity evamādi || 8.305 ||

_yataś caitad evam, ataḥ |_

	**yo'rakṣan balim ādatte karaṃ śulkaṃ ca pārthivaḥ |**

**	prītibhogaṃ ca daṇḍaṃ ca sa sadyo narakaṃ vrajet || 8.306 ||**

tathā śiṣṭasmaraṇapravādaḥ || 8.306 ||

	**arakṣitāraṃ rājānaṃ baliṣaḍbhāgahāriṇam |**

**	tam āhuḥ sarvalokasya samagramalahārakam || 8.307 ||**

**	anapekṣitamaryādaṃ nāstikaṃ vipralopakam |**

**	arakṣitāram attāraṃ nṛpaṃ vidyād adhogatim || 8.308 ||**

stenaprakaraṇe ca rakṣārthaṃ stenanigrahānuṣṭhānaṃ saṃstutya, tannigrahasvarūpam adhunedam āha || 8.308 ||

	**adhārmikaṃ tribhir nyāyair nigṛhṇīyāt prayatnataḥ |**

**	nirodhanena bandhena vividhena vadhena ca || 8.309 ||**

tāḍanādinā yathāparādham | yo yathāparādhyati, taṃ tathāparādhānurūpeṇa daṇḍena yojayed arāgadveṣo dharmatulām āśritya | kasya punar hetoḥ | yena — || 8.309 ||

	**nigraheṇa ca pāpānāṃ sādhūnāṃ saṃgraheṇa ca |**

**	dvijataya ivejyābhiḥ pūjante satataṃ nṛpāḥ || 8.310 ||**

nirbījastutyarthāsaṃbhavena ca yathāśruta upakāro rājño dharmalakṣaṇas tannigrahāt pratīyate, nigrāhyasya ca stenasya | tathā ca "rājabhir dhṛtadaṇḍā" iti vakṣyati | jānapadasaṃrakṣaṇāc ca dharmasaṃbandhaḥ siddhaḥ | yataḥ evam ātmāparānugrahabhūyastvā[t rakṣā] yā na pramādyaḥ pāpa[nigrahasādhu]saṃrakṣaṇārtho rājeti | atha tv evāsāmyena prajāsu vartamānaṃ mohāt kaścit kṣipet | tatas tena || 8.310 ||

	**kṣantavyaṃ prabhunā nityaṃ kṣipatāṃ kāryiṇāṃ nṛṇām |**

**	bālavṛddhā[turāṇāṃ ca kurvatā hitam ātmanaḥ || 8.311 ||**

arthavāda]m āha, upadiṣṭārthānuṣṭhānaprarocanārtham || 8.311 ||

	**yaḥ kṣipto marṣayaty ārtais tena svarge mahīyate |**

**	yas tv aiśvaryān na kṣamate narakaṃ tena gacchati || 8.312||**

evam iyaṃ kṣ[amānuṣṭhānastutiḥ | ci]ttasaṃkṣobhaheūpanipāte 'pi rājñā kṣamobhayalokopārjanasādhanaṃ prayatnato bhāvanīyā | vākyasvābhāvyāc ceyam ubhayathātra śloke kṣamānuṣṭhānastuti[ḥ] | rājasaṃbandhāc ca stenaprāyaścittasyedam etatprakaraṇa evocyate || 8.312 ||

	**rājā stenena gantavyo muktakeśena dhīmatā |**

**	ācakṣāṇena tat steyam evaṃkarmāsmi śādhi mām || 8.313 ||**

pātakaṃ yasya suvarṇāder abhisaṃbandhenāyaṃ stena ucyate, na dravyamātrasya, prāyaścittamahattvopadeśāt | tathā ca prāyaścittaprakaraṇe viśeṣayiṣyati "suvarṇasteyakṛt" ity evamādi | anye tu dravyamātrāpahārakaṃ stenaṃ manyante | atra tatpratyavamarśātmakasya śraddadhānatayā rājābhigamanaṃ svayaṃ **dhīmatā** "vividhena vadhena ca" śuddhihetur idaṃ prāyaścittaśāstrasāmarthyād ity evaṃ jānatānena | anye tu "dhāvatā" iti paṭhanty ādarārtham | na ceyān eva stenasya rājopagamanaṃ dharmaḥ, kiṃ tarhi, ayaṃ cānyaH || 8.313 ||

	**skandhenādāya musalaṃ lakuṭaṃ vāpi khādiram |**

**	śaktiṃ vobhayatas tīkṣṇām āyasaṃ daṇḍam eva vā || 8.314 ||**

ekārthaviṣayo vikalpo musalādīnāṃ brāhmaṇavarjam | anye tu varṇakrameṇaiṣāṃ musalādīnām upadeśaṃ manyante | evaṃ ca sa svayam upagataḥ śraddadhānatayā kṣatriyādir yathāśāstram || 8.314 ||

	**śāsanād [vā vimokṣād vā stenaḥ steyād vimucyate |**

**śāsanād** vā] vadhalakṣaṇād aparādhamahattvāpekṣayā nirdhanatayā **vimokṣād** vā dhanadaṇḍitaḥ san | aparādhamahattve 'pi brāhmaṇaḥ stenaḥ steyād vimucyate | etasmād eva kāraṇād ayaṃ daṇḍavikalpaḥ | tathā ca gautamaḥ asminn eva prakaraṇe "na śārīro brāhmaṇadaṇḍaḥ" ity āha | yas tu svayam anupagato brāhmaṇasteno rājapuruṣair ānīyate viditāparādhair balāt tasyāpi ca na vadhaḥ | kiṃ tarhi "karmaviyogavikhyāpanavivāsanāṅkakaraṇāni" | tathāpi ca sarvasya hiraṇyādistenasya daṇḍavidhir ayam upadiṣṭaḥ; yataḥ svayam upagatayor brāhmaṇābrāhmaṇayor evaṃ daṇḍyataiva syāt | tathā ca sati |

	**aśāsitvā tu taṃ rājā stenasyāpnoti kilbiṣam || 8.315 ||**

evaṃ ca saty etad anayoḥ prāyaścittaṃ śuddhihetutvād vijñeyam | tathā ca rājābhigamanaṃ svayam anayor arthavad bhavatīti | vakṣyati hi 'rājabhiḥ kṛtadaṇḍās tu" iti | yas tu rājñā balād daṇḍyate vadhyate vā na tasya tena daṇḍena niṣkṛtir asti | yataḥ tena daṇḍena daṇḍitenāpi satā prāyaścittaṃ kartavyam eva | yaś ca svayam eva prāyaścittam ārabhate na tatra rājño hastaprakṣepo 'sti | tathā ca vakṣyati "prāyaścittaṃ tu kurvānāḥ" iti | tuṣṭyutpattiś ca dhanasvāmino 'nena daṇḍitenāpi kāryaiva | akurvaṃś caiva rājā stenanigraham ātmāpaghātaṃ kuryāt || 8.315 ||

_yasmād āha |_

	**annāde bhrūṇahā mārṣṭi patyau bhāryāpacāriṇī |**

**	gurau śiṣyaś ca yājyaś ca steno rājani kilbiṣam || 8.316 ||**

annam attīty **annādaḥ** | tasmin **annāde bhrūṇahā kilbiṣaṃ mārṣṭi** | evam itare 'pi yojyāḥ | ataḥ sthitaprajñena rājñā niśśaṅkena tadanigrahadoṣam ātmanaḥ pariharatā stenanigrahe yathāśāstraṃ vartitavyam ātmaparānugrahārtham iti | yataḥ svayam upagatatvāc ca kadācid ayaṃ bhinnadṛṣṭir upahatapratijñānas tannigrahe na pravarteta || 8.316 ||

_yatra ayaṃ yatna āsthīyate tad upakārasaṃbandhāpekṣayaivam |_

	**rājabhir dhṛtadaṇḍās tu kṛtvā pāpāni mānavāḥ|**

**	nirmalāḥ svargam āyānti santaḥ sukṛtino yathā || 8.317 ||**

prakaraṇāt steyapāpanirharaṇaviṣayam eva nirmalavacanaṃ, yena steyanimittam evedaṃ asya prāyaścittam | ato yuktam idam | yat te **nirmalāḥ svargam** āgaccheyuḥ, pūrvopāttena svargārohaṇikena kuśalakarmaṇā | evaṃ ca saty ubhayor apy anayā śiṣṭakriyayā tatkālopakārasaṃbandhāpekṣāyām idaṃ rājābhigamanapakṣe praśaṃsāvacanaṃ, na nirbījam iti || 8.317 ||

_idānīm anyat steyasaṃbandhenedam āha |_

	**yas tu rajjuṃ ghaṭaṃ kūpād dhared bhidyāc ca yaḥ prapām |**

**	sa daṇḍaṃ prāpnuyān māṣaṃ tac ca tasmin samāharet || 8.318 ||**

māṣo mukhyatvād aviśeṣābhidhāne sati hiraṇyasya syāt || 8.318 ||

	**dhānyaṃ daśabhyaḥ kumbhebhyo harato 'bhyadhikaṃ vadhaḥ |**

**	śeṣe 'py ekādaśaguṇaṃ dāpyas tasya ca taddhanam || 8.319 ||**

tāḍane 'pi vadhaḥ prayujyate | iha tu yadi brāhmaṇādiṣu praspare ca dhānyāpaharaṇe idam; hīnavarṇaś ca syād ayam apahartā, tato [doṣa]mahattvāt tasya na nairguṇyād vidhir māraṇe draṣṭavyaḥ | anyatra tu kalpanā svayam evohyā | daśānāṃ cārvāg **ekādaśaguṇo** daṇḍo, na **vadhaḥ** || 8.319 ||

	**tathā dharimameyānāṃ śatād abhyadhike vadhaḥ |**

**	[suvarṇarajatādīnām uttamānāṃ ca vāsaām || 8.320 ||**

dharimṇā] tulayā yāni mīyante tāni **dharmameyāni** suvarṇādīni | suvarṇādigrahaṇaṃ ca ghṛtādinvṛttyartham | tathā cānantaram eva ghṛtādīnāṃ tanmūlyād (?) dviguṇaṃ damaṃ vakṣyati | [evaṃ ca] "suvarṇarajatādīnām" ity evamādi grahaṇaṃ sarvalohopasaṃgrahārtham | ye punaḥ dharmebhyaḥ pṛthaṅmeyāny ācakṣate dhānyādīni teṣāṃ "dhānyaṃ daśabhyaḥ kumbhebhyaḥ" ity anenedaṃ punaruktam āpadyate | ghṛtādīnāṃ ca meyatve kalpyamāne vakṣyamāṇair ghṛtādibhiḥ paunaruktyam | yatas tathā **dharimameyānām** ity asya yathokta eva vigrahaḥ | **uttamānāṃ ca vāsasāṃ** navādīnām || 8.320 ||

	**pañcāśatas tv abhyadhike hastacchedanam iṣyate |**

**	śeṣe 'py ekādaśaguṇaṃ mūlyād daṇḍaṃ prakalpayet || 8.321 ||**

adhike pañcāśato hastacchedaḥ | ūne 'py ekādaśaguṇo daṇḍaḥ || 8.321 ||

	**puruṣāṇāṃ (?) kulīnānāṃ nārīṇāṃca viśeṣataḥ |**

**	mukhyānāṃ caiva ratnānāṃ haraṇe vadham arhati || 8.322 ||**

atra hriyamāṇahartṛjātiguṇāpekṣayā vidhiprapañcaḥ kalpanīyaḥ|| 8.322 ||

	**mahāpśūnāṃ haraṇe śastrāṇām auṣadhasya ca |**

**	kālam āsādya kāryaṃ ca daṇḍaṃ rājā prakalpayet || 8.323 ||**

**mahāpaśavo** hastyaśvoṣṭrādayaḥ, dṛṣṭopakāramahattvāt | parimāṇataś ca mahāpaśavo rājñas tatprakṛtīnāṃ caite sāmarthād viśeṣato vijñeyāḥ śastragrahaṇasāhacaryāc ca | tāni rājahitagocana eva mahānti guṇataḥ śastrāṇi prāyeṇa bhavanti | tathā mahac chabdo 'trādhikārārtha vijñeyaḥ | evam **auṣadham** api vyākhyeyam | eteṣāṃ haraṇe **kālam āsādya** rājā vigrahetaralakṣaṇaṃ deśaviplavarūpaṃ vā durbhikṣasubhikṣākhyaṃ vā, **kāryaṃ mahāpaśūnām** apaharaṇaprayujanaṃ vijñāya, kiṃ dyūtādiprayojana eṣām apahāraḥ, atha vairānubandhena, uta kṣudavasannātmakuṭumbasvatantrasya tatsthityarthaṃ dharmāyaiva nāsadupayogāya | **daṇḍaṃ rājā prakalpayed** iti prakṛtam anantaram eva dhānyaśloke vadham avadham ekādaśaguṇamūlyaṃ vā daṇḍaṃ deśakālakāryāvasthāṃ vijñāya jātiguṇaṃ vāpahartuḥ | uktaṃ caitad daṇḍavidhiśloke "anubandhaṃ parijñāya" ity evam ādiḥ || 8.323 ||

	**goṣu brāhmaṇasaṃsthāsu sthūrikāyāś ca bhedane |**

**	paśūnāṃ haraṇe caiva sadyaḥ kāryo 'rdhapādikaḥ || 8.324 ||**

pūrvaśloke tu mahāpaśugrahaṇena yad gor agrahaṇaṃ tato 'sya viśeṣārtha ārambhaḥ | atha punar anugṛhīte 'to 'pūrvārthaḥ | gāvaś ca brāhmaṇe saṃsthā yajñakarmaśeṣā ārambhasāmarthyād asya vijñāyante | evaṃ ca sati yāgaśīlād brāhmaṇād gām apaharataḥ tadapahartur ardhapādanaṃ **sadya** 'navekṣya kālakāryādīn daṇḍavikalpahetūn pūrvaślokotān asya syād iti | anyathā "mahāpaśūnāṃ haraṇe" ity anenaiva siddhatvād "goṣu brāhmaṇasaṃsthāsu" ity etad anārambhasamaṃ prasajyeta | kālādyanapakṣāyāṃ satyām ārabdhavyam idam | ato viśeṣārtha evam asyārambho, na punaruktatvādiyukta iti | atha tu yathā vyākhyātaḥ pūrvaślokopekṣya rājatantraviṣaya eva | ato 'syāpūrvakalpanāyām ayam adoṣa eva | **sthūrikāyāś ca bhedana** eṣa eva daṇḍaḥ syād ātmīyāyā api kṛt etat ārambhasāmarthāt | sthūrikā vandhyā gaur deśāntare 'bhidhīyate | tāṃ ca lāṅgalādiṣu vāhayanto 'vaśyaṃ pratodena bhinanti | evaṃ ca sati tadbhedanaṃ vāhopalakṣaṇaṃ tasyā vijñeyam | yaḥ punar etad anyathā paṭhati **sthūrikāyāś ca vāhana** iti, tasya sākṣād abhidhānāt anumānagatir nāsti | anyas tv āha, pārṣṇyāś caturaṅgulād ūrdhvaḥ pradeśaḥ **sthūrikā**, tadbhedane chedane vā nidarśanārthatvād bhedanagrahaṇasyaiṣa eva daṇḍaḥ syāt | **paśūnāṃ haraṇe** caiva yathokto daṇḍaḥ | ayaṃ c(h?)āgopaśvartha ārambhaḥ | brāhmaṇapaśūnām eva yajñīyānāṃ chāgaprabhṛtīnām apaharaṇe bahūnāṃ ca | anyas tv āha: akarmiṇo brāhmaṇasya gavām eva bahvīnām, arthāc ca kṣatriyavaiśyayoḥ karmaśīlayoḥ | karmaśeṣagavām upasaṃgrahaṇārtham idaṃ punaḥ paśugrahaṇam | ye punar vyākhyāyanti "goṣu brāhmaṇasaṃsthāsu" yad dadhi kṣīraṃ vā tadapaharaṇadaṇḍaḥ, tat prakaraṇābhāvād [asaṃgatam || 8.324 ||

	**sūtrakārpāsakiṣvānāṃ] gomayasya guḍasya ca |**

**	dadhnaḥ kṣīrasya takrasya pānīyasya tṛṇasya ca || 8.325 ||**

**	veṇuvaidalabhāṇḍānāṃ lavaṇānāṃ tathaiva ca |**

**	mṛnmayānāṃ ca haraṇe (?) mṛdo bhasmana eva ca || 8.326 ||**

**	matsyānāṃ pakṣiṇāṃ caiva tailasya ca ghṛtasya ca |**

**	māṃsasya madhunaś caiva yac cānyat paśusaṃbhavam || 8.327 ||**

**	anyeṣāṃ caivamādīnām adyānāmodanasya ca |**

**	pakvānnānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ tanmūlyād dviguṇo damaḥ || 8.328 ||**

athoktānāṃ dravyāṇāṃ mūlyād dviguṇo damaś caturbhiḥ ślokair ucyate | sūtrādiślokagaṇe cātra yad bhasmano mṛdaś ca grahaṇaṃ tatsarvapradarśanārthaṃ vijñayate | tathā ca nigamayati "anyeṣāṃ caivamādīnām" iti || 8.325–28 ||

	**puṣpeṣu harite dhānye gulmavallīnageṣu ca |**

**	alpeṣv aparipūteṣu daṇḍaḥ syāt pañcakṛṣṇalaḥ || 8.329 ||**

[harita ity] apakvaṃ ca dhānyānāṃ rāśyapekṣam || 8.329 ||

	**paripūteṣu dhānyeṣu śākamūlaphaleṣu ca |**

**	niranvaye śataṃ daṇḍaḥ sānvaye 'rdhaśataṃ damaḥ || 8.330 ||**

**niranvaye** ārakṣānadhiṣṭhite grahaṇam ayuktataram iti śataṃ daṇḍa ucyate, **sānvaye** tūbhayatra doṣāt sāhasatvād vārdham ucyate | anyas tv āha: **niranvaye** niranugame yadi nānunayati tato haraṇaṃ śatadaṇḍyo bhavati | athānugamayati tataḥ pañcāśat || 8.330 ||

_anye tv āhuḥ |_

	**syāt sāhasaṃ tv anvayavat prasabhaṃ karma yat kṛtam |**

**	niranvayaṃ bhavet steyaṃ kṛtvāpavyayate ca yat || 8.331 ||**

yat sārakṣaṃ **prasabham** avisaṅkitena kriyate tat sāhasam | **niranvayaṃ** tu yad anadhiṣṭhitam ārakṣe tan na steyam | yac ca **sānvayam** api kṛtvāpavyayate tad api steyam eva || 8.331 ||

	**yas tv etāny upakḷptāni dravyāṇi stenayen naraḥ |**

**	taṃ śataṃ daṇḍayed rājā yaś cāgniṃ corayed gṛhāt || 8.332 ||**

ya etāni sūtrādīni yathoktāny upakḷptāni yathākathaṃcid avaguptāny api prasabhaṃ stenayet taṃ rājā prasaṅganivṛttyartham alpe mahati vā śatam aviśeṣeṇa daṇḍayet | agneś cādarārthaṃ pṛthaggrahaṇam | api ca sūtrādau gaṇe mūlyād dviguṇo dama ucyate | na cāgneḥ krayavikray[au, athaḥ taṃ śataṃ daṇḍ]ayed rājā yaś cāgniṃ corayed gṛhāt | bhogāyopakḷptāni: etāni yathāsaṃbhavaṃ bhogābhimukheṣu yo 'paharet tasyādyo daṇḍaḥ, yaś ca parigṛhīto 'gniḥ tam eva vā dauḥśīlyād upaharet | sādhanaṃ vā sruksruvolūkhalamusalādy agnyarthatvād agniśabdenocyate guṇataḥ || 8.332 ||

	**yena yena yathāṅgena steno nṛṣu viceṣṭate |**

**	tat tad eva hared asya pratyādeśāya pārthivaḥ || 8.333 ||**

yasyāṅgasya hastasya vā pādasya vā balam āśritya stenaḥ steye pravartate tat tad evāsya chettavyam | tad yathā | granthicchedako hastabalaṃ hastācchedakaḥ pādabalam | yaś ca daṇḍito 'pi paunah punyena vartate aparigaṇayya pūrvadaṇḍaṃ tasyāyam aṅgacched ucyate | tad uktam "vadhadaṇḍam ataḥ param" iti | evaṃ ca kvacic chedanavidhānam arthavad bhavati | yathā sati chedane hastacchedanam asya || 8.333 ||

	**pitācāryaḥ suhṛn mātā bhāryā putraḥ purohitaḥ |**

**	nādaṇḍyo nāma rājño 'sti yaḥ svadharme na tiṣṭhati || 8.334 ||**

prakaraṇāt suvarṇasteyadaṇḍo 'yam | yadi tv anyatrāpi kāryasāmānyāt kupyate tato 'yaṃ sarvavyatikrameṣu prakaraṇānukrameṇa daṇḍaḥ pitrādīnāṃ vijñeyaḥ | gurutvāt paripālanīyatvaṃ yenaiṣām atyantam | ato 'daṇḍyāśaṅkānivṛttyartham eṣām idaṃ daṇḍavacanam | anye tv arthavādam imaṃ steyadaṇḍasyānyapuruṣaviṣayasya kalpayanti | tad ayuktam, uttaraśloke rājadaṇḍavirodhāt || 8.334 ||

_tathā ca darśayati |_

	**kārṣāpaṇaṃ bhaved daṇḍo yatrānyaḥ prākṛto janaḥ |**

**	tatra rājā bhaved daṇḍyaḥ sahasram iti dhāraṇā || 8.335 ||**
