rājño 'pi dharmavyatikramam āsevya yathoktāt sahasraguṇo daṇḍaḥ varuṇāyāpsu praveśyo 'yaṃ brāhmaṇebhyo vā vidvadbhyaḥ upapādyaḥ | anyasyāpi ca daṇḍahiraṇyasyāitām eva taddvayīṃ pratipattiṃ vakṣyati | yktaṃ ca yan mahādaṇḍo rājñaḥ syād alpe 'py aparādhe yenāsau dharmajñas tadvyavasthāhetuś ca san dharmavyatikrame vartate | tathā [sati 'vi]duṣo 'tikrame daṇḍabhūyastam" jyāyaso 'py āhuḥ || 8.335 ||

	**aṣṭāpādyaṃ tu śūdrasya steye bhavati kilbiṣam |**

**	ṣoṣaśaiva tu vaiśyasya dvātriṃśat kṣatriyasya tu || 8.336 ||**

**	brāhmaṇasya catuḥ ṣaṣṭis taddoṣaguṇavid dhi saḥ |**

**	dviguṇā vā catuḥ ṣaṣṭis taddoṣaguṇavid dhi saḥ || 8.337 ||**

uktaśeṣāṇāṃ ca dravyāṇām apaharaṇe eṣa daṇḍaḥ syāt | eteṣām eva vā steyābhyāse suvarṇa[steye vā | viduṣo 'tira]me daṇḍabhūyastvam | evaṃ rājño 'pi syāt | tathāyaṃ pūrvaśeṣatvād arthavāda eṣa, na daṇḍavidhiḥ | yadi cāsyārthavādatvaṃ bhavati tato vāgdaṇḍapāruṣyādiṣu [yat yat] daṇḍālapatvam uktaṃ tat samañjasaṃ bhavati | atha śrutisāmarthyād yathopadeśam ayaṃ daṇḍavikalpa iṣyate, yathā prakāśarahasyaprāyaścitteṣu tato 'sya vidhitvam | evaṃ ca sati brāhmaṇadaṇḍavikalpaś ca vṛddhasvādhyāyyapakṣayā (?) veditavyaḥ, yathānyatra | steyāpavādārthaṃ tv idam adhunocyate || 8.337 ||

	**vānaspatyaṃ mūlaphalaṃ dārv agnyarthaṃ tathaiva ca |**

**	tṛṇaṃ ca gobhyo grāsārtham asteyaṃ manur abravīt || 8.338 ||**

agnigrahaṇāc ca liṅgāt sarvam etad yajñārtham apratyavāyakaram | tathā ca vakṣyati: "āharet trīṇi vā dve vā" iti | taskarapratigrahādikartur brāhmaṇasya vijānataś corasamatvapradarśanārtham idam āha daṇḍārtham || 8.338 ||

	**yo 'dattādāyino hastāl lipseta brāhmaṇo dhanam |**

**	yājanādhyāpanenāpi yathā stenas tathaiva saḥ || 8.339 ||**

evaṃ ca corasamatvāc coravad daṇḍyo 'sau | adhunā nimitte svalpam anujānāti parādānam || 8.339 ||

	**dvijo 'dhvagaḥ kṣīnavṛttir dvāvikṣū dve ca mūlake |**

**	ādadānaḥ parakṣetrān na daṇḍaṃ dātum arhati || 8.340 ||**

evaṃ ca rājadaṇḍapratiṣedārtho 'yam ārambho 'rthalakṣaṇe sati steye, na tu cauryābhyanujñā | etenādoṣaḥ | śākamatsyādigrahaṇaṃ vyākhyātam || 8.340 ||

	**asanditānāṃ sandātā sanditānāṃ ca mokṣakaḥ |**

**	dāsāśvarathahartā ca prāptaḥ syāc corakilbiṣam || 8.341 ||**

aśvarathagrahaṇaṃ ca vāhanasāmānyād uṣṭrādipradarśanārtham idaṃ draṣṭavyam || 8.341 ||

	**anena vidhinā rājā kurvāṇaḥ stenanigraham |**

**	yaśo 'smin prāpnyuyāḷ loke pretya cānuttamaṃ sukham || 8.342 ||**

upasaṃhārārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 8.342 ||

_sāhasam adhunocyate |_

	**aindraṃ sthānam adhiprepsu yaśaś cākṣayam avyayam |**

**	nopekṣeta kṣaṇam api rājā sāhasikaṃ naram || 8.343 ||**

sāhasopanyāsārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 8.343 ||

	**vāgduṣṭas taskaraś caiva daṇḍenaiva ca hiṃsakaḥ |**

**	sāhasasya naraḥ kartā vijñeyaḥ pāpakṛttamaḥ || 8.344 ||**

_yataś caitad evam ataḥ |_

	**sāhase vartamānaṃ tu yo marṣayati pārthivaḥ |**

**	sa vināśaṃ vrajaty āśu vidveṣaṃ vādhigacchati || 8.345 ||**

_evaṃ ca sati |_

	**na mitrakāraṇād rājā vipulād vā dhanāgamāt |**

**	samutsṛjet sāhasikān sarvabhūtabhayāvahān || 8.346 ||**

sāhasikanindaiṣā tannigrahādarārthā vijñeyā | anyāyyaśastragrahaṇasya varṇasya śastragrahaṇaṃ sāhasam | tena yo vartate sa sāhasikaḥ | evaṃ ca sati taddoṣapratiṣedhārthaṃ nimittataḥ śastragrahaṇaṃ dvijāter idaṃ tadapavādabhūtam ārabhyate || 8.346 ||

	**śastraṃ dvijātibhir grāhyaṃ dharmo yatroparudhyate |**

**	dvijātīnāṃ ca varṇānāṃ viplave kālakārite || 8.347 ||**

**	ātmanaś ca paritrāṇe dakṣiṇānāṃ ca saṅgare |**

**	strīviprābhyavapattau ca ghnan dharmeṇa na duṣyati || 8.348 ||**

arthakāritatvāc chastragrahaṇasya nāyaṃ vidhiḥ | kiṃ tarhy arthaprāptānuvādo 'yaṃ daṇḍapratiṣedhārthaḥ | kṣatriyasya prajāsaṃrakṣaṇopadeśasāmarthyāt prāptaṃ śastragrahaṇam | taditaradvijātiviṣayo 'yam upadeṣaḥ pratīyate | śastraṃ dvijātibhir grāhyam iti tadgrahasyādhunā nimittaṃ darśayati | dharmo yatra deśe kāle voparudhyate varṇāśramiṇām | idaṃ ca sūtrasthānam | anyad asya bhāṣyaṃ bhavati | dvijātīnāṃ ca varṇānāṃ viplave varṇasaṅkarādau vyavasthābhaṅge, kālakārite rājavyasanena kenacit kadācic ca dharmoparodhād atra śastragrahaṇam adoṣam | yatop 'sya na tatra sāhasikadaṇḍo yujyate | kiṃ cātmanaś ca paritrāṇe paritaḥ sarvatas trāṇe sakuṭumbadraviṇasyātmanaḥ dakṣiṇānāṃ cāpahāraparitrāṇa iti vartate | dakṣīṇāgrahaṇaṃ sarvayājñīyadravyopalakṣaṇārtham | saṅgare yuddhe na tu chale | strīviprābhyavapattau ca gṛhītaśastraḥ dharmoparodhahetum upāttaśastraḥ ghnan dharmeṇa na kūṭayuddhena na duṣyati paratreha ca śāstropadeśasāmarthyāt | tallakṣaṇatvāc ca dharmādharmayor anatiśaṅkyam etat | strīgrahaṇaṃ ca sarvānugrahyāṇāṃ bālavṛddhāturāṇāṃ pradarśanārthaṃ kāryasāmānyād vi[dheḥ], vipragrahaṇaṃ ca sarvaśreyasām ācāryādīnām iti || 8.8.347–48 ||

_dharmoparodhe gṛhītaśastra ātatāyinaṃ ghnan dharmāṇa na duṣyatīti yad uktam asyārthavādaḥ |_

	**guruṃ vā bālavṛddhau vā brāhmaṇaṃ vā bahu[śrutam |**

**	ātatāyinam āyāntaṃ hanyā]d evācivārayan || 8.349 ||**

"ācāryaṃ ca pravaktāraṃ pitaraṃ mātaraṃ gurum" ity evamādibhiḥ śāstrair atyantāpakāriṇo 'py ete gurvādayo na vadhyāḥ ity uktaṃ yataḥ idaṃ pūrvavidhyarthav[ādārtham | gu]rvādayo 'py ātatāyino 'nena nimittena vadhyāḥ syur atyantāvadhyāḥ santaḥ, kiṃ punas tebhyo 'nya ity atiśayārthavādo yathā loke || 8.349 ||

_tathā cedam āha |_

	**nātatāyivadhe doṣo [hantur bhavati] kaścana |**

**	prakāśaṃ vāprakāśaṃ vā manyus taṃ manyam ṛcchati || 8.350 ||**

manyuḥ krodho vadhyasya, taṃ ghātakamanyuḥ krodha ṛcchati nivartayati | sāhasapraśaṃsārthaṃ cedaṃ ślokadvayam | tatpraśaṃsā ca rājadaṇḍanivṛttyarthā | evaṃ cāsyānenātatāyivadhe rājadaṇḍābhāvavat pratyavāyābhāvo 'pi gamyate | tathā ca vyāso bhīṣmajāmadagnyarāmasaṃvāde:

	yo hanyāt samare kruddho yuddhyantam apalāyinam | 

	brahmahatyā na tasyāsti iti darmeṣu niścayaḥ || iti | 

īṣatpratyavāyāyānye 'trātatyino gurvādayo 'pi vadhyā bhavantīti śiṣṭānām apy ātatāyināṃ vadham icchanti | apare hīnātatāyivadhaṃ nirvikalpaṃ manyante, same tu vikalpa ātmanaḥ parasya vā viśiṣṭe ātmatyāgada evākuśalārambhasāmarthād iti | tad etad yathāsaṃbhavam uktaparihāraṃ pūrvaślokavivaraṇa eveti | sāhasasya ca pratiṣedha evātra śrūyate, na tu daṇḍavidhiḥ kaścid, yataḥ alpamadhyamottamāparādheṣu sāhasikasya yathākramaṃ prathamamadhyamottamasāhasadaṇḍā eva yathāparibhāṣitāḥ syuḥ | atha vā steyasādṛśyāt sāhasike 'pi tasyānukto 'pi sāmarthyāt steyadaṇḍavikalpaḥ syād iti || 8.350 ||

_adhunā dramaprāptaṃ strīsaṃgrahaṇam ucyate |_

	**paradārābhimarśeṣu pravṛttān nṝn mahīpatiḥ |**

**	udvejanakaraira daṇḍaiś cihnayitvā pravāsayet || 8.351 ||**

ye tu bahuśo 'pi vāryamāṇā nāvatiṣṭheran tatra teṣām ayaṃ pravāsanavidhi sacihnaḥ | tathā coktam aparādhasamuccaye: "vāgdaṇḍaṃ prathamaṃ kuryāt" ity evamādi || 8.351 ||

_yasmāt_ |

	**tatsamutthito hi lokasya jāyate varṇasaṃkaraḥ |**

**	yena mūlaharo 'dharmaḥ sarvanāśāya kalpate || 8.352 ||**

paradārikanigrahapraśaṃsārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 8.352 ||

	**parasya patnyā puruṣaḥ saṃbhāṣaṃ yojayed rahaḥ |**

**	pūrvam ākṣārito doṣaiḥ prāpnuyāt pūrvasāhasam || 8.353 ||**

ākṣāritaḥ āśaṅkyamānadoṣaḥ | saṃvyavahārārtham api na saṃbhāṣeta || 8.353 ||

	**yas tv anākṣāritaḥ pūrvam abhibhāṣeta kāraṇāt |**

**	na doṣaṃ prāpnuyāt kiṃcin na hi tasya vyatikramaḥ || 8.354 ||**

saṃvyavahārārthaṃ prakāśasaṃbhāṣaṇam anāśaṅkyamānasyābhyanujñāte (?) || 8.354 ||

	**parastriyaṃyo 'bhibhavet tīrthe 'raṇye vane 'pi vā |**

**	nadīnāṃ vāpi saṃbhede sa saṃgrahaṇam āpnuyāt || 8.355 ||**

tīrthādiṣu vijaneṣu kāraṇād apy abhibhāṣamāṇaḥ **saṃgrahaṇam āpnuyād** anākṣārito 'pi pūrvam || 8.355 ||

_kiṃ ca ¦_

	**upakārakriyā keliḥ sparśo bhūṣaṇavāsasām |**

**	saha khaṭvāsanaṃ caiva sarvaṃ saṃgrahaṇaṃ smṛtam || 8.356 ||**

**bhūṣaṇavāsasām** upadeśāt strīgatānāṃ puruṣagatānāṃ ca sparśanād ubhayāparādhaḥ | yac cānyat snigdhadṛṣṭinipātanāṅgavikārādi tad api saṃgrahaṇam eva vijñeyam || 8.356 ||

_idaṃ cānyat |_

	**striyaṃ spṛśed adeśe yaḥ spṛṣṭo vā marṣayet tayā |**

**	parasparasyānumate sarvaṃ saṃgrahaṇaṃ smṛtam || 8.357 ||**

sarva evaite saṃgrahaṇe samāveditavyāḥ yathoktāḥ parārthāḥ striyaś caturmātraiḥ ślokaiḥ, na tu saṃgrahaṇam eva ca | yato naiṣāṃ saṃgrahaṇasamo daṇḍaḥ syāt | taduktaṃ aparādhaṃ parijñāyeti | atha tu sarveṣv eteṣu saṃgrahaṇadaṇḍaḥ kalpyate, saṃpūrṇe kiṃ kariṣyati, na viṣamasamīkaraṇaṃ nyāyyam || 8.357 ||

	**abrāhmaṇaḥ saṃgrahaṇe prāṇāntaṃ daṇḍam arhati |**

**	caturṇām api varṇānāṃ dārā rakṣyatamāḥ sadā || 8.358 ||**

saṃyatayā anicchantyā brāhmaṇyā saha saṃgrahaṇe **abrāhmaṇaḥ** śūdraḥ **prāṇāntaṃ daṇḍam arhati** | kṣatriyavaiśyābhyāṃ tu varṇavat tadūnā daṇḍaparikalpanā | evaṃ kṣatriyavaiśyayoḥ brāhmaṇīsaṃgrahaṇe 'nayāivāpekṣayā daṇḍaḥ kalpayitavyaḥ, vaiśyasya ca kṣatriyayā | icchantīṣu ca brāhmaṇakṣatriyāvaiśyāsu asaṃyatāsu ca pūrvavad daṇḍaḥ kalpanīyaḥ | saṃbhāṣaṇapratiṣedhapratiprasavārth[am idam ucyate], kiṃcid viśeṣeṇa || 8.358 ||

	**bhikṣukā vandinaś caiva dīkṣitāḥ kāravas tathā |**

**	saṃbhāṣaṇaṃ gṛhe strībhiḥ kuryur aprativāritāḥ || 8.359 ||**

bhikṣukādīnām asaty api kāraṇe saṃbhāṣaṇaṃ gṛheṣv abhyanujñāyate | tābhiḥ saha tīrthādiṣu tu vijaneṣu saty api kāraṇe bhikṣukādayo nābhibhāṣeran, śaṅkāsthāneṣu || 8.359 ||

	**na saṃbhāṣāṃ parastrībhiḥ [pratiṣiddhaḥ samācaret |**

**	niṣiddho] bhāṣamānas tu suvarṇaṃ daṇḍam arhati || 8.360 ||**

parastriyā saha saṃbhāṣaṇaṃ śāstreṇa pratiṣiddham | vyatikrame daṇḍam arhati || 8.360 ||

	**naiṣa cāraṇadāreṣu vidhir nātmopajīviṣu |**

**	sajjayanti hi te nārīr nigūḍhāś cārayanti ca || 8.361 ||**

saṃbhāṣaṇānujñānaṃ caivaitat, nopagamanasya | yato 'tra rājadaṇḍābhāvamātram, na tv atyantam adṛṣṭadoṣābhāvaḥ | yataḥ īṣaddoṣas tūpagantuḥ syād iti | yataḥ nāyaṃ pūrvapratiṣedhaviṣayaḥ | yasmād aparaiṣā veśajātiḥ | evaṃ ca kāraṇād ṛte 'py ābhiḥ saha saṃbhāṣamāṇe na saṃgrahaṇaṃ prāpnuyāt || 8.361 ||

	**kiṃcid eva tu dāpyaḥ syāt saṃbhāṣāṃ tābhir ācaran |**

**	preṣyāsu caikabhaktāsu rahaḥ pravrajitāsu ca || 8.362 ||**

**raha** iti caitad viśeṣaṇaṃ sarvaśeṣam || 8.362 ||

_strīprasaṅgāc ca kanyāgatam apīdam ucyate |_

	**yo 'kāmāṃ dūṣayet kanyāṃ sa sadyo vadham arhati |**

**	sakāmāṃ dūṣayans tulyo na vadhaṃ prāpnuyān naraḥ || 8. 363 ||**

ata ūrdhvaṃ vidhir ucyamānaḥ kanyāgato veditavyaḥ || 8.363 ||

	**kanyāṃ bhajantīm utkṛṣṭaṃ na kiṃcid api dāpayet |**

**	jaghanyaṃ sevamānāṃ tu saṃyatāṃ vāsayed gṛhe || 8.364 ||**

ṛjvarthaḥ || 8.364 ||

	**uttamāṃ sevamānas tu jaghanyo vadham arhati |**

**	śulkaṃ dadyāt sevamānaḥ samām icchet pitā yadi || 8.365 ||**

aviśeṣābhidhānāt sakāmām akāmāṃ cottamāṃ sevamānasya jaghanyasya vadha eva | **samāṃ** tu sakāmāṃ sevamānasya śulkadānaṃ tatsamo vā daṇḍaḥ | etacchlokanibandhanaś ca pūrvaḥ saṃgrahaṇaprakaraṇe ślokaḥ "abrāhmaṇaḥ saṃgrahaṇe prāṇāntaṃ daṇḍam arhati" iti || 8.365 ||

	**abhiṣahya tu yaḥ kanyāṃ kuryād darpeṇa mānavaḥ |**

**	tasyāśu kalpye aṅgulyāū daṇḍaṃ cārhati ṣaṭśatam || 8.366 ||**

akāmāṃ sevamānasyāṅgulicchedenaṃ daṇḍaṃ ca **ṣaṭśatam** | anyeṣāṃ tu pāṭhaḥ: "aviṣahyāṃ tu yaḥ kanyāṃ kuryād darpeṇa mānavaḥ" iti || 8.366 ||

	**sakāmāṃ dūṣayāṇas tu nāṅgulicchedam āpnuyāt |**

**	dviśataṃ tu damaṃ dāpyaḥ prasaṅgavinivṛttaye || 8.367 ||**

asamāsv (?) etat syāt kanyāsūttamasya || 8.367 ||

	**kanyaiva kanyāṃ yā kuryāt tasyāḥ syād dviśato damaḥ |**

**	śulkaṃ ca dviguṇaṃ dadyāc chiphāś ca prāpnuyād daśa || 8.368 ||**

śulkaṃ gomithunaṃ dviguṇaṃ kanyāpitre dadyāt dviśataṃ rājadaṇḍam || 8.368 ||

	**[yā tu kanyāṃ prakuryāt strī sā sadyo mauṇḍyaṃ arhati |**

**	aṅgulyor eva vā chedaṃ kareṇodvahanaṃ tathā || 8.369 ||**

mauṇḍyā]ṅgulicchedayor vikalpaḥ || 8.369 ||

	**bhartāraṃ laṅghayed yā tu strī jñātiguṇadarpitā |**

**	tāṃ śvabhiḥ khādayed rājā saṃsthāne bahusaṃsthite || 8.370 ||**

jñātidarpeṇa strī guṇavadbhartṛvyatikrame śvabhir asau khādayitavyā rājñā | anyasyās tu yaḥ puṃsaḥ paradāreṣu so 'syā daṇḍaḥ syāt | tac ca darśayati, "yat puṃsaḥ paradāreṣu" iti prāyaścittavidhau || 8.370 ||

	**pumāṃsaṃ dāhayet pāpaṃ śayane tapta āyase |**

**	abhyādadhyuś ca kāṣṭāni tatra dahyeta pāpakṛt || 8.371 ||**

anayaiva saṃgṛhītasyāyaṃ vidhiḥ | anyasya tu yathokta eva daṇḍaḥ syāt || 8.371 ||

_tac ca darśayati |_

	**saṃvatsarābhiśaptasya duṣṭasya dviguṇo damaḥ |**

**	vrātyayā saha saṃvāse cāṇḍālyā tāvad eva tu || 8.372 ||**

yo yasyām abhigṛhītaḥ sa cet saṃvatsare 'tīte punas tasyām evābhigṛhyet tasya yathopadeśād dviguṇo daṇḍaḥ kartavyaḥ | yas tu saṃvatsarād arvāk punar api gṛhyate tasya prathamamāse dvādaśaguṇo daṇḍaḥ evaṃ māsānumāsaṃ bhāgahrāsena tāvad daṇḍaprakḷptiḥ | yāvat saṃvatsare 'tīte dviguṇo daṇḍa iti | evaṃ saṃvatsarād ūrdhvaṃ bhāgadvādaśabhāgahrāsena māsānumāsa eva daṇḍaḥ prakalpyaḥ | yāvad eka eva bhāgo 'vaśiṣṭa iti | evaṃ pratyāgamane yo daṇḍaḥ prakalpyate tasyāpy eṣaiva prakḷptir anūdyate | caṇḍālīgamane ca daṇḍaṃ vakṣyati "sahasraṃ tv antyajastriyam" iti || 3.372 ||

	**śūdro guptam aguptaṃ vā dvaijātaṃ varṇam āvasan |**

**	aguptaikāṅgasarvasvī gupte sarveṇa hīyate || 8.373 ||**

**ekāṅgaṃ** ca pradhānam atra yad aparādhasādhanaṃ tat pragṛhyate | tenāsya hāniḥ kartavyā | gupte tūbhayena hīyate | saty api cāviśeṣavacane varṇānām auttamādharyavad daṇḍo 'pi tathā syāt, yathānyatra | viṣamasamīkaraṇaṃ tu daṇḍasāmānyād anyāyyaṃ syāt || 3.373 ||

	**vaiśyaḥ sarvasvadaṇḍyaḥ syāt (?) saṃvatsaraniro[dhataḥ] |**

**	sahasraṃ kṣatriyo daṇḍyo mauṇḍyam mūtreṇa cārhati || 8.374 ||**

anicchantyāṃ brāhmaṇyām evaitayor ubhayadaṇḍaḥ sāmarthyād vijñeyaḥ || 8.374 ||

	**brāhmaṇīṃ yady aguptāṃ tu gacchetāṃ vaiśyapārthivau |**

**	vaiśyaṃ [pañcaśataṃ kuryāt kṣatriyaṃ tu sahasriṇam] || 8.375 ||**

kṣatriyasya daṇḍādhikyaprayojanam uktam "viduṣo 'tikrame daṇḍabhūyastvam" iti | atrāparādhābhyāsānubandhād vaitad asya syāt || 8.375 ||

	**ubhāv api hi tāv eva brāhmaṇyā guptayā saha |**

**	[viplutau śūdravad da]ṇḍyau dagdhavyau vā kaṭāgninā || 8.376 ||**

ayaṃ tu **kaṭāgninā** dāhaḥ śūdradaṇḍasya vaikalpikas tato jñeyaḥ || 8.376 ||

	**sahasraṃ brāhmaṇo daṇḍyo viprāṃ guptāṃ balād vrajan |**

**	śatāni pañca daṇḍyaḥ syād icchantyā saha saṅgataḥ || 8.377 ||**

**balād** ity avivakṣitam | yo hi guptāṃ vrajati balād evāsau gato bhavati | evaṃ sakāmām akāmām ity anyatra guptāguptavyapadeśo vivakṣitaḥ | ṛjv anyat || 8.377 ||

	**mauṇḍyam prṇāntiko daṇḍo brāhmaṇasya vidhīyate |**

**	itareṣāṃ tu varṇānāṃ daṇḍaḥ prāṇāntiko bhavet || 8.378 ||**

sarvatra prāṇāntikeṣu brāhmaṇasya mauṇḍyaṃ kartavyam | muṇḍayitvā ca **samagradhano 'kṣato** rāṣṭrād bahiḥ kartavyaḥ | evaṃ sarvāṅgacchedaneṣu brāhmaṇasya muṇḍanavivāsane eva kārye | smṛtyantare cāviśeṣeṇa smaryate: "na śārīro brāḥmaṇadaṇḍaḥ" iti || 8.378 ||

_yenātaḥ |_

	**na jātu brāhmaṇaṃ hanyāt sarvapāpeṣv avasthitam |**

**	rāṣṭrāt tv enaṃ bahiṣ kuryāt samagradhanam akṣatam || 8.379 ||**

_asyārthavādaḥ_ |

	**na brāhmaṇavadhād bhūyān adharmo vidyate bhuvi |**

**	tasmād asya vadhaṃrājā manasāpi na cintayet || 8.380 ||**

pratiṣiddhasya nindārthavādo nivṛttyarthaḥ || 8.380 ||

	**vaiśyaś cet kṣatriyāṃ guptāṃ vaiśyāṃ vā kṣatriyo vrajet |**

**	yo brāḥmaṇyām aguptāyāṃ tāv ubhau daṇḍam arhataḥ || 8.381 ||**

"vaiśyaṃ pañcasataṃ kuryāt" ity evamādy aguptāyāṃ brāhmaṇyām uktam || 8.381 ||

	**sahasraṃ brāhmaṇo daṇḍaṃ dāpyo gupte tu te vrajan |**

**	śūdrāyāṃ kṣatriyaviśoḥ sāhasro vai bhaved damaḥ || 8.382 ||**

avacanād anyasya śūdrāyāṃ guptāyām ayam eva daṇḍaḥ syād brāhmaṇasya || 8.382 ||

	**agupte vaiśyarājanye śūdrāṃ ca brāhmaṇo vrajan |**

**	śatāni pañca dāpyaḥ syāt sahasraṃ tv antyajastriyam || 8.383 ||**

sarvāntyaś cāṇḍālo varṇāpasadaḥ | tasya strī | antyajastrīsaṃgame 'yaṃ daṇḍaḥ | avidhānāc ca guptāguptayor aviśeṣeṇāyaṃ daṇḍaḥ syāt | atha vādhikārād aguptāyām eva syāt | guptāyāṃ tu viśiṣṭataraḥ kāryaḥ || 8.383 ||

	**yasya stenaḥ pure nāsti nānyastrīgo na duṣṭavāk |**

**	na sāhasikadaṇḍaghnau sa rājā śakralokabhāk || 8.384 ||**

_yataś vaitad evam ataḥ |_

	**eteṣāṃ nigraho rājñaḥ pañcānāṃ viṣaye svake |**

**	sāmrājyakṛt sajātyeṣu loke caiva yaśaskaraḥ || 8.385 ||**

nigrahastutiḥ ślokadvayena | prasaṅgāc cedam aparaṃ sāhasaprakaraṇa evocyate || 8.385 ||

	**ṛtvijaṃ yas tyajed yājyo jājyaṃ cartvik tyajed yadi |**

**	śaktaṃ karmaṇy aduṣṭaṃ ca tayor daṇḍaḥ śataṃ satam || 8.386 ||**

ṛjvarthaḥ ślokaḥ || 8.386 ||

	**na mātā na pitā na strī na putras tyāgam arhati |**

**	tyajann apatitān etān rājñā daṇḍyaḥ śatāni ṣaṭ || 8.387 ||**

prāyaścittaprāptāv akurvantas tāni tyājyā na tu dveṣādinā || 8.387 ||

	**āśrameṣu dvijātīnāṃ kārye vivadatāṃ mithaḥ |**

**	na vibrūyān nṛpo dharmaṃ cikīrṣan hitam ātmanaḥ || 8.388 ||**

tapasvivdhyarthaḥ ślokaḥ || 8.388 ||

	**yathārham etān abhyarcya brāhmaṇaiḥ saha pārthivaḥ |**

**	sāntvena praśamayyādau svadharmaṃ pratipādayet || 8.389 ||**

**	prativeśyānuveśyau ca kalyāṇe viṃsati (?) dvije |**

**	arhāv abhojayan vipro daṇḍaṃ arhati māṣakam || 8.390 ||**

pārśvaveśmānāv apy arthagṛhītau vijñeyau | anyas tu pāṭhāntare 'rtham āh**ānuveśyas** tadanugāmī | **prativeśyas** tatsammukhaḥ || 8.390 ||

	**śrotriyaḥ śrotriyaṃ sādhuṃ bhūtikṛtyeṣv abhojayet |**

asamīpagṛham apy ekagrāmam |

	**tad annaṃ dviguṇaṃ dāpyo hairṇyaṃ caiva māṣakam || 8.391 ||**

arhabrāhmaṇātikramadaṇḍo 'yam | **bhūtikṛtyeṣv** iti vacanād ārambhasāmarthyāc ca pūrvasmāt kalyāṇān mahattaram idaṃ vijñāyate | etau ca daṇḍāv arhādāne sati syātām || 8.391 ||

	**andho jaḍaḥ pīṭhasarpī saptatyā sthaviraś ca yaḥ |**

saptatyāḥ prabhṛti sthaviro gṛhyate |

	**śrotriyeṣūpakurvaṃś ca na dāpyaḥ kenacit karam || 8.392 ||**

abrāhmaṇā api santaḥ brāhmaṇā api vānarhantaḥ || 8.392 ||

	**śrotriyaṃ vyādhitārtau ca bālavṛddhāv akiṃcanam |**

**	mahākulīnam āryaṃ ca rājā saṃpūjayet sadā || 8.393 ||**

**śrotriyaḥ** śāstraprasiddhyā brāhmaṇo gṛhyate | vyādhitārtabālavṛddhākiṃcanā aśrotriyā api santaḥ | **mahāulīnam**, [saguṇakulajātam], **āryaṃ ca rājā saṃpūjayet sadā** | prakaraṇāt karāgraheṇa grāsācchādanena vā sthityarthena | karāgrahaṇādikena tapasviśrotriyaprasaṅgāc cāyaṃ vyavahāramadhye kārudharma ucyate || 8.393 ||

	**[śālmalīphala]ke ślakṣṇe nijyād vāsāṃsi nejakaḥ |**

**	na ca vāsāṃsi vāsobhir nirharen na ca vāsayet || 8.394 ||**

pratītārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 8.394 ||

	**tantuvāyo daśapalaṃ dadyād ekapalādhikam |**

**	ato 'nyathā vartamāno dāpyo dvādaśakaṃ damam || 8.395 ||**

chinnaṃ dvādaśaguṇaṃ dāpyaḥ | evaṃ sarvadravyāṇāṃ lohādīnāṃ chedane | sāhasaprakaraṇe ca tatsādṛśyād imau ślokāv ucyete || 8.395 ||

	**śulkasthāneṣu kuśalāḥ sarvapaṇyavicakṣaṇāḥ |**

**	kuryur arghaṃ yathāpaṇyaṃ tato viṃśaṃ nṛpo haret || 8.396 ||**

dravyasyāgamanirgame deśakālāpekṣayā arghanipātena viṃśabhāgaḥ śulkaḥ || 8.396 ||

	**rājñaḥ prakhyātabhāṇḍāni pratiṣiddhāni yāni ca |**

**	tāni nirharato lobhāt sarvahāraṃ haren nṛpaḥ || 8.397 ||**

yad yatra pracuraṃ yatra ca durlabhaṃ tat tasya rājñaḥ **prakhyātaṃ** bhavati | tathodīcyeṣv ājāneyā aśvāḥ, kuṃkumaṃ kāśmīreṣu, prācyeṣv agarukarpūrādi tadanyatra na nirhāryam | anirhṛtaṃ hi durlabhatvāt | itaretaraṃ rājñāṃ kāryapratibandhād upāyanaṃ bhavati | yasya ca dharmārthopāyanasya dharmajanakasyārthajanakasya ca krayavikrayapratiṣedho rājñā kṛto bhavati | yathā mākṣikasya madhunaḥ | tac ca na nirharyam | vaṇigbhir nirharato nṛpaḥ sarvabhāgaṃ haret || 8.397 ||

	**śulkasthānaṃ pariharaṇṇ akāle krayavikrayī |**

**	mithyāvādī ca saṃkhyāne dāpyo 'ṣṭaguṇam atyayam || 8.398 ||**

kaḥ śakṣyati kāle divā śulkasthānaṃ parihartum iti svabhāvasiddhaṃ kālam anuvadati | na tv etena tato 'nyakālo 'bhyanujñāyate, divākāle pariharato na doṣa iti | śulkam aṣṭaguṇaṃ dāpyam | tathā yāvatī saṃkhyā tāvatīm apy aṣṭaguṇāṃ dāpayet mithāvacanena | āgamopayogau dravyasyāniyatāv itīdam ucyate || 8.398 ||

	**āgamaṃ nirgamaṃ sthānaṃ tathā vṛddhikṣayāv ubhau |**

**	vicārya sarvapaṇyānāṃ kārayet krayavikrayau || 8.399 ||**

āgamādi dravyasyāpekṣya krayivikrayiṇoś ca vṛddhikṣayau tayor arghanipātena krayavikrayau kārayet || 8.399 ||

	**pañcarātre pañcarātre pakṣe pakṣe tathāgate |**

**	kurvīta caiṣāṃ pratyakṣam arghasaṃsthāpanaṃ nṛpaḥ || 8.400 ||**

_āgamopayogau dravyasyāniyatāv ity ata idam ucyate |_

	**tulā mānaṃ pratīmānaṃ sarvaṃ pārthivalakṣitam |**

**	ṣaṭsu ṣaṭsu ca māeṣu punar etat parīkṣayet || 8.401 ||**

trayam apy etad rājamudrāṅkitam anādhṛṣyaṃ bhavati | ṛjv anyat || 8.401 ||

	**paṇaṃ yānaṃ tare dāpyaṃ pauruṣo 'rdhapaṇaṃ bharaḥ |**

**	pādaṃ paśuś ca yoṣic ca pādārdhaṃ raktakaḥ pumān || 8.402 ||**

riktaṃ **yānaṃ** rathādi paṇaṃ dadyāt | puruṣavāhyo bhāro 'rdhapaṇam | prakṛtasya paṇasya **pādaṃ paśuś ca** riktakā **yoṣic ca** | **pādārdhaṃ riktakaḥ pumān** || 8.402 ||

	**bhāṇḍapūrṇāni yānāni tāryaṃ dāpyāni sārataḥ |**

**	riktabhāṇḍāni yat kiṃcit pumāṃsaś cāparicchadāḥ || 8.403 ||**

karmadravyānurūpyeṇa pūrṇāni yānāni dadyuḥ | aparicchadā api yat kiṃcid dadyuḥ | riktakasyaiko 'rdhapādaḥ || 8.403 ||

	**dīrghe 'dhvani yathākālaṃ yathādeśaṃ taro bhavet |**

**	nadītīreṣu tad vidyāt samudre nāsti lakṣaṇam || 8.404 ||**

dīrghe yātavye 'dhvani kalpyas taraḥ kṣayalābhān avekṣya | tathā nadīvaipulyam apekṣya pāragamane | ṛjv anyat || 8.404 ||

	**garbhiṇī tu dvimāsādis tathā pravrajito muniḥ |**

**	brāhmaṇā liṅginaś caiva na dāpyās tārikaṃ tare || 8.405 ||**

pratītārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 8.405 ||

	**yan nāvi kiṃcid dāśānāṃ viśīryetāparādhataḥ |**

**	tad dāśair eva dātavyaṃ samāgamya svatoṃśataḥ (?) || 8.406 ||**

nigadavyākhyātaḥ ślokaḥ || 8.407 ||

	**eṣa nauyāyinām ukto vyavahārasya nirṇayaḥ | \
	dāśāparādhatas toye daivike nāsti nigrahaḥ || 8.407 ||**

na kiṃcid vaktavyaṃ sphuṭatvāc chlokasya || 8.407 ||

	**vāṇijyaṃ kārayed vaiśyaṃ kusīdaṃ kṛṣim eva ca |**

**	paśūnāṃ rakṣaṇaṃ caiva dāsyaṃ sūdraṃ dvijanmanām || 8.408 ||**

vaiśyaśūdrau vāṇijyādisvakarmākurvāṇau balād rājñā kārayitavyau | akurvāṇau ca daṇḍadaṇḍyau syātām | evamarthaś ca rājadharme[ṣu pu]na[rārambhaḥ] || 8.408 ||

	**kṣatriyaṃ caiva vaiśyaṃ ca brāhmaṇo vṛttikarśitau |**

**	bibhṛyād ānṛśaṃsyena svāni karmāṇi kārayan || 8.409 ||**

na tu dāsakarmaṇā vāsobhāṇḍadhāvanādinā | yena dāsakarmapratiṣedhārtho [kārayan] imau svāni karmāṇy ānṛśaṃsyena bharaṇīyāv eva || 8.409 ||

	**dāsyaṃ tu dārayan mohād brāhmaṇaḥ saṃskṛtān dvijān |**

**	anicchataḥ prabhāvatvād rājñā dāpyaḥ śatāni ṣaṭ || 8.410 ||**

dvijagrahaṇāc cātra brāhmaṇo 'pi samānatvā[d | na] caite icchanto 'nicchanto vā dāsyaṃ kārayitavyāḥ | etāvāṃs tu viśeṣaḥ | anicchatāṃ karaṇe 'yaṃ daṇḍaḥ | icchatāṃ tu karaṇe kalpayitavyaḥ | evam arthaṃ ca rājadharmeṣūktam idam iti || 8.410 ||

	**śūdraṃ tu kārayed dāsyaṃ krītam akrītam eva vā |**

**	dāsyāyaiva hi sṛṣṭo 'sau brāhmaṇasya svayaṃbhuvā || 8.411 ||**

bhaktadāsakrītayor ayaṃ kartavyatāyāṃ viśeṣo nāsti | brāhmaṇagrahaṇaṃ ca dvijātipradarśanārtham || 8.411 ||

_evaṃ ca sati —_

	**na svāminā nisṛṣṭo 'pi śūdro dāsyād vimucyate |**

**	nisargajaṃ hi tat tasya kas taṃ tasmād apohati || 8.412 ||**

yathaivādhyāpanādi brāhmaṇādīnāṃ nisargajam evaṃ śūdrasya [dāsyam] | yathaitat tena kartavyam ity uktam eva śāstre || 8.412 ||

_tatprasaṅgena ceme **dāsayonaya** ucyante |_

	**dhvajāhṛto bhaktadāso gṛhajaḥ krītadattrimau |**

**	paitriko daṇḍadāsaś ca saptaite dāsayonayaḥ || 8.413 ||**

**dhvajāhṛto** yuddhanirjitaḥ | **bhaktadāsa** udarapraviṣṭaḥ | **gṛhajo** dāsīputraḥ | **kṛītadattrimau** prasiddhau | **paitriko** dāsīputraḥ pitṛparyāyāgataḥ | daṇḍadāsas tv avidyamānadhano daṇḍitaḥ daṇḍenātmānaṃ praveśayati | etāḥ sapta **dāsayonayaḥ** | āsām madhye anyatamayāpy upeto dāsākhyaṃ labhate | yas tu vidyamānavibhavaḥ śūdraḥ svaśaktyā jīvati nāsau paramārthato dāso veditavyaḥ | itarathāsyānarthakyam asya dāsayonyarthasya ślokasya syāt || 8.413 ||

	**bhāryā putraś ca dāsaś ca traya evādhanāḥ smṛtāḥ  |**

**	yat te samadhigacchanti yasya te tasya tad dhanam || 8.414 ||**

bhāryāputragrahaṇam atra dāsadṛṣṭāntarthaṃ tatsamānatvād etatprakaraṇe 'svārtham | evaṃ ca sati trayāṇām apy eṣāṃ nirdhanatvaṃ na paramārthataḥ | kiṃ tarhi tatanujñātadra[vya]vyavahārārthaṃ vijñeyam | kasya punar hetoḥ | yena yad upārjyate na tat tasmād vyāvartayituṃ śakyate | adravyatve caiṣāṃ putrādīnāṃ karmabhir asaṃbandhaḥ syāt | na caitad iṣṭam, śāstraśiṣṭatvāt teṣāṃ karmaṇaḥ | evaṃ ca sati gauṇam eṣāṃ nirdhanatvaṃ vijñeyam | uttarārthaṃ ca || 8.414 ||

_yataś caitad evam ataḥ |_

	**visrabdhaṃ brāhmaṇaḥ śūdrād dravyopādānam ācaret |**

**	na hi tasyāsti kiṃcit svaṃ bhartṛhāryadhano hi saḥ || 8.415 ||**

dāsādhikārād dāsaḥ | śūdrāt tasmāt tatsvāmine | nābrāhmaṇasya pratigrahapakṣo draṣṭavyo brāhmaṇasya svadāsapratigrahaḥ | atha vetarasmāc chūdrād adāsāl laghīyān ayaṃ pratigraho vijñeyaḥ | na hy akasmāt tataḥ praśaṃsāvarṣavacanaṃ yuktam | na tu śūdrasyettaṃbhūtasyāpi dvijātibhiḥ sāmyaṃ yuktaṃ kartum iti | yata evamabhiprāya evāyaṃ nirdeśo veditavyaḥ || 8.415 ||

	**vaiśyaśūdrau prayatnena svāni karmāṇi kārayet |**

**	tau hi cyutau svadharmebhyaḥ kṣobhayetām idaṃ jagat || 8.416 ||**

"vāṇijyaṃ kārayed viśyam" ity asya ślokasya prakaraṇāt prayatnataḥ svakarma kārayitavyā [iti] viśeṣeṇādāv uktasyāyam upasaṃhārārthaḥ ślokaḥ | atha vā śūdro dvaijātaṃ karma kurvan dharmasaṃkarāj jagato mahad bhayaṃ vidadhāti | vaiśyo 'pi kṛṣyādiṣv avartamāno 'nnādikṣayāt | tasmād imau rājñā prayatnataḥ svakarmakārayitavyau viśeṣeṇa | na ca tayor nirdeśād brāhmaṇakṣatriyayor etad anupadiṣṭaṃ bhavati | viśeṣārthaś cārambho vaiśyaśūdrayor vijñeyaḥ || 8.416 ||

	**ahany ahany avekṣeta karmāntān vāhanāni ca |**

**	āyavyayau ca niyatāv ākarān kośam eva ca || 8.417 ||**

lokasthityarthasya rājyatantrahetoś ca paurajānapadānāṃ vyavahārajātasyānurodheneti vyavahāradarśana[ṃ kṛtvā] || 8.417 ||

	**evaṃ sarvān imān rājā vyavahārān samāpayan |**

**	vyapohya kilbiṣaṃ sarvaṃ prāpnoti paramāṃ gatim || 8.418 ||**

rājño yathoktavyavahāradarśanasya śāstrasāmarthyāt phalavidhir ayam | tadanuṣṭhā[na sāmā]nyāc cāyaṃ vyavahāropasaṃhāraḥ pūrveṣāṃ vyavahāranittānām aparisamāpteṣv api vyavahārāspadeṣu strīpuṃdharmaprabhṛtiṣu caturṣv apīti || 8.418 ||

**iti bhāruceḥ kṛtāv aṣṭamo 'dhyāyaḥ |**
## 09
**navamo 'dhyāyaḥ **

	**puruṣasya striyāś caiva dharmye vartmani tiṣṭhatoḥ |**

**	saṃyoge viprayoge ca dharmān vakṣyāmi śāsvatān || 9.1 ||**

dharmye vartmanīty anyonyāvyabhicāralakṣaṇe tiṣṭhator dampatyoḥ saṃyoge jīvati patyau saṃnihite vā viprayoge ca mṛte proṣite vā tayor dharmān vakṣyāmi niyogavṛttiniyamādīn | śāśvatagrahaṇaṃ cānayor anuṣṭhānastutyartham | idaṃ tāvat prāk prasiddham eva || 9.1 ||

_yathā_ |

	**asvatantrāḥ striyaḥ kāryāḥ puruṣaiḥ svair divāniśam |**

**	viṣaye sajjamānāś ca saṃsthāpyā ātmano vaśe || 9.2 ||**

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanv āsām</span> asvātantryaṃ strīdharme niṣṭham eva pañcame 'dhyāye |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | strīdharmā eva te | ime tu vakṣyamāṇāḥ strīpuṃsayoḥ | tathā ca sati pratijñeyaṃ puruṣasy striyāś caiveti | śāstrānukramaṇyāṃ caivam evoktam | "sākṣipraśnavidhānaṃ ca dharmaḥ strīpuṃsayos tathā" iti | punaś ca vyavahārānukraṇyām aṣṭame 'dhyāye samastayor eva nirdeśaḥ | "strīpuṃdharmo vibhāgaś ca" iti | atha vottarārtham etat syāt | evaṃ ca sati yad uktam āsāṃ strīdharmeṣu pāratantryaṃ tat kutaḥ syād ity ata idaṃ tatsaṃbandhenocyate || 9.2 ||

	**pitā rakṣati kaumāre bhartā rakṣati yauvane |**

**	putras tu sthavire bhāve na strī svātantryam arhati || 9.3 ||**

evaṃ ca sati [na] rājani bhartary eva vāsām asvātantryam, kiṃ tarhi yathāvayaḥ pitrādiṣu | tatsaṃrakṣaṇapare ca vākye na pitrādayo vayovibhāgāśrayeṇa hitrādistrīṇāṃ rakṣitāro niyamyante | evaṃ ca sati sarvadā sarveṣāṃ tadrakṣaṇopadeśo 'yaṃ sāmarthyād vijñeyaḥ | sarvatra laḍ draṣṭavyo vidhyarthe rakṣed ity evaṃ chāndasatvāviśeṣāt | smṛter yuktaṃ tallakṣaṇam atra | yataś caitad evam ataḥ || 9.3 ||

	**kāle 'dātā pitā vācyo vācyaś cānupayan patiḥ |**

**	mṛte bhartari putras tu vācyo mātur arakṣitā || 9.4 ||**

sarvadā tatsaṃrakṣaṇam akurvantaḥ kanyādānādi ca yathāsaṃbhavaṃ vācyā vacanīyāḥ syuḥ | yata etaddoṣaparihārārtham ebhiḥ || 9.4 ||

	**sūkṣmebhyo 'pi prasaṅgebhyaḥ striyo rakṣyā viśeṣataḥ |**

**	dvayor hi kulayoḥ śokam āvaheyur arakṣitāḥ || 9.5 ||**

sūkṣmaprasaṅgāś cāsāṃ vyabhicārahetavo loke prasiddhāḥ parivrājikādisaṃsargākhyāḥ ananuśiṣṭā api || 9.5 ||

	**imaṃ hi sarvavarṇānāṃ paśyanto dharmam uttamam |**

**	yatante rakṣituṃ bhāryāṃ bhartāro durabalā api || 9.6 ||**

kiṃ punar itare | tac ca dharmottamatvaṃ strīrakxaṇasya yathā bhavati tathedam adhunocyate sarvartham || 9.6 ||

	**svāṃ prasūtiṃ caritraṃ ca kulam ātmānam eva ca |**

**	svaṃ ca dharmaṃ prayatnena jāyāṃ rakṣan hi rakṣati || 9.7 ||**

svāṃ prasūtim apatyaśuddhiṃ jāyāṃ rakṣan hi rakṣati yathā tathaiva | caritram ācāram | bhāryā saṃrakṣaṇiyety evam | kulaṃ ca pūrvapuruṣān | ātmānaṃ ca, pretaṃ santam asaṃkīrṇāpatyapiṇḍodakariyayā, jīvantaṃ cāpatyasaṃkaraparihāreṇa | tathā ca smṛtyantara:

	abhirūpāḥ kule jātā vidyāśīlasamanvitāḥ |

	satputraśiṣyās trāyante mātaraṃ pitaraṃ gurum ||

svadharmaṃ śrautaṃ yenāsaṃkīrṇāpatyasyādhānādibhir adhikāraḥ bhavati gauṇaṃ vā tad iti vakṣyāmaḥ | nāmadheyaṃ ca striyāḥ saṃrakṣaṇārthavādī kurvann idam āha || 9.7 ||

	**patir bhāryāṃ saṃpraviśya garbho bhūtveha jāyate |**

**	jāyāyās tad dhi jāyātvaṃ yad asyāṃ jāyate punaḥ || 9.8 ||**

vedasmṛtiśāstranyāyavirodhaś cāyam arthavādo bhāryāsaṃrakṣaṇārthaḥ | tathā ca prakaraṇam | dṛṣṭaś cāyaṃ lokapravādas tatsaṃrakṣaṇārthaḥ | aparo 'rthavāda ucyate || 9.8 ||

	**yādṛśaṃ bhajate hi strī sutaṃ sūte tathāvidham |**

**	tasmāt prajāviśuddhyarthaṃ striyaṃ sūte tathāvidham || 9.9 ||**

tatsaṃrakṣaṇāc cāpatyaśuddhyā sarvakarmādhikāro 'tyantotkarṣaprayojano yasmāt | ataś cāyam ukto muhur muhur ādareṇa tatsaṃrakṣaṇe || 9.9 ||

	**[na kaścid yoṣitaḥ śaktaḥ pra]sahya parirakṣitum |**

**	etair upāyayogais tu śakyāḥ syuḥparirakṣitum || 9.10 ||**

pūrvāparavirodhaḥ śāstre na nyāyyo bhinnaprakaraṇe 'pi, kiṃ punar ekaprakaraṇe | yata eva[ṃ na kaścid] yoṣitaḥ śaktaḥ prasahya parirakṣitum itīdaṃ vakṣyamāṇopaya(?)stutyartham | evaṃ ca pūrvaṃ strīsaṃrakṣaṇopadeśo na virudhyate || 9.10 ||

_ke punas tadrakṣaṇopāyāḥ | yatas tān darśayati |_

	**arthasaṃrahaṇe caināṃ vyaye caiva niyojayet |**

**	sauce (?) dharme 'nnapaktyāṃ ca pāriṇahyasya cekṣaṇe || 9.11 ||**

pārīṇahyam āsanaśayanopadhānāstraṇādi "patnī hi pārīṇahyasyeśe" iti śruteḥ || 9.11 ||

	**arakṣitā gṛhe ruddhāḥ puruṣair āptakāribhiḥ |**

**	ātmānam ātmanā yās tu rakṣeyus tāḥ surakṣitāḥ || 9.12 ||**

anantaraślokotena copāyenaitā **ātmānam ātmanā** rakṣanti tasmāt tatstutiparam evedam | na tu gṛhoparodhāptapuruṣopagrahalakṣaṇayos strīrakaṣaṇahetvor ayaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ, sāmarthyāt prakaraṇāc ceti | atha vā nārīsaṃdūṣaṇaparivarjanastutiparam etat, **ātmānam ātmanā yās tu rakṣeyus tāḥ surakṣitā** iti | yatas tatparivarjanārthaṃ tāni darśayati || 9.12 ||

	**pānam durjanasaṃsargaḥ patyā ca viraho 'ṭanam |**

**	svapno 'nyagehavāsaś ca nārīsaṃdūṣaṇāni ṣaṭ || 9.13 ||**

parivarjanārtha eṣām upadeśas tatpuruṣāṇām | yataś ca pānādivyabhicārakaraṇeṣu vartamānāḥ || 9.13 ||

	**naitā rūpaṃ parīkṣante nāsāṃ vayasi saṃsthitiḥ |**

**	vrūpaṃ rūpavantaṃ vā pumān ity eva bhuñjate || 9.14 ||**

etāsv avasthāsu vartamānā visaṃjñāḥ satyaḥ | yataḥ pānādīn varjayeyuḥ || 9.14 ||

	**pauṃścalyāc calacittāc ca naiḥsnehyāc ca svabhāvataḥ |**

**	rakṣitā yatnato 'pīha bhartṛṣv etā vikurvate || 9.15 ||**

āsu pānādyavasthāsu | ato na pūrvaviśvāsāt pānādiṣupekṣyāḥ (?) || 9.15 ||

	**evaṃ svabhāvaṃ jñātvāsāṃ prajāpatinisargajam |**

**	paramaṃ yatnam ātiṣṭhet puruṣo rakṣaṇaṃ prati || 9.16 ||**

vyabhicārātmakatvam āsāṃ svabhāvataḥ | atas taṃ viditvā nityam etā rakṣyāḥ | na viśvāsād upekṣaṇīyāḥ gṛhītavinayā iti kṛtvā || 9.16 ||

_yataś ca |_

	**śayyāsanam alaṃkāraṃ kāmaṃ krodham anāryatām |**

**	drohabhāvaṃ kucaryāṃ ca strībhyo manur akalpayat || 9.17 ||**

ataś ca yuktās tāḥ prayatnato rakṣitum evaṃ svabhāvatvāt | tatra tu **śayyā** bhāvo nādhikaraṇaṃ supyate 'syām iti | evam āsanālaṃkārakāmakrodhāḥ, mākye bhāvapratyayābhāve 'pi | **anāryatā drohabhāva** ity atra svaśabdenaiva bhāva upadiṣṭaḥ | caraṇaṃ caryā **kucaryā** utsitā caryā | sarva ete bhāvāḥ | evam "svabhāvaṃ jñātvāsām" iti prakṛtatvād asya | evaṃ ca sati tannindāvacanaṃ rakṣārtham || 9.17 ||

_yataś ca |_

	**nāsti strīṇāṃ kriyā mantrair iti dharme vyavasthitam |**

**	nirindriyā hy amantrāś ca striyo 'nṛtam iti sthitiḥ || 9.18 ||**

"amantrikā tu kāryeyaṃ strīṇām āvṛd aśeṣataḥ" ity uktam yad tad idam ucyate: "nāsti strīṇāṃ kriyā mantraiḥ" iti | vivāhasaṃskāraś ca mantrataḥ puruṣasaṃbandhāpekṣayā na svātantryeṇa sādhāraṇo vā | yato na vyāghātaḥ | arthavādārthaṃ caitan nindāvacanam | indriyaṃ prajñādhairyādi | tadabhāvāt striyo 'nindriyā ity ucyante, nānyathā | evaṃ cābalā ity evam etāḥ prasiddhāḥ | yato nirindriyā amantrāś ca striyaḥ atas tāsāṃ svavīryasyābhāvāt svayam ātmasaṃrakṣaṇe sāmarthyaṃ nāsti | amantratvāc ca puruṣavan mantravatā saṃskāreṇa śuddhir nāsti | amantratvāc ca puruṣavan mantravatā saṃskāreṇa śuddhir nāsti | ātmasaṃyamane tv āsāṃ suddhir eṣitavyā | ataś caitā nirindriyā nirvīryā nissaṃjñatvān nirvijñānāḥ satyo 'nṛtaśabdena nindyante | vyabhicārātmakatvena vā prakṛtena || 9.18 ||

	**tathā ca śrutayo bahvyo gaditā nigameṣv api |**

**	svālakṣaṇyaparīkṣārthaṃ tāsāṃ ca śṛṇutākṛtim || 9.19 ||**

**svālakṣaṇyam** āsāṃ vyabhicāraḥ | yatas tāsāṃ vyabhicār**ākṛtim** imāṃ **śṛṇuta** || 9.19 ||

	**yan me mātā pralulubhe vicaranty ap[ativratā |**

**	tan me retaḥ pitā vṛ]ṅktām ity asyaitan nidarśanam || 9.20 ||**

kasmiṃścit kila karmaṇi yajamāna idam āha: yady api me mātā parapuruṣalobhā vyabhicāriṇī bhavet tathāpi tad retaḥ pitaiva me vṛṅktā[m iti | asya]itan nidarśanam: vede 'pi ca svabhāvavyabhicāritvaṃ strīṇāṃ dṛśyate | tatas tatsaṃrakṣaṇārtham ayaṃ vaidiko nigama udāhṛtaḥ || 9.20 ||

_anyac cāha |_

	**dhyāyaty aniṣṭaṃ yat kiṃcit pāṇi[grāhasya cetasā |**

**	tasyaiṣa vyabhicārasya] nihnavaḥ samyag ucyate || 9.21 ||**

evaṃ ca manovyabhicāre etad vijñeyam | "yādṛgguṇena bhartrā strī saṃyujyeta yathāvidh", tādṛgvyabhicārasya nihnavaḥ pramārjanaṃ prāyaścittam asya mantra[dvāreṇa] | na kevalaṃ manovyabhicārapradarśakam etat, kiṃ tarhi karmavyabhicāraprāyaścittam eva vijñeyam || 9.21 ||

	**yādṛgguṇena bhartrā strī saṃyujyeta yathāvidhi |**

**	tādṛēgguṇā sā bhavati samudreṇeva nimnagā || 9.22 ||**

ātmasaṃyamanenāpy etāḥ śakyā rakṣituṃ manuṣyeṇety upāyāntaranirdeśaḥ | na kevalam asaṃyatatayātmānam evopahanti manuṣyāḥ, kiṃ tarhi striyā apy upaghāta evaṃvṛtto vartata ity asyārthasya nidarśanam || 9.22 ||

	**akṣamālā vasiṣṭhena saṃyuktādhamayonijā |**

**	śāraṅgī mandapālena jagamābhyarhaṇīyatām || 9.23 ||**

_yasmāc ca |_

	**etāś cānyāś ca loka 'sminn apakṛṣṭaprasūtayaḥ |**

**	utkarṣaṃ yoṣitaḥ prāptāḥ svaiḥ svair bhartṛguṇaiḥ śubhaiḥ || 9.24 ||**

ataś cātmasaṃyame yatnaḥ kartavyaḥ, strīrakṣaṇārthataḥ tasyeti || 9.24 ||

	**eṣoditā lokayātrā nityaṃ strīpuṃsayoḥ śubhā|**

**	preteha ca sukhodarkān prajādharmān nibodhata || 9.25 ||**

kasya prajā, kiṃ kṣetriṇo, bījina, ubhayor veti || 9.25 ||

	**prajanārthaṃ mahābhāgāḥ pūjārhā gṛhadīptayaḥ |**

**	striyaḥ śriyaś ca geheṣu na viśeṣo 'sti kaścana || 9.26 ||**

eṣo 'syābhiprāyaḥ: sarvadoṣāvaskannānām api hi strīṇāṃ prajananāyogān mahāprayojanatve saty ayuktas tāsāṃ parityāgaḥ prāyaścittapratyāharaṇīyatvāt | tathā ca vakṣyati saṃyatāṃ vāsayed gṛhe, "yat puṃsaḥ paradāreṣu tac cainaṃ cārayed vratam" iti vacanāt | na cākasmāt stutiḥ pravartata iti kṛtvāvaśyam etad abhyupagantavyam || 9.26 ||

_yataś ca |_

	**utpādanam apatyasya jātasya paripālanam |**

**	pratyahaṃ lokayātrāyāḥ pratyakṣaṃ strīnibandhanam || 9.27 ||**

ayam aparaḥ strīpraśaṃsārthaḥ ślokaḥ pūrvoktaprayojanārtha eva vijñeyaḥ || 9.27 ||

_kiṃ cānyat, yena |_

	**apatyaṃ dharmakāryāṇi śuśrūṣā ratir uttamā |**

**	dārādhīnas tathā svargaḥ pitṝṇām ātmanas ca hi || 9.28 ||**

ataś ca yathokta evārtho vijñeyaḥ || 9.28 ||

_evaṃ ca sati |_

	**patiṃ yā nāticarati manovāgdehasaṃyatā |**

**	sā bhartṛlokān āpnoti sadbhiḥ sādhvīti cocyate || 9.29 ||**

**	vyabhicārāt tu bhartuḥ strī loke prāpnoti nindyatām |**

**	sṛgālayoniṃ cāpnoti pāparogaiś ca pīḍyate || 9.30 ||**

yasmāt tasmād ābhiḥ bhartṛpāratantryaṃ na moktavyam || 9.29–30 ||

	**putraṃ praty uditaṃ sadbhiḥ pūrvajaiś ca maharṣibhiḥ |**

**	viśvajanyam imaṃ puṇyam upanyāsaṃ nibodhata || 9.31 ||**

yathā viśvajany 'sau tathedam ucyate || 9.31 ||

	**bhartuḥ putraṃ vijānanti śrutidvaidhaṃ tu kartari |**

**	āhur utpādakaṃ kecid apare kṣetriṇaṃ viduḥ || 9.32 ||**

apareṣāṃ pakṣa ubhayoḥ || 9.32 ||

_asyā vipratipatteḥ kāraṇam āha |_

	**kṣetrabhūtā smṛtā nārī bījabhūtaḥ smṛtaḥ pumān |**

**	kṣetrabījasamāyogāt saṃbhavaḥ sarvadehinām || 9.33 ||**

ata etasmāt kāraṇād yukteyaṃ vipratipattiḥ || 9.33 ||

_asyāṃ ca vipratipattau sthitaṃ pakṣaṃ darśayati |_

	**viśiṣṭaṃ tu kvacid bījaṃ**

kaiścit parigṛhītam |

			**strīyonis tv eva kutracit |**

apareṣāṃ pakṣaḥ |

	**ubhayaṃ tu samaṃ yatra sā prasūtir viśiṣyate || 9.34 ||**

ity ayaṃ sthitaḥ pakṣa ācāryasya vijñeyaḥ || 9.34 ||

_atra pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ pradarśyate |_

	**bījasya caiva yonyāś ca bījam utkṛṣṭam ucyate |**

yasmāt,

	**sarvabhūtaprasūtir hi bījalakṣaṇalakṣitā || 9.35 ||**

tathā sati,

	**yādṛśaṃ tūpyate bījaṃ kṣetre kālopapādite |**

**	tādṛg rohati tat tasmin bījaṃ svair vyañjitaṃ guṇaiḥ || 9.36 ||**

ataś ca bījānāṃ tatprādhānyam || 9.36 ||

_yena ca,_

	**iyaṃ bhūmir hi bhūtānāṃ śāśvatī yonir ucyate |**

**	na ca yoniguṇān kāṃścid bījaṃ puṣyati puṣṭiṣu || 9.37 ||**

ataś ca taddharmānanuvṛtter bījasya kṣetram apradhānam || 9.37 ||

yataś ca |

	**bhūmāv apy ekakedāre kāloptāni kṛṣīvalaiḥ |**

**	nānarūpāṇi jāyante bījānīha svabhavataḥ || 9.38 ||**

bījānuvidhānena bhūmijātyananuvidhānena ca || 9.38 ||

_tathā ca darśayati |_

	**vrīhayaḥ śālayo mudgās tilā māṣās tathā yavāḥ |**

**	[yathābījaṃ prarohanti laśunānīkṣava]s tathā || 9.39 ||**

evaṃ ca sati pratyakṣataḥ |

	**anyad uptaṃ jātam anyad ity etan nopapadyate |**

**	upyate yad dhi yad bījaṃ tat tad eva prarohati || 9.40 ||**

etāvadbījaprādhānyapakṣaḥ | adhunā [kṣetraprādhānyapakṣaḥ pradarśya]te || 9.40 ||

	**tat prājñena vinītena jñānavijñānavedinā |**

**	āyuṣkāmena vaptavyaṃ na jātu parayoṣiti || 9.41 ||**

kṣetraprādhānyāt, mā bhūt parakṣetre bījāpahāraḥ | [anādiparaṃparāsiddhaṃ ca yataḥ parakṣetrajātaṃ na] bījino 'patyam || 9.41 ||

_evaṃ ca |_

	**atra gāthāṃ yamodgītāṃ kīrtayanti purāvidaḥ |**

**	yathā bījaṃ na vaptavyaṃ puṃsā paraparigrahe || 9.42 ||**

**	naśyatīṣur yathā viddhaḥ khe viddham anuviddhya[taḥ |**

**	tathā naśyati vai kṣipraṃ bījaṃ para]parigrahe || 9.43 ||**

parigrahe saty anyasya | paścād asvāmitvāt phalābhāvaṃ darśayati || 9.43 ||

	**pṛthor apīmāṃ pṛthivīṃ bhāryāṃ pūrvavido viduḥ |**

**	sthāṇucchedasya kedāram āhuḥ śalyavato mṛgam || 9.44 ||**

ataś ca pūrvaparigṛhītuḥ kṣetriṇaḥ kṣetram | yasya tat kṣetraṃ tasya ca kṣetraphalaṃ vijñeyam, na bījinaḥ | tathā cāgamaḥ || 9.44 ||

	**etāvān eva puruṣo yajjāyātmā prajeti ha |**

**	viprāḥ prāhus tathā caitad yo bhartā sā smṛtāṅganā || 9.45 ||**

yataś caitad evam |

	**na niṣkrayavisargābhyāṃ bhartur bhāryā vimucyate |**

**	etad dharmaṃ vijānīmaḥ prāk prajāpatinirmitam || 9.46 ||**

etad darśayaty anena na parastrī kenacit krayeṇa pratigraheṇa vātmīyā dharmataḥ śakyā kartum | yato 'sya bījanāśaḥ parasyāvaśyaṃbhāvī kṣetraprādhānyāt | tathā ca loke || 9.46 ||

	**sakṛd aṃśo nipatati sakṛt kanyā pradīyate |**

**	sakṛd āha dadānīti trīṇy etāni satāṃ sakṛt || 9.47 ||**

kanyāto anyad api deyadravyaṃ dātā pratigrahītre | evaṃ ca sati **trīṇy etāni satāṃ sakṛt** | ataś ca sa punardānāsaṃbhavas tasyāḥ | tathā ca na bījaprādhānyaṃ paraparigrītāyām | katham || 9.47 ||

	**yathā go'śvoṣṭradāsīṣu tv ajāvimahiṣīṣu ca |**

**	notpādakaḥ prajābhāgī tathaivānyāṅganāsv api || 9.48 ||**

evam,

	**te 'kṣetriṇo bījavantaḥ parakṣetrapravāpiṇaḥ |**

**	te vai sasyasya jātasya na labhante phalaṃ kvacit || 9.49 ||**

**	yad anyagoṣu vṛṣabho vatsānāṃ janayec chatam |**

**	gominām eva te sarve moghaṃ vṛṣabhaceṣṭitam || 9.50 ||**

**	yathā cākṣetriṇo bījaṃ parakṣetrapravāpiṇaḥ |**

**	karoti kṣetriṇām arthaṃ na bījī labate phalam || 9.51 ||**

prakṛtasyārthasya sarva ete dṛṣṭāntaślokāḥ prarūpaṇāya | evaṃ yonibalīyastvāt parakṣetrajātā na bījino bhavantīti || 9.49–51 ||

	**phalaṃ tva anabhisaṃdhāya kṣetriṇāṃ bījināṃ tathā |**

**	pratyakṣaṃ kṣetriṇām artho bījā yonir balīyasī || 9.52 ||**

evaṃ ca sati **phalaṃ tv anabhisaṃdhāyeti** vacanāt |

	**kriyābhyupagamāt tv eva bījārthaṃ yat prakīryate |**

**	tasyeha bhāginau dṛṣṭau bījī kṣetrika eva ca || 9.53 ||**

evaṃ ca saṃvidā bījī phalaṃ labhate, nānyathā | ayaṃ ca saṃvidā karaṇena tṛtīyaḥ pakṣo vijñeyaḥ | yatra tv evam ubhayoḥ saṃvin nāsti tatra || 9.53 ||

	**oghavātāhṛtaṃ bījaṃ yasya kṣetre prarohati |**

**	taj jñeyaṃ kṣetrikasyaiva na vaptā labhate phalam || 9.54 ||**

oghavātagrahaṇaṃ ca pradarśanārthaṃ vijñeyam | ataś ca yaś cauryād balād vā pārakṣetravāpī na tasyāsti bhāga iti gamyate || 9.54 ||

	**eṣa dharmo gavāśvasya dāsyuṣṭrājāvikasya ca |**

**	vihaṅgamahiṣānāṃ ca vijñeyaḥ prasavaṃ prati || 9.55 ||**

gardabhasyānanukrāntasyāpi paśusāmānyād ayam eva dharmaḥ syāt || 9.55 ||

	**etad vaḥ sāraphalgutvaṃ bījayonyoḥ prakīrtitam |**

**	ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi yoṣitāṃ dharmam āpadi || 9.56 ||**

upasaṃhāropanyāsārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 9.56 ||

	**bhrātur jyeṣṭhasya yā bhāryā gurupatnyanujasya sā |**

**	yavīyasas tu yā bhāryā snuṣā jyeṣṭhasya sā smṛtā || 9.57 ||**

etasyāṃ ca vyavasthāyāṃ satyām |

	**jyeṣṭho yavīyaso bhāryāṃ yavīyān vāgrajastriyam |**

**	patitau bhavato gatvā niyuktāv apy anāpadi || 9.58 ||**

āpadupagamastutyarthaṃ ślokadvayam | **niyuktāv apy anpadīti** vacanād evam āpady apy aniyuktau patitau bhavataḥ | evaṃ ca sati jyeṣṭhena kaniṣṭhena vā niyuktena ca gurubhir āpadi copagamaḥ pratipādanīyaḥ || 9.58 ||

idānīm āpad ucyate |

	**devarād vā sapiṇḍād vā striyā samyaṅ niyuktayā|**

**	prajepsitādhigantavyā santānasya parikṣaye || 9.59 ||**

evaṃ ca sati jyeṣṭhakaniṣṭhāv ubhāv api **devara**śabdena [vijñeyau | ata eva tayor aviśe]ṣāpekṣo niyoga iti gamyate | tathā ca vakṣyati: "nijo vindeta devaraḥ" iti | āpat santānābhāvo 'nutpannāpatyatayā mṛtapu[tratvena vā | anye tu varṇay]anti: "paśyec cej jīvato mukham" iti vacanāt, janmanaiva kṛto 'nena santatyartha iti | tad ayuktam, śāstravirodhāt | evaṃ hi śrūyate: "tasmāt putram anuśiṣṭaṃ [tallokyam āhus tasmād enam anuśāsati]" iti vājasaneyināṃ saṃpratividhāv etad rahasyabrāhmaṇam | tathā ca smṛtyantaram: "satputraśiṣyās trāyante" iti | evaṃ ca mṛtaputrasyāpi niyogaḥ | tathā cāviśeṣaśāstram idaṃ **santānasya parikṣaya** iti | yathānutpannaputrasya santānaparikṣayaḥ evaṃ vinaṣṭasyāpīty ayam ucyate | yataḥ kālasāmānyād ukta ubhayatrāpi niyogaḥ | evaṃ ca sati "dvitīyam eke prajanam" ity etad yuktarūpaṃ bhavati | idānīm upagamavidhir ayam ucyate || 9.59 ||

	**vidhavāyāṃ niyuktas tu ghṛtākto vāgyato niśi |**

**	ekam utpādayet putraṃ na dvitīyaṃ kathaṃcana || 9.60 ||**

**vidhavā**grahaṇasya darśanarthatvād avidhavyām api niyogo na [niṣiddha iti] vijñāyate | vakṣyati hi "yady arthitā tu dāraiḥ syāt klībādīnāṃ kathaṃcana" iti | evaṃ ca pāṇḍor avidhavāniyogād evāpatyotpattiḥ smaryate | divā ca pratiṣedhān **niśīty** ayam andhakāropadeśaḥ, tathā ca vyāsopagamaḥ smaryate || 9.60 ||

	**dvitīyam eke prajanaṃ manyante strīṣu tadvidaḥ |**

**	anirvṛttaṃ niyogārthaṃ paśyanto dharmatas tayoḥ || 9.61 ||**

anayoḥ smṛtyor dvitīyaputrajananasmṛtir jyāyasī, santānānugrahāt | kāraṇam atra gṛhyata iti ced ubhayatra kāraṇagrahaṇād apravṛttir evaṃ sati syāt || 9.61 ||

	**vidhavāyāṃ niyogārthe nivṛtte tu yathāvidhi |**

**	guruvac ca snuṣāvac ca varteyātāṃ parasparam || 9.62 ||**

etasmāc ca jyeṣṭhaniyogo vijñāyate | tathā ca paribhāṣoktā: "jyeṣṭho yavīyaso bhāryām" iti | ubhayoś ca devaraśabdena grahaṇaṃ yuktam "devarād vā sapiṇḍād vā" ity atra | asya pratiṣedhavidher arthavādaḥ || 9.62 ||

	**niyuktau yau vidhiṃ hitvā varteyātāṃ tu kāmataḥ |**

**	tāv ubhau patitau syātāṃ snuṣāgagurutalpagau || 9.63 ||**

vidhavāniyogavidhīnāṃ sarveṣāṃ vyatikramanindārthavādo 'yam aviśeṣād vijñeyaḥ, na kevalam anantaraślokasya niyogārthanirvṛttyuttarakālapratiṣedhasya | eṣa tāvad eva kāraṇād vidhavāniyogaḥ | asya pratiṣedhaḥ || 9.63 ||

	**nānyasmin vidhavā nārī niyoktavyā dvijātibhiḥ |**

**	anyasmin hi nyuñjānā dharmaṃ hanyuḥ sanātanam || 9.64 ||**

	**nodvāhikeṣu mantreṣu niyogaḥ kīrtyate kvacit |**

liṅgato vacanato vā,

	**na vivāhavidhāv uktaṃ vidhavāvedanaṃpunaḥ || 9.65 ||**

**vivāhavidhiḥ** śāstra ity arthaḥ |

	**ayaṃ dvijāir hi vidvadbhiḥ paśudharmo vigarhitaḥ |**

**	manuṣyāṇām api prokto vene rājyaṃ praśāsati || 9.66 ||**

**	sa mahīm akhilāṃ bhuñjan rājarṣipravaraḥ purā |**

**	varṇānāṃ saṃkaraṃ cakre kāmopahatacetanaḥ || 9.67 ||**

**	tadā prabhṛti yo mohāt pramītapatikāṃ striyam |**

**	niyojayaty apatyārthe taṃ vigarhanti sādhavaḥ|| 9.68 ||**

ime niyogapratiṣedhārthāḥ sapurākalpāḥ pañcaślokāḥ | uktapratiṣiddhatvāc ca niyogasya vikalpaḥ | anayos tu smṛtyoḥ katarā jyāsasīti | kiṃ naḥ | etena śakyate tv etad evaṃ vaktum | ubhayatrābhyudayaḥ, yenaikatrāpatyam, anyatra saṃyamaḥ | ubhayaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ saṃskṛtam, yato niyogo 'py abhyudayāya | na hi mṛtasya jīvato vā patyur niyoktuḥ [vā] kācid indriyaprītir asti, nāpi pitrādīnām | vidhānasāmarthāc ca pitrādīnām api yogyābhyudayāyeti gamyate | pratiṣedhopadeśasāmarthāc cāniyoge 'py anatyayaḥ | vidhavāniyogasāmyāc ca tatprakaraṇa evāyaṃ kanyāniyogaḥ śiṣyate || 9.64–68 ||

	**yasyā mriyeta kanyāyā vācā satye kṛte patiḥ |**

**	tām anena vidhānena nijo vindeta devaraḥ || 9.69 ||**

**vidhānaṃ** vidhir vivāho yathoktaḥ, **vindeteti** vacanāt | itarathā hy anūḍhām upagacchataḥ kanyādūṣaṇam upapataṃ syāt | niymārthaś caivam ārambhaḥ | etasmād eva ca liṅgāt prāg vivāhāt vākpradānam asti, yasmin nirvṛtte mṛte bhartari sānyasmai dīyeta || 9.69 ||

	**yathāvidhyadhigamyaināṃ śuklavastrāṃ śucivratām |**

**	mitho bhajetāprasavāt sakṛt sakṛd ṛtāv ṛtau || 9.70 ||**

**yathāvidhyadhigamyaināṃ** vidhivad ūḍhām | **śuklavastrām** iti niyamaḥ | **śucivratāṃ** manovāgādisaṃyatām | **mitho bhajetāprasavāt sakṛt sakṛd ṛtāv ṛtau** | kāyasāmānyād vidhavāniyoge 'py evam eva syāt | pūrvaṃ ca ghṛtā[ktatvādi yad uktaṃ] tad iha sarvaṃ syāt, samānatvān niyogasya || 9.70 ||

	**na datvā kasyacit kanyāṃ [punar dadyād vicakṣaṇaḥ |**

**	datvā punaḥ] prayacchan hi prāpnoti puruṣānṛtam || 9.71 ||**

"sahasraṃ puruṣānṛtam" iti | datvānyasya kasyacid dānāśaṅkayā pratiṣedhānuvādo 'yam || 9.71 ||

	**vidhivat pratihṛtyāpi tyajet kanyāṃ vigarhitām |**

**	vyādhitāṃ vi[praduṣṭāṃ vā chadmanā copapāditām || 9.72 ||**

pratigṛ]hītāpi saty eva nimitte tyājā (?) nānyatra "niṣkrayavisargābhyām" iti vacanāt | ato 'syāḥ tyāganimittair vinā yathākāmaṃ na tyāgo 'sti, yathocchiṣṭadravyāṇām || 9.72 ||

	**yas tu doṣavatīṃ kanyā[m anākhyāyopapādayet |**

**	tasya tad vitathaṃ kuryā]t kanyādānaṃ durātmanaḥ || 9.73 ||**

chadmanopapāditā tyājyetyasyāyam anuvādaḥ kāraṇatas tyāge dośā(?)bhāvapradarśanārtham || 9.73 ||

	**vidhāya vṛttiṃ bhāryāyāḥpravaset kāryavā[n naraḥ |**

**	avṛttikarṣitā hi strī praduṣyet sthitimaty api] || 9.74 ||**

kāryārthaṃ niyamena grāsācchādanapravidhānaṃ kuryād bhāryāyāḥ | asya niyamavidher arthavāda uttaraḥ ślokārdhaḥ | kāryavataś ca manuṣyasya pravāsopadeśād vinā kāryeṇa bhāryāṃ muktvānyatra gamanaṃ pratiṣedhati || 9.74 ||

	**vidhāya proṣite vṛttiṃ jīven niyamam āsthitā |**

**	proṣite tv avidhāyaiva jīvec chilpair agarhitaiḥ || 9.75 ||**

etasyām avasthāyām agarhitaśilpajīvanam abhyanujñāyate tasyā jālikādikaraṇam | etena vidhavāyā ajātaputrāyā vṛttyupāyo vyākhyātaḥ | **garhitaṃ** ca vastranirṇejanādi | pravāsaprayojanaviśeṣeṇa tadājīvanāpekṣayā kālavikalpam idānīṃ darśayati || 9.75 ||

	**proṣito dharmakāryārthaṃ pratīkṣyo 'ṣṭau naraḥ samāḥ |**

**	vidyārthaṃ ṣaḍ yaśo 'rthaṃ vā kāmārthaṃ trīṃs tu vatsarān || 9.76 ||**

agarhitenājīved iti | avidhāyety adhikārāt | tasyā evāyaṃ kālaniyamaḥ, agarhitaśilpajīvanena | ūrdhvaṃ tu kālād etasmād garhitenāpi jīvec chilpena | evaṃ ca viruddhaśilpapratiprasavo 'yaṃ vijñeyaḥ | **dharmakāryaṃ** guruvacanādi | **kāmārthaṃ** rūpājīvanānugamaḥ | na tu vyabhicāraḥ, **pratīkṣyo 'ṣṭau naraḥ samāḥ** ity evamādivacanād, yena śāstraviruddhas tāsāṃ vyatikramaḥ, atyantaṃ saṃyamopadeśāt | tathā ca sati vidhavāniyoga eva tāvat kathaṃcil labdhaḥ, kuta eva vyabhicāraḥ | anyas tv āha: ata ūrdhvaṃ vyabhicāradoṣābhāvaḥ, pratiprasavasāmarthyāt | na tu niyamena vyabhicāropadeśaḥ | na hi proṣite 'nyoḍhāyogo 'sti yato guruniyuktāpatyārthaṃ pravartate | evaṃ ca saty atyantam ajīvantyāḥ prāṇavṛttimātrārtho rahasijanyo vā vyabhicāramātrapratiprasavo 'yaṃ vijñeyaḥ | "yā patyā vā parityaktā" ity evaṃ parityāgopāyajanyapaunarbhavaviṣayaḥ | tat tv etad atyantaśāstravirodhād ayuktam | apare tv idaṃ manuṣyāṇām eva pravāsakālaniyamārthaṃ varṇayanti | ataḥ paraṃ proṣitasyāvasthāne dharmārtham api pratyavāyaḥ syād iti | yo 'yam anyārthe vākye sāmarthyagamyo 'rthaḥ, na tu śabdārthatayā śakyaḥ kalpayitum || 9.76 ||

	**saṃvatsaram udīkṣeta dviṣāṇāṃ yoṣitaṃ patiḥ |**

**	ūrdhvaṃ saṃvatsarāt tv enāṃ dāyaṃ hṛtvā na saṃvaset || 9.77 ||**

na saṃvased ity upagamanivṛttiḥ na nirvāsanam | pātake 'pi tasyāḥ [tan na] yuktaṃ "nirundhyād ekaveśmani" iti tatra prāyaścittopadeśāt | anyas tu tyāgam evāha | evaṃ ca sati tyajato nātidoṣaḥ kāraṇopadeśāt | na tv anyatra | sarvaś ca strītyāgaḥ prāg agnyādheyāt vijñeyaḥ, nottaratra, tayā sārdham asya prajākarmasahatvopadeśād iti kaścit || 9.77 ||

	**mattaṃ yā vā pramattaṃ vā rogartaṃ vātivartate |**

**	sā trimāsān parityājyā vibhūṣaṇaparicchadā || 9.78 ||**

atrāsaṃbhogas tyāgaḥ, na hi nirvāsanam || 9.78 ||

	**unmattaṃ patitaṃ vyaṅgam abījaṃ pāparogiṇam |**

**	na tyāgo 'sti dviṣāṇāyā na ca dāyāpavartanam || 9.79 ||**

atra nimitte 'tyāga eva tasyāḥ || 9.79 ||

	**madyapāsatyavṛttā ca pratikūlā ca yā bhavet |**

**	vyādhitā vādhivettavyā hiṃsrārthaghnī ca sarvadā || 9.80 ||**

atra kaścid āha: saty api jātyarthāviśeṣe "devānām aśnatā haviḥ" iti liṅgāt puṃsa eva brāhmaṇasya surāpānapratiṣedho niyamana gamyate, brāhmaṇyās tu kxatriyavaiśyavad apratiṣedhas talliṅgād vijñāyate | tathā ca tadvadhe kṣatriyavaiśyavadhaprāyaścittam upapātakaṃ vakṣyati | upasparśane ca śūdrasāmyam | strīśūdrocchiṣṭabhakṣaṇe ca | smṛtyantare ca parisaṃkhyātaṃ tāsāṃ pātakam | "brūṇahani hīnavarṇasevāyāṃ ca strī patati" | śrutau ca śatakumbhāsurāsaṃpradānaṃ vihitam | strīśrāddhe viśeṣaḥ | "prati[ṣi]ddhāpi ced yā tu madyam abhyudayeṣv api" iti vacanān madyapānaṃ sarvastrīṇāṃ pratiṣiddham, na tu viśiṣṭasurāyāḥ | dvijātistrīṇāṃ kṣatriyavaiśyavat | evaṃ ca sati niyamapakṣamātrāyāḥ svayaṃ guruvacanena [vā pratiṣiddhāyā madyapāne 'dh]ivedanaṃ tasyā veditavyam iti | tad ayuktam | "pataty ardhaṃ śarīrasya yasya bhāryā surāṃ pibet" ityādismṛtyantaradarśanāt | "devānām aśnatā haviḥ" ity asyārthavādārthatvāc ca | brāhma[ṇyāpi] surāpānaṃ na kartavyam iti | adhivedanaṃ nāma tad upary anyā[vi]vāhaḥ | eteṣv api ca nimitteṣu dharmahānau; na niyamenādhivedanam; tatra hi prāyaścittair ardha[pāpa]hāniḥ tāsāṃ [śakyatvāt] ṛjūkartum || 9.80 ||

	**vandhyāṣṭame 'dhivedyābde daśame tu mṛtaprajā |**

**	ekādaśe strījananī sadyas tv apriyavādinī || 9.81 ||**

dharmahānau satyām | etad āsām adhivedananiyamato vijñeyam, yena jātaputrasyādhikāraḥ śrauteṣu | apriyavādinyās tv anityam adhivedanam, jātaputratve sati tayā sahādhikṛtatvāt karmasu || 9.81 ||

	**yārogiṇī syāt tu hitā saṃpannā caiva śīlataḥ |**

**	sānujñāpyādhivettavyā navamānyā hi karhicit || 9.82 ||**

asyāś cāvamānapratiṣedhād itarā na kevalam adhivedyāḥ, kiṃ tarhi śiṣṭyartham paribhāṣyāś ca || 9.82 ||

	**adhivinnā tu yā nārī nirgacched ruṣitā gṛhāt |**

**	sā sadyaḥ saṃniroddhavyā tyājyā vā kulasaṃnidhau || 9.83 ||**

ukteṣu nimitteṣv adhivinnāyā nirgatāyāḥ krodhena, tyāgaḥ śrutikarmādhikārāvirodhe **kulasaṃnidhau**, asaṃbhogo vā tyāgaḥ saṃnirodho vā tasyāḥ | apare tu prajākarmasahatvanivṛttyartham idaṃ tyāgavacanaṃ kathayanti śrautakarmāvirodhena || 9.83 ||

	**pratiṣiddhāpi ced yā tu madyam abhyudayeṣv api |**

**	prekṣāsamājaṃ gacched vā sā daṇḍyā kṛṣṇalāni ṣaṭ || 9.84 ||**

pratiṣedho madyapānasya na prekṣāsamājagamane | atha vā prasaṅganivṛttyartham | evaṃ ca sati daṇḍasyālpatvād apratiṣedhe 'sty anujñāleśo 'bhyudayādinā nimittena | tac ca madyam asurā dvijātistrīṇāṃ vijñeyam | tathā ca sati pūrvatrāpy adhivedananimittena madyapāna eṣaiva vyākhyā "madyapāsatyavṛttā ca" ity atra | itaravarṇaviṣayaṃ caitatpratiṣedharūpaṃ vijñeyam || 9.84 ||

	**yadi svāś cāparāś caiva vinderan yoṣito dvijāḥ |**

**	tāsāṃ varṇakrameṇa syāj jaiṣṭhyaṃ pūjā ca veśmani || 9.85 ||**

"imāḥ syuḥ kramaśo 'parāḥ" ity etatkrameṇaiva dārakarmoktam | iha tūtsṛjyeti krameṇādyūḍhānāṃ varṇakrameṇaiva jyaiṣṭhyādi syāt | prayojanam asya dāyavibhāgaḥ | pūjā caitenaiva ca savarṇānām anukrameṇaiva jyaiṣṭhyaṃ vijñeyam, na tu janmanā || 9.85 ||

	**bhartuḥ śarīraśuśrūṣāṃ dharmakāryaṃ na naityakam |**

**	svā svaiva kuryāt sarveṣāṃ nāsvajātiḥ kathaṃcana || 9.86 ||**

agniśaraṇopalepanādi**dharmakāryaṃ** yat striyā kartavyaṃ tad gṛhyate | puruṣasyāpi dharmakāryapravṛttasyaivopasparśanadānādilakṣaṇā **śarīraśuśrūṣā** dharmakāryasāhacaryād gṛhyate | na tu pādanirṇejanādisvarūpā, dharmakāryeṇāsarūpatvāt || 9.86 ||

	**yas tu tat kārayen mohāt svajātyā sthitayānyayā |**

**	yathā brāhmaṇacaṇḍālaḥ pūrvadṛṣṭas tathaiva saḥ || 9.87 ||**

śuśrūṣāniyamārthavādo 'yam | evaṃ ca sati nānyayā kāryaḥ | yas tu vyatikrame vartate tasyāyam nindārthavādaḥ kenacit sāmānyena || 9.87 ||

	**utkṛṣṭāyābhirūpāya varāya sadṛśāya vā |**

**	aprāptām api tāṃ tasmai kanyāṃ dadyād yathāvidhi || 9.88 ||**

ātmano vidyādibhir utkṛṣṭakāraṇair **utkṛṣṭāyābhirūpāya varāya** tadabhāve **sadṛśāya vā** | ṛjv anyat | "uttamair uttamair nityaṃ saṃbandhān ācaret" ity atroktam apy etat sadṛśadānārthaṃ punar ārabhyate | evaṃ ca guṇahīne dadataḥ pratyavāyaḥ | tathā cedam anūdyate || 9.88 ||

	**kāmam ā maraṇāt tiṣṭhed gṛhe kanyartumaty api |**

**	na caivaināṃ prayacchet tu guṇahīnāya karhicit || 9.89 ||**

anena cāprāptakāladānena parasyāprāptakālasya kanyāpratigraho 'numīyate | yena prāpnoty aprāptāṃ na pratigrahīṣyati | arthagṛhītatvāc ca prāptakālasaṃyogasyāprāpte kāle dānakīrtanaṃ nārthavādikriyate || 9.89 ||

	**trīṇi varṣāṇy upāsīta kumāry ṛtumatī satī |**

**	[ūrdhvaṃ tu kālā]d etasmād vindeta sadṛśaṃ patim || 9.90 ||**

kanyāyā ayam upadeśaḥ | sā ca dvādaśavarṣartuṃ paśyatīti smaryate | yata etasmāt kālād ūrdhvaṃ varṣatrayaṃ svayaṃvarāt grahaṇaṃ tasyāḥ | ūrdhvaṃ tu || 9.90 ||

	**adīyamānā bhartāram adhigacched yadi svayam |**

**	nainaḥ kiṃcid avāpnoti na ca yaṃ sādhigacchati || 9.91 ||**

yaṃ varaṃ svayaṃ kanyādhigacchati tasyādoṣārthaṃ kanyāyā adoṣavacanam || 9.91 ||

	**alaṃkāraṃ nādadīta pitryaṃ kanyā [svayaṃvarā |**

**	mātṛkaṃ bhrā]tṛdattaṃ vā steyaṃ syād yad idaṃ haret || 9.92 ||**

anye tv evam imaṃ ślokaṃ paṭhanti: "nādadīta tv alaṃkāraṃ pitryaṃ kanyāsvayaṃvare, mātṛkaṃ bhrātṛdattaṃ vā stenaḥ syād yadi taṃ haret" | evaṃ cāpāṭhe puruṣaviṣayaḥ sloko bhavati || 9.92 ||

	**pitre na dadyāc chulkaṃ tu kanyām ṛtumatīṃ haran |**

**	sa ca svāmyād atikrāmed ṛtūnāṃ pratirodhanāt || 9.93 ||**

smṛtyantareṣv ayaṃ śloko na tv atra samāmnāyate || 9.93 ||

	**triṃśadvarṣodvahet kanyāṃ hṛdyāṃ dvādaśavarṣikīm |**

**	tryaṣṭavarṣo 'ṣṭavarṣāṃ vā dharma sīdati satvaraḥ || 9.94 ||**

guruṇānumat iyatā kālena yavīyasīm udvahet kanyām || 9.94 ||

	**devadattāṃ patir bhāryāṃ vindate necchayātmanaḥ |**

**	tāṃ sādhvīṃ bibhṛyān nityaṃ devānāṃ priyam ācaret || 9.95 ||**

svaprayatnād ṛte pitropanītā devadattā bhavati, svavyāpārapāptā vā | upadeśaprayojanaṃ tāṃ sādhvīṃ dviṣatīm api dveṣyāṃ ca satīṃ bibhṛyāt | yenedṛśyā sahadharmacāriṇyā yajamānena haviḥ prattaṃ devatābhiḥ pratigṛhyate | prasavaśuddhā ca sā devapitṛmauṣyāṇām anṛṇye hi nimittam bhavati | yatas tām īdṛśīṃ dveṣyatādibhir api kāraṇair na parityajet | yena || 9.95 ||

	**prajanārthaṃ striyaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ santānārthaṃ ca mānavāḥ | **

**	tasmāt sādhāraṇo dharmaḥ śrutau patnyā sahoditaḥ || 9.96 ||**

evam anayoḥ prajāsahatvavat karmasahatvaṃ smaryate | yenātas tāṃ na parityajed adhikārānugrahāya || 9.96 ||

	**kanyāyāṃ dattaśulkāyāṃ mriyeta yadi śulkadaḥ |**

**	devarāya pradātavyā yadi kanyānumanyate || 9.97 ||**

kenacid viśeṣeṇāsya punar ārambhaḥ | evaṃ ca sati "yasyā mriyeta kanyāyā vācā satye kṛte patiḥ" ity uktaṃ tad adattaśulkāyā vidhānaṃ syāt | devaragrahaṇāc ca punaḥ sapiṇḍanivṛttir gamyate | yuktā ca tannivṛttiḥ | sā hi krītatvāt taddravyābhisaṃbandhiny eva devare 'bhyanujñātuṃ yuktā, śulkapaṇyatvāt tasyāḥ || 9.97 ||

	**ādadīta na śūdro 'pi śulkaṃ duhitaraṃ dadan |**

**	śulkaṃ hi gṛhṇan kurute channaṃ duhitṛvikrayam || 9.98 ||**

**na śūdro 'pīti** vacanāt śulkagrahaṇaṃ doṣavad ity etad darśayati | na tu śūdrasya pratiṣedhaḥ || 9.98 ||

	**etat tu na pare cakrur nāpare jātu sādhavaḥ |**

**	yad anyasyābhyanujñāya punar anyasya dīyate || 9.99 ||**

anena dānam anyatra nāsti | prakṛtāpekṣam etat || 9.99 ||

	**nānuśuśruma jātv etat pūrveṣv api hi janmasu |**

**	śulkasaṃjñena mūlyena channaṃ duhitṛvikrayam || 9.100 ||**

evaṃ ca sati śulkadoṣān niyogo 'pi sapiṇḍe nāsti | ato devarābhāvapakṣe niyataḥ prajanavibhāgaḥ || 9.100 ||

	**anyonyasyāvyabhicāro bhaved āmaraṇāntikaḥ |**

**	eṣa dharmaḥ samānena jñeyaḥ strīpuṃsayoḥ subhaḥ || 9.101 ||**

avyabhicāro 'nyopagamaparityāgaḥ striyāḥ | na tu puruṣasya strīvad anyopagamapratiṣedhaḥ | "tasmād ekasya bahvyo jāyā bhavanti naikasyā bahavaḥ saha patayaḥ" iti srutiḥ | striyās tu puruṣāntarasaṃkalpenāpi vyabhicāra ity utaṃ ca | evaṃ sati || 9.101 ||

	**tathā nityaṃ yateyātāṃ strīpuṃsau tu kṛtakriyau |**

**	yathā nāticaretāṃ tau viyuktāv itaretaram || 9.102 ||**

vihitasya strīpuṃdharmasyānekaprakārasyāsmin prakaraṇe tadanuṣṭhānādarārtham idam uktānukīrtanam || 9.102 ||

	**eṣa strīpuṃsayor ukto dharmo vo ratisaṃhitaḥ |**

**	āpady apatyaprāptiś ca dāyadharmaṃ nibodhata || 9.103 ||**

pūrvayoḥ prakaraṇayor upasaṃhāropanyāsavacanam idaṃ śrotṛsaṃbodhanārtham || 9.103 ||

	**ūrdhvaṃ pituś ca mātuś ca sametya bhrātaraḥ saha |**

**	bhajeran paitṛkaṃ riktham anīśās te hi jīvatoḥ || 9.104 ||**

tadanujñātā jīvadpitṛmātṛkā api dharmakāryāpekṣayā bhajerann ity etad arthād āpadyate | tathā ca gautama āha: "jīvati cecchati pitari" iti | mātur api cordhvaṃ tadīyadravyavibhāgaḥ pākṣiko vijñeyo bhaginībhiḥ saha || 9.104 ||

	**jyeṣṭha eva tu gṛhṇīyāt pitryaṃ dhanam aśeṣataḥ |**

**	śeṣās tam upajīveyur yathaiva pitaraṃ tathā || 9.105 ||**

eṣa kāraṇataḥ pākṣiko 'vibhāgo vijñeyaḥ | [yadi tat kāra]ṇaṃ na syāt tadā jyeṣṭhamadhyamakaniṣṭhānāṃ vibhāgam anekaprakāraṃ vakṣyati | jyeṣṭhagrahaṇapakṣe cāyam arthavādo bhavati || 9.105 ||

	**jyeṣṭhena jatamatreṇa putrī bhavati mānavaḥ |**

**	[pitṝṇām anṛṇaś caiva sa tasmāt] sarvam arhati || 9.106 ||**

yataś ca,

	**yasminn ṛṇaṃ saṃnayati yena cānantyam aśnute |**

**	sa eva dharmajaḥ putraḥ kāmajān itarān viduḥ || 9.107 ||**

sa śiṣṭaḥ syāt | avibhāgapakṣe ceyaṃ jyeṣṭhasya kanīyassu vṛttir ucyate || 9.107 ||

	**piteva [pālayet putrāñ jyeṣṭho brātṝn] yavīyasaḥ |**

**	putravac cāpi varteta jyeṣṭhe bhrātari dharmataḥ || 9.108 ||**

yenaivaṃguṇaḥ,

	**jyeṣṭhaḥ kulaṃ vardhayati vināsayati (?) vā punaḥ |**

anevaṃguṇaḥ, tasmāt kāraṇāt |

	**jyeṣṭhaḥ pūjyatamo loke**

ataś cāsau,

		**jyeṣṭhaḥ sadbhir agarhitaḥ || 9.109 ||**

evaṃ ca sati,

	**yo jyeṣṭho jyeṣṭhavṛttiḥ syān māteva sa piteva ca |**

**	ajyeṣṭhavṛttir yas tu syāt sa saṃpūjyas tu bandhuvat || 9.110 ||**

gurukāryanivṛttyartham idaṃ bandhuvacanam | tathā ca sati || 9.110 ||

	**evaṃ saha saseyur vā pṛthag vā dharmakāmyayā |**

**	pṛthag vivardhate dharmas tasmād dharmyā pṛthakkriyā || 9.111 ||**

atra kāraṇam idam ucyate | yadi jyeṣṭho guṇavattayā dharmādhikārārho bhavati, itare cānadhikṛtā asamarthāś ca dharmānuṣṭhāne, ato 'yam avibhāgo draṣṭavyaḥ | yadi tv ajyeṣṭhavṛttir jyeṣṭhaḥ syāt guṇavān api san gato (?) 'samartheṣv api dharmānuṣṭhāne kanīyassu ayam avibhāgo na syāt | uktaṃ hi "yo jyeṣṭho jyeṣṭhavṛttiḥ syāt" iti | tathā "jyeṣṭhavṛttir yas tu syāt" iti ca | evaṃ ca sati dharmānuṣṭhānasamartheṣv adhikārārheṣu kanīyassu daṇḍāpūpikayā pratiṣiddha evāyam avibhāgo draṣṭavyaḥ, saty api jyeṣṭhasya guṇavattve jyeṣṭhavṛttitve ca | tathā coktam "tasmād dharmyā pṛthakkriyā" iti | na ca dharmye vibhāge saty avibhāgo yuktaḥ kāraṇopadeśāt | tathā ca tad uktam eva | etena pitāputravibhāgo vyākhyātaḥ | tulyahetutvāt | na cāyaṃ nāstīti mantavyaḥ "ūrdhvaṃ pitur" vibhāgopadeśāt | yasmād vakṣyati, "na tatsutair bhajet sārdham" iti | tato liṅgāt pitāputrayor vibhāgo vijñeyaḥ | yataś ca sarveṣv adhikārārheṣu dharmānuṣṭhānasamartheṣu ca dharmyā pṛthakkriyā | ata idam ucyate || 9.111 ||

	**jyeṣṭhasya viṃśa uddhāraḥ sarvadravyāc ca yad varam |**

**	tato 'rdhaṃ madhyamasya syāt turīyaṃ tu yavīyasaḥ || 9.112 ||**

**jyeṣṭhasya** viṃśatibhāgaḥ **sarvadravyeṣu ca yad varam** | **madhyamasya** **tato 'rdhaṃ** catvāriṃśad bhāgaḥ | varadravyānantaraś coddhāro madhyamasya | evaṃ caturthas tv aśītibhāgo yavīyasaḥ sarvadravyebhyaś ca hīnaḥ uddhāraḥ | "dravyebhyaś ca varaṃ varam" ity asmin pāṭhe madhyamakaniṣṭhayos tadanurūpaivāṃśakalpanā vijñeyā | evaṃ ca madhyagā uddhṛtya yad anyac chiṣyate tasya samo vibhāgaḥ kāryaḥ | trayāṇāṃ cāyaṃ samaguṇānāṃ vibhāgavidhiḥ, trayāṇām uddhāradarśanāt | ayam aparo vibhāgaḥ || 9.112 ||

	**jyeṣṭhaś caiva kaniṣṭhaś ca saṃharetāṃ yathoditam |**

**	ye 'nye jyeṣṭhakaniṣṭhābhyāṃ teṣāṃ syān madhyagaṃ dhanam || 9.113 ||**

bahuputrasya jyeṣṭhakaniṣṭhayor guṇavator yathoktam uddhṛtya nirguṇānāṃ bahūnām api madhyamānāṃ guṇavato madhyamasya yaś catvāriṃśadbhāga ukto 'nantaraśloke sa bahubhir api ca madhyamair vibhajanīyaḥ | samaguṇānāṃ tu madhyamānāṃ sarveṣām ekaikasya pūrvavac ca[tvā]riṃśad bhāga uddhāryaḥ || 9.113 ||

	**sarveṣāṃ dhanajātānām ādadītāgryam agrajaḥ |**

**	yac ca sātiśayaṃ kiṃcid daśataś cāpnuyād varam || 9.114 ||**

dhanajātād dhanajātād yac chreṣṭhaṃ yac caikam api sātiśayaṃ sarvasmāc ca dhanajātād daśabhāgaḥ | etaj jyeṣṭhasyoddhṛtya pūrvavad anyat samadhā vibhajeran | yatraiva ca jyeṣṭho mahāguṇaḥ itare ca guṇahīnāḥ tatrāyaṃ vidhiḥ sāmarthyād vijñeyaḥ | tathā cottaraśloke caitam arthaṃ sphuṭīkariṣyaty eva | apare tu "daśataś cāpnuyād varān" iti dvitiyā(?)bahuvacanaṃ paṭhanti | gā aśvān vā tathā caitad daśa paśava eva smṛtyantare viśeṣitāḥ "daśakaṃ paśūnāṃ naikaśaphadvipadānām" iti || 9.114 ||

	**uddhāro na daśasv asti saṃ[pannānāṃ sva]karmasu |**

**	yat kiṃcid eva deyaṃ tu jyāyase mānavardhanam || 9.115 ||**

pūrvaśloke ya uddhāro jyeṣṭhasyoktaḥ sa nivartyate | **uddhāro daśasv** api paśuṣu **nāsti** jyeṣṭhasya, prāg evānyatra yatho[ktadhanajātādiṣu | yan]nimittenāyaṃ jyeṣṭhāṃśāpavādas taṃ darśayati | **saṃpannānāṃ svakarmasu** tadbhrātṝṇām | evaṃ vaiṣām adhyayanavijñāne karmasaṃpadvacanād arthagṛhīte | etad api [jñeyam] | **yat kiṃcid eva deyaṃ tu jyāyase mānavardhanaṃ** noddhāraḥ pūrvaḥ | tathā ca samaguṇeṣu bhrātṛṣv ayaṃ vibhāgo vijñeyaḥ | uddhāragrahaṇapakṣe cedam ucyate || 9.115 ||

	**evaṃ samuddhṛtoddhāre samān aṃśān prakalpayet |**

**	uddhāre 'nuddhṛte tv eṣām iyaṃ syād aṃśakalpanā || 9.116 ||**

evaṃ yathoktanyāyāvirodhenoddhṛtya śiṣṭasya samo vibhāgaḥ || 9.116 ||

	**ekādhikaṃ harej jyeṣṭhaḥ putrao 'dhyardhaṃ tato 'nujaḥ |**

**	aṃśam aṃśaṃ yavīyāṃsa iti dharmo vyavasthitaḥ || 9.117 ||**

guṇādhike jyeṣṭhe īṣadprakṛṣṭaguṇe ca tadanantaraje tadavareṣu ca tābhyāṃ nikṛṣṭaguṇeṣu sameṣu vāyaṃ vibhāgaḥ sāmarthyād vijñāyate | "sametya bhrātaraḥ saha" iti vacanāt pratiṣiddhaṃ bhaginībhyaḥ pitryadhanāṃśadānam | iṣyate ca tāsām anūḍhatayā nimittena tatprāptiḥ | yata idaṃ tadapavādārtham ārabhyate || 9.117 ||

	**svebhyo 'ṃśebhyas tu kanyābhyaḥ pradadyur bhrātaraḥ pṛthak |**

**	svāt svād aṃśāc caturbhāgaṃ patitāḥ syur aditsavaḥ || 9.118 ||**

anūḍhānāṃ bhaginīnāṃ niyamena dānam idam ucyate, sāntānikādidānavat | "patitāḥ syur aditsavaḥ" iti vacanāt | etac ca svāṃśato na samudāyataḥ | udvāhamātraprayojanaṃ deyaṃ svadharmānuparodhena, na caturbhāgo yathāśrutaḥ | evaṃ hi bahubhrātṛkāṇām alpatvāc ca kanyānāṃ dhanaṃ bahutaram āpadyeta, dvyekayoś ca bhrātror bahvīnāṃ bhaginīnāṃ dāne nirdhanatvaṃ prasajyeta | na caitad iṣṭam, "dharmyā pṛthakriyā" iti vacanāt | atha vā "pradadyur bhrātaraḥ pṛthak" ity atra ślokapade **pṛthag**vacanāt bhinnamātṛkā evaite sodaryābhyo bhaginībhyaḥ pūrvavad dadyur iti || 9.118 ||

	**ajāvikaṃ caikaśaphaṃ na jātu viṣamaṃ bhajet |**

**	ajāvikaṃ tu viṣamaṃ jyeṣṭhasyaiva vidhīyate || 9.119 ||**

ajāvikaṃ tu vibhāgakāle yadi viamasaṃkhyayā vibhaktum aśakyaṃ taj jeṣṭhasyaiva syāt | na tad anyasya dravyāṃśapātena samatāṃ nayet, virīya vā tanmūlyaṃ khaṇḍayet || 9.119 ||

	**yavīyāñ jyeṣṭhabhāryāyāṃ putram utpādayed yadi |**

**	samas tatra vibhāgaḥ syād iti dharmo vyavasthitaḥ || 9.120 ||**

jyeṣṭhāṃśāpavādārtho 'yam ārambhaḥ | evaṃ ca jyeṣṭhāpatyatayā tadaṃśādhiko bhāgo na syāt, guṇavato 'pi kanīyasotpannatvāt kṣetrajatvāc ca | nāpy ardhāṃśaḥ, kiṃ tarhi "samas tatra vibhāgaḥ syāt" | kena, pitṛvyena pituḥ kanīyasotpādakeneti | ayaṃ ca niyuktāsutaḥ kṣetrajo vijñeyaḥ | aniyuktāsutasya tv anaṃśārhatvam eva vakṣyate | jyeṣṭhaputrasya tu guṇavataḥ pitur iva soddhāro dhaṇāṃśa ity etad api ca sāmarthyād gamyate || 9.120 ||

	**upasarjanaṃ pradhānasya dharmato nopapadyate |**

**	pitā pradhānaḥ prajane tasmād dharmeṇa taṃ bhajet || 9.121 ||**

ayaṃ pūrvaślokārthavādaḥ | **upasarjanam** apradhānaṃ pituḥ kanīyān bhrātā kṣetrajasyotpādayitā, yasmād ataḥ **pradhānasya** jyeṣṭhasya bhrātuḥ samāṃśam ity etad **dharmataḥ** śāstrato **nopapadyate** | tathā coktaṃ jyeṣṭhasyāṃśadānam | evaṃ ca sati **pitā pradhāno** 'patya**prajane** | tathā ca vakṣaty aurasaprādhānyam, na cāyaṃ kṣetrajaḥ pitrā jātaḥ | **tasmād darmeṇa taṃ bhajet**: dharma pūrvaślokaśāstram, "samas tatra vibhāgaḥ syāt" ity etat | kecid "ardhena taṃ bhajet" iti paṭhanti | tad ayuktam, pūrvoktavyāghātaprasaṅgāt | na cātra vikalpo yuktaḥ, avidhitvād asya | avidhitvaṃ ca pūrvaślokārthavādatvād iti | atha **vopasarjanaṃ** kṣetrajaḥ **pradhāna**syaurasasy samāṃśa iti etad **dharmato nopapadyate** | tathā ca vakṣyati "eka evaurasaḥ putraḥ pitryasya vasunaḥ prabhuḥ" iti | yataś ca **pitā pradhānaḥ prajane** na cāyaṃ tena jātaḥ, tasmād asya samāṃśataiva yuktā | pūrvaśāstra [samaṃ] pitṛdānaṃ tataḥ | atha **vopasarjanaṃ** kṣetrajaḥ **pradhānasya** kṣetriṇaḥ samāṃśam ity etad **dharmato nopapadyata** iti | anyat samānam || 9.121 ||

	**putraḥ kaniṣṭho jyeṣṭhāyāṃ kaniṣṭhāyāṃ ca pūrvajaḥ |**

**	[kathaṃ tatra vibhāgaḥ syā]d iti cet saṃśayo bhavet || 9.122 ||**

kiṃ mātur udvāhakrameṇa jyaiṣṭhyam utāpatyajanmakrameṇety evaṃ [saṃśaya], ayaṃ nirṇayakramo vidhīyate || 9.122 ||

	**ekaṃ vṛṣabham uddhāraṃ [saṃhareta sa pūrvajaḥ |**

**	tato 'pare 'jyeṣṭhavṛ]ṣās tadūnānāṃ svamātṛtaḥ || 9.123 ||**

pūrvasyāṃ jātaḥ **pūrvajaḥ** kanīyān ucyate na pūrvajātaḥ | evaṃ ca saty etad atra samañjasaṃ jyeṣṭhagrahaṇaṃ bhavati | tato 'pi **ajyeṣṭha**[**vṛṣā** ekaśaḥ] **tadūnānām** | tasmād ūnās tadūnāḥ na vyastaḥ, kiṃ tarhi svamātṛtaḥ | tathā ca sati mātṛto jyaiṣṭhyam atra putrāṇām, na janmataḥ|| 9.123 ||

	**jyeṣṭhas tu jāto jyeṣṭhāyāṃ hared vṛṣabhaṣoḍaśam |**

**	tataḥ svamātṛtaḥ śeṣā bhajerann iti dhāraṇā || 9.124 ||**

ṛjvarthaḥ ślokaḥ | etad ekīyamatam, manus tu bhagavān āha || 9.124 ||

	**sadṛśastrīṣu jātānāṃ putrāṇām aviśeṣataḥ |**

**	na mātṛto jyaiṣṭhyam asti janmato jyaiṣṭhyam ucyate || 9.125 ||**

asyārthavādaḥ:

	**janmajyeṣṭhena cāhvānaṃ subrahmaṇyāsv api smṛtam |**

**	yamayoś caikagarbhe 'pi janmato jyeṣṭhatā smṛtā|| 9.126 ||**

ekakālaniṣiktayor api satoḥ | atra kaścit "sadṛśastrī" vacanāt pūrvavidhim asadṛśastrīviṣayaṃ manyate | tad ayuktam, yena viṣamasamīkaraṇam anyāyyam | "sadṛśastrī"grahaṇaṃ cātra vidhyantarasaṃbandhenocyamānaṃ na pūrvavidher asadṛśastrīvixayatvaṃ darśayituṃ samartham | yataś ca vakṣyati, "etad vidhānaṃ vijñeyaṃ vibhāgasyaikayoniṣu, bahvīṣu caikajātānāṃ nnāstrīṣu nobodhata" iti | ataś ced asamañjasaṃ paunaruktyād āpadyate || 9.126 ||

	**aputro 'nena vidhinā sutāṃ kurvīta putrikām |**

**	yad apatyaṃ bhaved asyāṃ tan mama syāt svadhākaram || 9.127 ||**

yathaivaurasābhāve kṣetrajādyabhidhānaṃ dāyavibhāgaprakaraṇe 'ṃśaprāptyarthaṃ tathaiva putrikāputravidhānaṃ vijñeyam | aputrasyaivaitat syāt putrikāputravidhānam | anayā saṃvidā "yad apatyaṃ bhaved asyāṃ tan mama syāt svadhākaram" piṇḍodakapradam ity arthaḥ | asyārthavādaḥ parakṛtirūpa udāhriyate || 9.127 ||

	**anena tu vidhānena purā cakre 'tha putrikāḥ |**

**	vivṛddhyarthaṃ svavaṃśasya svayaṃ dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ || 9.128 ||**

prajāpatir hi prajāvidhijñaḥ | yataḥ sa evodāhṛtaḥ || 9.128 ||

	**dadau sa daśa dharmāya kāśyapāya trayodaśa |**

**	somāya rājñe satkṛtya prītātmā saptaviṃśatim || 9.129 ||**

satkāravacanaṃ ca sarvārthaṃ liṅgam apareṣāṃ putrikākarmaṇi || 9.129 ||

	**yathaivātmā tathā putraḥ putreṇa duhitā samā |**

**	tasyām ātmani tiṣṭhantyāṃ katham anyo dhanaṃ haret || 9.130 ||**

pitari prete saputrā aputrā vā putrikā dhanaṃ haret tadīyam || 9.130 ||

	**mātus tu yautakaṃ yat syāt kumārībhāga eva saḥ |**

**	dauhitra eva tu hared aputrsyākhilaṃ dhanam || 9.131 ||**

asyeśiny eva sā | putrikāputras tv aputre mātāmahe pramīte 'khilaṃ dhanaṃ haret, putrikā vā | yadā putrikāyāṃ kṛtāyāṃ mātāmahasya tu putro jāyate daivāt kathaṃcit, tadā bhrātraṃśasyaiva putrikāputra īśata iti | atha tu putrikā kṛtā tathāpi prāk prayāṇāt ptur na pitū rikthabhāginī || 9.131 ||

	**dauhitro hy akhilaṃ riktham aputrasya hared yadi |**

**	sa eva dadyāt tatpiṇḍaṃ pitre mātāmahāya ca || 9.132 ||**

yasmin pakṣe 'putro mātāmahaḥ putrikāsutaś cākhiladravyahārī, tasmin pakṣe tasya piṇḍadānaniyamaḥ | yadā tu mātāmahaḥ saputraḥ saṃpadyate daivāt putrikāputre sati, tadā putrikāputro 'pi san naiva piṇḍaṃ mātāmahāya dadyāt | hared yadi, yasmin pakṣa ity arthaḥ | tac ca piṇḍadānaṃ pitṛmātāmahayoḥ prathamam | evam uttarayor api dvayor dvayoḥ piṇḍo deyaḥ | yasmāt || 9.132 ||

	**pautradauhitrayor loke na viśeṣo 'sti dharmataḥ |**

kāraṇam atra bravīti, yena:

	**tayor hi mātāpitarau saṃbhūtau tasya dehataḥ || 9.133 ||**

putrikāputrastutiḥ pūrvavidhyarthā || 9.133 ||

	**putrikāyāṃ kṛtāyāṃ tu yadi putro 'nujāyate |**

**	samas tatra vibhāgaḥ syāj jyeṣṭhatā nāsti hi striyāḥ || 9.134 ||**

evaṃ ca sati putrāṃśadānam ajyeṣṭhatvān nāsti || 9.134 ||

	**aputrāyāṃ mṛtāyāṃ tu putrikāyāṃ kathaṃcana |**

**	dhanaṃ tatputrikābhartā haretaivāvicārayan || 9.135 ||**

putrikāyāḥ pitary aputre uparate, taddhane ca sarvasmin putrikayā gṛhīte, yady aputr[ā putrikā mriyeta tadā taddhanaṃ] bhartuḥ syāt | nāsau śvaśurasapiṇḍair jñātibhir vānuyojyaḥ || 9.135 ||

	**akṛtā vā kṛtā vāpi yaṃ vindet sadṛśāt sutam |**

**	pautrī mātāmahas tena dadyāt piṇḍaṃ [hared dhanam || 9.136 ||**

dhanagrahaṇasya piṇḍa]dānanimittatvāt niyamato dhanaharaṇaṃ piṇḍadānaṃ ca | akṛtāyāṃ tu putrikāyāṃ dauhitrasyecchāsaṃniyogaśiṣyaṃ piṇḍadānaṃ dhanaharaṇaṃ ca syāt | yady abhyupa[gamyate vika]lpo niyamo vā bhavat | tataḥ putrikāvidhinārthaḥ syāt | tasmāt kṛtāyāṃ niyamaḥ, anyatra tu vikalpa ity uktam | yad āha | 9.136 ||

	**putreṇa lokañ jayati pautreṇānantyam aśnute |**

**	atha putrasya pautreṇa bradhnasyāpnoti viṣṭapam || 9.137 ||**

dauhitrapraśaṃsārthaḥ ślokaḥ | katham | pautra evāyaṃ dauhitra iti kṛtvā stūyate mṛtasyopakāraviśeṣasaṃbandhena | katham | putriṇo hi pramītāḥ pitṛgaṇāpannāḥ pitṛvat pūjārhāḥ putrapautraprapautrair vidhisāmarthyād upahṛtasya kavyasya pratigrahamātrabhogād ā caturthāt puruṣāt saṃsāram āpannāḥ tatrāsata iti | śāstrasāmarthyād etad gamyate | evaṃ hi putrādibhir lokādīñ jayatīty ayaṃ saṃstava upapadyate | tathā ca nāmadheyanirvacanam atra darśayati || 9.137 ||

	**puṃnāmno narakād yasmāt trāyate pitaraṃ sutaḥ |**

**	tasmāt putra iti proktaḥ svayam eva svayaṃbhuvā || 9.138 ||**

gamyamānasya nāmadheyagatasyārtharūpasyātra pramāṇabhāvo nāmadheyanirvacanena pradarśitaḥ | yataś caitad evam ataḥ kāryasāmānyāt || 9.138 ||

	**pautradauhitrayor loke viśeṣo nopapadyate |**

**	dauhitro 'pi hy amutrainaṃ saṃtārayati pautravat || 9.139 ||**

uktārthopasaṃhārārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 9.139 ||

	**mātuḥ prathamataḥ piṇḍaṃ nirvapet putrikāsutaḥ |**

**	dvitīyaṃ tu pitus tasyās tṛtīyaṃ tu pituḥ pituḥ || 9.140 ||**

"sa eva dadyāt tatpiṇḍaṃ pitre mātāmahāya ca" ity atroktam api sat punar ucyate | kim artham | kathaṃ nāma punaruktiḥ | tatra mātāmahaprakramāt putrikāputradānaṃ mātāmahaprakramaṃ yuktam | tasmād ayam aparaḥ kalpaḥ putrikāputrapiṇḍadānasya **mātuḥ prathamataḥ piṇḍaṃ nirvapet** ity evamādi | anyeṣāṃ tu pāṭho 'rthaś cāsya ślokasa: "mātuḥ prathamataḥ piṇḍaṃ nirvapet putrikāsutaḥ, dvitīyaṃ tu pituḥ svasya" ity evam, arthaś ca mātuḥ prathamaṃ māmasaṃkīrtanaṃ tataḥ pituḥ svasya | tato mātāmahapitāmahayoḥ yatparayoś ceti | tat punar yuktāyuktatayā vicāraṇīyam || 9.140 ||

	**upapanno guṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ putro yasya tu dattrimaḥ |**

**	sa haretaiva tadrikthaṃ saṃprāpto 'py anyagotrataḥ || 9.141 ||**

aputrādhikārād aputrasya sato dattako rikthaṃ haret | pradarśanaṃ cedaṃ kṛtrimādīnāṃ draṣṭavyam | evaṃ ca sarva eva putrapratinidhayo 'viśeṣeṇāputrasya dhanabhājo yuktāḥ | yac ca kānīnādīnāṃ ṣaṇṇām adāy[ād]atvam ucyate pākṣikaṃ tadvijñeyam | yad aurasa uttarakālam utpannaḥ uttarebhyaḥ prajīvanamātraṃ prayacchati tadā kānīnādīnāṃ vikalpena dadātīty evaṃ kānīnādīnām adāyādatvam ucyate || 9.141 ||

	**gotrarikthe janayitur na hared dattrimaḥ sutaḥ |**

**	gotrarikthānugaḥ piṇḍo vyapaiti dadhataḥ svadhā || 9.142 ||**

gotrarikthe piṇḍadānaṃ ca janayitur dattrimo na gṛhṇīyāt | yasmai tu dīyate 'sau tadīye tasya gotrarikthe syātām | piṇḍadānaṃ ca tatsaṃniyogena | yasmād gotrānugaḥ piṇḍaḥ | ata etasmāt kāraṇād **vyapaiti dadhataḥ svadhā** piṇḍadānopalakṣaṇam | **svadhā** sā ca **vyapaiti janayituḥ**, tena tasyānyasmai dattatvāt | anyas tv āha: "gotrarikthe janayitur na hared anyasmai dīyamāno 'pi" | tathā dvyāmuṣyāyaṇo 'sau saṃpadyate | gautamas taṃ viseṣayitvāha: "piṇḍagotrarṣis[aṃbandhā rikthaṃ bhajeran" iti sa eva] gotrarikthe bhajeteti || 9.142 ||

	**aniyuktāsutaś caiva putriṇy āptaś ca devarāt |**

**	ubhau tau nārhato bhāgaṃ jārajātakakāmajau || 9.143 ||**

**aniyuktāsutaś caive**[ti devarāj jāto] jyeṣṭhabhāryāyām ity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca sati niyuktāsutasya tatra samāṃśatvam uktaṃ vijñeyam | **putriṇy āptaś ca devarād** ity etad anapatyāy[ā eva devarotpannasya nānyotpannasya bhāgahara]tvam | devarād api kim, utānyasmād ity "api"śabdalopaḥ sāmarthyād vijñeyaḥ | **devara**grahaṇaṃ cobhayaviśeṣaḥ | asyārthavādaḥ yasmāt tau **jārajāta**[**kakāmajau** iti] kathaṃcin nindeyam ubhayoḥ, yena tannindāvacanam ubhayatra yujyate, avidhinotpannatvād ubhayoḥ || 9.143 ||

	**niyuktāyām api pumān nāryāṃ jāto 'vidhānataḥ |**

**	naivārhaḥ paitṛkaṃ rikthaṃ patitotpādito hi saḥ || 9.144 ||**

**niyuktāyām api** "ghṛtākto vāgyataḥ" iti vacanād vidhyatikramajāto na rikthabhāgaḥ syāt | yena patitena patitābhyāṃ vāsāv utpāditaḥ | ubhayor niyamaśravaṇāt tadvyatikramanindaiṣā veditasyā|| 9.144 ||

	**hared eva niyuktāyāṃ putro jāto yathaurasaḥ |**

**	kṣetrikasya tu tad bījaṃ dharmataḥ prasavaś ca saḥ || 9.145 ||**

**jāto yathaurasa** ity etadguṇavataḥ kṣetrajasya pitryāṃśaprāptyarthaṃ vacanam | evaṃ ca sati pūrvoktāyās samāṃśatāyā ayam apavādaḥ guṇavadapatyatayārambhasāmarthyād vijñeyaḥ | itarathā hi pūrvaślokārthapattisiddhatvād anārabhyam etat syāt | evaṃ cātra stutyarthaṃ praśaṃsāvacanam upapadyate idaṃ **kṣetrikasya tu tadbījaṃ dharmataḥ prasavaś ca saḥ** iti | na cākasmāt praśaṃsāvacanam idaṃ bhavitum arhati | tathā ca || 9.145 ||

	**[dhanaṃ yo bibhṛyād bhrātur mṛtasya striyam eva ca |**

**	so 'patyaṃ bhrātur utpādya dadyāt tasyaiva taddhanam] || 9.146 ||**

daṇḍāpūpikayaurasasya | **bhrātur utpādyeti** niyogādividhyapkeṣitam idaṃ vacanam | apare tv āhuḥ: aniyuktāyām api pitryaṃ dadyād iti | tat tv idaṃ yuktāyuktatvena vicāraṇīyam || 9.146 ||

	**yā niyuktānyataḥ putraṃ devarād vāpy avāpnuyāt |**

**	taṃ kāmajam arikthīyaṃ nithyotpannaṃ pracakṣate || 9.147 ||**

vidhijātāpatyastutir iyam, avidhijātāpatyanindayā, pitṛdhanāṃśaprāptyartham | anyas tv āha: yad uktaṃ "devarād vā sapiṇḍād vā" niyuktāsuto rikthabhāg iti [tasyā]yaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ | uktaniṣiddhatvāc ca vikalpena rikthabhāktvaṃ vijñeyam | guṇopekṣayā cānyataram adhyavasitavyam || 9.147 ||

	**etad vidhānaṃ vijñeyaṃ vibhāgasyaikayoniṣu |**

**	bahvīṣu [caikajātānāṃ nānā]strīṣu nibodhata || 9.148 ||**

vakṣyamāṇaprakaraṇaupanyāsikaḥ ślokaḥ || 9.148 ||

	**brāhmaṇasyānupūrvyeṇa catasras tu yadi striyaḥ |**

**	tāsāṃ putreṣu jāteṣu vibhāge 'yaṃ vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ || 9.149 ||**

**ānupūrvya**grahaṇam [anuvādārtha]m | **yadi**grahaṇaṃ cānityārtham | tathā coktam "kāmatas tu pravṛttānām imāḥ syuḥ kramaśo 'varāḥ" iti || 9.149 ||

	**kīnāśo govṛṣo yānam alaṅkaraś ca veśma ca |**

**	viprasyauddhārikaṃ deyam ekāṃśas ca pradhanataḥ || 9.150 ||**

**kīnāśaḥ** karṣakaḥ | tathā ca mantraḥ "indra āsīt sīrapatiḥ śatakratuḥ, kīnāśā āsan marutas sudānavaḥ" iti | **govṛṣas** sektā gavām | **yānaṃ** gantryādi | **alaṃkāraś ca** pitryāṅgulīyakādi | evaṃ **veśma** | ekaś cāṃśo yaḥ prādhānyena lakṣyate | etad **viprasyoddhārikam** | etad uddhṛtya madhyakāt śiṣṭasyāṃśavibhāgo yena nyāyena so 'yam ucyate || 9.150 ||

	**tryaṃśaṃ dāyād dhared vipro dvāv aṃśau kṣatriyāsutaḥ |**

**	vaiśyājo 'dhyardham evāṃśaṃ śūdrāputro 'rdham eva tu || 9.151 ||**

nigadavyākhyātāṃśaprakḷptiḥ | dvibahuṣv api samasaṃkhyeṣv evaṃ vibhajya paścāt sajātayo vibhajeran pūrvavat | viṣamasaṃkhyeṣu tu śāstraliṅgād utprekṣyāṃśakalpanāḥ || 9.151 ||

	**sarvaṃ vā rikthajātaṃ tad daśadhā parikalpya ca |**

**	dharmyaṃ vibhāgaṃ kurvīta vidhinānena dharmavit || 9.152 ||**

dharmyavacanād atra sarveṣu yathoktakāriṣv ayaṃ vibhāgaḥ | so 'yam ucyate || 9.152 ||

	**caturo 'ṃśān hared vipras trīn aṃśān kṣatriyāsutaḥ |**

**	vaiśyāputro hared dvyaṃśam aṃśaṃ śūdrāsuto haret || 9.153 ||**

ṛjvarthāṃśakalpanā | atrāpi pūrvavat samaviṣamasaṃkhyeṣu vibhāgo vijñeyaḥ || 9.153 ||

	**yady api syāt tu satputro yady aputro 'pi vā bhavet |**

**	nādhikaṃ daśamād dadyāc chūdrāputrāya dharmataḥ || 9.154 ||**

santaḥ putrā [dvijāta]yo yasya so 'yaṃ satputraḥ | yady aputro 'pi vā bhavet tad abhāve kevalaḥ śūdrāputraḥ | evam api nādhikaṃ daśabhāgāt tasmai deyam, anyat sapiṇḍā hareyuḥ | tadabhāve taddhanasya [ta evādhikāriṇaḥ syuḥ] | etasmād eva liṅgat kṣatriyasyātām | itarathā hi śūdrapratiṣedho 'narthakaḥ syāt || 9.154 ||

	**brāhmaṇakṣatriyavi[śāṃ śūdrāputro na rikthabhāk |**

**	yad evā]sya pitā dadyāt tad evāsya dhanaṃ bhavet || 9.155 ||**

pitradhīno 'syāṃśa ity ayam aparaḥ kalpo guṇasaṃbandhāpekṣaḥ pūrvavidheḥ | evaṃ ca sati pūrvottarayor virodhād anayor vikalpo guṇa[saṃbandhāpe]kṣaḥ | atha vā anūḍhāśūdrāputrasyāyaṃ vidhir jñeyaḥ | pūrvas tūḍhāputrasya | tathā ca gautamaḥ śūdraprakaraṇa āhāparigṛhītāsv api "śuśrūṣuś cel labheta vṛttimūlam antevāsividhinā" || 9.155 ||

	**samavarṇāsu vā jātāḥ sarve putrāḥ sujanmanām |**

**	uddhāraṃ jyāyase dattvā bhajerann itare samam || 9.156 ||**

**samavarṇāsu vā jātā** jyāyase mānavardhanaṃ yat kiṃcid **datvā bhajerann itare samam** | hīnajātiguṇavattareṣv ayaṃ vidhiḥ sāmarthyād vijñeyaḥ || 9.156 ||

	**śūdrasya tu savarṇaiva nānyā bhāryā vidhīyate |**

**	tasyāṃ jātāḥ samāṃśāḥ syur yadi putraśataṃ bhavet || 9.157 ||**

śūdrāyāṃ śuddhāyām idam ucyate | anyāsūtkṛṣṭāpakṛṣṭāsu dharmādharmāpekṣeyā (?) vibhāgaḥ kalpayitavyaḥ || 9.157 ||

	**putrān dvādaśa yān āha nṛṇāṃ svāyaṃbhyvo manuḥ |**

**	teṣāṃ ṣaḍ bandhdāyādāḥ ṣaḍ adāyādabāndhavāḥ || 9.158 ||**

dāyavibhāgaprakaraṇāpekṣaḥ putrāṇām ayam upadeśo 'tra | sūtrasthānīyasyedaṃ bhāṣyaṃ tatsvarūpanirdeśārthaṃ bhavati || 9.158 ||

	**aurasaḥ kṣetrajaś caiva dattaḥ kṛtrima eva ca |**

**	gūḍhotpanno 'paviddhaś ca dāyādā bāndhavāś ca ṣaṭ || 9.159 ||**

	**kānīnaś ca sahoḍaś ca krītaḥ paunarbhavas tathā |**

**	svayaṃdattaś ca śaudraś ca ṣaḍ adāyādabāndhavāḥ || 9.160 ||**

kāryārtho 'yaṃ vargapravibhāgaḥ putrāṇām, tac ca vakṣyati | sahopadeśād aurasena sāmyaṃ mā bhūt kṣetrajādīnām iti | ata idam ucyate || 9.159–60 ||

	**yādṛśaṃ guṇam āpnoti kplavaiḥ santaraṃ jalam |**

**	tādṛśaṃ guṇam āpnoti kuputraiḥ santaraṃs tamaḥ || 9.161 ||**

anena liṅgena sarve kṣetrajādayo 'putrasya putrakāryāṇi kuryuḥ, sarve ca dāyaṃ gṛhṇīyuḥ | kānīnādīnām adāyādatvam uktaṃ pākṣikaṃ tad iti vyākhyātam || 9.162 ||

	**yady ekarikthinau syātām aurasakṣetrajau sutau |**

**	yasya yat paitṛkaṃ rikthaṃ sa tad gṛhṇīta netaraḥ || 9.162 ||**

[aura]se sati kṣetrajo bhavtīti sāmarthāt vaktavyam, kṣetraje vā saty aurasa iti | evaṃ ca saty aniyuktāsuta evāyaṃ vijñeyo guṇataḥ | tathā hi [yadā putriṇyāṃ kṣetrajo jāyeta yadā votpādite kṣetraja auraso jāyeta tadā ta]ddhanasya tayor ayaṃ vibhāgaḥ | yad yasya pitryam iti | etena darśanenāniyuktāsutādaya itaratrānaṃśārhatvād bījino 'ṃśaṃ labhante | anyas tv āha yadi jātāpatyo 'tharvaṇapakṣakriyayā punaḥ sarvaṃ kṛtvā putrān utpādayet, tayoś ca bījikṣetriṇor dhanaṃ strīgataṃ syāt, tayor eṣa vibhāgaḥ || 9.162 ||

	**eka evaurasaḥ putraḥ ptryasya vasunaḥ prabhuḥ |**

**	śeṣāṇām ānṛśaṃsyārthaṃ pradadyāt tu prajīvanam || 9.163 ||**

evaṃ kṣetrajādīnām aurase sati paścād utpanne vānaṃśatve prāpte vidhir ayaṃ vikalpārtham ucyate | itarebhyaḥ kṣetrajādibhyaḥ **prajīvana**mātraṃ deyam iti || 9.163 ||

	**ṣaṣṭhaṃ tu kṣetrajasyāṃśaṃ pradadyāt paitṛkād dhanāt |**

**	auraso vibhajan dāyaṃ pitryaṃ pañcamam eva vā || 9.164 ||**
