kṣetrajasya tṛtīyo 'yaṃ vikalpo niyuktāsutasya mukhyatvāt | ṣaṣṭapañcamabhāgavikalpaś ca guṇāpekṣaḥ || 9.164 ||

	**aurasakṣetrajau putrau pitṛrikthasya bhāginau |**

**	daśāpare tu kramaśo gotrarikthāṃśabhāginaḥ || 9.165 ||**

evaṃ ca pūrvasmin pūrvasmin sati uttarottaraḥ rajīvanamātreṇāṃśena yujyate | etasmāc ca yasmāt pūrvasya pūrvasya jyāyastvaṃ gotrabhāktvaṃ ca jñātikāryaṃ ca kānīnādibhir api kāryam | eṣām idānīṃ lakṣaṇam ucyate || 9.165 ||

	**sve kṣetre saṃskṛtāyāṃ tu svayam utpādayed dhi yam |**

**	tam aurasaṃ vijānīyāt putraṃ prātamakalpikam || 9.166 ||**

yā yasya svarṇā sā tasya **kṣetram** | tasyām utpannaḥ **prāthamakalpika auraso** 'pi **vijñeyaḥ** | kṣatriyavaiśyayos tu jātā na saṃpūrṇalakṣaṇā aurasāḥ sutāḥ | atas teṣām [vibhā]go nyāyavirodhena kalpayitavyaḥ | apare tu kṣatriyavaiśyāv evāurasau kṣetrajādibhyo jyāyāṃsau manyante || 9.166 ||

	**yas talpajaḥ pramītasya klībasya vyādhitasya vā |**

**	svadharme[ṇa niyuktāyāṃ sa putraḥ kṣetrajaḥ smṛtaḥ] || 9.167 ||**

nigadavyākhyātaḥ ślokaḥ || 9.167 ||

	**mātā pitā ca dadyātāṃ yam adbhiḥ putram āpadi |**

**	sadṛśaṃ prītisaṃyuktaṃ sa jñeyo dattrimaḥ sutaḥ || 9.168 ||**

ye tu "mātā pitā vā dadyātām" iti paṭhanti [tad ayukta]m ucyate | samastābhyāṃ dānaniyamād anyatarāpāye dattako na grāhyaḥ | "mātā pitā vā" ity asmiṃs tu vikalpapakṣe samastayor dānaniyamo nāsti | **sadṛśaṃ** savarṇam, [jāty]āditaḥ || 9.168 ||

	**sadṛśaṃ tu prakuryād yaṃ guṇadoṣavicakṣaṇam |**

**	putraṃ putraguṇair yuktaṃ sa vijñeyas tu kṛtrimaḥ || 9.169 ||**

kṛtrimo 'pi savarṇa eva pitṛmātṛvihīnaś ca || 9.169 ||

	**utpādyate gṛhe yasya na ca jñāyeta kasya saḥ |**

**	sa gṛhe gūḍham utpannas tasya syād yasya talpajaḥ || 9.170 ||**

avijñātabījino mātṛjātīyo gūḍhotpanno vijñeyaḥ | tathā ca vyāsadarśanam || 9.170 ||

	**mātāpitṛbhyām utsṛṣṭaṃ tayor anyatareṇa vā |**

**	yaṃ putraṃ parigṛhṇīyād apaviddhaḥ sa ucyate || 9.171 ||**

anyatare pramīte 'nyatarotsarga ucyate | itarathā hi mātāpitror jīvator anyatarotsarge 'paviddhatāsya na yuktā | ayam api ca savarṇa eva || 9.171 ||

	**pitṛveśmani kanyā tu yaṃ putraṃ janayed rahaḥ |**

**	taṃ kānīnāṃ vaden nāmnā voḍhuḥ kanyāsamudbhavam || 9.172 ||**

savarṇārthaṃ sadṛśotpannaḥ | apare tu **raha** iti vacanād atr[āpi bī]jino 'vijñānāt kānīnaṃ mātṛjātīyam evāhuḥ || 9.172 ||

	**yā garbhiṇī saṃskriyate jñātājñātāpi vā satī |**

**	voḍhuḥ sa garbho bhavati sahoḍha iti cocyate || 9.173 ||**

ayam api sahoḍho mātṛjātīyaḥ || 9.173 ||

	**krīṇīyād yas tv apatyārthe mātāpitror yam antikāt |**

**	sa krītakaḥ sutas tasya sadṛśo 'sadṛśo 'pi vā || 9.174 ||**

apare tv āhuḥ krītaḥ sadṛśo 'sadṛśo veti guṇataḥ kalpyate | varṇato hi kalpanāyām asamavarṇagrahaṇe nyāyavirodhaḥ | anyas tu brāhmaṇavixayam eva nyāyavirodham āha || 9.174 ||

	**yā patyā vā parityaktā vidhavā svecchayātmanaḥ |**

**	utpādayet punar bhūtvā sa paunarbhava ucyate || 9.175 ||**

savarṇaḥ paunarbavo 'savarṇo 'pi vā, asavarṇas tu guṇataḥ || 9.175 ||

	**sā ced akṣatayoniḥ syād gatapratyāgatāpi vā |**

**	paunarbhavena bhartrā sā punas saṃskāram arhati || 9.176 ||**

pāṇigrahaṇamātreṇa dūṣitā yady api bhartṛgṛhād gatapratyāgatā bhavet akṣatayoni[ḥ punaḥ saṃskāryā || 9.176 ||

	**mā]tāpitṛvihīno yas tyakto vā syād akāraṇe |**

**	ātmānaṃ sparśayed yasmai svayaṃdattas tu sa smṛtaḥ || 9.177 ||**

savarṇa eva syāt, na tathetaraḥ || 9.177 ||

	**yaṃ brāhmaṇas tu śūdrāyāṃ kāmād utpādayet sutam |**

**	sa pārayann eva śavas tasmāt pāraśavaḥ smṛtaḥ || 9.178 ||**

yaḥ śaudra iti prāg abhihitaḥ | **yaṃ brāhmaṇa** iti kṣatriyavaiśyayor api pradarśanārtham | tathā ca pāraśavagrahaṇavān sa **pārayann eva** jīvann eva **śavaḥ** | puruṣārthaprayojanaviśiṣṭakarmaṇānabhisaṃbandhitvāt tasya **pāraśavaḥ smṛtaḥ** || 9.178 ||

	**dāsyāṃ vā dāsadāsyāṃ vā śūdro yasya suto bhavet |**

**	so 'nujñāto hared aṃśam iti dharmo vyavasthitaḥ || 9.179 ||**

śūdraṃ prati pitur anujñāvacanād brāhmaṇādīnāṃ snehād rāgād vā dāyaṃ praty anujñānaṃ nāsti || 9.179 ||

	**kṣetrajādīn sutān etān ekādaśa yathoditān |**

**	putrapratinidhīn āhuḥ kriyālopān manīṣiṇaḥ || 9.180 ||**

ekādaśānām aviśeṣeṇa pratinidhivacanāt kānīnādayo 'pi pūrvair aviśiṣṭāḥ pratīyante | ato yad eṣām adāyādabāndhavatvam uktaṃ prajīvanaviṣaye pākṣikadānārthaṃ tat syād iti vyākhyātam, kiṃ ayaṃ pradhānena viśiṣṭakāryapratinidhiḥ yathā mīmāṃsakā āhur iti | nety ucyate, viṣamasamīkaraṇasyāyuktatvāt | tathā coktam "tādṛśaṃ guṇam āpnoti kuputraiḥ saṃtaraṃs tamaḥ" ity evamādi | tathā cedam āhaiṣām nindāvacanaṃ samānabalatvapratiṣedhārtham || 9.180 ||

	**ya ete 'bhihitāḥ putrāḥ prasaṅgād anyabījajāḥ |**

**	yasya te bījato jātās tasya te netarasya tu || 9.181 ||**

paunarbhavaśaudrau dvau parityajya nava putrā **anyabījajāḥ** ucyante | teṣām aurasenānirastānāṃ bījināṃ sati saṃbhave bhāgitva[m | yeṣāṃ tu] bījī na jñāyeta yathā gūḍhotpannakānīnasahoḍhānāṃ teṣām ubhayatrābhāgitve kevalaṃ prajīvanamātram ebhyo dīyate, tac cānṛśaṃsāvacanāt sarveṣām [abhyanu]jñātam | aurasapraśaṃsārtho 'yaṃ ślokaḥ ity apare, yena kiṃcid api na vidhīyate pratiṣidhyate vā | atha vā pratinidh[eḥ pradh]ānāsamānakāryatvapradarśanārtho 'yaṃ ślokaḥ || 9.181 ||

	**[brātṝṇām e]kajātīnām ekaś cet putravān bhavet |**

**	sarvāṃs tāṃs tena putreṇa putriṇo manur abravīt || 9.182 ||**

sati bhrātṛputra ete pratinidhayaḥ [na] kartavyāḥ ity evaṃparam etat | atha vā [tatputrasya] prathamaṃ dattakādinyāyena pratinidhitvam anena ślokena vijñāyate | alabhyamāne tv asati vā bhrātṛputre 'nye kalpā āśrayaṇīyā iti || 9.182 ||

	**bahvīnām ekapatnīnām ekā cet putriṇī bhavet |**

**	sarvās tās tena putreṇa prāha putravatīr manuḥ || 9.183 ||**

iyaṃ na niyoktavyety etasmād gamyate | na caitayaikākinyā dattakādiputragrahaṇaṃ kāryam || 9.183 ||

	**śeyasaḥ śreyaso 'bhāve pāpīyān riktham arhati |**

**	bahavaś cet tu sadṛśāḥ sarve rikthasya bhāginaḥ || 9.184 ||**

sarvasmin rikthavibhāe bījabhūto 'yaṃ ślokaḥ | evaṃ ca saty asyānurodhena rikthavibhāge 'nāgato 'tikrāntaś ca varṇanīyaḥ || 9.184 ||

	**na bhrātaro na pitaraḥ putrā rikthaharāḥ pituḥ |**

**	pitā hared aputrasya rikthaṃ bhrātara eva ca || 9.185 ||**

ya ete aurasādayaḥputrāḥ prakṛtās ta eva rikthaharāḥ syuḥ | kṣetrajādayo 'py aurasāsaṃbhave | kuta etat | prakaraṇasāmarthyāt saty api saṃnikṛṣṭataratve pitur bhrātuś ca naiva rikthabhājaḥ syuḥ | **aputrasya pitā haret**, tadabhāve bhrātaraḥ | evaṃ caurasasya pitṛdhanaprāptau siddhāyāṃ kṣetrajādisutaprāptyartho 'yam ārambhaḥ | yathś cedam āha || 9.185 ||

	**trayāṇām udakaṃ kāryaṃ triṣu piṇḍaḥ pravartate |**

**	caturthaḥ saṃpradātaiṣāṃ pañcamo nopapadyate || 9.186 ||**

prakṛtasya saṃnikarṣasya vibhavanārtho 'yaṃ ślokaḥ || 9.186 ||

	**anantaraḥ sapiṇḍād yas tasya tasya dhanaṃ bhavet |**

**	ata ūrdhvaṃ sakulyāḥ syur ācāryaḥ śiṣya eva vā || 9.187 ||**

sakulyagrahaṇena samānodakā gṛhyante | **ācāryaḥ śiṣyo vā** | tadabhāve || 9.187 ||

	**sarveṣām apy abhāve tu brāhmaṇā rikthabhāginaḥ |**

**	traividyāḥ śucayo dāntās tathā dharmo na hīyate || 9.188 ||**

**sarveṣām apy abhāve** ity etasmād gamyate tatstrīṇām apy abhāve yathoktaguṇasaṃbandha [iti | tathā ca] sati || 9.188 ||

	**ahāryaṃ brāhmaṇadravyaṃ rājñā nityam iti sthitiḥ |**

**	itareṣāṃ tu varṇānāṃ sarvābhāve haren nṛpaḥ || 9.189 ||**

ṛjvarthaḥ ślokaḥ || 9.189 ||

	**saṃsthitasyānapatyasya sagotrāt putram āharet |**

**	tatra yad rikthajātaṃ syāt tat tasmin pratipādayet || 9.190 ||**

kṣetrajasya devarasapiṇḍābhyām uktatvād iha sagotragrahaṇaṃ tadutpannasyāpi dhanāṃśaprāptyartham | itarathā hi "devarād vā sapiṇḍād vā" iti vacanād adevarasapiṇḍāt sagotrāt utpannasya kṣetrajasyānaṃśārhatā syāt | klībakasya dattakasya tu dattkṛtrimasvayaṃdattāḥ syuḥ || 9.190 ||

	**dvau tu yau vivadeyātāṃ dvābhyāṃ jātau striyā dhane |**

**	tayor yady asya pitryaṃ syāt tat saṃgṛhṇīta netaraḥ || 9.191 ||**

yā punarbhūḥ sāpatyā sadhanā ca parasmin puruṣe punar bhavati tatrāyaṃ vibhāgaḥ | idaṃ ca punarbhūputrasyāṃśaharatve darśanam || 9.191 ||

	**jananyāṃ saṃsthitāyāṃ tu samaṃ sarve sahodarāḥ |**

**	bhajeran mātṛkaṃ rikthaṃ bhaginyaś ca sanābhayaḥ || 9.192 ||**

samavacanān nāsty atra jyeṣṭhāṃśaḥ | bhaginyaś ca sanābhaya ūḍhā anūḍhāś ca gṛhyante | anūḍhā eveti kecit | baginyabhāve tu || 9.192 ||

	**yās tāsāṃ syur duhitaras tāsām ai yathārhataḥ |**

**	mātāmahyā dhanāt kiṃcit pradeyaṃ prītipūrvakam || 9.193 ||**

ūḍhānām anūḍhānāṃ ceti kṛtavicāram etat | **prītipūrvakam** iti vacanān na niyataṃ dānam idaṃ vijñāyate || 9.193 ||

	**adhyagnyādhyāvāhanikaṃ dattaṃ ca prītikarmaṇi |**

**	bhrātṛmātṛpitṛprāptaṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ strīdhanaṃ smṛtam || 9.194 ||**

ṣaḍvidhasya niyamāt maitralabdhasya strīdhanatvaṃ nāsti | adhyagnīyam agnisamīpa uhyamānāyai dattam | adhyāvāhanikaṃ patyā svagṛham ānīyamānāyai dīyate || 9.194 ||

	**anvādheyaṃ ca yad dattaṃ patyā prītena caiva yat |**

**	patyau jīvati vṛttāyāṃ prajāyās tad dhanaṃ bhavet || 9.195 ||**

ṛjvarthaḥ ślokaḥ || 9.195 ||

	**brāhmadaivārṣagāndharvaprājāpatyeṣu yad dhanam |**

**	aprajāyām atītāyāṃ bhartur eva tad iṣyate || 9.196 ||**

eteṣu pañcadheṣu (?) bhartur dhanam abhyanujñāyate || 9.196 ||

	**yat tv asyāḥ syād dhanaṃ dattaṃ vivāheṣv āsurādiṣu |**

**	aprajāyām atītāyāṃ mātāpitros tad iṣyate || 9.197 ||**

eteṣv āsurādiṣu kalyā[neṣu tayoḥ] pratyarpayitavyaṃ dhanam || 9.197 ||

	**striyāṃ tu yad bhaved vittaṃ pitrā dattaṃ kathaṃcana |**

**	brāhmaṇī tad dharet kanyā tadapatyasya vā bhavet || 9.198 ||**

ṣaḍvidhasyā[pi strīdhana]syāputrāyām [atītāyāṃ grahaṇe nyāyye] sati **pitrā dattam** ity etad atra nidarśanārthaṃ sarvastrīdhanānāṃ vijñeyam | [mṛta]putrāyāś ca vibhāgaṃ vakṣyati | **brāhmaṇī tad dharet kanyā** iti niyamāt kṣatriyādikanyānām [ayaṃ niya]maḥ | etad brāhmaṇādīnām | brāhmaṇīkṣatriyāvaiśyāsūḍhāsv asavarṇastryuparame brāhmaṇādikanyābhyo dhanadānaṃ vijñeyam || 9.198 ||

	**na nirhāraṃ striyaḥ kuryuḥ kuṭumbād bāhumadhyagāt |**

**	svakād api ca vittād dhi svasya bhartur anājñayā || 9.199 ||**

**nirhāra**pratiṣedhāc caitat vijñāyate yadi kācid īśatvāt taddhanaṃ nirharet, tatas tatpunarādāya bhrātṛbhir vibhaktavyam eva || 9.199 ||

	**patyau jīvati yaḥ strībhir alaṅkāro dhṛto bhavet |**

**	na taṃ bhajeran dāyādā bhajamānāḥ patanti te || 9.200 ||**

dāyādānām ayaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ | ātmīyānāṃ tv aurasaputrāṇām anujñāto vibhāgaḥ || 9.200 ||

	**anaṃśau klībapatitau jātyandhabadhirau tathā |**

**	unmattajaḍamūkāś ca ye ca kecin nirindriyāḥ || 9.201 ||**

ity anena pīṭhasarpipaṃgvādayo 'pi gṛhyante sāmarthyāt || 9.201 ||

	**sarveṣām api tu nyāyyaṃ dātuṃ śaktyā manīṣiṇā |**

**	grāsācchādanam atyantaṃ patito hy adadad bhavet || 9.202 ||**

prakaraṇāt klībādīnām idam ucyate grāsācchādanadānaṃ yāvajjīvam || 9.202 ||

	**yady arthitā tu dāraiḥ syāt klībadīnāṃ kathaṃcana |**

**	teṣām utpannatantūnām apatyaṃ dāyam arhati || 9.203 ||**

**klībādīnām** iti cātra sāmarthyān na bahuvrīhau tadguṇasaṃvijñānaṃ bhavati | evaṃ ca klībād apare tu gṛhyante | yena dharmaprajārthaṃ dārāṇāṃ saṃgrahaḥ yatas tad abhāvāt klībasya nāsti saṃgrahaḥ | aputrasyānadhikārād ādhāne | atha smārtakarmāpekṣo dārasaṃgrahaḥ | tataḥ klībasyāpy atra grahaṇaṃ yuktaṃ tadguṇasaṃvijñānabahuvrīhiṇā || 9.203 ||

	**yat kiṃcit pitari prete dhanaṃ [jyeṣṭho] 'dhigacchati |**

**	bhāgo yavīyasāṃ tatra yadi vidyānupālinaḥ || 9.204 ||**

jyeṣṭhalabdhasya vaidyāḥ santo bhāgino yavīyāṃsaḥ, na tu kaniṣṭhalabdhasya jyāyān ity etad arthāl [labhyate] || 9.204 ||

	**avidyānāṃ tu sarveṣām īhātaś ced dhanaṃ bhavet |**

**	samas tatra vibhāgaḥ syād apitrya iti dhāraṇā || 9.205 ||**

īhātaḥ ceṣṭātaḥ kṛṣyādita ity arthaḥ | sarve cec ceṣṭante samas tatra vibhāgaḥ syāt, na tu guṇāpekṣaḥ kaścid vibhāgakalpa āśrayitavyaḥ || 9.205 ||

	**vidyādhanaṃ tu yad yasya tat tasyaiva dhanaṃ bhavet |**

**	maitram audvāhikaṃ caiva mādhuparkikam eva ca || 9.206 ||**

**audvāhika**grahaṇena sarvaṃ śvaśuragṛhāl labdhaṃ gṛhyate || 9.206 ||

	**bhrātṝṇām yas tu neheta dhanaṃ śaktaḥ svakarmaṇā |**

**	sa nirbhājyaḥ svakād aṃśāt kiṃcid dattvopajīvanam || 9.207 ||**

adadatām api tu naiva virodho 'sti || 9.207 ||

	**anupaghnan pitṛdravyaṃ srameṇa yad upārjayet |**

**	svayam īhitalabdhaṃ tan nākāmo dātum arhati || 9.208 ||**

arthāt kāmasya dānam anujānāti || 9.208 ||

	**paitṛkaṃ tu pitā dravyam anavāptaṃ yad āpnuyāt |**

**	na tat putrair bhajet sārdham akāmaḥ svayam arjitam || 9.209 ||**

pitāmahadhanasyetare 'pīśata ity anayā śaṅkayā pratiṣedhaḥ | anena ca darśanena satyāṃ vibhāgapratipattau vittaṃ sarvaṃ vibhajanīyam | pitrā putravibhāgasyaitad darśanam | jīvapitṛkāṇām asti vibhāga ity etad darśayati || 9.209 ||

	**vibhaktāḥ saha jīvanto vibhajeran punar yadi |**

**	samas tatra vibhāgaḥ syāj jyaiṣṭhyaṃ tatra na vidyate || 9.210 ||**

saṃsṛṣṭānāṃ yo jyeṣṭhaḥ nāsau jyeṣṭāṃśaṃ gṛhṇīyāt | yatra tu jyeṣṭhaḥ saha jyeṣṭhāṃśena saṃsṛjyate tatra punar asya jyṣṭhāṃśa uddhriyate || 9.210 ||

	**yeṣāṃ jyeṣṭhaḥ kaniṣṭho vā [hīyetāṃśapradānataḥ |**

**	mri]yetānyataro vāpi tasya bhāgo na lupyate || 9.211 ||**

proṣitasya mṛtasya vā bhāgam uddhṛtya || 9.211 ||

	**sodaryā vibhajeraṃs taṃ sametya sahitāḥ samam |**

**	bhrātaro ye ca saṃsṛṣṭā bhaginyaś ca sanā[bhayaḥ || 9.212 ||**

asaṃsṛṣṭāṇāṃ soda]rāṇāṃs taṃ vibhajeran na sāpatnāḥ, sati tu saṃsarge ye saṃsṛṣṭās te vibhajeran, na sodaryā apy asaṃsṛṣṭāḥ || 9.212 ||

	**yo jyeṣṭho vinikurvīta lobhād bhrātṝn yavīyasaḥ |**

**	[so 'jyeṣṭhaḥ syā]d abhāgaś ca niyantavyaś ca rājabhiḥ || 9.213 ||**

vinikaraṇam anyāyena yavīyasāṃ nyakkaraṇaṃ dhanopayogaś ca tān atisaṃdhāya | arthāc ca kaniṣṭho 'pi sutarāṃniyantavya ity āpadyate || 9.213 ||

	**sarva eva vikarmasthā nārhanti bhrātaro dhanam |**

**	na cādattvā kaniṣṭhebhyo jyeṣṭhaḥ kurvīta yautakam || 9.214 ||**

ye kuṭumbakārya 'vyutpannās te dyūtādinā vikarmasthāḥ prakaraṇasāmarthyād vijñāyate | patitānā[m a]naṃśārhatoktā || 9.214 ||

	**bhrātṝṇām avibhaktānāṃ yady utthānaṃ bhavet saha |**

**	na tatra bhāgaṃ viṣamaṃ pitā dadyāt kathaṃcana || 9.215 ||**

**	ūrdhvaṃ vibhāgāj jātas tu pitryam eva hared dhanam |**

**	saṃsṛṣṭās tena vā ye syur vibhajeta sa taiḥ saha || 9.216 ||**

ye 'nyonyopārjitadhanāḥ pitrā snehena guṇāpekṣayā vā teṣāṃ viṣamo vibhāgo na kartavyaḥ | idaṃ ca darśanaṃ pitur abhiprāye na sati | api tu pitrabhiprāyeṇa vibhāge vaikalpikaṃ grahaṇaṃ tadabhiprāyeṇa syāt, nānyathā || 9.216 ||

	**anapatyasya putrasya mātā dayādyam āpnuyāt |**

**	mātary api ca vṛttāyāṃ pitur mātrā hared dhanam || 9.217 ||**

jīvatyāṃ mātari pitāmahyāṃ ca na sodarā īśante 'napatyasya svadhanasya, nāpi tatpitāsodaryā vā bhrātaraḥ || 9.217 ||

	**ṛṇe dhane ca sarvasmin pravibhakte yathāvidhi |**

**	paścād dṛśyeta yat kiṃcit tat sarvaṃ samatāṃ nayet || 9.218 ||**

draṣṭrā na tad grāhyam ity evamarthaṃ punar upadeśaḥ, jyeṣṭhāṃśapratiṣedhārtho vā, dvyaṃśaḥ pūrvajaḥ ity evam uktaṃ jyeṣṭhasya tad atra na syāt || 9.218 ||

	**vastraṃ patram alaṃkāraṃ kṛtānnam udakaṃ striyaḥ |**

**	yogakṣemapracāraṃ ca na vibhājyaṃ pracakṣate || 9.219 ||**

etān apīcchayā vibhajetan | "nākāmo dātum arhati" ity etad anuvādo 'yaṃ draṣṭavyaḥ | sarvatraivecchāto dānam ayuktaṃ pratiṣeddhum | sarvatra dhanavibhāge prāpte: **vastraṃ** [prasiddham | **patraṃ**] pataty anenety aśvādiḥ | **alaṃkāraṃ** sāmarthyāt pitari jīvati yad yena parigṛhītam | **kṛtānnaṃ** taṇḍulādi | **udakaṃ** tadādhārakūpādiḥ | **striyaḥ** upabhogadāsyaḥ pratiniyatāḥ | **yogakṣemapracāraṃ ca** yena dravyeṇa yogakṣemarthaṃ parcaranti | **yogo** 'nupāttaparilābhaḥ, **kṣemam** upāttaparipālanam | **yogakṣemaṃ** vā tadarthaṃ rājñāpi dīyamānaṃ draṣṭavyam | **pracāraṃ ca** pracaraṇabhūmijam indhanakādi, **na vibhājyaṃ pracakṣate** || 9.219 ||

	**eṣa ukto vibhāgo vaḥ putrāṇāṃ ca kriyāvidhiḥ |**

**	kramasaḥ kṣetrajādīnāṃ dyūtadharmaṃ nibodhata || 9.220 ||**

upasaṃhāropanyāsārthaḥ slokaḥ || 9.220 ||

	**dyūtaṃ samāhvayaṃ caiva rājā rāṣṭrān nivārayet |**

**	rājyāntakaraṇāv etau dvau doṣau pṛthivīkṣitām || 9.221 ||**

yena,

	p**rakāśam etat tāskaryaṃ yad evanasamāhvayau |**

ataḥ,

	**tayor nityaṃ pratīghāte nṛpatir yatnavān bhavet || 9.222 ||**

dyūtasamāhvayabhedapradarśanārtham idam adhunocyate:

	**aprāṇibhir yat kriyate tal loke dyūtam ucyate |**

**	prāṇibhiḥ kriyate yas tu sa vijñeyaḥ samāhvayaḥ || 9.223 ||**

**	dyūtaṃ samāhvayaṃ caiva yaḥ kuryat kārayeta vā |**

**	tān sarvān ghātayed rājā śūdrāṃś ca dvijaliṅginaḥ || 9.224 ||**

sabhikā api kārayato dyūtaṃ tāḍayitavyāḥ na kevalaṃ kartāraḥ | pratiṣedhaparatvāc ca vadhopadeśasyānyenāpy upāyena teṣāṃ pratiṣedhaḥ kartavyo rājatantravirodhinām | yena na hy atra dharmātikramaḥ kaścid asti | evaṃ ca saty atra vadhis tāḍanārthaḥ eva vijñeyaḥ | dharmavyavasthābhedinas tu śūdrān dvijaliṅgino ghātayed eva | dvijaliṅginaś ca śūdrā yajño[pavī]tapātradhāriṇo bhośabdavādinaḥ parivrājakādiveṣadhāriṇaś ca | vyākaraṇādhyayanam api ca dvijaliṅgam iti śakyaṃ vaktum || 9.224 ||

	**kitavān kuśīlavān krūrān pāṣaṇḍasthāṃś ca mānavān |**

**	[vikarmasthān śauṇdi]kāṃś ca kṣipraṃ nirvāsayet purāt || 9.225 ||**

krūrābhinnaduṣṭayor varṇalopena guṇavṛttyocyante | "kelān" ity aparaḥ pāṭhaḥ, te cātikāmukāḥ kelījīvi[naḥ | "kailān" ity apare] paṭhanti: saṅketakāriṇaḥ | **pāṣaṇḍasthāṃś ca mānavān** śrutismṛtibāhyeṣv āśramaliṅgeṣu vyavasthitān | [**vikarmastho**] 'dhikāravirodhena karmasthaḥ [iti] śabdas satantraḥ, śauṇḍikaviśeṣaṇā[rtho va(ā)] | sarvān etān **nirvāsayet purāt** | pravāsanakāryasya caviśeṣād rāṣṭrād apy ete 'rthato nirvāsyāḥ | atra ca kitavaprasaṅgena kuśīlavādīnām api pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate | yena || 9.225 ||

	**ete rāṣṭre vartamānā rājñaḥ pracchannataskarāḥ |**

**	vikarmakriyayā nityaṃ bādhante bhadrikāḥ prajāḥ || 9.226 ||**

yasmād ete rājadhānyām avasthitāḥ mahato 'narthāya rājñaḥ | ataś caiṣāṃ rāṣṭrād api nirvāsanam ucyate || 9.226 ||

	**dyūtam etat purā kalpe dṛṣṭaṃ vairakaṃ mahat |**

**	tasmād dyūtaṃ na seveta hāsyārtham api buddhimān || 9.227 ||**

yudhiṣṭhirādayo 'parakālāḥ | devāsuradṛṣṭaṃ tu dyūtaṃ ciravṛttatvād atrodāhriyate "te devāḥ ekataḥ" iti śruteḥ | evaṃ cāyaṃ dyūtanindārthavādo vijñeyaḥ | yataś caitad evam ataḥ || 9.227 ||

	**pracchannaṃ vā prakāśaṃ vā tan niṣeveta yo naraḥ |**

**	tasya daṇḍavikalpaḥ syād yatheṣṭaṃ nṛpates tathā || 9.228 ||**

evaṃ ca sati yena yena daṇḍaprakāreṇa dyūtanivṛttaḥ syāt taṃ taṃ daṇḍaprakāraṃ kalpayed ātmecchayā || 9.228 ||

	**kṣatraviṭśūdrayonis tu daṇḍaṃ dātum aśaknuvan |**

**	ānṛṇyaṃ karmaṇā gacched vipro dadyāc chanaiḥ śaniaḥ || 9.229 ||**

yathoktaṃ daṇḍaprakāram aśaknuvanto nirdhanatvāt kṣatriyādayo daṇḍānurūpāṇi karmāṇi kuryuḥ | brāhmaṇas tu svadharmānurodhena **śanaiḥ śanair** daṇḍanīyaḥ | tad etad uktam apy adhunā punar ucyate daṇḍaviṣayārtham | pūrvaṃ tu kusīdaprakaraṇe tadgatam || 9.229 ||

	**strībālonmattavṛddhānāṃ daridrānātharogiṇām |**

**	śiphāvidalarajjvādyair vidadhyān nṛpatir damam || 9.230 ||**

vikarmasthānām etad aparādhānurūpataḥ śiphādibhis tāḍanam | na pātakinām api cāpalatā vijñeyā || 9.230 ||

	**ye niyuktās tu kāryeṣu hanyuḥ kāryāṇi kāryiṇām |**

**	dhanoṣmaṇā pacyamānās tān niḥsvān kārayen nṛpaḥ || 9.231 ||**

dhanoṣmaṇā kasyacid vyavahārataḥ sāhāyyaṃ kurvanti | te niḥsvāḥ kāryāḥ | atha vā adhikṛtāḥ santo dhanaṃ gṛhītvā ye 'nyathā kāryāṇi kuryuḥ te niḥsvāḥ kāryā iti || 9.231 ||

	**kūṭaśāsanakartṝṃś ca prakṛtīnāṃ ca dūṣakān |**

**	strībālabrāhmaṇaghnāṃś ca hanyād dviṭsevinas tathā || 9.232 ||**

[te]ṣāṃ rājyatantravirodhe vartamānānāṃ niyamato vadhaḥ | dviṭsevinaś chamāgatikāḥ || 9.232 ||

	**tīritaṃ cānuśiṣṭaṃ ca yatra kvacana yad bhavet |**

**	kṛtaṃ taddharmato vidyān na tad bhūyo nivartayet || 9.233 ||**

evaṃ ca sati maitryā kāruṇyena vānyena vā kāraṇāntareṇa na nivartayet | arthād aśāstrakṛtaṃ nivartayet | tathā ca sati || 9.233 ||

	**amātyaḥ prāṅvivāko vā yat kuryuḥ kāryam anyathā |**

**	tat svayaṃ nṛpatiḥ kuryāt tān sahasraṃ ca daṇḍayet || 9.234 ||**

**amātyo** rājñā niyukto brāhmaṇaḥ vyavahārarakṣaṇe | tathā coktam: "tadā niyuñjyād vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ kāryadarśane" iti | **prāṅvivākās** tu pṛthag vedaśāstrajñātāraḥ | tathā coktam: "yasmin dese niṣīdanti viprā vedavidas trayaḥ" iti | ete yat kuryuḥ kāryam anyathā rāgādibhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ, asaṃnihite rājani, **tat svayaṃ nṛpatiḥ kuryāt** | punas **tān sahasraṃ daṇḍayet** | paṇānām ity uktaparibhāṣam etat | samudāye caiṣāṃ daṇḍacodanā, yathā "gārgyāś śataṃ daṇḍyantām" iti || 9.234 ||

	**brahmahā ca surāpaś ca taskaro gurutalpagaḥ |**

**	ete sarve pṛthag vedyā mahāpātakino narāḥ || 9.235 ||**

aparaḥ pāṭho 'tra śloke:

	brāhmaṇaghnaṃ surāpaṃ ca taskaraṃ gurutalpagam |

	etān vidyāt pṛthak sarvān mahāpātakino narān ||

atra pātakasaṃbandhāt suvarṇasteyakṛt taskaro gṛhyate | brahmahatyāyāṃ sarveṣāṃ vyatikramaḥ | surāyāṃ madhurāmadyapāne ca viśeṣaṃ varṇāśrayaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ | caurye ca sarvavarṇādhikāraḥ | sa gurutalpe || 9.235 ||

	**caturṇām api caiteṣāṃ prāyaścittam akurvatām |**

**	śarīradhanasaṃyuktaṃ daṇḍaṃ dharmyaṃ prakalpayet || 9.236 ||**

**caturṇām apīti** vacanāt tatsaṃbandhī pañcamo gṛhyate | strībālabrāhmaṇavadhe [va]dhadaṇḍa uktaḥ | **caturṇām api caiteṣām** ity atra śloka [aṅka]na[ṃ] dhanadaṇḍaś ca | tad etat pātakānurūpaṃ kāryam | śūdrasya tu brahmahatyāprāyaścittam akurvato daṇḍadvayam || 9.236 ||

	**gurutalpe bhagaḥ [kār[yaḥ surāpāne surā]dhvajaḥ |**

**	steye ca śvapadaḥ kāryo brahmanaṇy aśirāḥ pumān || 9.237 ||**

lalāṭe 'ṅkanapratiṣedhavidhau lalāṭagrahaṇāt || 9.237 ||

	**asaṃbhogyā hy asaṃyojyā asaṃpāṭyāvivāhinaḥ |**

**	careyuḥ pṛthivīṃ dīnāḥ sarvadharmabahiṣkṛtāḥ || 9.238 ||**

eṣa eva teṣāṃ tyāgo vijñeyaḥ | tad eva darśayati || 9.238 ||

	**jñātisaṃbandhibhis tv ete tyaktavyāḥ kṛtalakṣaṇāḥ |**

**	nirdayā nirnamaskārās tan manor anuśāsanam || 9.239 ||**

naite rājñā dhṛtadaṇā iti kṛtvā jñātisaṃbandhibhiḥ parigrāhyāḥ | evaṃ ca sati vyādhyādiyoge 'py eṣu dayā na kartavyā | jyaiṣṭhyādiguṇayoge ca naite namaskāryāḥ, pratyutthānādibhiḥ | eṣa eva cātra vacanasāmarthyād dharmo vijñeyaḥ | na tu svātantryeṇa dayā vinayo vā pūrvopadiṣṭa iti || 9.239 ||

	**prāyascittaṃ tu kurvāṇāḥ pūrve varṇā yathoditāḥ |**

**	nāṅkyā rājñā lalāṭeṣu dāpyās tūttamasāhasam || 9.240 ||**

pūrve varṇāḥ brāhmaṇādayaḥ | pramādavadhe ca pañcaśato daṇḍa ity etad arthād gamyate || 9.240 ||

	**āgassu brāhmaṇasyaiṣu kāryo madhyamasāhasaḥ |**

**	vivāsyo vā bhaved rāṣṭrāt sadravyaḥ saparicchadaḥ || 9.241 ||**

akāmata ity uttaraśloke vakṣyati | tad ihāpi vijñeyam | evaṃ ca saty eteṣv evāgassu brāhmaṇo madhyamasāhasaṃ daṇḍyaḥ | kāmaṃ vivāsyo rāṣṭrāt | evaṃ nigrahadvayaṃ vikalpenāsya syāt, vṛttasvādhyāyāpekṣayā || 9.241 ||

	**itare kṣtavantas tu pāpāny etāny akāmataḥ |**

**	sarvasvahāram arhanti kāmatas tu pravāsanam || 9.242 ||**

etāny eva mahāpātakāni kṛtavantaḥ kṣatriyādayo 'kāmataḥ sarvasvaharaṇaṃ kāryāḥ pūrvoktaṃ vottamasāhasaṃ daṇḍyāḥ | evaṃ brāhmaṇasya prāyaścittam aku[rva]to 'kāmato madhyamasāhaso daṇḍaḥ, kāmato vivāsanam | kṣatriyavaiśyayor akāmata uttamasāhasaḥ sarvasvaharaṇaṃ vā | kāmataś ca vadhaḥ | śūdrasya tv akāmataḥ sarvasvaharaṇam aṅkanaṃ ca | kāmatas tu vadhaḥ || 9.242 ||

	**nādadīta nrpaḥ sādhur mahāpātakināṃ dhanam |**

**	ādadānas tu tal lobhāt tena doṣeṇa tapyate || 9.243 ||**

yata etad evam ataḥ |

	**apsu praveśya taṃ daṇḍaṃ varuṇāyopapādayet |**

**	śrutavṛttopapanne vā brāhmaṇe pratipādayet || 9.244 ||**

atra pratipattividhau kāraṇaṃ vakti, yasmāt |

	**īśo daṇḍasya varuṇo rājñāṃ daṇḍadharo hi saḥ |**

**	īśaḥ sarvasya jagato brāhmaṇo vedapāragaḥ || 9.245 ||**

tasmāt tad dhanaṃ rājñā na grāhyam | kiṃ cānyat || 9.245 ||

	**yatra varjayate rājā pāpakṛdbhyo dhanāgamam |**

**	tatra kālena jāyante mānavā dīrghajīvinaḥ || 9.246 ||**

**	niṣpadyante ca sasyāni yathoktāni viśāṃ pṛthak |**

**	bālāś ca na pramīyante vikṛtaṃ ca na jāyate || 9.247 ||**

daṇḍaviniyogastutiślokau || 9.246–47 ||

	**brāhmaṇāt bādhamānaṃ tu kāmād avaravarṇajam |**

**	hanyāc citrair vadhopāyair udvejanakarair nṛpaḥ || 9.248 ||**

atra citrair vadhopāyair vadha eva niyamena prāyaścittam akurvato 'sya śuddhaya upadiśyate | yathāparādhaṃ tāḍanabandhanādibhiḥ śūdrasya | trayāṇāṃ caike, yasmāt || 9.248 ||

	**yāvān avadhyasya vadhe tāvān vadhyasya mokṣaṇe |**

**	adharmo nṛpater dṛṣṭo dharmas tu viniyacchataḥ || 9.249 ||**

yuktaś ca tadrakṣaṇād adhikṛtasya rājño vadhyamokṣaṇe pratyavāyaḥ | viśeṣeṇa tu baliṣaḍbhāgahāriṇaḥ śāstrapratyayād doṣanirhāraṇasya yathāśrutair evopāyair doṣanirharaṇaṃ yuktam | prāyaścittavat | tathā ca śāstralakṣaṇaiva dharmādharmavyavasthety uktam | evaṃ ca tadutpattiprāmāṇyavat pāpakṣaye 'sya prāmāṇyaṃ syāt | adṛṣṭārtheṣu tāvad evam | dṛṣṭārtheṣu tu rājyatantravidhyartha upadeśe yad vadhaśravaṇaṃ yathā "dviṭsevinaś ca hanyāt" ity uktaṃ ta[tra dṛṣṭapra]yojanārthatvād upadeśasya na niyato vadhaḥ | evaṃ ca saty upāyāntareṇāpi bandhanādinā viniyacchato na doṣaḥ || 9.249 ||

	**udito 'yaṃ vistaraśo mitho vivadamānayoḥ |**

**	aṣṭādaśasu mārgeṣu vyavahārasya nirṇayaḥ || 9.250 ||**

sarvavyavahāropasaṃharārthaślokaḥ || 9.250 ||

	**evaṃ kāryāṇi sarvāṇi kurvan samyaṅ mahīpatiḥ |**

**	deśān alabdhāṃl lipseta labdhāṃś ca paripālayet || 9.251 ||**

yena copāyena [prajāparipālanaṃ rājño bhavati sa idānīm ucyate | evamarthaś ca pūrva upasaṃhāro vijñeyaḥ || 9.251 ||

	**samyaṅ niviṣṭadeśas tu kṛtadurgaś ca śāstrataḥ |**

**	kaṇṭakaoddharaṇe nityam āti[ṣṭhed yatna]m uttamam || 9.252 ||**

asya praśaṃsārthavādaḥ phalavidhirūpaḥ || 9.252 ||

	**rakṣaṇād āryavṛttānāṃ kaṇṭakānāṃ ca śodhanāt |**

**	narendrās tridivaṃ yānti prajāpālanatatparāḥ || 9.253 ||**

ubhayānugrahād yuktaṃ rājñāṃ tridivagamanaṃ rakṣatām | ataḥ saṃrakṣaṇīyadharmāpakṣam api caitad yuktam | evaṃ cāvaśyaṃ rakṣaṇīyāḥ | vṛttisaṃrakṣaṇāc ca | na cāsati phalasaṃbandhe iyatī stutir upalabhyate | śāstralakṣaṇatvāc ca dharmādharmayor utpattivat phalārambho 'pi phalāc chraddadhanīyaḥ | yataś caitad evam ataḥ || 9.253 ||

	**aśāsaṃs taskarān yas tu baliṃ gṛhṇāti pārthivaḥ |**

**	tasya prakṣubhyate rāṣṭraṃ svargāc ca parihīyate || 9.254 ||**

**	nirbhayaṃ tu bhaved yasya rāṣṭraṃ bāhubhalāsritam |**

**	tasya tad vardhate nityaṃ sicyamāna iva drumaḥ || 9.255 ||**

dṛṣṭārthasaṃbandheneyam adṛṣṭaphalastutiḥ || 9.254–55 ||

	**dvividhāṃs taskarān vidyat paradravyāpahāriṇaḥ |**

**	prakāśāṃś cāprakāśāṃś ca cāracakṣur mahīpatiḥ || 9.256 ||**

cāracakṣurbhiḥ pārthivaiḥ paradravyanirharatāṃ tāskaryaṃ vijñeyam | ādarārthaṃ cāyam upadeśaḥ ādāv eṣāṃ vijñeyaḥ || 9.256 ||

	**prakāśavañcakās tv eṣāṃ nānāpaṇyopajīvinaḥ |**

**	pracchannavañcakās tv ete stenāṭavyādayo janāḥ || 9.257 ||**

tatra ye kraye vikraye mānatulādiviśeṣeṇa muṣṇanti dravyāṇām āgamasthānanirgamān anavekṣya te **prakāśā vañcakāḥ** | pracchannās tu rātrisattrās, taskarā ity arthaḥ | na ca kevalam ata eva kiṃ tarhīme cānye yān ita ūrdhvaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ || 9.257 ||

	**utkocakā aupadhikā vañcakāḥ kitavās tathā |**

**	maṅgalādeśavṛttāś ca bhadrāś caikṣaṇikais saha || 9.258 ||**

**	asamyak kāriṇaś caiva mahāmātrāś cikitsakāḥ |**

**	śilpopacārayuktāś ca nipuṇāḥ paṇyayoṣitaḥ || 9.259 ||**

**	evamādyān vijānīyāt prakāśāṃl lokakaṇṭakān |**

**	nigūḍhacāriṇaś cānyān anāryān āryaliṅginaḥ || 9.260 ||**

**	tān viditvā sucaritair gūḍhais tatkarmakāribhiḥ |**

**	cāraiś cānekasaṃsthānaiḥ protsāhya vaśam ānayet || 9.261 ||**

**	teṣāṃ doṣān abhikhyāpya sve sve karmaṇi tattvataḥ |**

**	kurvīta śāsanaṃ rājā samyak sārāparādhataḥ || 9.262 ||**

kasya punar hetos tatra daṇḍānuṣṭhānaṃ rājñaḥ śiṣyate. yena,

	**na hi daṇḍād ṛte śakyaḥ kartuṃ pāpavinigrahaḥ |**

**	stenānāṃ pāpabuddhīnāṃ nibhṛtaṃ caratāṃ kṣitau || 9.263 ||**

janapadakaṇṭakānām etal lakṣaṇam uktaṃ tan nigrahārtham | kaṇṭakātutyaupamita eṣām eṣa śabdo vijñeyaḥ | tadgrahaṇopāya idānīm ucyate || 9.263 ||

	**sabhāprapāpūgaśālāveśamadyānnavikrayāḥ |**

**	catuṣpathāś caityavṛkṣāḥ samājāḥ rakṣaṇāni ca || 9.264 ||**

**	jīrṇodyānāny araṇyāni kārukāveśanāni ca |**

**	śūnyāni cāpy agārāṇi vanāny upavanāni ca || 9.265 ||**

**	evaṃvidhān nṛpo deśān gulmaiḥ sthāvarajaṅgamaiḥ |**

**	taskarapratiṣedhārthaṃ cāraiś cāpy anucārayet || 9.266 ||**

**	tān sahāyais tv anugatair nānākarmapravedibhiḥ |**

**	vidyād utsāhayec caiva nipuṇaiḥ pūrvataskaraiḥ || 9.267 ||**

	**bhakṣyabhojyāpadeśaiś ca**

caṇḍikādiyāgāt sarvanimittm,

		**brāhmaṇānāṃ ca darśanaiḥ |**

vidyāgatāgatayogajñānām, yadbalāt sukaraṃ mahāphalaṃ cauryaṃ bhavati yatheṣṭam,

	**śauryakarmāpadeśaiś ca teṣāṃ kuryāt samāgamam || 9.268 ||**

tacchīlināṃ balātiśayavyavahāriṇām | evaṃ ca sati |

	**ye tatra nopasarpeyur mūlapraṇihitāś ca ye |**

**	tān prasahya nṛpo hanyāt samitrajñātibāndhavān || 9.269 ||**

**ye** taskarāḥ prakaraṇe nopagacchanti rājaśāsanān, **ye ca mūlapraṇihitās** taskarā nopagacchanti caṇḍikā[yāgā]diṣu | tāṃś ca tebhya evāgamayya **hanyāt** | evam api ca vartamānaś coranigrahe || 9.269 ||

	**na hoḍhena vinā coraṃ ghātayed dhārmiko nṛpaḥ |**

**	sahoḍhaṃ sopakaraṇaṃ hanyād evāvicārayan || 9.270 ||**

hoḍho [loptram | saha] tena grastaḥ syāt, nānyathā | yadi tāval loptraṃ darśanavicāryamānaṃ pramāṇataḥ śuddhaṃ bhavati | evam upakaraṇaṃ vivarasādhanādi vijñeyam || 9.270 ||

	**grāmeṣv api ca ye kecic corāṇāṃ bhaktadāyakāḥ |**

**	bhāṇḍāvakāśadāś caiva sarvāṃs tān api ghātayet || 9.271 ||**

vicārya pratyakṣāgamānumānaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ | yenāvijñānād api hy etat sarvaṃ bhavati || 9.271 ||

	**rāṣṭreṣu rakṣādhikṛtān sāmantāṃś caiva coditān |**

**	abhyāghāteṣu madhyasthāñ chiṣyāc caurān iva drutam || 9.272 ||**

ātyayikeṣv etān ananudhātatāñ corasaṃvādena pramādād vā coravac chiṣyāt | nimittabhedāc cānuśāsanabhedo vijñeyaḥ || 9.272 ||

	**yaś cāpi dharmasamayāt pracyuto dharmajīvanaḥ |**

**	daṇḍenaiva tam apy oṣet svakād dharmād dhi vicyutam || 9.273 ||**

brāhmaṇo **dharmajīvanaḥ** | sa hy anupakṛtya jīvati | yatas tasyāpi svadharmasthāpanārthaṃ daṇḍo 'parādhānurūpaḥ praṇeyaḥ || 9.273 ||

	**grāmaghāte hiḍābhaṅge pathi corādidarśane |**

**	śaktās tv anabhidhāvanto nirvāsyāḥ saparicchadāḥ || 9.274 ||**

ālasyenānabhidhāvanto nirvāsyāḥ, ye tu cropakṣepān nānudhāvanti te coravadhena vadhyāḥ || 9.274 ||

	**rājakośāpahartṝṃś ca prātikūleṣu ca sthitān |**

**	arīṇām upajaptṝṃś ca ghātayed vividhair vadhaiḥ || 9.275 ||**

aparādhānurūpataḥ svatantrapīḍāpekṣayā eṣāṃ nigrahaḥ syāt || 9.275 ||

	**saṃdhiṃ chitvā tu ye caryaṃ rātrau kurvanti taskarāḥ |**

**	teṣāṃ chitvā nṛpo hastau tīkṣṇe śūle niveśayet || 9.276 ||**

cauryopalakṣaṇārthaṃ ca **saṃdhi**grahaṇam | evaṃ cāskandhāvāra eva praviśya cauryaṃ kurvato 'yam eva nigrahaḥ syāt | hastayoś chedanaṃ śule vā niveśam | ekasyaivety apare | etac ca varṇaviseṣāpakṣayā ubhayam atrāsya prayojanānubandhāpekṣayā kalpyam, na yathāśrutam | tathā ca darśayati || 9.276 ||

	**aṅgulīr granthibhedasya chedayet prathame grahe |**

**	dvitīye hastacaraṇau tṛtīye vadham arhati || 9.277 ||**

kṛtanigrahasyāpi nigrahopadeśaś chinnahastacaraṇo 'pi punaḥ kenacid upāyāntareṇa cauryam āsevataḥ || 9.277 ||

	**agnidān bhaktadāṃś caiva tathā śastrāvakāśadān |**

**	saṃnidhātṝṃś ca moṣasya śiṣyāc corān iveśvaraḥ || 9.278 ||**

vijñāya corāṃs tatsāhāyyenāitāni kurvatāṃ coravac chiṣṭis tāḍanabandhanaparibhāṣaṇādirūpā | na tu varāṅgacchedo 'rthadaṇḍanaṃ vā śiṣṭiḥ | prathamam evānuktāpi cauryaṃ varṇānāṃ coravac chiṣṭir alpeṣv aparādheṣu corasyāpi syāt || 9.278 ||

	**taṭākabhedakaṃ hanyād apsu śuddhavadhena vā |**

**	yad vāpi pratisaṃskuryād dadyāc cottamasāhasam || 9.279 ||**

vapraṃ taṭākasya bhitvodakaṃ harato vadho 'psv anyatra vā sthale 'śaktasya pratisaṃskāre, śaktasyāpi daṇḍanam | puṇyānubandha evobhayor apy anugrahaḥ kalpito bhavati, taṭākasvāminaḥ taṭākabhedakasya ca | pratisaṃskārapakṣe cāsyottamasāhasaḥ paṇasahasram || 9.279 ||

	**koṣṭhāgārāyudhāgāradevatāgārabhedakān |**

**	hastyaśvarathaharṝṃś ca hanyād evāvicārayan || 9.280 ||**

devatāgārabhedakād ṛte itareṣāṃ svatantrarakṣaṇaprayojanatvād vadhopadeśasya na niyamena vadhaḥ kriyate | pratiprasavabhāvāc ca nivṛttāv api nābhyudayaḥ | devatāgārabhedakasyāpi pratikartuṃ daṇḍaṃ ca dātum aśaktasya vadhaḥ syāt | tathā coktaṃ pūrvaśloke | evaṃ cādhikārād uttamasāhaso daṇḍaḥ | "saṅkramadvajayaṣṭīnām" ity asmin vakṣyamāṇaśloke devatāpratimābhedakasyāpi daṇḍaṃ vakṣyati vadharahitam | evaṃ ca sati yadi devatāgārabhedakasya niyogato vadha ucyate, tato nyāyavirodhyayuktarūpa upadeśaḥ | ataḥ pākṣiko vadho vijñeyaḥ || 9.280 ||

	**yas tu pūrvaniviṣṭasya taṭākasyodakaṃ haret |**

**	āgamaṃ vāpy apāṃ bhindyāt sa dāpyaḥ pūrvasāhasam || 9.281 ||**

devatāghātakatvāt pūrvaniveśa ucyate | itarathā vā | tatra yad uktam: sasyasakāryaṃ **yo haret** anāgata evodakasy[ālādi]n**āgamaṃ** **vā bhindyāt sa** daṇḍyaḥ **pūrvasāhasam** | evaṃ ca sati yad uktam, daṇḍaṃ dātum aśaktāḥ kṣatriyādayaḥ "ānṛṇyaṃ karmaṇā" gaccheyur iti, tatkāryasāmānyād atra sarvatra pratyetavyam || 9.281 ||

	**samutsṛjed rājamārge [yas tv ame]dhyam anāpadi |**

**	sa dvau kārṣāpaṇau dadyād amedhyaṃ cāsu śodhayet || 9.282 ||**

kārṣāpaṇaparimāṇaṃ vyākhyātam || 9.282 ||

	**āpadgato 'tha vā vṛddho garbhiṇī bāla eva vā |**

**	paribhāṣaṇam arhanti tac ca śodhyam iti sthitiḥ || 9.283 ||**

**āp**[**adgata** iti sahopa]deśād atyanta**vṛddho**, **garbhiṇī**, **bālo** veditavyaḥ || 9.283 ||

	**cikitsakānāṃ sarveṣāṃ mithyā pracaratāṃ damaḥ |**

**	amānuṣeṣu prathamo mānuṣeṣu tu madhyamaḥ || 9.284 ||**

prathamamadhyamau sāhasottarapadāv etau draṣṭavyau | vinā śāstreṇa | [atha]vā sati śāstrādhyayane mithyā ye cikitsāyāṃ vartante mānuṣāmānuṣeṣu teṣām eṣa damaḥ || 9.284 ||

**	saṃkramadhvajayaṣṭīnāṃ pratimānāṃ ca bhedakaḥ |**

**	pratikuryāc ca tat sarvaṃ pañca dadyāc chatāni ca || 9.285 ||**

nadīgartādiṣu yaiḥ saṃkrāmanti te saṃkramāḥ | dhvajo rājñāṃ devatāyataneṣu vā, yaṣṭir nāgāyatane, baliyaṣṭir vā grāmeṣu | ayaṃ ca vicārito 'rthaḥ | pūrvaśloke vkalpārthaṃ vadhadaṇḍasya kenacid atrānubandhādinā kāraṇena pratimābhedakasyehopadeśaḥ || 9.285 ||

	**adūṣitānāṃ dravyānāṃ dūṣaṇe bhedane tathā |**

**	maṇīnām apy avedhe ca daṇḍaḥ prathamasāhasaḥ || 9.286 ||**

kuṃkumādidravyāṇāṃ tat sadṛśena māyākusumbhādinā dūṣaṇam | bhedanaṃ tu maṇibhiḥ saṃbadhyate | maṇīnāṃ bhedane vināśe 'vedhe 'sthānavedhe ca maṇīnām eva sārānurūpo daṇḍaḥ | evaṃ ca sati prathamasāhasagrahaṇaṃ pradarśanārthaṃ vijñeyam | yena maṇayo hi kākaṇikamūlyā api santi anekasāhasrāś ca | ato nāviśeṣeṇa yukto 'tra daṇḍa iti | etasmāt kāraṇāt prathamasāhasagrahaṇasya pradarśanārthatā kalpyate || 9.286 ||

	**samaiś ca viṣamaṃ yaś ca prakaren mūlyato 'pi vā |**

**	sa prāpnuyād damaṃ pūrvaṃ naro madhyamam eva vā || 9.287 ||**

aparicchinnārdhānāṃ dravyāṇām ajñātatayā kāryavattāṃ vāvedkṣya kretur yo 'nyathā vikrīṇīte bhāvadoṣeṇa tasya [vi]kretur dravyāpekṣayā prathamamadhyamau kalpyau | atha vā kretari prathamaḥ kāryaḥ vikretur madhyamaḥ || 9.287 ||

	**bandhanāni ca sarvāṇi rājamārge niveśayet |**

**	duḥkhitā yatra dṛśyeran vkṛtāḥ pāpakāriṇaḥ || 9.288 ||**

pṛthagjanasya pāpanivṛttyupāyopadeśaḥ || 9.288 ||

	**prākārasya ca bhettāraṃ parikhāṇāṃca pūrakam |**

**	dvārāṇāṃ caiva bhaṅktāraṃ kṣipram eva pravāsayet || 9.289 ||**

purasya rājakulasya durgasya vā | pravāsanam atrobhayathā rājakāryavirodhāpekṣayā vijñeyam | evaṃ ca saty atra rājñaḥ svatantrasaṃrakṣaṇatvād upadeśasya na niyogena vyatikramakāriṇāṃ vadha upadiśyate || 9.289 ||

	**abhicāreṣu sarveṣu kartavyo dviśato damaḥ |**

**	mūlakarmaṇi cānāptaiḥ kṛtyāsu vividhāsu ca || 9.290 ||**

śrutismṛtibāhyeṣv abhicāreṣu khādirasūcīnikhananapadapāṃśugrahaṇādiṣv idam ucyate | atrābhicārārhasyāyaṃ daṇḍo na vidyate | tathāyaṃ prāyaścittaṃ vakṣyaty anabhicaraṇīyasyābhicāre "abhicāram ahīnaṃ ca tribhiḥ kṛcchrair vyapohati" iti | **mūlakarmaṇi cānāptaiḥ** kriyamāṇe | na mātṛbhaginyādibhiḥ, adhikārāt tāsām | **kṛtyāsu** ca vaitāḷādyāsu bhūtatantravihitāsv asaṃbandhakṛtāsv eva | apare tu **sarva**grahaṇasāmarthyāt sarvābhicāreṣv etad daṇḍam āhuḥ || 9.290 ||

	**abījavikrayī yaś ca bījotkṛṣṭaṃ tathaiva ca |**

**	maryādābhedakaś caiva vikṛtaṃ prāpnuyād vadham || 9.291 ||**

bījam iti kṛtvābījaṃ yo vikrīṇīte 'rthinaś ca kretṝn dṛṣṭvā bījamūlyata utkarṣaṃ nayati | **maryādāś** ca kṣetrakedāragatā yo bhinatti, na grāmadeśasaṅghamaryādāḥ, bījakrayavikrayādisāhacaryāt | sa karṇanāsācchedanākhyaṃ **vikṛta**tvakāraṇam arhati | aparādhasamuccayena sānubandhena ca māraṇam, yena na hi dṛṣṭaprayojana itīyān nigraha upapadyate | ayam api daṇḍo na niyamataḥ syād eteṣv evāparādheṣu, dṛṣṭārthatvād asya nigrahopadeśasya || 9.291 ||

	**sarvakaṇṭakapāpiṣṭhaṃ hemakāraṃ tu pārthivaḥ |**

**	pravartamānam anyāye chedyel lavaśaḥ kṣuraiḥ || 9.292 ||**

sarvavarṇebhyaḥ suvarṇāpahārapravṛtte brāhmaṇasuvarṇāpaharaṇe vā mahāpātakābhyāsaśīlasyedam ucyate | taṃ nikaṣaparivartanatulāsaṃcaraṇādiṣu anyāyeṣu pravṛttam "yena yena yathāṅgena" ity anayā paribhāṣayā jihvāhastapādaśiraścakṣurādinā suvarṇaguptiṃ kurvantaṃ **lavaśo** ghātayet, aparāddhābhyāsānubandhena | apare tv āhuḥ: sarvavarṇasuvarṇāpaharaṇa etad ucyate | hemakartur bahutvālpatvāpekṣayāyaṃ chedanopadeśaḥ pradarśanārthaḥ | apare tu suvarṇakārasyāpīdaṃ na śodhanam ity upadiśanti, rakṣitāpaharaṇe 'pi surāprāyaścittavat || 9.292 ||

	**sītādravyāpaharaṇe śastrāṇām auṣadhasya ca |**

**	kālam āsādya kāryaṃ ca rājā daṇḍaṃ prakalpayet || 9.293 ||**

**sītādravyāṇi** kalayuga, pratodādīni | **śastrāṇi** phaladātrādīni tatsāhacaryāt | **auṣadhaṃ** tadgataṃ laśunādi | atha vā [o]ṣadhayo sāmānyena grahaṇaṃ yuktam, samānatvād aparādhasya | **kālam āsādya** **kāryaṃ** ca teṣāṃ **daṇḍaṃ rājā** yatheṣṭaṃ kuryāt | tad aparādhanivṛttihetum anyeṣām api || 9.293 ||

	**svāmyamātyau puraṃ rāṣṭraṃ kośadaṇḍau tathā suhṛt |**

**	sapta prakṛtayo hy etāḥ samastaṃ rājyam ucyate || 9.294 ||**

**	saptānāṃ prakṛtīnāṃtu rājyasyāsāṃ yathākramam |**

**	pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ gurutaraṃ jānīyād vyasane nṛpaḥ || 9.295 ||**

asyopadeśaprayojanaṃ **svāmy**ādīnāṃ **pūrvasmin pūrvasmin vyasanaṃ gurutaraṃ** rājyatantravināśakaraṇaṃ parijñāya pariharen **nṛpa** iti || 9.294–95 ||

	**saptāṅgasyāsya rājyasya viṣṭabdhasya tridaṇḍavat |**

**	anyonyaguṇavaiśeṣyān na kiṃcid atiricyate || 9.296 ||**

yasmāt,

	**teṣu teṣu hi kāryeṣu tat tad aṅgaṃ viśiṣyate |**

svaviṣayaniyamād indriyavat | evaṃ ca sati,

	**yena yat sādhyate kāryaṃ tat tasmiñ chreṣṭham ucyate || 9.297 ||**

bhavati hi tat kāryaṃ rājño, yatra laghīyān api prakṛti padārtho garīyān bhavati | tasmāt sarva evaite sarvadā samīkṣitavyāḥ tatpuruṣāś ca | evamarthaś cāyaṃ punar ihopadeśo rājaprakṛtīnām, yasmāt prāyeṇa hi rājyakaṇṭakā amātyādiprakṛtisaṃśrayā eva bhavanti | rājavallabhāmātyamahiṣīkumārādyāśritās te hi rājoṣmaṇā niḥśaṅkā santaḥ sutarāṃ janapadaṃ muṣṇanti || 9.297 ||

	**[cāreṇotsāhayogena kriyayaiva ca karmaṇām |**

**	svaśaktiṃ paraśaktiṃ ca nityaṃ vidyān mahīpatiḥ] || 9.298 ||**

ata eṣāṃ punar ihopadeśaḥ kaṇṭakoddharaṇaprakaraṇe | yathaitatsaṃśrayād idam upadiśyate **nitya**grahaṇam | evaṃ ca paracakrasaṃrakṣaṇavaj janapadaḥ svacakrapīḍāto 'pi rakṣaṇīyaḥ | saiṣā kaṇṭakoddharaṇādarārthā punar iha rājadharmoktir vijñeyā || 9.298 ||

	**pīḍanāni ca sarvāṇi vyasanāni tathaiva ca |**

**	gurulāghavato jñātvā tataḥ kāryaṃ samācaret || 9.299 ||**

**pīḍanāni** jagatām aśanipātadurbhikṣādīni | svakṛtāni **vyasanāni** trayāṇi dehadaivātmagatāni kṣayahetūni | **jñātvā** lokasya **gurulāghvataḥ**, tato daṇḍagurutvalaghutvaṃ **samācaret** nṛpatir nāviśeṣeṇa | evaṃ ca rājadharmeṣu vartamāno yāvajjīvam || 9.299 ||

	**ārabhetaiva karmāṇi śrāntaḥ śrāntaḥ punaḥ punaḥ |**

**	karmāṇy ārabhamānaṃ hi puruṣaṃ srīr niṣevate || 9.300 ||**

evaṃ ca śramād alasatvād na karmārambhān nivartitavyam | mā māivaṃ gṛhṇīyād yugānurūpam mayā vartitavyam iti, yasmāt |

	**kṛtaṃ tretāyugaṃ caiva dvāparaṃ kalir eva ca |**

**	rājño vṛttāni sarvāṇi rājā hi yugam ucyate || 9.301 ||**

tathā ca kaliyugam iti kṛtvā nodāsīnaḥ syāt | yena ca rājavṛttenāyaṃ kaliyugādibhir vyapadiśyate rājā| tad darśayati || 9.301 ||

	**kaliḥ prasupto bhavati sa jāgrad dvāparaṃ yugam |**

**	karmasv abhyuditas tretā vicaraṃs tu kṛtaṃ yugam || 9.302 ||**

anutthānaśīlaḥ **prasupto bhavati**, yo jānānaś cotkarṣopāyam anutiṣṭhet **sa jāgrad** bhavati | vyavasitakarmaprayogas **tretā**yugaṃ bhavati | anutiṣṭhaṃś ca sarvakarmāṇi yathāśāstraṃ karmaphalasaṃpadā **kṛtayugaṃ** bhavati | evaṃ ca rājanimittatvāt sarvārambhāṇāṃ yuktā tadvṛttastutiḥ || 9.302 ||

	**indrasyārkasya vātasya yamasya varuṇasya ca |**

**	candrasyāgneḥ pṛthivyāś ca tejovṛttaṃ nṛpaś caret || 9.303 ||**

evaṃvṛtto hi rājā kaṇṭakoddhāraṇena pratāpānurāgāv ātmany utpādayan sakalamahīmaṇḍalādhipatyenāntyena yujyate | **indrā**dilokapālavṛttatāṃ rājñaḥ kenacit sāmānyena pradarśyate || 9.303 ||

	**vārṣikāṃś caturo māsān yathendro 'bhipravarṣati |**

**	tathābhivarṣet svaṃ rāṣṭraṃ kāmair indravrataṃ caran || 9.304 ||**

**	aṣṭau māsān yathādityas toyaṃ harati raśmibhiḥ |**

**	tathā haret karaṃ rāṣṭrān nityam arkavrataṃ hit tat || 9.305 ||**

**	praviśya sarvabhūtāni yathā carati mārutaḥ |**

**	tathā cāraiḥ praveṣṭavyaṃ vratam etad dhi mārutam || 9.306 ||**

**	yathā yamaḥ priyadveṣyau prāpte kāle niyacchati |**

**	tathā rājñā niyantavyāḥ prajās tad dhi yamavratam || 9.307 ||**

**	varuṇena yathā pāśair baddha eva hi dṛśyate |**

**	tathā pāpān nibadhnīyād vratam etad dhi vāruṇam || 9.308 ||**

**	parpūrṇaṃ yathā candraṃ dṛṣṭvā hṛṣyanti mānavāḥ |**

**	tathā prakṛtayo yasmin sa cāndravratiko nṛpaḥ || 9.309 ||**

**	pratāpayuktas tejasvī nityaṃ syāt pāpakarmasu |**

**	duṣṭasāmantahiṃsraś ca tad āgneyaṃ vrataṃ smṛtam || 9.310 ||**

**	yathā sarvāṇi bhūtāni dharā dhārayate samam |**

**	tathā sarvāṇi bhūtāni bibhrataḥ pārthivaṃ vratam || 9.311 ||**

**	etair upāyair anyaiś ca yukto nityam atandritaḥ |**

**	stenān rājā nigṛhṇīyāt svarāṣṭre para eva ca || 9.312 ||**

aṣṭābhiḥ ślokair uktam api rājavṛttam arthanirmalatvāya punar uktam | daṇḍyeṣu daṇḍapātanaṃ yathāparādhaṃ kurvan lokapālavat samaḥ prajāsu yathā syād iti daṇḍaprakaraṇe punar ādarārtham ucyata iti || 9.304–12 ||

	**parām apy āpadaṃ prāpto brāhmaṇān na prakopayet |**

**	te hy enaṃ kupitā hanyuḥ sadyaḥ sabalavāhanam || 9.313 ||**

abhicārābhiśāpābhyām | tathā ca tatpratāpaṃ darśayati || 9.313 ||

	**yaiḥ kṛtaḥ sarvabhakṣo 'gnir apeyaś ca mahodadhiḥ |**

**	kṣayī cāpyāyitaḥ somaḥ ko na naśyet prakopya tān || 9.314 ||**

kiṃ ca,

	**lokān anyān sṛjeyur ye lokapālāṃś ca kopitāḥ |**

**	devān kuryur adevāṃś ca kaḥ kṣiṇvaṃs tān samṛdhnuyāt || 9.315 ||**

**	yān samāśritya tṣṭhanti lokā devāś ca sarvadā |**

**	brahma caiva dhanaṃ yeṣāṃ ko hiṃsyāt tāñ jijīviṣuḥ || 9.316 ||**

na cāvidvān iti paribhavanīyo 'sau, yasmāt |

	**avidvāṃś caiva vidvāṃś ca brāhmaṇo daivataṃ mahat |**

**	[praṇītaś cāpraṇītaś ca yathāgnir daivataṃ mahat || 9.317 ||**

**	śmaśāneṣv api tejasvī pāvako naiva duṣyati |**

**	hūyamānas ca yajñeṣu bhūya evābhivardhate || 9.318 ||**

**	evaṃ yady apy aniṣṭeṣu vartante sarvakarmasu |**

**	sarvathā brāhmaṇāḥ pūjyāḥ paramaṃ daivataṃ hi tat] || 9.319 ||**

**	kṣatrasyātipravṛddhasya brāhmaṇān prati sarvataḥ |**

**	brahmaiva saṃniyantṛ syāt kṣatraṃ him brahmasaṃbhavam || 9.320 ||**

**	adbhyo 'gnir brahmataḥ kṣatram aśmano loham utthitam |**

**	teṣāṃ sarvatragaṃ tejaḥ svāsu yoniṣu śāmyati || 9.321 ||**

**	nābrahma kṣatram ṛdhnoti nākṣatraṃ brahma vardhate |**

**	brahmakṣatre ca saṃpṛkte iha cāmutra ṛdhnutaḥ || 9.322 ||**

daśabhiḥ ślokair daṇḍyanigrahaprakaraṇe brāhmaṇāḥ praśasyante | saty api śāstre tadapekṣayāiṣāṃ kṣāntim āśritya mṛdūpakramo nigraho yathā syāt svavṛttasthāpanārtham ity evamartham idam || 9.313–22 ||

	**datvā dhanaṃ tu viprebhyaḥ sarvadaṇḍasamutthitam |**

**	putre sarvaṃ samāsṛjya kurvīta prāyaṇaṃ raṇe || 9.323 ||**

prāyaṇaṃ ca rājñaḥ prathamakalpaḥ | atas tadabhāva itare kalpā yathā syuḥ svakāmaprāyaṇāvirodhaś cāsya vyākhyātaḥ || 9.323 ||

	**evaṃ caran sadā yukto rājadharmeṣu pārthivaḥ |**

**	hiteṣu caiva lokasya sarvabhṛtyān niyojayet || 9.324 ||**

**	eṣo 'khilaḥ karmavidhir ukto rājñaḥ sanātanaḥ |**

**	imaṃ karmavidhiṃ vidyāt kramaśo vaiśyaśūdrayoḥ || 9.325 ||**

ślokadvayena rājadharmopasaṃhāro [vaiśya]śūdravṛttidharmopakṣepaviśeṣārtho vijñeyaḥ | tathā ca taṃ viśeṣaṃ pradarśayati: yatkṛto 'sya punarārambhaḥ || 9.324–25 ||

	**vaiśyas tu kṛtasaṃskāraḥ kṛtvā dāraparigraham |**

**	vārtāyāṃ nityayuktaḥ syāt paśūnāṃ caiva rakṣaṇe || 9.326 ||**

ānantaryārtho viśeṣārthaś cāyam upadeśaḥ | asyārthavādaḥ || 9.326 ||

	**prajāpatir hi vaiśyāya sṛṣṭvā paridade paśūn |**

**	brāhmaṇāya ca rājñe ca sarvāḥ paradade prajāḥ || 9.327 ||**

**	na ca vaiśyasya kāmaḥ syān na rakṣeyaṃ paśūn iti |**

**	vaiśye cecchati nānyena rakṣitavyāḥ kathaṃcana || 9.328 ||**

rājño 'yam upadeśaḥ, tathānyamanuṣyasya brāhmaṇādeḥ | idaṃ cānyad vaiśeṣikaṃ vaiṣyasya vṛttikarmaṇā || 9.327–28 ||

	**maṇimuktāpravāḷānāṃ lohānāṃ tāntavasya ca |**

**	gandhānāṃ ca rasānāṃ ca vidyād arghabalābalam || 9.329 ||**

**	bījānām uptivic ca syāt kṣetrabījaguṇasya ca |**

**	mānayogaṃ ca jānīyāt tulāyogāṃś ca sarvaśaḥ || 9.330 ||**

**	sārāsāraṃ ca bhāṇḍānāṃ deśānāṃ ca guṇāguṇam |**

**	lābhālābhaṃ ca paṇyānāṃ paśūnāṃ ca vivardhanam || 9.331 ||**

**	bhṛtyānāṃ ca bhṛtiṃ vidyād bhāṣāś ca vividhā nṛṇām |**

**	dravyāṇāṃ sthānayogāṃś ca krayaṃ vikrayam eva ca || 9.332 ||**

**	dharmeṇa ca dravyavṛddhāv ātiṣṭhed yatnam uttamam |**

**	dadyāc ca sarvabhūtānām annam eva prayatnataḥ || 9.333 ||**

aṣṭābhiḥ ślokair uktāpi satī vaiśyavṛttir viśeṣārthaṃ punar abhidhīyate | sa ca viśeṣo 'yam: **na ca vaiśyasya kāmaḥ syān na rakṣeyaṃ paśūn** iti | evaṃ ca saty asyānyābhyo vṛttibhyaḥ paśurakṣaṇavṛttir eva dharmyeti vijñāyate | **maṇimuktā**digrahaṇaṃ ca sarvadravyadarśanārtham | tathā ca sati nāsya kiṃcid api akreyam iti gamyate | anyac ca hiraṇyādidānaṃ parihāpyānnaṃ viśeṣato dadyāt, **sarvabhūtānām** iti vacanāti | na kevalaṃ guṇavadbrāhmaṇebhyaḥ | śūdrasyā[pi vṛttir idān]īm ucyate dharmyā ca || 9.329–33 ||

	**viprāṇāṃ vedaviduṣāṃ gṛhasthānāṃ yaśasvinām |**

**	śuśrūṣaiva tu śūdrasya dharmo naiḥśreyasaḥ paraḥ || 9.334 ||**

śūdro viśeṣataḥ itthaṃbhūtaguṇavatāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ [śuśrūṣayā niḥśreyasaṃ labhate] || 9.334 ||

	**śucir utkṛṣṭaśuśrūṣur mṛduvāg anahaṃkṛtaḥ |**

tad evaṃvṛttah,

	**brāhmaṇāpāśrayo nityam utsṛṣṭāṃ jātim aśnute || 9.335 ||**

brāhmaṇāpāśritaśūdrasya tadāśrayaphalārthavādo 'yam | phalavidhir vāyaṃ nyāyaśāstrāvirodhād yuktaḥ || 9.335 ||

	**eṣo 'nāpadi varṇānām ukto dharmavṛttiḥ śubhaḥ |**

**	āpady api ca yas tv eṣām [kramaśas tan nibodhata] || 9.336 ||**

**vṛttiḥ dharmaś** ceti siddhyarthaṃ dvaividhyam || 9.336 ||

**iti bhārucikṛte manuśāstravivaraṇe navamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||**


## 10
**daśamo 'dhyāyaḥ**

	**[adhīyīraṃs trayo varṇāḥ svakarmasthā dvijātayaḥ |**

**	prabrūyād brāhmaṇas tv eṣāṃ netarāv iti niścayaḥ] || 10.1 ||**

vaiśyaśūdropacārānantaraṃ śāstrānukraṇyapekṣayā saṃkīrṇānāṃ saṃbhavo vaktavyaḥ | yatas tadupodghātārthaṃ brahmacāriprakaraṇopadiṣṭ[ādhyayanāpekṣyātra] "adhīyīrann" ity uktam | evaṃ cātrādhipūrvasyeṅo (?) vedaśabdakriyasya vedaśabdaviṣayataiva jñāyate, **adhīyīran** vedaṃ paṭheyur ity arthaḥ | īdṛśaṃ ca tatrāśrutam api vidhivākyam utprekṣyam anuvādasāmarthyāt | tathā ca brahmacāriprakaraṇa evaṃ ca niyamārtham idam uktam: "vedaḥ kṛtsno 'dhigantavyaḥ" ityevamādi | svakarmasthā iti caitatsāmarthyād brahmacāriprakaraṇoktān eva gurūpasadanābhivādanādīn adyayanavratadharmān gṛhṇāti | arthāc ca trayāṇām adhyāpane prāpta idaṃ niyamārtham ucyate kṣatriyavaiśyayoḥ **prabrūyād brāhmaṇas tv eṣām** iti | evaṃ ca **netarāv** ity etadarthasiddhatvād anārabhyaṃ sad ucyate viśeṣārtham | **netarāv** ity anāpadviṣayaṃ pratiṣedhaṃ kalpayāmaḥ | tad idam ucyate: āpai tv itarāv api kṣatriyavāiśyau prabrūyātām | tathā ca kṛtvā tat samañjasaṃ bhavati yad uktaṃ brāhmaṇādhyayanam anāpatkāle vidhīyata iti | atha vāpadi śūdrādhyayanapratiṣedhārtham | itareṣāṃ **netarāv** ity etat | evaṃ cāpadi kṣatriyavaiśyāv eva prabrūyātām, na śūdraḥ | saty apy aviśeṣavacana etasminn abrāhmaṇād adhyayanaprāptiṃ śūdrasya kṛtvedam uktam, na śāstrāt | tathā ca tad yuktarūpaṃ bhavati yad uktam apāṅkteyaprakaraṇe "śūdraśiṣyo guruś caiva" iti | atha vā **netarau** sāṅgaṃ vedam adhikṛtaṃ prabrūyātām, anyat tu rājaśāstradharnurvedahastiśikṣāyurvedāhyāpahaṃ tayor na hi vāryate | tad ayuktam, adhyayanānuvāde vakṣyamāṇaprakaraṇābhisaṃbandhārthe | atha vā **prabrūyād brāhmaṇas tv eṣāṃ netarāv** ity evamartho vijñeyaḥ | tathā ca tu vyākhyātam etat | apare tv āhuḥ: ayam eva vedādhyayanavidhis trayāṇām | tat punar yuktāyuktatayā vicāraṇīyam, uktaṃ ceti | yataś caitad evam ataḥ || 10.1 ||

	**sarveṣāṃ brāhmaṇo vidyād vṛttyupāyān yathāvidhi |**

**	prabrūyād itarebhyaś ca svayaṃ caiva tathā bhavet || 10.2 ||**

vṛttaye upāyān vidyāt | atha vā vṛttiṃ ca vidyādharmaprāptyupāyāṃś ca | sarvagrahaṇaṃ cādhikārād varṇadvayāpekṣam eva | atha vā asyobhayasyāpy arthavādaḥ || 10.2 ||

	**vaiśeṣyāt prakṛtiśraiṣṭhyān niyamasya ca dhāraṇāt |**

**	saṃskārasya viśeṣāc ca varṇānāṃ brāhmaṇaḥ prabhuḥ || 10.3 ||**

viśiṣṭatvād jñānata itarebhyaḥ | atha vā pratijñaiveyam | tato 'tra kāraṇaṃ vakti: **prakṛtiśraiṣṭhyaṃ** tasya mukhodbhavatvam uktaṃ prathame 'dhyāye brāhmaṇastutau "uttamāṅgodbhavāt" ity etat | **niyamasya ca dhāraṇāt** kṛtsne vedādhyayane dhāraṇābhyāsalakṣaṇasya brāhmaṇakartṛkasyaivopadeṣāt | evaṃ cātiśayaviśeṣāpekṣād etad itarābhyāṃ vijñeyam | **saṃskārasya** ca śrautasmārtasyopanayanādeḥ śmaśānakaraṇāntasya dvijātiviṣayasya brāhmaṇahetukatvāt tasya viśiṣṭatvam | atha vālpe karmaṇy agnihotrāder ekaśatavidhasyāgner darsanena saṃpādanam aśvamedhāder vā varṇāntarakarmaṇo darśanena saṃpādanāpekṣayedam ucyate | saṃskārasya viśeṣo 'yam evamādiḥ brāhmaṇasyaiva | **ca**sabdāj jyeṣṭhopasaṃgrahaḥ prathame 'dhyāya brāhmaṇastutiprakaraṇopadiṣṭaḥ samuccīyate | yataś caivam evaṃ[lakṣaṇa]brāhmaṇasya sarvavarṇaprabhutvād adhyāpanādyadhikṛtaṃ kāryam ity arthavādaḥ || 10.3 ||

	**brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyas trayo varṇā dvijātayaḥ |**

**	caturtha ekajātis tu śūdro nāsti tu pañcamaḥ || 10.4 ||**

"adhīyīraṃs trayo varṇā[ḥ" ity atra] viśeṣa eva varṇaśabda uktaḥ yatas tadvyatirekeṇa śūdre na prāpte iṣyate ca | tasyāpi syād ity atas tadartho 'yaṃ ślokārambhaḥ | vyavahārārtho vāyaṃ brāhmaṇādīnāṃ caturṇām api varṇasaṃjñopadeśaḥ śāstre | tathā cānayā vyavahāra eṣāṃ sarvatra śāstre dṛśyate | varṇāpaśadeṣu vā vakṣyamāṇeṣu tadabhāvajñāpanārthaṃ tāvad darśayati **nāsti tu pañcama** iti | evaṃ ca saty eta eva catvāro varṇāḥ svatas siddhāḥ | katham | rasavat | yathā ṣaṭpra[kārā] rasāḥ svatas siddhāḥ | yas tu teṣāṃ parasparaṃ saṃparkād rasaviśeṣa upalabhyate, nāsau jātyantaras tebhyo bhavati, evaṃ varṇānām api parasparasaṃparkād caṇḍālādir upalabhyate | śāstre nāsau jātyantaraṃ tebhyo bhavitum arhati | brāhmaṇaśūdrāv eva varṇau pratilomataḥ saṃpṛktau yaṃ janayataḥ sa caṇḍālākhyāṃ labhate | yeṣām apy utpadyate varṇadvayasaṃparkāj jātyanatram iti pakṣaḥ, teṣām api svato nāstīti kṛtvā yuktao varṇāpaśadeṣu varṇasaṃjñāpratiṣedhaḥ | etāvāṃs tu viśeṣaḥ | utkarṣāpakarṣayos teṣāṃ karmasaṃbandhasya ca smṛtinimittatvād yathāśāstram etaddvayaṃ vijñāyate | nanu ca saṃskārānupadeśād eva śūdrasyaikajātitvaṃ siddham iti | evaṃ tarhy amantrato '[py] upanayanasaṃskārapratiṣedhārtham idam ekajātigrahaṇaṃ śūdrasya | tathā coktam "mantravarjaṃ na duṣyanti praśaṃsāṃ prāpnuvanti ca" iti | tathā saty aniyatakālādisādhanopanayanasaṃskārapratiṣedhārtham idaṃ śūdrasyaikajātigrahaṇaṃ yuktam, mā bhūt pākayajñavad asyāmantrakasya prāptir iti, uktānuvādo 'yaṃ pādapūraṇārthaḥ | evaṃ cānyapare 'sminn ekajātinirdeśe nāsti codyāvakāsaḥ | athavottarārthaḥ | tathā ca darśayati || 10.4 ||

	**sarvavarṇeṣu tulyāsu patnīṣv akṣatayoniṣu |**

**	ānulomyena saṃbhūtā jātyā jñeyās ta eva te || 10.5 ||**

**sarvavarṇeṣv** iti, na dvijātiṣv eva yathādhikṛteṣu | **tulyāsu** nārīṣu | kena | patibhiḥ | katham | tulyāsu jātitaḥ akxatayoniṣv iti śāstrata ūḍhāsv ity arthaḥ | nanu ca patnīgrahaṇād evākṣatayonitvaṃ siddham | yena yajñīyāḥ patnyo bhavanti tā akṣatayonaya eva netarāḥ | nārīśabdapāṭhe na codyam idam | patnīpāṭhe 'pi tu hetvartho 'yam akṣatayonyupadeśaḥ | patnī kasmāt, akṣatayonitvāt | guṇato 'pi ca patnīśabdo dṛṣṭaḥ | yato akṣatayonivacanaṃ mukhyārthaṃ vijñeyam | **sarvavarṇeṣu tulyāsv** ity anena c**ānulomya**grahaṇam ihānarthakaṃ sad anantaraślokārthaṃ veditavyam | ata etābhyāṃ ye saṃbhūtāḥ varṇās te **jātyā jñeyās ta eva** | **ta evety** anena pitṛvarṇagrahaṇam ity etad uktārtham, yathā brāhmaṇajātibhyāṃ mātāpitṛbhyāṃ saṃbhūto varṇas taj jātir bhavati | evaṃ kṣatriyādibhyo 'pi saṃbhūtās tajjātīyā vijñeyāḥ gavādivat | nanu caivaṃ saty avaktavyam evedaṃ jātilakṣaṇaṃ bhavati | vaktavyam eva brāhmaṇatvasyānyakāraṇanivṛttyartham | tathā cārthavādās tattvadṛṣṭisaṃvādanahetavaḥ, "vṛttastham api caṇḍālaṃ devā brāhmaṇaṃ viduḥ" ity evamādayaḥ | yato na saṃskārādhyayanavṛttādibhir brāhmaṇam, kiṃ tarhy ubhayābhijanataḥ yathāvocāmeti, jātis tv adhikaraṇakāraṇaṃ saṃskārādīnāṃ vijñeyam | na ca vṛttir evotkarṣahetuḥ | yataś ca na brāhmaṇādīnāṃ jātibhedaḥ pratyakṣo 'numeyo vā manuṣyatvāviśeṣe tadvyatiriktasaṃsthānaviśeṣānupalabdheḥ gomahiṣāśvakharādivat | evaṃ ca sati pratyakṣānumānābhyām aprāpte śāstram arthavad idaṃ bodhavyam | yathā kuśalākuśalakarmaṇoḥ puruṣavyāpārābhisaṃbandha iti | evaṃ ca samānaprasavātmakatvamātre gavādaya udāharaṇatvena jñeyāḥ | tathā cābhyupagatam etad bhavaty ekavarṇajananasaṃniyogenāyaṃ brāhmaṇatvādijātisaṃbandha iti | yady evam a[pa]tyaṃ janayitṛjātisadṛśaṃ bhavatīti manyase janayitros tarhīdaṃ jātilakxaṇam etad eva, sādhāraṇatvāt tallakṣaṇasyeti | nanv evaṃ saty anavasthā | bhavatu | ko doṣaḥ | anavasthāyām evaital lakṣaṇaṃ samarthaṃ bhavati, nānyathā, gavādivat | na caivaṃ sati dṛṣṭavirodhaḥ śāstravirodho vā | yato na kiṃcid etad iti || 10.5 ||

	**strīṣv anantarajātāsu dvijair utpāditān sutān |**

**	sadṛśān eva tān āhur mātṛdoṣavigarhitān || 10.6 ||**

kim artham idam | adhikārād anulomastutyartham | **dvijair** hi brāhmaṇādibhiḥ kṣatriyādyāsu **strīṣv anantarajātāsū**tpāditān sutān **sadṛśān eva tān āhuḥ** | kena | pitrā | na tu tajjātīyatvam eva sādṛśyavacanāt | yathā gosadṛśo gavaya iti | atra kāraṇām vakti | yasmān mātṛdoṣavigarhitās te | uktaṃ cāsmābhir jātilakṣaṇam "sarvavarṇeṣu tulyāsu" iti | ye tu mātṛsadṛśān āhuḥ teṣām etad virudhyate: **mātṛdoṣavigarhitān** iti | yasmād anulomeṣv evaitat samarthaṃ bhavati, pitṛdoṣād dhi vigarhaṇāt pratilomeṣu | evaṃ ca sati kiṃciddhīnās te pitṛbhya iti gamyate | mātṛtaś cotkṛṣṭāḥ | tathā ca satyānulomyavacanaṃ pūrvaślokoktam adhikārārthaṃ veditavyam, na tacchlokārthārthaḥ, anantarābhidhānasāmarthyād, bahuvacanāc ca, **dvijāir** iti || 10.6 ||

	**anantarāsu jātānāṃ vidhir eṣa sanatanaḥ |**

**	dvyekāntarāsu jātānāṃ dharmyaṃ vidyād imaṃ vidhim || 10.7 ||**

anulomādhikārād ayam apy ekāntaradvyantarāsu pūrvavad dharmyo **vidhir** vacanasāmarthyād vijñeyaḥ | so 'yam ekāntarāsūcyate || 10.7 ||

	**brāhmaṇād vaiśyakanyāyām ambaṣṭho nāma jāyate |**

**	[niṣādaḥ śūdrakānyāyāṃ (?) yaḥ pāraśava ucyate] || 10.8 ||**

nāmataḥ na varṇataḥ | yaḥ smṛtyantare bhṛjyakaṇṭhanāmā | dvyantarāyāṃ tu brāhmaṇād eva niṣādaḥ śūdrakanyāyām || 10.8 ||

	**[kṣatriyāc chūdrakanyāyāṃ] krūrācāravihāravān |**

**	kṣatraśūdravapur jantur ugro nāma prajāyate || 10.9 ||**

kṣatriyanimittasya krūrācāratāsya vidhīyate | evaṃ ca saty anulomyena saṃbhūtā ity ekādhikārasāmarthyān na kevalam anantarajātā evānulomā utkṛṣṭā bhavanti, "strīṣv anantarajātāsu" ity evamādivacanāt, kiṃ tarhy ekāntaradvyantarā apitṛsadṛśā mātṛdoṣavigarhaṇāt jñeyāḥ | tathā ca darśayati || 10.9

	**viprasya triṣu varṇeṣu nṛpater varṇayor dvayoḥ |**

**	vaiśyasya varṇe vaikasmin ṣaḍ ete 'pasadāḥ smṛtāḥ || 10.10 ||**

mātṛdoṣavigarhaṇāyāpaśadā ucyante | avasannā mātṛjātibhyo 'nyebhyo manuṣyebhyaḥ | evaṃ ca saty āpekṣiko 'yam apaśadas teṣu vijñeyaḥ | utkṛṣṭeṣv eva punas tripratilomahīnatayāpaśadāḥ | **apaśadā** ity apaśīrṇāḥ śadārthavān | putrakāryād hīnā ity arthaḥ | svarṇāsutāpekṣyocyante | evam anulomānantaram adhunā pratilomān āha || 10.10 ||

	**kṣatriyād viprakanyāyāṃ sūto bhavati jātitaḥ |**

**	vaiśyāṇ māgadhavaidehau rājapriprāṅganāsutau || 10.11 ||**

prātilomyena yathākramaṃ kṣatriyād brāhmaṇyāṃ sūtaḥ | visyāt kṣatriyāyāṃ māgadhaḥ| brāhmaṇyāṃ vaidehakaḥ || 10.11 ||

	**śūdrād āyogavaḥ kṣattā caṇḍālaś cādhamo nṛṇām |**

**	vaiśyarājanyaviprāsu jāyante varṇasamkarāḥ || 10.12 ||**

evaṃ prātilomyena śūdrād vaiśyāyām āyogavaḥ, kṣatriyāyāṃ kṣattā, brāhmaṇyāṃ caṇḍāla iti | atra tu śloke vaiśyarājanyayor varṇanirdeśāt strīliṅgam avivakṣitam | tadavivakṣā ca padyagranthānuvidhānena, itarathā hi strīliṅgāpāṭhe ślokabhaṅgaḥ syād iti | evam etān pratilomān uktvā tadviśeṣavivkṣayedam adhunocyate || 10.12 ||

	**ekāntare tv ānulomyād ambaṣṭhograu yathā smṛtau |**

**	kṣattṛvaidehakau tadvat prātilomye tu janmani || 10.13 ||**

ekāntarāv anulomāv ambaṣṭhograu yathā saṃsparśanādau vyavahāre avarjīyau, evaṃ pratilomāv api gantau kṣattṛvaidehakau tadvad vijñeyau | sūtamāgadhāyogavānāṃ tu **prātilomye** 'nantaratvād daṇḍāpūikayā siddhaḥ kṣattṛvaidehakābhyām utkarṣa iti | evaṃ ca caṇḍālaprayudāso 'tra vivakṣitaḥ | tathā coktam eva "divākīrt[im udaky]āṃ ca" ityevamādiḥ || 10.13 ||

	**putrā ye 'nantarastrījaḥ krameṇoktā dvijanmanām |**

**	tān anantarnāmno hi mātṛdoṣān pracakṣate || 10.14 ||**

brāhmaṇād anantarā kṣatriyā | tasyāṃ jāto varṇenānantaranāmā bhavati | mātṛjātiḥ kṣatriyaśabdenocyate | prayojanaṃ kṣatriyajāti[vihiteṣu vyavahā]reṣv asyāpi grahaṇaṃ yathā syād iti | kathaṃ ca na syāt | mātṛjātito yasmād utkṛṣṭā anulomā uktāḥ "strīṣv anantarajātāsu dvijair utpāditān sutān, sadṛśān eva tān āhur mātṛdoṣavigarhitān" [iti pūrva]śloke | ata ubhayavarṇajarjitānām ubhayatrāprāptau satyām idam āha | evaṃ kṣatriyeṇa vaiśyāyām jāto vaiśynāmā bhavati | tatprayojanaṃ coktam | nanv evaṃ sati brāhmaṇena vaiśyānām ānantaryābhāvāt tatrotpannasya vaiśyavyapadeśo na prāpnoti | evaṃ kṣatriyeṇa śūdrāyāṃ brāhmaṇena vā | naiva doṣaḥ | ānantaryasyāvivakṣitatvād aparavarṇāsu strīṣu jātāḥ santaḥ strījātināmānas te bhavantīti | evaṃ ca sati brāhmaṇakṣatriyābhyāṃ varṇadvayajānām anulomānāṃ trayāṇām upanayanādisaṃskārārtham idaṃ vijñeyam | tathā ca sati śūdrāyām utpannās trayo 'pi brāhmaṇādibhyas tannāmāno mātṛdoṣāc chūdravad asaṃskāryāḥ | evaṃ ca gautamaḥ: "pratilomās tu dharmahīnāḥ," ity uktvānantaram evāha: "śūdrāyāṃ ca," (GDh 4.25–26) anulomā apīti | idānāīṃ yatra mātṛjātitvam utkṛṣṭajāter api necchati tatremaṃ pratiṣedham ārabhate || 10.14 ||

	**brāhmaṇād ugrakanyāyām āvṛto nāma jāyate |**

na mātṛjātiḥ, kiṃ tarhi jātyantara eva:

	**ābhīro 'mbaṣṭhakanyāyām**

jāto veditavyaḥ | brāhmaṇād iti vartate | anulomastrīṣu tāvad evam utkṛṣṭatvāt | yathā cānulomastrīṣu jātyāntaram, evaṃ pratilomastrīṣv api darśayati:

		**āyogavyāṃ tu dhigvaṇaḥ || 10.15 ||**

brāhmaṇajāta eva na mātṛjātir bhavati | yathā ca brāhmaṇādibhyaḥ kṣatriyādyāsv anulomajātā mātṛnāmāno bhavanti mātṛdoṣavigarhaṇayā, evaṃ śūdrādibhyo vaiśyādyāsu jātāḥ pratilomāḥ pitṛdoṣavigarhaṇayāpi ca na tajjātīyā bhavanti, kiṃ tarhy ubhayajātivivarjitā jātyantaram | yatas tān darśayati || 10.15 ||

	**āyogavaś ca kṣattā ca caṇḍālaś cādhamo nṛṇām |**

**	prātilomyena jāyante śūdrād apaśadās trayaḥ || 10.16 ||**

yathā ca śūdrād ete trayās triṣu, evam:

	**vaiśyān māgadhavaidehau**

utkṛṣṭavarṇadvaye yathāsaṃkhyena pratilomau bhavataḥ,

		**kṣatriyāt sūta eva tu |**

evaṃ ca,

	**pratīpam ete jāyante pare'py apaśadās trayaḥ || 10.17 ||**

tathā ca nidarśanārtham anyān api darśayati:

	**jāto niṣādāc chūdrāyāṃ jātyā bhavati pulkasaḥ |**

ubhayavarjito jātyantaram | evam eva:

	**śūdrāj jāto niṣādyāṃ tu sa vai kukkuṭakaḥ smṛtaḥ || 10.18 ||**

ayaṃ niṣādo 'smiñ chloke na śūdrāyāṃ brāhmaṇāj jāto yathoktaḥ | pratilomādhikārasāmarthyāt | itarathā hi brāhmaṇajātaḥ śūdrāyāṃ yo niṣāda uktaḥ tasmāc chūdrāyāṃ jātasyānulomyāt pulkasatvam ayuktam, pratilomatvāt pulkasajāter iti | evam eva,

	**kṣattur jātas tathogrāyāṃ śvapāka iti kīrtyate |**

**	vaidehakena tv ambaṣṭhyām utpanno veṇa ucyate || 10.19 ||**

utkarṣāpakarṣau caiteṣāṃ śāstrataḥ kalpayitavyau | varṇasaṃkaraprakaraṇe cāpratilomā api saṃkīrṇayonayo vrātyāj jātā vaktavyā iti | yata idam ucyate || 10.19 ||

	**dvijātayaḥ savarṇāsu janayanty avratāsu yān |**

**	tān sāvitrīpraibhraṣṭān vrātyān ity abhinirdiśet || 10.20 ||**

sāvitrīpatitād vrātyo jāyate | na tu sāvitrīpatito vrātyo bhavati | evaṃ ca vrātyastomaprāyaścittaṃ sāvitrīpatito vrātyo bhavati | evaṃ ca vrātyastomaprāyaścittaṃ sāvitrīpatitasya na bhavati, anyat tv asya prāyaścittaṃ kalpyam | itaḥ prabhṛti caite vrātyā jātāḥ | putrapautrā vrātyā iti kecit | tad ayuktam | uktatvād vrātyalakṣaṇasyopanayanaprakarṇe, "ata ūrdhvaṃ trayo 'py ete" ityādi | tasmān nedaṃ vrātyalakṣaṇam, avratād yo jāyate sa vrātya iti, kiṃ tarhy avrata eva vrātya ity uktam | yataḥ tenāsya virodhād anartho 'yam | vipratiṣiddhaṃ caitat | yadi **dvijātayaḥ** katham avratāḥ | athāvratāḥ kathaṃ dvijātayaḥ | kathaṃ tarhy asya pā[ṭhaḥ], "dvijātayaḥ savarṇāsu janayanty avratāṃs tu yān tān sāvitrīparibhraṣṭān" — upanayanādisaṃskārakīnān — "vrātyān ity abhinirdiśet" | uktavrātyalakṣaṇānuvāda uttaraprakaraṇādisaṃbandharthaḥ | so 'ya[m eva] || 10.20 ||

	**vrātyāt tu jāyate viprāt pāpātmā bhūrjakaṇṭhakaḥ |**

**	āvantyavātadhānau ca puṣadhaś śaikha eva ca || 10.21 ||**

vrātyād viprād varṇāyām eva, tasyāḥ pūrvaśloke 'dhikṛtatvād ihāvacanāt strī[jāteḥ | tasyāṃ yo jātaḥ] sa bhūrjakaṇṭhanāmā bhavati vrātyābhijanaḥ | smṛtyantare vaiśyāyāṃ brāhmaṇāj jāto bhṛjjakaṇṭhaḥ smaryate | sa cānulomatvād apāpātmā | yataḥ idaṃ tadapekṣaṃ viśeṣaṇam ucyate: pāpātmatvam asya vrātyāj jātatvād asaṃskṛtātmanaḥ | tato 'pi brāhmaṇyām evāvantyaḥ pāpataraḥ, na tu bhūrjakaṇṭaḥ striyāṃ tasyāṃ hi jāto 'varṇas tannāma bhavati | ata idaṃ viśeṣyate | brāhmaṇyām eva | etenottarā vyākhyātāḥ: evam avantyād vātadhānaḥ pāpatamaḥ, tasmāt puṣpadhaḥ, tato 'pi śaikha iti | īṣadvikāratvād vayam nirdeśaḥ, pañcadhā brāhmaṇavrātyajātānāṃ nidarśanārtho vā | evam uttarayor api boddhavyam | kxatriyavrātyāj jātāḥ kṣatriyāyām adhunocyante || 10.21 ||

	j**hallo mallaś ca rājanyād vrātyāl licchavir eva ca |**

**	naṭaś ca karaṇaś caiva khaso draviḍa eva ca || 10.22 ||**

ete ca pūrvavad vyākaraṇīyaāḥ || 10.22 ||

	**vaiśyāt tu jāyate vrātyāt sudhanvācārya eva ca |**

**	kāruṣaś ca nijaṅghaś ca maitraḥ sātvata eva ca || 10.23 ||**

vaiśyāc ca vrātyāt sudhanvādayaḥ pūrvavad vijñeyāḥ | nāmanirdeśe ca prayojanam | ya ebhir nāmabhiḥ kasmiṃścid deśa ucyante 'varṇāḥ ta evaṃprakārā vijñeyāḥ, avijñetayonayo (?) pi santaḥ | kim arthaṃ punar antaraprabhavānām abhidhānaprakaraṇe brāhmaṇādivrātyajātā ucyante iti | yasmāt || 10.23 ||

	**vyabhicāreṇa varṇānām avedyāvedanena ca |**

**	svakarmaṇāṃ ca tyāgena jāyate varṇasaṃkaraḥ || 10.24 ||**

vyabhicāro varṇānāṃ pratilomastrīgrahaṇena mukhyaḥ, anulome 'pi mukhyavarṇāpekṣayocyate | **avedyāvedanaṃ** punar etatvilomacāripunarbhuvādistrīparigraheṇa | svakarmaṇāṃ ca tyāgaḥ upanayanasaṃskārahānir adhikṛtā[nām] | evaṃ ca sati varṇasaṃkarahetupradarśanārtham idaṃ yuktābhidhānaṃ parihārārthaṃ caiṣām || 10.24 ||

	**saṃkīrṇayonayo ye tu pratilomānulomajāḥ |**

**	anyonyavyatiṣaktāś ca pravakṣyāmy aśeṣataḥ || 10.25 ||**

anyonyavyatiṣaktānāṃ pratilomair anulomaiś caivam anulomā api vijñeyāḥ | vakṣyamāṇārthopakṣepataś cittapraṇidhānārtham | yatas tadartham ayaṃ pūrvaślokotānāṃ pratilomānām anuvāda uttarārthaḥ || 10.25 ||

	**sūto vaidehakaś caiva caṇḍālaś ca narādhamaḥ |**

**	māgadhaḥ kṣattṛjātiś ca tathāyogava eva ca || 10.26 ||**

uttaravivakṣārtham eṣāṃ punargrahaṇam | tad idam ucyate || 10.26 ||

	**ete ṣaṭ sadṛśān varṇāñ janayanti svayoniṣu |**

**	mātṛjātau prasūyante pravarāsu ca yoniṣu || 10.27 ||**

ete sūtādayas svayoniṣv eva sadṛśān janayanti | tad yathā | āyogava āyogavyām eva sadṛśaṃ janayati | yathāmbaṣṭho 'mbaṣṭhyām sadṛśāyām eva vaiśyayāṃ (?) caivātmano hīnāyāṃ vaiśyaṃ janayati | nānyasyām | evam itare 'py anulomāḥ pāraśavādayaḥ | yady api caiteṣām ambaṣṭhādīnāṃ kevalavaiśyādibhya utkarṣato viśeṣo 'sti, tathāpīdaṃ sādṛśyam ucyate, yenobhayeṣām apy eteṣāṃ vaiśyādidharmān prati viśeṣo nāsti | yata idam ucyate, svayonyāṃ mātṛjātau ca sadṛśān janayatīti | tathā coktam,

	putrā ye 'nantarastrījāḥ krameṇoktā dvijanmanām |

	tān anantaranāmnas tu mātṛdoṣān pracakṣate || iti |

āyogavādayas tu pratilomajātā **mātṛjātau prasūyamānā** **pravarāsu ca yoniṣu** dharmahīnatarān janayanti | evam ānulomyā apy ambaṣṭhādayo veditavyāḥ || 10.27 ||

	**yathā trayāṇāṃ varṇānāṃ dvayor ātmāsya jāyate |**

**	ānantaryāt svayonyāṃ tu tathā bāhyeṣv api kramaḥ || 10.28 ||**

yathā brāhmaṇakṣatriyābhyāṃ janayitṛbhyāṃ kṣatriyāvaiśyayor **ātmāsya** dvijatvaṃ **jāyate** jātaḥ sann adhikārasāmarthyād dvijo bhavati, evam eva bāhyeṣv api prātilomyena vartamāneṣu dvābhyām eva vaiśyakṣatriyābhyāṃ kṣatriyābrāhmaṇayor **ātmā** dvijatvaṃ bhavati | sati ca dvijatva upanayanādeḥ saṃskārasy[āni]ṣedhaṃ vakṣyati, "ṣaḍ ete dvijadharmāṇo bhavanti" iti | etāvāṃs tu viśeṣaḥ | yathaivānulomajātāḥ mātṛdoṣān mātṛhānyā na mātṛjātīyāḥ, evaṃ pratilomajātāḥ pitṛhānyā na pitṛjātīyāḥ | [evaṃ ca vaiśyakṣatriyābhyāṃ] prātilomyena kṣatriyābrāhmaṇyor yau māgadhasūtau tayor anulomajātābhyāṃ sāmānyāpādanaṃ stutyartham, stutiś ca vyavahārārtha | atha vā caṇḍālādipratilomaparyudāsārthā stutiḥ || 10.28 ||

	**te cāpi bāhyān subahūṃs tato 'bhyadhikadūṣitān |**

**	parasparasya dāreṣu janayanti vigarhitān || 10.29 ||**

te cāyogavādayaḥ ṣaḍ api bāhyān **subahūn** parasparasya dāreṣu, tad yathā āyogavaḥ kṣattryāṃ kṣattrāyoga[vam i]ty evaṃ janayantas **tato 'bhyadhikadūṣitān** anantarān janayanti | tad yathā āyogavaḥ kṣattryām ātmano bahyaṃ hīnataraṃ janayati | tato 'pi bāhyataraṃ caṇḍālyām | tathā kṣattā āyogavyām ātmano bāhyataraṃ janayati, tato 'pi caṇḍālyām | evaṃ caṇḍālaḥ kṣattryām ātmano bāhyataram | [evam] āyogavyām | anenaiva nyāyena māgadho vaidehyām ātmano bāhyataraṃ janayati | tato 'pi bāhyataraṃ sūtāyām | tathā vaidehako māgadhyām [ātmano] bāhyataraṃ janayati | tato bāhyataraṃ sūtāyām | tathā ca sūta ātmano bāhyataraṃ māgadhyām, tato 'pi vaidehyām | evam anena krameṇa punaḥ punar abhyāvṛttiṃ janayantaḥ parasparadāreṣu **subahūn** pañcadaśavidhān janayanti | evaṃ ca parasparasya dāreṣu vyākhyāya "cāturvarṇye" tv ācaṣṭe || 10.29 ||

	**yathaiva śūdro brāhmaṇyāṃ bāhyaṃ jantuṃ prasūyate |**

**	tathā bāhyataraṃ bāhyaś cāturvarṇye prasūyate || 10.30 ||**

tad idānīm ucyate:

	**pratikūlaṃ vartamānā bāhyā bāhyatarān punaḥ |**

**	hīnā hīnān prasūyante varṇān pañcadaśaiva tu || 10.31 ||**

eta eva ṣaṭ cāturvarṇye prasūyamānā ātmano bāhyatarān janayanti | tad yathā caṇḍālaḥ śūdrāyām ātmano hīnataraṃ janayati | tato 'pi bāhyataraṃ vaiśyāyāṃ tato 'pi kṣatriyāyāṃ tato 'pi brāhmaṇyām | evam eva kṣattā caturṣu varṇeṣu caturo janayan parasparam ātmano bāhyataraṃ janayati | tathāyogavaś caturṣu varṇeṣv evam eva navataraṃ navataraṃ janayati | ete śūdraprabhavebhyaś caṇḍālakṣattrāyogavebhyaś caturṣu varṇeṣu dvādaśa varṇabhedā jāyante | ātmānaś ca trayaś caṇḍālakṣattrayogavā[ḥ | evaṃ] śūdraprabhavāḥ pratilomena pañcadaśavarṇabhedā bhavanti | ete ca śūdraprabhavāḥ pañcadasavarṇāḥ punaḥ punaś cāturvarṇye bāhyatarān antaryakalpān janayanti | atha vaiśyaprabhavāḥ pratilomāḥ pañcadaśavarṇāḥ ucyante | vaiśyasya dvau pratilomau, ekas tv anulomajaḥ | māgadhavaidehakau kṣatriyāyāṃ brāhmaṇyāṃ ca, śūdrāyāṃ tv asyānulomajaḥ | eteṣāṃ vaiśyena śūdrāyām jāto yadā cāturvarṇye prasūyate tadā śūdrād ātmano bāhyataraṃ śūdram janayati | tato 'pi hīnataraṃ vaiśyāyām āyogavaḥ | tato 'pi hīnataraṃ kṣatriyāyāṃ kṣattā | tasmād api hīnataraṃ brāhmaṇyāṃ caṇḍālaḥ | ete tu pūrvebhyaḥ kevalaśūdraprabhavebhyaḥ utkṛṣṭatarā vijñeyāḥ | evaṃ māgadhaḥ śūdrāyāṃ janayan kevalavaiśyajātāc chūdrād dhīnataraṃ janayati | evaṃ kṣatriyāyām ātmano hīnataraṃ māgadhaṃ janayati | tathā brāhmaṇyāṃ kevalavaiśyajātād vaidehakād dhīnataraṃ janayati | evaṃ māgadhaś cāturvarṇya caturo janayati | evaṃ vaidehakasya vakṣyāmaḥ | vaidehakaḥ śūdrāyāṃ janayan kevalavaiśyajātād dhīnataraṃ janayati | evaṃ vaiśyāyāṃ kxatriyāyāṃ brāhmaṇyāṃ ca kevalavaiśyajātebhyo māgadhajātebhyaś ca hīnataraṃ janayati | evaṃ vaidehako 'pi cāturvarṇye caturo janayati | evam etebhyo vaiśyaprabhavebhyas tribhyaḥ cāturvarṇye dvādaśa bhavanti | ātmānaś ca traya iti evaṃ vaiśyaprabhavā api pañcadasavarṇā veditavyāḥ | atha kṣatriyasya vaiśyāyāṃ [śūdrāyāṃ cānulomajau], brāhmaṇyāṃ pratilomajaḥ | kṣatriyeṇa jātaḥ śūdrāyāṃ cātruvarṇye prasūyamānaḥ ugranāmā śūdrāyām ātmano hīnataraṃ janayati, vaiśyajātāt tu śūdrād utk[ṛṣṭam | tathā vaiśyāyāṃ kṣatriyāyāṃ] brahmāṇyāṃ (?) cāyogavakṣattṛ(?)caṇḍālānuttarottaraṃ hīnaṃ janayati | ete tu vaiśyaprabhavebhyaḥ āyogavādibhya utkṛṣṭatarā veditavyāḥ | evam eta ugraputrāś catvāraḥ | kṣatriyeṇa vaiśyāyāṃ jātaś cāturvarṇye prasūyamānaḥ śūdrāyām ātmano hīnataraṃ janayati | ete kṣatriyāyāṃ tu māgadhaṃ janayan[to] kevalavaiśyajātān māgadhād utkṛṣṭataraṃ janaya[n]ti | tathā brāhmanyāṃ vaidehakaṃ janayanto kevalavaiśyavaidehakād utkṛṣṭataraṃ janaya[n]ti | tathā pratilomajāḥ — kxatriyeṇa brāhmaṇyāṃ jātaḥ sūtanāmā cāturvarṇye prasūyamānaśūdrāyām ātmano hīnataraṃ janayati, māgadhavaidehakaśūdrebhyas tūtkṛṣṭam | evaṃ vaiśyāyāṃ kṣatriyāyāṃ brāhmaṇyāṃ cātmano hīnataraṃ māgadhavaidehakajātebhyas tūkṛṣṭataram | evaṃ sūtanāmā cāturvarṇye caturo janayati | evaṃ kṣatriyaputrebhyo dvādaśa, ātmānaś ca traya iti kṣatriyaprabhavāḥ pañcadasa varṇā bhavanti | brāhmaṇasya tv anulomajā eva trayaḥ | tatra pāraśavaḥ sarvaśūdrebhya utkṛṣṭas cāturvarṇye prasūyamānaḥ śūdrāyām ātmano hīnataraṃ janayati, kevalavaiśayātāc cotkṛṣṭam, kxatriyajātāt tūgrād dhīnataram | tathā vaiśyāyām ātmano hīnataraṃ janayati, vaiśyajātāc cotkṛṣṭam | kṣatriyāyāṃ tu kevalavaiśyakṣatriyābhyām utkṛṣṭataraṃ māgadhaṃ janayati | evaṃ vaidehakaṃ brāhmaṇyāṃ janayati | evam vaidehakaṃ brāhmaṇyāṃ janayan pūrvābhyāṃ kṣatriyavaiśyaprabhavābhyāṃ sūtavaidehakābhyām utkṛṣṭataraṃ janayati | evam eteṣu putrāś catvāraḥ | tathā ca kṣatriyāyāṃ brāhmaṇena jātaś cāturvarṇye prasūyamānaḥ śūdrāyāṃ putraṃ janayan ātmano hīnataraṃ janayati, kṣatriyaprabhavāt tūgrād utkṛṣṭataraṃ janayati | evam eteṣu putrāś catvāraḥ | tathā ca kṣatriyāyāṃ brāhmaṇena jātaś cāturvarṇye prasūyamānaḥ śūdrāyāṃ putraṃ janayan ātmano hīnataraṃ janayati, kṣatriyaprabhavāt tūgrād utkṛṣṭataram | tathā vaiśyāyāṃ janayann ātmano hīnataraṃ janayati, vaiśyakṣatriyajātābhyām utkṛṣṭataram | tathā kṣatriyāyām ātmano hīnataraṃ janayati, kevalakṣatriyāt tūtkṛṣṭataram | evaṃ brāhmaṇyāṃ sūtaṃ janayann ātmano hīnataraṃ janayati pūrvasūtād utkṛṣṭam | evaṃ ca brāhmaṇajātāt kṣatriyāc catvāraḥ | ta evaṃ brāhmanaprabhavebhyas tribhyo dvādaśa ātmanaś ca traya ity evaṃ brāhmaṇaprabhavāḥ pañcadaśa varṇā bhavanti | evam ete caturbhyo varṇebhyaḥ ṣaṣṭir varṇāḥ | ātmānaś catvāraḥ ity ete catuḥṣaṣṭtivarṇabhedāḥ yathāsthūlaṃ veditavyāḥ | eteṣāṃ punaḥ punar bhidyamānā asaṃkhyeyā varṇabhedāh bhavanti | tad evam "saṃkīrṇayonayo ye tu pratilomānulomajāḥ, anyonyavyatiṣaktāś ca" ity asyāyaṃ ślokasya prapañco vijñeyaḥ | varṇāpaśadā api santo varṇavad upacaryante | "iva"śabdalopena varṇā iva **vārṇāḥ** | tathā coktam: "brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyas trayo varṇā dvijātayaḥ, caturtha ekajātīyaḥ śūdro nāsti tu pañcamaḥ" iti || 10.31 ||

	**prasādhanopacārajñam adāsaṃ dāsajīvanam |**

**	sairandhraṃ vāgurāvṛttiṃ sūte dasyur āyogave || 10.32 ||**

**prasādhanopacārajñam** iti, vṛttyupadeśaḥ | adāsas san dāsyajīvanaḥ | prasādhanopacarajñatayā | paramatajīvī yasmāt | sairandhram iti varṇanāmedam | anyas tv āha, granthikāraḥ sairandraḥ draupadīdarśanāt | **vāgurāvṛttitvam** āraṇyapasuhiṃsanākhyaṃ yuktam āryāṇāṃ devapitrartham auṣadhārthaṃ ca | prāṇayātrāmātrārthaṃ vā putradārātyayam prāptasya || 10.32 ||

	**maitreyakaṃ tu vaideho mādhūkaṃ saṃprasūyate |**

**	nṝn praśaṃsaty ajasraṃ yo ghaṇṭātāḍo 'ruṇodaye || 10.33 ||**

**maitreyakaṃ** tu nāmnā maireyakaṃ vā pāṭhāntareṇa vaidehako janayati, vaiśyajāto brāhmaṇyāṃ ya uktaḥ | maitreyakaṃ ca guṇena viśinaṣṭi **mādhūkaṃ** madhurabhāṣiṇam | saṃprasūyate āyogavyām evādhikṛtāyām | tasya vṛttinirdeśaḥ: **nṝn praśaṃsaty ajasraṃ yo ghaṇṭātāḍo 'ruṇodaye**, prātar gāyaṃs tu vandanādibhiḥ || 10.33 ||

	**niṣādo mārgaraṃ sūte dāśaṃ naukarmajīvanam |**

**	kaivartam ity yaṃ prāhur āryāvartanivāsinaḥ || 10.34 ||**

niṣādo nāma brāhmaṇajātāt śūdrāt pratilomo veditavyah, pratilomādhikārasāmarthyāt | na tu brāhmaṇajātaḥ śūdrāyām | anulomatvāt | sa niṣādo 'dhikṛtāyām evāyogavyāṃ mārgaravarṇaṃ nāmnā janayati dāsadvitīyanāmānam | tasya vṛttyupadeśaḥ naukarmajīvanam iti | **kaivartam iti yaṃ prāhus** tṛtīyeṇa nāmnā **āryāvartanivāsino** jānapadāḥ | āyogavī pitṛbāhyatarā veditavyāḥ, niṣādavat, na tu śūdreṇa vaiśyāyāṃ jātā | tathā ca darśayati || 10.34 ||

	**mṛtavastrabhṛtsu nārīṣu garhitānnāśanāsu ca |**

**	bhavanty āyogavīṣv ete jātihīnāḥ pṛthak trayaḥ || 10.35 ||**

tribhyo yathopadiṣṭebhyo varṇebhyo dasyuvaidehakaniṣādebhyaḥ ślokatrayādhikṛtebhyaḥ | ye tu punaḥ "sūto dasyur āyogave" (?) ity evaṃ prathamaślokasyāntyapādaṃ paṭhanti teṣāṃ tatra kṣatriyajāto brāhmaṇyāṃ sūta uktaḥ | evaṃ sūtavaidehakaniṣādebhyaḥ evaṃvidhebhya āyogaviṣu ślokatrayopadiṣṭā nāmato varṇā jāyante || 10.35 ||

	**kārāvaro niṣādāt tu carmakāraḥ prasūyate |**

**	vaidehakād andramedau bahir grāmapratiśrayau || 10.36 ||**

vaidehyām eva jāyate iti, vakṣyamāṇaślokaliṅgān | niṣādāt kārāvaranāmā varṇaś carmakaraṇavṛttir vaidehyāṃ jāyate | vaidehakād andhramedau kārāvaraniṣādavarṇayoḥ striyoḥ, anyayor asaṃbhavād, etacchlokopadiṣṭayoś ca varṇayoḥ saṃnihitatvād, vaidehakāc ca vaidehyām andhramedayor varṇayor asaṃbhavāt pariśeṣāt kārāvaraniṣādastriyāv eva gṛhete | evaṃ hi strīvarṇabhede vaidehakād andhramedau bhinnavarṇau yuktau na tu vaidehyām || 10.36 ||

	**caṇḍālāt pāṇḍusopākas tvaksāravyavahāravān |**

**	āhiṇḍiko niṣādena vaidhyām eva jāyate || 10.37 ||**

caṇḍālād vaidehyām ekajātau varṇadvayam idaṃ pāṇḍusopākhāhiṇḍikalakṣaṇaṃ jāyate | evaṃ cātra varṇāpaśadaprakaraṇe mātṛbhedād vā ekavarṇajātayor api bhedaḥ, pitṛbhedād vā ekasyām eva striyāṃ bhedo vijñeyaḥ || 10.37 ||

	**caṇḍālena tu sopāko mūlavyasanavṛttimān |**

**	pulkasyāṃ jāyate pāpaḥ sadā sajjanagarhitaḥ || 10.38 ||**

**mūlavyasanaṃ** māraṇavṛttir ity arthaḥ | vadhyamāraṇaṃ rājadeśād anāthaśavanirharaṇaṃ tadvastrādigrahaṇaṃ pretapiṇḍabhojanam ity evamādivṛttiḥ **pulkasyāṃ caṇḍālena jāyate** || 10.38 ||

	**niṣādastrī tu caṇḍālāt putram antyāvasśyinam |**

**	śmaśānagocaraṃ sūte bāhyānām api garhitam || 10.39 ||**

śmaśānagocaras tadvṛttis tatsthānanivāsaś ca | evaṃ ca saty ayaṃ caṇḍālād api pāpataro vijñeyaḥ | tad etad ānantyāt saṃkarasya pradarśanamātraṃ vijñeyam || 10.39 ||

	**saṃkare jātayas tv etāḥ pitṛmātṛpradarśitāḥ |**

**	pracchannā vā prakāśā vā veditavyāḥ svakarmabhiḥ || 10.40 ||**

karmaṇā śāstropadiṣṭajātir anumātavyā | jātipradarśanāc ca svakarmasv ete niyojyāḥ || 10.40 ||

	**svajātijānantarajāḥ ṣaṭ sutā dvijadharmiṇaḥ |**

**	śūdrāyāṃ tu sadharmāṇaḥ sarve 'padhvaṃsajāḥ smṛtāḥ || 10.41 ||**

svajāti jās tribhyo dvijātibhyaḥ trayo brāhmaṇīkṣatriyāvaiśyāsu jātāḥ saṃskārārhāḥ tathānantarajāḥ brāhmaṇakxatriyābhyāṃ kṣatriyavaiśyayor jātāḥ **ṣaṭ sutā dvijadharmiṇaḥ** | evaṃ ca svajātijānām anantarajārthaṃ grahaṇam, na svārtham | nanu ca brāhmaṇakṣatriyābhyām anantarvarṇayoḥ kṣatriyāviśyayor jātau dvāv eva bhavataḥ, yena brāhmaṇajātaḥ vaiśyāyāṃ nānantarajaḥ | asāv apy anantaraja eva, anulomārthatvāt | dvijadharmatvaṃ pravartan nivartayati, "śūdrāyāṃ tu sadharmāṇaḥ sarve 'padhvaṃsajāḥ smṛtāḥ" iti brāhmaṇādijātā api santaḥ | evaṃ ca naibhiḥ sahedaṃ ṣaḍ grahaṇam, kiṃ tarhi svajātijaiḥ sahānantarajānām | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "pratilomās tu dharmahīnāḥ, śūdrāyāṃ ca" iti | nanu ca "putrā ye 'nantara[strī]jā" [ity atroktā]rthe 'yaṃ punaruktaḥ śloka iti. [na] punaruktaḥ | tatra hy uktam "tān anantaranāmno hi mātṛdoṣān pracakṣate" iti | anantaranāmatvaṃ cobhayathā prasajyate vyavahārārthaṃ [saṃ]jñayā, saṃskārārthaṃ ca yataḥ saṃdehanivṛttyartham idaṃ trayāṇāṃ dvijātidharmatvābhidhānam | atha vā hetvartham idaṃ pūrvaślokasya | katham | "tān anantaranāmno hi mātṛdośān pracakṣate" ity atra kāraṇaṃ vakti | yasmāt **ṣaṭ sutā** dvijadharmāṇa iti evam apunaruktatvam asya pūrvaślokād vijñeyam || 10.41 ||

	**tapobījaprabhāvaiś ca te gacchanti yuge yuge |**

**	utkarṣaṃ cāpakarṣaṃ ca manuṣyeṣv iha janmataḥ || 10.42 ||**

ayaṃ ca śloko brāhmaṇādijātānāṃ kṣatriyādyāsu pūrvaślokavihitasya saṃskārasya stutyartho vijñeyaḥ | tathā vakṣyati "śūdrāyāṃ brāhmaṇāj jātaḥ" ityevamādi | evaṃ ca saty eṣa varṇavibhāga utkarṣāpakarṣasaṃbandho manuṣyaviṣaya eva draṣṭavyaḥ | na gavādiṣu | ataś ca gavādīnāṃ matari svasari vā jātasyāparihāraḥ (?) || 10.42 ||

	**śanakais tu kriyālopād imāḥ kṣatriyajātayaḥ |**

**	vṛṣalatvaṃ gatā loke brāhmaṇādarśanena ca || 10.43 ||**

	yvabhicāreṇa varṇānām avedyāvedanena ca |

	svakarmaṇāṃ ca tyāgena jāyate varṇasaṃkaraḥ || (MDh 10.24)

iti yad uktaṃ tasya prapañco 'yam | śūdravat karmānadhikāraḥ | kriyālope cātra hetuḥ **brāhmaṇādarśanena ceti** | tadabhāvāt prāyaścittābhāvam āha | atha vobhayārthaṃ brāhmaṇādarśanaṃ kriyālopahetuḥ prāyaścittābhāvahetuś ca | apakarṣahetupradarśanaṃ ca parihārārtham | yatas te pradarśyante || 10.43 ||

	**puṇḍrakāś coḷadramilāḥ kāmbojā yavanāḥ śakāḥ |**

**	pāradā pallavāś cīnāḥ kirātā daradās tathā || 10.44 ||**

puṇḍrakādayo daradānrāḥ kṣatriyāḥ santaḥ kriyālopāc chūdrībhūtāḥ || 10.44 ||

	**mukhabāhūrupajjānāṃ yā loke jātayo bahiḥ |**

**	mlecchavācaś cāryavācaḥ sarve te dasyavaḥ smṛtāḥ || 10.45 ||**

na kevalaṃ kṣatriyāṇām, kiṃ tarhi sarvavarṇānām eva kriyālopād bāhyatvaṃ brāhmaṇādarśanena ceti | yataś caitad evam atas trayo 'py apabhraṃśahetavo yatnataḥ pariharaṇīyāḥ | te ca barvarā maṇḍikā ity evamādayaḥ | "sūte dasyur āyogave" ity atrāpy ayam eva veditavyaḥ || 10.45 ||

	**ye dvijānām apaśadā ye cāpadhvaṃsajāḥ smṛtāḥ |**

**	te ninditair vartayeyur dvijānām eva karmabhiḥ || 10.46 ||**

dvijātistrīṣu śūdrābhiḥ pratilomajātā āyogavādayaś caṇḍālavarjaṃ ye cāpadhvaṃsajāḥ śūdrāyāṃ dvijātibhir anulomā api santaḥ | tathā coktam: "śūdrāyāṃ tu sadharmāṇaḥ sarve 'padhvaṃsajāḥ smṛtāḥ" | **te ninditair vartayeyur** ātmānam | vṛttiniyamārtho 'yam upadeśas teṣām | tathā ca darśayati || 10.46 ||

	**sūtānām aśvasārathyam ambaṣṭhānāṃ ciktisitam |**

tatrāmbaṣṭhajātaḥ pratilomo gṛhyate sāmarthyāt | ambaṣṭhyāṃ vā pratilomena |

	**vaidehakānāṃ strīkāryam**

strīrakṣāntaḥpurādiṣu kāñcukīyatvena

		**māgadhānāṃ vaṇkpathaḥ || 10.47 ||**

haṃsapathavāripathākhyāḥ | evam || 10.47 ||

	**matsyaghāto niṣādānāṃ tvaṣṭir āyogavasya tu |**

**	medāndhracuñcamadgūnām āraṇyapaśuhiṃsanam || 10.48 ||**

niṣādaprabhavā bāhyāḥ niṣādaśabdena gṛhyante sāmarthyāt | tathā ca kṛtavyākhyānam etat purastād iti || 10.48 ||

	**kṣattrugrapulkasānāṃ tu bilaukavadhabandhanam |**

**	dhigvaṇānāṃ tu carmārthaṃ veṇānāṃ bhāṇḍavādanam || 10.49 ||**

**	caityadrumaśmaśāneṣu śaileṣūpananeṣu ca |**

**	vaseyur ete vijñānā vartayantaḥ svakarmabhiḥ || 10.50 ||**

**	caṇḍālaśvapacānāṃ tu nirgrāmaḥ syāt pratiśrayaḥ |**

**	apapātrāś ca kartavyā dhanam eṣāṃ svagardabham || 10.51 ||**

**	vāsāṃsi mṛtacelāni bhinnabhāṇḍeṣu bhojanam |**

**	kārṣṇāyasam alaṃkāraḥ parivrajyā ca nityaśaḥ || 10.52 ||**

**	na taiḥ samayaṃ anvicchet puruṣo dharmam ācaran |**

**	vyavahāro mithas teṣāṃ vivāhaḥ sadṛśaiḥ saha || 10.53 ||**

**	annam eṣāṃ parādhīnaṃ deyaṃ syād bhinnabhājane |**

**	rātrau na vicareyus te grāmeṣu nagareṣu ca || 10.54 ||**

**	divā careyuḥ kāryārthaṃ chinitā rājaśāsanaiḥ |**

**	abāndhavaṃ śavaṃ caiva nirhareyur iti sthitiḥ || 10.55 ||**

**	vadhyāṃś ca hanyuḥ satataṃ yathā śāstraṃ nṛpājñayā |**

**	vadhyavāsāṃsi gṛhṇīyuḥ śayyāś cābharaṇāni ca || 10.56 ||**

vṛttinivāsaprakaraṇaṃ varṇāpaśadānām evaitat | āgamābhāve cānumānataḥ etaṃ pratilomaṃ ninditakarmābhyāsasāmarthād avijñātam āgatam ity āhuḥ || 10.56 ||

	**[varṇāpetam avijñātaṃ] naraṃ kaluṣayonijam |**

**	āryarūpam ivānāryaṃ karmabhiḥ svair vibhāvayet || 10.57 ||**

**varṇebhyo** brāhmaṇādibhyo [**'petam** a]nāryaṃ **karmabhiḥ svaiḥ** **kaluṣayony**anurūpair ity arthaḥ | kāni punas tāni | yata idam ucyate || 10.57 ||

	**anāryatā niṣṭhuratā krūratā niṣkriyātmatā |**

**	puruṣaṃ vyañjayantīha loke kaluṣayonijam || 10.58 ||**

[anāryam antyajam anārya]bāṣyam imaṃ vetu [**anāryatā**] **niṣṭhuratā krūratā niṣkriyātmateti** evamādīnāṃ kaluṣayoniliṅgānāṃ nidarśanārthāny etāni nānyanivṛttyarthāni | evaṃ ca saty evamādīni **puruṣaṃ vyañjayantīha loke kaluṣayonijaṃ** mukhyakulasaṃbhūtam api | kasya punar hetoḥ | bījānuvidhānāt tatkāryāṇām | tathā darśayati || 10.58 ||

	**pitryaṃ vā bhajate śīlaṃ matur vobhayam eva vā |**

evaṃ ca loke kāryāṇāṃ kāraṇānuvidhānaṃ dṛṣṭam | yataś caitad evam ataḥ |

	**na kathaṃcana duryoniḥ prakṛtiṃ svāṃ niyacchati || 10.59 ||**

evaṃ cāgamato 'vijñātasya pratipattaye 'numānaṃ yuktam | evaṃ ca darśayati |

	**kule mukhye 'pi jātasya asya syād yonisaṃkaraḥ |**

pracchannatayāvijñātaḥ |

	**saṃśrayaty eva tac chīlaṃ naro 'lpam api vā bahu || 10.60 ||**

yathā[śvataro] rāsabhajātaḥ, tasmād avyabhicārye tadanumānaṃ vijñeyam | yathā bhadre 'nyamṛgasaṃkīrṇānāṃ jātiviśeṣāṇāṃ śāstralakṣaṇād anumānāt tadviśeṣapratipattiḥ, evam ihāpīti | asya copadeśaprayojanam | yathaivāgamato vijñātaiḥ varṇāpaśadaiḥ saha vyavahāro na kriyate, evam anumānato vijñataiḥ saheti | yataś caitad evam | ato varṇasaṃkaro rājño 'pi prayatnato rakṣaṇīyaḥ | yasmād āha || 10.60 ||

	**yatra tv ete paridhvaṃsāj jāyante varṇadūṣakāḥ |**
