ātmasthaṃ brahmabhāvanākhyaṃ yasmāt ataḥ **kāyagatam** ity arthavādo 'yam | **brāhmaṇa**grahaṇaṃ cātra ślokatraye dhāraṇārtham | anantaraśloke gauḍīmādvyoḥ brāhmaṇapratiṣedhāt tadapekṣayā | atha tu pūrvaślokapratiṣedhāpekṣo 'pi tataḥ pūrvasya pratiṣedhasyottarasya ca sāmānyenāmī ślokatrayārthavādāḥ | etasmiṃś ca pakṣe brāhmaṇagrahaṇaṃ nidarśanārthaṃ yathāsaṃbhavaṃ vijñeyam | anye tūktapratiṣiddhatvāt kṣatriyavaiśyayor vikalpaṃ manyante gauḍīmādhvyoḥ pratiṣedhasya | tad idaṃ yktam ayuktaṃ veti vicāraṇīyam, granthagauravabhayāt tu na likhyate | kiṃ cātaḥ yadi jātinimittaḥ sarvāvastham apeyam | atha madaguṇanimitte tato 'pi naṣṭe tasminn alpaṃ vā peyaṃ syāt | yata idam ucyate guṇanimitto 'yaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ | evaṃ sati pratyastamitamadaguṇaṃ dayaṃ kutracid ācaranti brāhmaṇāḥ | tathā coktam: "amedhye vā paten mattaḥ" ity evamādiṣu madaguṇanimitta eva pratiṣedho madyasyeti vijñayate | anutpannamadaguṇaṃ ca mādhvīkam aparyuṣitaṃ ca pīyate | yataḥ guṇāpekṣa eva pratiṣedhaḥ | [an]ye 'pi ca nācaranti vinaṣṭamadaguṇam api san madyam | tathā ca vakṣyat "surābhāṇḍasthitas tathā" ity evamādi || 11.96 ||

	**eṣā vicitrābhihitā surāpānasya niṣkṛtiḥ |**

**	ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi suvarṇasteyaniṣkṛtim || 11.97 ||**

upasaṃhāropanyāsārthaḥ slokaḥ || 11.97 ||

	**suvarṇasteyakṛd vipro rājānam abhigamya tu |**

**	svakarma khyāpayan brūyān māṃ bhavān anuśāstv iti || 11.98 ||**

**	gṛhītvā musalaṃ rājā sakṛd dhanyāt tu taṃ svayam |**

**	vadhena śudhyati steno brāhmaṇas tapasaiva vā || 11.99 ||**

**	tapasāpanunutsus tu suvarṇasteyajaṃ phalam |**

**	cīravāsā dvijo 'raṇye cared brahmahaṇo vratam || 11.100 ||**

tribhiḥ ślokaiḥ suvarṇasteyaprāyaścittavidhiḥ | kṣatriyādīnāṃ ca viśeṣeṇa prāyaścittavidher anāmnātatvāt **suvarṇasteyakṛd vipra** iti yad idaṃ vipragrahaṇam etat sarvavarṇapradarśanārthaṃ vijñeyam | tathā "brāhmaṇas tapasaiva vā" iti yad uktam atredam ucyate | na hi tapaś śakyate kṣatriyādivarṇānāṃ pratiṣeddhum | apare tv etasmād yatnāt brāhmaṇasyāivaikasya tapaḥ netareṣāṃ varṇānām iti manyante | rājābhigamanasya ca rājadharmeṣu siddhasyāpi sataḥ punar ihopadeśaḥ prāyaścittārthaḥ, tatra ca rājadaṇḍārthaḥ, tapovidhitsayā vā punargrahaṇam | brāhmaṇasya ca vadho nāstīti tatraivoktam | nigadavyākhyātam anyat || 11.98–100 ||

	**etair vratair apoheta pāpaṃ steyakṛtāṃ naraḥ |**

**	gurustrīgamanīyaṃ tu vratair ebhir apānudet || 11.101 ||**

upasaṃhāropanyāsaḥ pūrvottaraprakaraṇayoḥ || 11.101 ||

	**gurutalpy abhibhāṣyainas tapte svapyād ayomaye |**

**	sūrmīṃ jvalantīṃ svāśliṣyen (?) mṛtyunā sa visudhyati || 11.102 ||**

**	svayaṃ vā śiśnavṛṣaṇāv utkṛtyādhāya cāñjalau |**

**	nairṛtīṃ diśam ātiṣṭhed ā nipātād ajihmagaḥ || 11.103 ||**

**	khaṭvāṅgī cīravāsā vā smaśrulo nirjane vane |**

**	prājāpatyaṃ caret kṛcchram abdam ekaṃ samāhitaḥ || 11.104 ||**

**	cāndrāyaṇaṃ vā trīn māsān abhyasen niyatendriyaḥ |**

**	haviṣyeṇa yavāgvā vā gurutalpāpanuttaye || 11.105 ||**

caturbhiḥ ślokaiḥ gurutalpaprāyaścittam idaṃ vaikṛtikam | **gurur** vyākhyāto vidyāguruḥ svayoniguruś ca | tadaṅganāṃ gato gurutalpaga iti guṇatas talpaśabdo gurubhāryāyāṃ vijñeyaḥ | haviṣyayavāgvoś ca grahaṇaṃ gobalīvardanyāyena | ṛjv anyat || 11.102–105 ||

	**etair vratair apoheyur mahāpātakino malān |**

**	upapātakinas tv evaṃ vividhair niyamair imaiḥ || 11.106 ||**

**	upapātakasaṃyukto goghno māsaṃ yavān pibet |**

**	kṛtavāpo vased goṣṭhe carmaṇā tena saṃvṛtaḥ || 11.107 ||**

**	caturthakālam aśnīyād akṣāralavaṇaṃ mitam |**

**	gomūtreṇa caret snānaṃ dvau māsau niyatendriyaḥ || 11.108 ||**

**	divānugacchet gās tās tu tiṣṭhann ūrdhvaṃ rajaḥ pibet |**

**	śuśrūṣitvā namaskṛtvā rātrau vīrāsano bhavet || 11.109 ||**

**	[tiṣṭhantīṣv anutiṣṭhet tu vrajantīṣv apy anuvrajet |**

**	āsīnāsu tathāsīno niyato vītamatsaraḥ || 11.110 ||**

**	āturām abhiśastāṃ vā vauravyāghrādibhir bhayaiḥ |**

**	patitāṃ paṅkalagnāṃ vā sarvopāyair vimocayet] || 11.111 ||**

**	uṣṇe varṣati śīte vā mārute vāti vā bhṛśam |**

**	na kurvītātmanas trāṇaṃ gor akṛtvā tu śaktitaḥ || 11.112 ||**

**	ātmano yadi vānyeṣāṃ gṛhe kṣetre 'tha vā khale |**

**	bhakṣayantīṃ na kathayet pibantaṃ caiva vatsakam || 11.113 ||**

**	anena vidhinā yas tu goghno gā anugacchati |**

**	sa gohatyākṛtaṃ pāpam tribhir māsair vyapohati || 11.114 ||**

kecit tu tribhir varṣair iti paṭhanti | tad ayuktam | adhastād atraiva prāyaścittaprakaraṇe māsatrayagrahaṇāt | sarvopapātakeṣu caitad eva vrataṃ kuryur iti vakṣyati cāndrāyaṇavaikalpikam avakīrṇivarjam | evaṃ ca varṣatrayeṇāsyāsamānavidhitvād anyāyyakalpaneyam || 11.106–114 ||

	**vṛṣabhaikādaśā gāś ca dadyāt sucaritavrataḥ |**

**	avidyamāne sarvasvaṃ vedavidbhyo nivedayet || 11.115 ||**

avidyamānāyām anantaradakṣiṇāyāṃ caritaprāyaścittasya sarvasvaṃ dakṣiṇā tac caikādaśabhyo gorūpebhyaḥ sarvasvam arvāg iti sāmarthyād gamyate | gāvo 'nyad vobhayaṃ vā || 11.115 ||

	**etad eva vrataṃ kuryur upapātakino dvijāḥ |**

**	avakīrṇivarjyaṃ śuddhyarthaṃ cāndrāyaṇam athāpi vā || 11.116 ||**

etad eva goghātaprāyaścittaṃ sarvopapātakeṣv atidiśyate | tadvikalpena cāndrāyaṇam eva | evaṃ ca sati gohatyāyāś cāndrāyaṇaṃ na syāt, tadvaikalpikasāmarthyāt, yathānyeṣūpapātakeṣu | ata eva pṛthaṅnirdeśaḥ | avakīrṇivarjyam iti cānena pratiṣedhaliṅgena govadhādau yad uktā vratāḥ syur iti tad avakīrṇino grahaṇam iti vijñāyate || 11.116 ||

	**avakīrṇī tu kāṇena gardabhena catuṣpathe |**

**	pākayajñavidhānena yajeta nirṛtiṃ niśi || 11.117 ||**

**	hutvāgnau vidhivad dhomān antataś ca samety ṛcā |**

**	vātendragurugahnīnāṃ juhuyāt sarpiṣāhutīḥ || 11.118 ||**

avakīrṇīpadārthaṃ prāyaścittanimittam avadhārayati || 11.117–118 ||

	**kāmato retasaḥsekaṃ vratasthasya dvijanmanaḥ |**

**	atikramaṃ vratasyāhur dharmajñā brahmavādinaḥ || 11.119 ||**

evaṃ cākāmato divā rātrau vā pracyutendriyasya laghutaraṃ prāyaścittaṃ syāt | tato 'pi svapna iti | tathā coktaṃ svapne retaḥseke brahmacāriṇaḥ "punar mām ity ṛcaṃ japet" iti || 11.119 ||

	**mārutaṃ puruhūtaṃ ca guruṃ pāvakam eva ca |**

**	caturo vratino hy eti brāhmaṃ tejo 'vakīrṇinaḥ || 11.120 ||**

yata evam ato 'vakīrṇī,

	**etasminn enasi prāpte vasitvā gardabhājinam |**

**	saptāgāraṃ cared bhaikṣaṃ svakarmaparikīrtayan || 11.121 ||**

**	tebhyo labdhena bhakṣeṇa vartayann ekakālikam |**

**	upaspṛśaṃs triṣavaṇam abdenaikena śudhyati || 11.122 ||**

vedabrahmacāriṇaḥ strīgamana etat prāyaścittaṃ vijñeyam | evaṃ ca samānakāryatvāt pravrajitānām apy evaṃvidham eva retaḥsekaprāyaścittaṃ pravrajyāvirodhi syāt | teṣāṃ ca skhalitānām anyaprāyaścittānupadeśāt || 11.121–122 ||

	**jātibhraṃśakaraṃ karma kṛtvānyatamam icchayā | **

**	caret sāntapanaṃ kṛcchraṃ prājāpatyam anicchayā || 11.123 ||**

sāntapanaṃ kṛcchraṃ prājāpatyaṃ ca vakṣyati || 11.123 ||

	**saṃkarāpātrakṛtyāsu māsaḥ śodhanam aindavaḥ |**

**	malinīkaraṇīyeṣu taptaḥ syād yāvakais tryaham || 11.124 ||**

anyatamam iti vartate | evaṃ cecchayā pratyekaṃ guruprāyaścittopadeśair aniccayā tasya laghutvam arthasiddham pūrvaśāstrād eva || 11.124 ||

	**turīyo brahmahatyāyāḥ kṣatriyasya vadhe smṛtaḥ |**

**	vaisye 'ṣṭamo 'ṃśo vṛttasthe śūdre jñeyas tu ṣoḍaśaḥ || 11.125 ||**

kṣatriyādīnām aparaḥ prāyaścittavidhir vaikalpika upapātakaprāyaścittāc cāndrāyaṇāt | yena strīśūdraviṭkṣatravadha upapātakamadhya upadiṣṭaḥ | sadasadvibhāgāpekṣayā ca kṣatriyādīnām idaṃ vaikalpikam anyat prāyaścittaṃ pūrvoktāt | tathā coktam, **vaiśya 'ṣṭamo 'ṃśo vṛttastha** iti | idaṃ param adhunā kxatriyādivadha eva kxatriyādiprāyaścittam upadiśyate, pūrvaślokopadiṣṭaprāyaścittād vaikalpikam || 11.125 ||

	**akāmatas tu rājanyaṃ vinipātya dvijottamaḥ |**

**	vṛṣabhaikasahasrā gā dadyāc chuddhyartham ātmanaḥ || 11.126 ||**

arthāc cedaṃ vittavataḥ prāyaścittam upadiśyate | pūrvaṃ cāvittasya tapaḥ | vakṣyati ca dānaṃ tasya [ca] tapasā vikalpaṃ "dānena vadhanirṇekaṃ sarpādīnām aśknuvan" ity evamādi | **akāmata** ity ayaṃ ca pramādastutyartho 'rthavādaḥ | yasmān na hy akāmato garīyaḥ prāyaścittam upapadyata ity uktaṃ purastāt | evaṃ tāvat saṃbhavadvittasya prāyaścittam idam anyad | daridrasya pūrvoktam anūdyate vaikalpikam etasya || 11.126 ||

	**tryabdaṃ cared vā niyato jaṭilo brahmahavartam |**

**	vasan dūratare grāmād vṛkṣamūlaniketanaḥ || 11.127 ||**

**jaṭila**vacanaṃ niyamārthatvād anyeṣāṃ khaṭvāṅgītyevamādīnāṃ nivṛttyartham || 11.127 ||

	**etad eva cared abdaṃ prāyaścittaṃ dvijottamaḥ |**

**	pramāpya vaiśyaṃ vṛttasthaṃ dadyād vaikaśataṃ gavām || 11.128 ||**

saṃbhavadvittasyedaṃ pūrvavad vaikalpikam | dvijottamagrahaṇaṃ cetaravarṇanidarśanārtham, nāvadhāraṇārtham || 11.128 ||

	**pramāpya śūdraṃ ṣaṇmāsān etad eva vratam caret |**

**	vṛṣabhaikādaśā vāpi dadyād viprāya gāḥ sitāḥ || 11.129 ||**

uktārthaḥ ślokaḥ | sitavarṇāgrahaṇaṃ cātra śuddhisāmānyāt | evaṃ ca trīṇy etāni prāyaścittāni kṣatriyādivadhe vikalpyante | pūrvoktaṃ cāndrāyaṇam iha ca prakaraṇe godānam | brahmahatyāprāyaścittavikalpaś ca kāmakṛtaḥ | kecit tu samuccayam etayor asmin prakaraṇa upadiṣṭayoḥ prāyaścittaṃ manyante | samuccayena ślokān paṭhanti "tryabdaṃ carec ca niyataḥ", tathā "pramāpya vaiśyaṃ vṛttasthaṃ dadyāc caikaśataṃ gavām" | evam eva vṛṣabhaikādaśāgāś cāpīti | tad etad ayuktaṃ śāstranyāyavirodhāt, etasyāṃ ca kalpanāyām upapātakaprāyaścittaṃ cāndrāyaṇaṃ laghu nopapadyeta, guruṇaḥ prāyaścittasya dānatapaḥsamuccayasyopadeśena | tathā ca loke vyavahāraḥ: "paṇalbhyaṃ hi na prājñaḥ krīṇāti daśabiḥ paṇaiḥ" iti | vaikalpikayor eva tāvad etayor upadeśe cāndrāyaṇasyānarthakyaṃ prāpnotīti | kiṃ punaḥ samuccitayoḥ | atyantagurutvā | tasmāt samuccayābhāvād **vā**śabdo vikalpārthaḥ paṭhitavyaḥ|| 11.129 ||

	**mārjāranakulau hatvā cāṣaṃ maṇḍūkam eva ca |**

**	śvagodholūkakākāṃś ca śūdrahatyāvrataṃ caret || 11.130 ||**

samuccitānāṃ vadha etat prāyaścittam | tathā ca vakṣyati "asthimatāṃ tu sattvānāṃ sahasrasya pramāpane" iti | apare tu laghutvād eteṣāṃ śūdrajātānāṃ pratilomānām āyogavakṣattṛcaṇḍālānāṃ yad vadhe prāyaścittaṃ tad etat samastavadha iti | pratyekaṃ tu vadha idam anyat prāyaścittaṃ pūrvasmāl laghūpadiśyate || 11.130 ||

	**payaḥ pibet trirātraṃ vā yojanaṃ vādhvano vrajet |**

asamarthaḥ sann adhvagamanasyātyantavṛddho gamyate |

	**upaspṛśet sravantyāṃ vā sūktaṃ vābdaivataṃ japet || 11.131 ||**

samudragāminyāṃ viśiṣṭāyāṃ snāyād ity arthaḥ | sapariṣkarasnānopadeśaparataś caitat sāmarthyād viśiṣṭam upadiśyate | **sūktaṃ vābdaivataṃ japet** | sarveṣu ca payaḥpānaṃ sāmarthyād upavāso vā trirātraṃ sapratyayāpratyayavadhopekṣayā || 11.131 ||

	**abhriṃ kārṣṇāyasīṃ dadyāt sarpaṃ hatvā dvijottamaḥ |**

**	palālabhārakaṃ ṣaṇḍe saisakaṃ caikamāṣakam || 11.132 ||**

palālenāsya māṣakasya ca samuccaya ānantaryasāmarthyād vijñeyaḥ | nābhryā | palālaṃ cārthāt gave gopataye vā brāhmaṇāya || 11.132 ||

	**ghṛtakumbhaṃ varāhe tu tiladroṇaṃ tu tittirim |**

**	śukaṃ dvihāyanaṃ vatsaṃ krauñcaṃ hatvā trihāyanam || 11.133 ||**

**	hatvā haṃsaṃ valākāṃ ca bakaṃ barhiṇam eva ca |**

**	vānaraṃ śyenabhāsau ca sparsayed brāhmaṇāya gām || 11.134 ||**

samastavadha etat prāyaścittaṃ vibhāgānupadeśāt, goś ca mahattvāt, yathā "mārjāranakulau hatvā" ity evamādi | yatra samastānām apy upadeśe pratyekam icchati tatra pṛthag grahaṇaṃ karoti | tathā copariṣṭāt pradarśayiṣyāmaḥ || 11.133–134 ||

	**vāso dadyād dhayaṃ hatvā pañca nīlān vṛṣān gajam |**

**	ajameṣāv anaḍvāhaṃ kharaṃ hatvaikahāyanam || 11.135 ||**

nigadavyākhyātaślokaḥ | ajāvikavadhaś ca saṃkīrṇakara uktaḥ | evaṃ ca tadīyaṃ prāyaścittam **ajameṣāv anaḍvāham** ity anenopadeśasāmarthyād vikalpeta | evam anyatrāpi yojyam || 11.135 ||

	**kravyādāṃs tu mṛgān hatvā**

vyāghrādīn

		**dhenuṃ dadyāt payasvinīm** |

dhenūpadeśād eva payaḥ siddham | evaṃ ca siddhasyopadeśo 'tiśayārtho vijñeyaḥ,

	**akravyādān vatsatarīm uṣṭraṃ hatvā tu kṛṣṇalam || 11.136 ||**

**	jīlakārmukabastāvīn pṛthag dadyād viśuddhaye |**

**	caturṇām api varṇānāṃ nārīr hatvānavasthtāḥ || 11.137 ||**

jīlaṃ carmapuṭaṃ dadyāt | brāhmaṇāya tadupabhogadeśe | brāhmaṇīm anavasthitāṃ hatvā | kṣatriyāṃ **kārmukaṃ** brāhmaṇāyaiva | tadbhṛtyāpaharaṇaṃ rakṣārthaṃ brāhmaṇatantrasya | vaiśyāṃ **bastam**, śūdrām **avim** | **pṛthag**grahaṇāc cātrānyatra samudāyeṣu prāyaścittaṃ na pṛthagbhāvād iti vijñeyam | gatveti kecit | na yuktam, tad dhiṃsāprakaraṇān **nārīr hatvānavasthitā** iti pāṭhāt | tathā copasaṃhāraṃ prakaraṇānte kariṣyati, "etair vratair apohyaṃ syād eno hiṃsāsamudbhavam" iti || 11.136–137 ||

	**dānena vadhanirṇekaṃ sarpādīnām aśaknuvan |**

**	ekaikaśaś caret kṛcchraṃ dvijaḥ pāpāpanuttaye || 11.138 ||**

anena ca gamyate prāyaścitteṣu dānaṃ prathamakalpikam, yena tadabhāve kṛcchram iha śāsti || 11.138 ||

	**asthanvatāṃ tu sattvānāṃ sahasrasya pramāpaṇe |**

**	pūrṇe cānasy anasthnāṃ tu śūdrahatyāvrataṃ caret || 11.139 ||**

samudāyahiṃsāṃ parijñāyāsthimatāṃ ca śūdrasyāvṛttasya hiṃsāyāṃ yat prāyaścittaṃ tac caret | eteṣām eva pratyekaṃ hiṃsāyām adhunocyate || 11.139 ||

	**kiṃcid eva tu viprāya dadyād asthimatāṃ vadhe |**

pratyekam ity asyārambhasāmarthyād vijñāyate |

	**anasthnāṃ caiva hiṃsāyāṃ prāṇāyāmena śudhyati || 11.140 ||**

kṛmikīṭavayohatyā malinīkaraṇeṣūktāḥ | evaṃ ca sati tadīyaṃ prāyaścittaṃ samānāśrayatvād anena vikalpena || 11.140 ||

	**phaladānaṃ tu vṛkṣāṇāṃ chedane japyam ṛksatam |**

**	gulmavallīlatānāṃ ca puṣpitānāṃ ca vīrudhām || 11.141 ||**

etac cāyajñīye chedana eṣāṃ prāyaścittam | tathā ca vakṣyati "vṛthālambhe 'nugacched gām" ity evamādiḥ || 11.141 ||

	**annādyajānāṃ sattvānāṃ rasajānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ |**

**	phalapuṣpodbhavānāṃ ca ghṛtaprāśo viśodhanam || 11.142 ||**

pūrvao 'sthimadanasthimadvidhir annādijātebhyo 'nyatra vijñeyaḥ, asyārambhasāmarthyāt || 11.142 ||

	**kṛṣṭajānām oṣadhīnāṃ jātānāṃ ca svayaṃ vane |**

**	vṛthālambhe 'nugacched gāṃ dinam ekaṃ payovrataḥ || 11.143 ||**

**	etair vratair apohyam syād eno hiṃsāsamudbhavam |**

**	jñānājñānakṛtaṃ kṛtsnaṃ śṛṇutānādyabhakṣaṇe || 11.144 ||**

upasaṃhāropanyāsārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 11.144 ||

	**ajñānād vāruṇīṃ pītvā saṃskāreṇaiva śudhyati |**

**	matipūrvam anirdeśyaṃ prāṇāntikam iti sthitiḥ || 11.145 ||**

taptakṛcchrasahitena punaḥsaṃskāreṇa śudhyatīty etad gautamād vijñāyate, na saṃskāreṇa mātreṇa tasyātyantālpatvāt | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "amatyā madyapāne payo ghṛtam udakaṃ vāyuṃ pratitryahaṃ taptāni sa kṛcchras tato 'sya saṃskāraḥ" (GDh 23.2) iti | ihāpi cābhakṣyaprkaraṇe kṛcchra uktaḥ, mūtrādiprāśane sapratyaye "matyā bhuktvācaret kṛcchraṃ reto viṇmūtram eva ca" iti | sa ca taptakṛcchro gautamīyād eva | atra punaḥsaṃskāraḥ sahakāritvena prāyascittatayā vijñāyate | evaṃ ca sati na mukhyasurāyāḥ paiṣṭyā amatyā pāna etat prāyascittam, kiṃ tarhi gauḍīmādvyor amatyā pāne, tatpratyāsatteḥ | tathā ca tatra gauḍīmādhvyor [matyā pā]ne kaṇapiṇyākam abdaṃ prāyaścittam uktam, na paiṣṭyaṃ prāṇāntikaprāyaścittavaikalpikam | itarathā hi samānārthatve ko daivaśapto laghuprāyaścittaṃ parityajya kaṇādibhakṣaṇam atyantābhipretamūlaharaṃ prāṇāntikaṃ kuryāt | tathā ca smṛtyantaram: "[a]surāmadyapāne cāndrāyaṇam abhyaset" iti | evaṃ ca sati mukhyasurāpānaprāyaścittasya prāṇāntikākhyasyānena laghunātyantaviprakarṣāt, gauḍīmādhvyor evāmatyāpāna etat prāyaścittam | na ca sapratyayāpratyayavyatikramaprāyaścittayor ekaviṣayayor ivābheda upapadyate | yathānyatra | etc ca sakṛt pāne asurāmadyayoḥ prāyaścittaṃ sāmarthyād vijñāyate | tathā ca smṛtyantaram:

	pramādān madyam asurāṃ sakṛt pītvā dvijottamaḥ |

	gomūtrayāvakāhāro daśarātreṇa śudhyati || iti |

**matipūrvaṃ** tu gauḍīmādhvayoḥ pānam abhyasataḥ **anirdeśyam** idaṃ prāyaścittam | kiṃ tarhy asyānyat prāṇāntikam eva sapratyayābhyāsadoṣādhikyena yathā paiṣṭyāḥ iti | etasmād eva ca sāmarthyān mukhyasurāpāne 'py apratyaye sapratyayaprāyaścittād īṣad ūnaṃ prāyascittāntaram utprekṣyam | tathā ca vakṣyati: "śaktiṃ cāvekṣya pāpaṃ ca prāyaścittam prakalpayet" iti || 11.145 ||

	**apaḥ surābhājanasthā madyabhāṇḍasthitās tathā |**

**	pañcarātraṃ pibet pītvā śaṅkhapuṣpīśritaṃ payaḥ || 11.146 ||**

**apaḥ surābhājanasthāḥ pītvā** kasya tatra pratiṣedhaḥ, yathāsaṃbhavaṃ dvijāteḥ | **pañcarātraṃ pibec chaṅkhapuṣpīśritaṃ payaḥ** | evaṃ cāsyānyāhārapratiṣedhaḥ | rasasya cāgrahaṇa idaṃ prāyaścittam | rasasya grahaṇe surāpānaprāyaścittam eva nyāyyam | asurāmadyabhāṇḍasthitās tv apaḥ pītvā tadūnaṃ nyāyyaṃ prāyaścittam | tathā ca kṛtavibhāgaprāyaścitte te mukhyāmukhyasure pūrvatra, tatsāmarthyād ihāpi prāyaścittayoḥ pūrvavad gurulaghutvavibhāgo vijñeyaḥ, tathā vibhāgavyākhyayā || 11.146 ||

	**spṛṣṭvā dattvā ca madirāṃ vidhivat pratigṛhya ca |**

**	śūdrocchiṣṭāś ca pītvāpaḥ kuśavāri pibet tryaham || 11.147 ||**

**vidhivac**chabdaḥ pratigraheṇaiva saṃbadhyate svastivacanādinā | atha vā dāne 'py eṣa eva vidhir jñeyaḥ, brāhmaṇasya surāpratigrahe | tatpratiṣiddhācaraṇe kusavāripānaṃ tryaham | pūrvavac cāhārapratiṣedhaḥ | śūdrocchiṣṭānāṃ cāpāṃ pāna etad eva syāt prāyaścittam | annasya tu śūdrocchiṣṭasyānyat prāyaścittaṃ vakṣyati: "saptarātraṃ yavān pibet" iti | na cātrāgamapramāṇe 'rthe nyāyāvatāro 'sti, yataḥ nātiśaṅkya eṣa śūdrocchiṣṭaprāyaścittavikalpaḥ || 11.147 ||

	**brāhmaṇas tu surāpasya gandham āghrāya somapaḥ |**

**	prāṇān apsu trir āyamya ghṛtaṃ prāśya viśuddhyati || 11.148 ||**

**surāpasya** surā**gandham** **āghrāy**aitat prāyaścittm kuryāt, nānyam | taccharīragandham | evaṃ ca surāyānyatrāvasthitāyā api gandhopalabdhāv etad eva prāyaścittam etasmāt sāmarthyād vijñāyate | somapāśabdaviśeṣaṇena cāsomapānāṃ brāhmaṇānām atra laghutaraṃ prāyaścittaṃ syāt || 11.148 ||

	**ajñānāt prāśya viṇmūtraṃ surāsaṃspṛṣṭam eva ca |**

**	punaḥ saṃskāram arhanti trayo varṇā dvijātayaḥ || 11.149 ||**

surāsaṃspṛṣṭaṃ casati rasagrahaṇe vijñeyam | etasmin vyabhicāre punaḥ saṃskāraḥ dvijātīnāṃ smṛtyantarasāmarthyāc ca sataptakṛcchraḥ | tathā ca gautamīyam atropasaṃharaṇīyam (?): "mūtrapurīṣaretasāṃ ca prāśane" (GDh 23.3) iti etat | evaṃ ca sati taptakṛcchrapunaḥsaṃskārau samuccitau prāyaścittam, na punaḥ saṃskāramātram | atyantalaghutvād, ihāpi ca "matyā bhuktvācaret kṛcchraṃ reto viṇmūtram eva ca" ity uktam abhojyaprakaraṇe | ata brūyāt tatra matipāna ukto mūtrādīnāṃ kṛcchraḥ, iha tv amatyeti | satyam etat, kalpāntaratvāt tu sapratyayāpratyayavyatikramayor avirodha iti | punaḥsaṃskāragarhaṇāc ca sarvasmiṃs taddharme prāpta idaṃ niyamārtham ārabhyate || 11.149 ||

	**vapanaṃ mekhalā daṇḍo bhaikṣacaryā vratāni ca |**

**	nivartante dvijātīnāṃ punaḥ saṃskārakarmaṇi || 11.150 ||**

nigadavyākhyātaḥ ślokaḥ || 11.150 ||

	**abhojyānāṃ tu bhuktvānnaṃ strīśudrocchiṣṭam eva ca |**

**	jagdhvā māṃsam abhakṣyaṃ ca saptarātraṃ yavān pibet || 11.151 ||**

patigrahaṇe ca tatstrīgrahaṇe dvijātinirdeśasāmarthyād eva siddhe punas tadgrahaṇaṃ sarvavarṇārtham idaṃ vijñeyam | eṣu **saptarātraṃ yavān pibet** | atra ca pānopadeśād yavaiḥ piṣṭair yavāgur upadisyate, yena dravadravyasādhanā hi pānakriyā | abhojyaś ca snātakavratakādhyāye vyākhyātaḥ || 11.151 ||

	**śuktāni ca kaṣāyāṃś ca pītvā medhyāny api dvijaḥ |**

**	tāvad bhavaty aprayato yāvat tan na vrajaty adhaḥ || 11.152 ||**

**medhyāni** yāni pratiṣiddhāni | atra cāpakaraṇam eva prāyaścittaṃ nāyat || 11.152 ||

	**viḍvarāhakhroṣṭrāṇāṃ gomayoḥ kapikākayoḥ |**

**	prāśya mūtrapurīṣāṇi dvijaś cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret || 11.153 ||**

amatyā prāśanam eṣām etad adhikārāt | tathā cottaraśloke vikṣyati: "ajñātaṃ caiva sūnāstham" iti | matipūrve tu prāśana eṣāṃ gurutaraṃ prāyaścittaṃ prakalpyaṃ pariṣadā || 11.153 ||

	**śuṣkāṇi bhuktvā māṃsāni bhaumāni kavakāni ca |**

**	ajñātaṃ caiva sūnāstham etad eva vrataṃ caret || 11.154 ||**

dvijaś cāndrāyaṇaṃ cared iti dvijagrahaṇāt prakaraṇāc cātra śūdrasya vyatikrame prāyaścittābhāvaḥ | brāhmaṇāpāśritaśūdrasya hi "yathā yathā hi sadvṛttam ātiṣṭhanty anusūyakaḥ" iti vacanāt pākṣikaṃ syāt prāyaścittaṃ pratiṣedhāt || 11.154 ||

	**kravyādasūkaroṣṭrāṇāṃ kukkuṭānāṃ ca bhakṣaṇe |**

**	narakākakharāṇāṃ ca taptakṛcchro viśodhanam || 11.155 ||**

**kravyādā** gṛdhrādayaḥ, **sūkaro** viḍvarāhaḥ, **kharā**disāhacaryād gamyate | evaṃ kukkṭo grāmakukkuṭo vijñeyaḥ | tasya pratiṣedhāt pūrvatra, kharādisāhacaryād vā | evaṃ ca māṃsabhakṣaṇapratiṣedho vijñeyaḥ | tatra mūtrapurīṣaṃ pratiṣiddham viḍvarāhaśloke | yeṣām api kravyādaprabhṛtīnāṃ tatra mūtrapurīṣam apratiṣiddham, teṣām apīha kharādisāhacaryāt pratiṣiddhaṃ tad vijñeyam || 11.155 ||

	**māsikānnaṃ tu yo 'śnīyād asamāvartako dvijaḥ |**

**	sa trīṇy ahāny upavased ekāhaṃ codake vaset || 11.156 ||**

svayaṃprārthanayā prārthitasyaitat prāyaścittaṃ **māsikānna**bhojane | yasmād uktam "kāmam abhyarthito 'śnīyāt" ity evamādi itarathā hi vihitapratiṣedhaḥ prasajyeta | tathā coktam, "vratastham api dauhitraṃ kāmaṃ śrāddhaṃ niyojayet" iti | evaṃ saty asmāt prāyascittopadeśāt viśeṣapratiṣedho 'yaṃ vijñeyaḥ | nātyantapratiṣedhaḥ || 11.156 ||

	**vratacārī tu yo 'śnīyān madhu māṃsaṃ kathaṃcana |**

**	sa kṛtvā prākṛtaṃ kṛcchraṃ vrataseṣaṃ samāpayet || 11.157 ||**

śrāddhe, anyatra vā || 11.157 ||

	**biḍālakākākhucchiṣṭaṃ jagdhvāśvanakulasya ca |**

**	keśakīṭāvapannaṃ ca pibed brahmasuvarcalām || 11.158 ||**

ekāham aviseṣopadeśāt | eteṣām ucchiṣṭabhakṣaṇa etatprāyaścittam | evaṃ ca kākādīnāṃ pratiṣiddhāni dharmaśāstre ucchiṣṭamūtrapurīṣamāṃsabhakṣaṇāni ślokatrayeṇa | viḍvarāhaśloke mūtrapurīṣapratiṣedhaḥ, kravyādasūkaraśloke māṃsabhakṣaṇasya, biḍālakākākhūcchiṣṭam ity atrocchiṣṭasya | evaṃ ca sati ya ekatropadiṣṭā anyatra śloke nopadiśyante kukkuṭādayas, teṣāṃ sāhacaryāc chlokatraye 'pi grahaṇaṃ vijñeyam | tac caitad evam ataḥ || 11.158 ||

	**abhojyam annaṃ nattavyam ātmanaḥ suddhim icchatā |**

**	ajñātajagdham udgāryaṃ śodhyaṃ vāpyāśu śodhanaiḥ || 11.159 ||**

**	eṣo 'nādyādanasyokto vratānāṃ vividho vidhiḥ |**

**	steyadoṣāpahartṝṇāṃ vratānāṃ śrūyatāṃ vidhiḥ || 11.160 ||**

nigadavyākhyātaḥ ślokaḥ || 11.160 ||

	**dhānyānnadhanacauryāṇi kṛtvā kāmād dvijottamaḥ |**

**	svajātīyagṛhād eva kṛcchrābdena viśudhyati || 11.161 ||**

**dhānyaṃ** vrīhyādi | **annaṃ** tad eva saṃskṛtaṃ bhojanīyam | **dhanaṃ** suvarṇam anyad [vā] vastrādi | **dhana**śabdenaiva ca sarvagṛhītatvād dhānyādinideśo gobalīvardavad eva | etad uktaṃ bhavati, "yat kiṃcid apahatyā" iti | **kāmād** iti cāvivakṣitam eva | na hy anyatra viniyogo 'sti, yathā surāpānaprāyaścitte | **dvijottama**śabdas ca brāhmaṇanirdeśārthaḥ, apiśabdaś cātra sāmarthyāl luptanirdeśo draṣṭavyaḥ, brāhmaṇo 'pi brāhmaṇagṛhād apahṛtyety arthaḥ | evaṃ ca sati daṇḍenāpūpo vyākhyāta iti | kṣatriyādīnām apy etat prāyaścittaṃ bhavati | itarathā hi svajātīyagṛhād iti kṣatriyādīnāṃ kṣatriyādigṛhebhya evaitat prāyaścittaṃ syāt, brāhmaṇagṛhāt tu sāmānyavihitaṃ prāyaścittaṃ cāndrāyaṇādi syāt | na caitad iṣṭam, mahattvāt kṛcchrābdaprāyascittasya | tasmād idaṃ prāyaścittaṃ sarveṣām eva brāhmaṇādīnāṃ brāhmaṇasvaharaṇe syat, brahmahatyā prāyascittavat | evam itaratrāpi vijñeyam || 11.161 ||

	**manuṣyāṇāṃ tu haraṇe strīṇāṃ kṣetragṛhasya ca |**

**	kūpavāpijalānāṃ ca śuddhiś cāndrāyaṇaṃ smṛtam || 11.162 ||**

jalāharaṇam ātmopabhogārthaṃ pratiṣiddham | kūpavāpyādes tv āharaṇaṃ paropabhogārtham api | atas tayoḥ svakābhisaṃbandhamatratvād evāpaharaṇadoṣa ity etasmād vailakṣaṇyāt pṛthaggrahaṇam | anyo vā samādhir vaktavyaḥ || 11.162 ||

	**dravyāṇām alpasārāṇāṃ steyaṃ kṛtvānyaveśmataḥ |**

**	caret sāntapanaṃ kṛcchraṃ tan niryāty ātmaśuddhaye || 11.163 ||**

alpasārāṇām alpamūlyānām alpopabhogānāṃ vā | bhakṣyabhojyādiṣv anyasya dravyajātasya gṛhītatvāt trapusīsādīnām idaṃ grahaṇaṃ vijñeyam || 11.163 ||

	**bhakṣyabhojyāpaharaṇe yānaśayyāsanasya ca |**

**	puṣpamūlaphalānāṃ ca pañcagavyaṃ viśodhanam || 11.164 ||**

atra ca saṃkhyā bhakṣyabhojyādīnām āvṛttyapekṣayā sapratyayāpratyayato vā || 11.164 ||

	**tṛṇakāṣṭhadrumāṇāṃ ca śuṣkānnasya guḍasya ca |**

**	celacarmāmiṣāṇāṃ ca trirātraṃ syād abhojanam || 11.165 ||**

tṛṇādīnāṃ sārāpekṣayā prāyaścittam | saty api ca peyatve paya ādīny api bhakṣyabhojyāntarbhūtāni draṣṭavyāni | **śuṣkānnaṃ** parpaṭakādi | **guḍa**grahaṇaṃ sarvaguḍavikārārtham | **cela**grahaṇaṃ śāṇakṣaumadukūlādyartham | kārpāsādīnāṃ tv anyat prāyaścittaṃ vakṣyati || 11.165 ||

	**maṇimuktāpravālānāṃ tāmrasya rajatasya ca |**

**	ayaḥkāṃsyopalānāṃ ca dvādaśāhaṃ kaṇānnatā || 11.166 ||**

atrāpi sārāsārāpekṣayā sakṛd dharaṇe āvṛttau ca || 11.166 ||

	**kārpāsakīṭajīrṇānāṃ dvisaphaikaśaphasya ca |**

**	pakṣigandhauṣadhīnāṃ ca rajjvāś caiva tryahaṃ payaḥ || 11.167 ||**

pūrvavad atrāpy apekṣā yojanīyā | hastyādīnāṃ ca sāmānyavihitam anyad draṣṭavyam iti || 11.167 ||

	**etair vratair apoheta pāpaṃ steyakṛtaṃ dvijaḥ |**

**	agamyāgamanīyaṃ tu vratair ebhir apānudet || 11.168 ||**

**	gurutalpavrataṃ kuryād retaḥ siktvā svayoniṣu |**

**	sakhyuḥ putrasya ca strīṣu kumārīṣv antyajāsu ca || 11.169 ||**

akumārīṣv api caṇḍālādistrīṣu cānyad api prāyaścittam vakṣyati | "caṇḍālāntyastriyo gatvā" ity evamādi || 11.168–169 ||

	**paitṛṣvaseyīṃ bhaginīṃ svasrīyāṃ mātur eva ca |**

**	mātuś ca bhrātus tanayāṃ gatvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret || 11.170 ||**

**	etās tisras tu bhāryārthe nopayacchet tu buddhimān |**

**	jñātitvenānupeyās tāḥ patati hy upayann adhaḥ || 11.171 ||**

mātṛṣavasṛmātuladuhitros tv "asapiṇḍās ca yāḥ mātuḥ" ity anena siddhe pratiṣedhe paitṛṣavasreyyāḥ pratiṣedhārthaṃ punar iha grahaṇam | anuvādārtho vāyaṃ śloko varṇanīyaḥ, "asapiṇḍā ca yā mātuḥ" ity anenaiva siddhātvād iti || 11.170–171 ||

	**amānuṣīṣu puruṣa udakyāyāṃ ayoniṣu |**

**	retaḥ siktvā jale caiva kṛcchraṃ sāntapanaṃ caret || 11.172 ||**

"amānuṣīṣv anaṅge ca paiśācyāṃ caiva yoṣiti" ity aparaḥ pāṭho 'sya ślokārdhasya | "khe ca" ity apare paṭhanti | **amānuṣīṣu** baḍabādyāsu | **puruṣe** cānaṅge | **udakyā** prasiddhā | ayonau ca jale ca retaḥ siktvā | vyavahiteṣu vakṣyaty anantaraśloke nauprabhṛtiṣu | **kṛcchraṃ sāntapanaṃ caret** | tac ca vakṣyati | baḍabādivad gavi prāyaścittam nayam etat | atas tasyānuktatvāt smṛtyantarād varṇanīyam: " . . . snuṣāyāṃ gavic ca [guru]talpasamaḥ" iti || 11.172 ||

	**maithunaṃ tu samāsevya puṃsi yoṣiti vā dvijaḥ |**

**	goyāne 'psu divā caiva savāsāḥ snānam ācaret || 11.173 ||**

puṃsy uparibhogye pūrvaśloka uktaṃ prāyaścittaṃ guru | idaṃ tv anyad anyatra pradeśe laghu prāyascittam | **yoṣiti vā dvija** iti dvijagrahaṇaṃ viseṣārtham | tatstrīpuṃsayor maithunaṃ viseṣayati | **goyāne 'psu** ca yāne **divā** **caivā**yāne 'pi **savāsāḥ snānam ācaret** | savastrasnānopadeśāc ca nityād adhikaṃ viśiṣṭam idaṃ naimittikaṃ snānam ucyate || 11.173 ||

	**caṇḍālāntyastriyo gatvā bhuktvā ca pratigṛhya ca |**

**	pataty ajñānato vipro jñānāt sāmyaṃ tu gacchati || 11.174 ||**

caṇḍālo 'ntyo yeṣām, āyogavādīnāṃ śūdraprabhavānāṃ ta ime caṇḍālāntyāh | teṣāṃ strīpratiṣedhaḥ | prāyaścittaṃ tu vakṣyāmaḥ | patanasāmyayoḥ ko viśeṣaḥ | prāyaścittena pratyāhāraḥ patane, prāyaścittābhāvas tu sāmye vijñeyaḥ || 11.174 ||

	**vipraduṣṭāṃ striyaṃ bhartā nirundhyād ekaveśmani |**

**	yat puṃsaḥ paradāreṣu tac caināṃ cārayed vratam || 11.175 ||**

**	sā cet punaḥ praduṣyet tu sadṛśenopamantritā |**

**	kṛcchraṃ cāndrāyaṇaṃ caiva tad asyāḥ pāvanaṃ smṛtam || 11.176 ||**

ṛjvarthaḥ ślokaḥ | etāvāṃs tu viśeṣaḥ | yat puṃsaḥ strīsaṃparke tad eva tasyā api striyāḥ puruṣasaṃparke | tad yathā yac chūdrasya brāhmaṇīgamane, tad eva brāhmaṇyā api śūdrasaṃparke | evaṃ sarvasaṃparke vyākhyeyam || 11.175–176 ||

	**yat karoty ekarātreṇa vṛṣalīsevanād dvijaḥ |**

**	tad bhaikṣabhug japan nityaṃ tribhir varṣair vyapohati || 11.177 ||**

caṇḍālāntyastrīgamane prāyaścittasyāvidhānāt, śūdrāyāḥ vṛṣalyāḥ pakṣe gamyatvād anadhikṛtatvāc ca, caṇḍālāntyastrīgamana idaṃ prāyaścittaṃ draṣṭavyam, adhikṛtatvāt tasyā iti | apare tv akrodhāṃ śūdrāṃ vṛṣalīm āhuḥ | pāṭhāntaraṃ ca kurvanti "tribhir māsaiḥ" iti | tat punar na nyāyyam anadhikṛtatvāt tasyā ity apare || 11.177 ||

	**eṣā pāpakṛtām uktā caturṇām api niṣkṛtiḥ |**

**	patitaiḥ saṃprayuktānām imāḥ śṛṇuta niṣkṛtīḥ || 11.178 ||**

**	saṃvatsareṇa patati patitena sahācaran |**

**	yājanādhyāpanād yaunān na tu yānāśanāsanāt || 11.179 ||**

yānāśanāsanair na **saṃvatsareṇa**, kiṃ tarhi sadya eva | ūrdhvaṃ tasmāt kālād arvāg vā saṃvatsarād yānāśanāsanamāgreṇeti sāmarthyād idaṃ vacanīyam | atha vāsyānyo 'rthaḥ smṛtyantarād ucyate | vyavahitakalpanayā **saṃvatsareṇa patati yānāśanāsanāt** | **na tu yājanādhyāpanād yaunāt**, kiṃ tarhi ebhir yājanādibhiḥ sadyaḥ patati | smṛtyantaradarśanāt | saṃparkasādṛśyena ca patanaṃ kalpayitavyam | tadīyaṃ ca tasya prāyaścittam | tathā ca darśayati || 11.178–179 ||

	**yo yena patitenaiṣāṃ saṃsargaṃ yāti mānavaḥ |**

**	sa tasyaiva vrataṃ kuryāt tatsaṃsargaviśuddhaye || 11.180 ||**

idam api ca prāyaścittaṃ mahāpātakibhir eva saṃbandhe syāt, goghātādisaṃbandhe tu sāmānyavihitaṃ kalpyam || 11.180 ||

	**patitasyodakaṃ kāryaṃ sapiṇḍair bāndhavair bahiḥ |**

**	nindite 'hani sāyāhṇe jñātyṛtviggurusaṃnidhau || 11.181 ||**

jīvata evety arthaḥ | tasyāyaṃ vidhir ucyate || 11.181 ||

	**dāsī ghaṭam apāṃ pūrṇaṃ paryasyet pretavat sadā|**

**	ahorātraṃ upāsīrann aśaucaṃ bāndhavaiḥ saha || 11.182 ||**

**	nivarteraṃś ca tasmāt tu saṃbhāṣaṇasahāsane |**

**	dāyādyasya pradānaṃ ca yātrā caiva hi laukikī || 11.183 ||**

**	jyeṣṭhatā ca nivarteta jyeṣṭhāvāpyaṃ ca yad dhanam |**

**	jyeṣṭhāṃśaṃ prāpnuyāc cāsya yavīyān guṇato 'dhikaḥ || 11.184 ||**

**	prāyaścitte tu carite pūrṇakumbham apāṃ navam |**

**	tenaiva sārdhaṃ prāsyeyuḥ snātvā puṇye jalāśaye || 11.185 ||**

**	sa tv apsu taṃ ghaṭaṃ prāsya praviśya bhavanaṃ svakam |**

**	sarvāṇi jñātikāryāṇi yathā pūrvaṃ samācaret || 11.186 ||**

ime api pātraviparyāsoddharaṇe ṣaṭslokokte mahāpātakasaṃbandha eva syāt | tac coktam "patitasyodakaṃ kāryam" ity evamādi | smṛtyantare tu "tyajet pitaram" ity evamādi keṣāṃcid eva || 11.182–186 ||

	**etam eva vidhiṃ kuryād yoṣitsu patitāsv api |**

**	vastrānnapānaṃ deyaṃ tu vaseyuś ca gṛhāntike || 11.187 ||**

nigadavyākhyātaḥ ślokaḥ || 11.187 ||

	**enasvibhir anirṇiktair nārthaṃ kiṃcit sahācaret |**

**	kṛtanirṇejanāṃś caiva na jugupseta karhicit || 11.188 ||**

"sarvāṇi jñātikāryāṇi" iti mahāpātakebhyo 'nujñānāt govadhārthaṃ prakalpyate | "na saṃsargaṃ vrajet sadbhiḥ prāyascitte 'kṛte sati" ity ubhayatrāpi śakyaḥ saṃparko jñāpayitum | bālaghnādyarthaṃ tu punar apodyate || 11.188 ||

	**bālaghnāṃś ca kṛtaghnāṃś ca viśuddhān api dharmataḥ |**

**	śaraṇāgatahantṝṃś ca strīhantṝṃś ca na saṃvaset || 11.189 ||**

saṃparkāpavādārtho 'syāraṃbhaḥ | atha vā pratyavāyātiśayajñāpanārthaḥ || 11.189 ||

	**yeṣāṃ dvijānāṃ sāvitrī nānūcyeta yathāvidhi |**

**	tāṃś cārayitvā trīn kṛcchrān yathāvidhy upanāyayet || 11.190 ||**

trayaḥ kṛcchrāḥ, ādyatvāt prājāpatyāḥ | kṛcchrātikṛcchraparākā ity apare || 11.190 ||

	**prāyaścittaṃ cikīrṣanti vikarmasthās tu ye dvijāḥ |**

**	brahmaṇā ca parityaktās teṣām apy etad ādiśet || 11.191 ||**

anadhītavedā **vikarmasthāś** ca ye 'dhītavedā api teṣāṃ apīdaṃ prāyaścittam | yad asya pratiṣiddhaṃ tat tasy vikarma | yathā śūdrasevanam āryāṇām || 11.191 ||

	**yad garhitenārjayanti karmaṇā brāhmaṇā dhanam |**

**	tasyotsargeṇa śudhyanti japyena tapasaiva ca || 11.192 ||**

pūrvasmin śloke dvijātīnām adhikṛtatvād **yad garhitenārjayanti karmaṇā brāhmaṇā dhanam** itīdaṃ brāhmaṇagrahaṇaṃ sarvadvijapradarśanārthaṃ vijñāyate | japyatapasor garhiteṣu sāmānyato 'bhidhānād yo yatra viśeṣeṇa vihitaḥ sa tatra pratyetavyaḥ | tayos ca prāptayor api sator dhanotsargārthaṃ grahaṇam || 11.192 ||

	**japitvā trīṇi sāvitryāḥ sahasrāṇi samāhitaḥ |**

**	māsaṃ goṣṭhe payaḥ pītvā mucyate 'satpratigrahāt || 11.193 ||**

**asatpratigrahasya** viśeṣavidhiḥ || 11.193 ||

	**upavāsakṛśaṃ taṃ tu govratāt punar āgatam |**

**	praṇataṃ prati pṛccheyuḥ sāmyaṃ saumyecchasīti kim || 11.194 ||**

**	satyam uktvā tu vipreṣu vikired yavasaṃ gavām |**

**	gobhiḥ pravartite tīrthe kuryus tasya parigraham || 11.195 ||**

ṛjvarthaṃ ślokadvayam || 11.194–195 ||

	**vrātyānāṃ yājanaṃ kṛtvā pareṣām antyakarma ca |**

**	abhicāram ahīnaṃ ca tribhiḥ kṛcchrair viśudhyati || 11.196 ||**

pareṣām asaṃbandhānām ity arthaḥ | tathā coktam:

	guroḥ pretasya śiṣyas tu pitṛmedhaṃ samācaran |

	pretāhāraiḥ samaṃ tatra daśarātreṇa śudhyati || iti |

yājanādhikārāc cābhicārāhīnayor api yājanārthaṃ vacanam | na tv ātmārthe pratiṣedhaḥ | evaṃ ca śrutir "ahīnayājanam akāryam" iti | anabhicaraṇīyābhicāre caitat prāyaścittam | tathā cokto 'bhicaraṇīyābhicāraḥ, "vākśastraṃ vai brāhmaṇasya tena hanyād arīn dvijaḥ" iti || 11.196 ||

	**śaraṇāgataṃ parityajya vedaṃ viplāvya ca dvijaḥ |**

**	saṃvatsaraṃ yavāhāras tatpāpam apasedhati || 11.197 ||**

evaṃ ca sati vidvadbhiḥ prāyaścittī śaraṇāgato na parityajanīyaḥ, kiṃ tarhi deyam eva tasya yathāśāstraṃ prāyaścittam | atha vā lokaprasiddha eva śaraṇāgataḥ tatparityāge, ubhayor vā | vedaviplāvanam anadhyāpyādhyāpanam anuyogadānaṃ vā dhanārtham | tathā ca smṛtyantaram "dattvānuyogān dhanahetoḥ patitān manur abravīt" iti || 11.197 ||

	**śvasṛgālakharair daṣṭo grāmyaiḥ kravyādbhir eva ca |**

**	narāśvoṣṭravarāhaiś ca prāṇāyāmena śudhyati || 11.198 ||**

**	ṣaṣṭhānnakālatā māsaṃ saṃhitājapa eva vā |**

**	homāś ca śākalā nityam apāṅktyānāṃ viśodhanam || 11.199 ||**

**apāṅktyāḥ** stenapatitādayaḥ | tathā coktam: "ye stenapatitaklībāḥ" ity evmādi | teṣāṃ yāny avihitaprāyaścittāny apaṅktyakaraṇāni | tatredaṃ prāyaścittam pūgayājanādau | śākalahomānāṃ na vikalpaḥ pūrveṇa nityavacanāt || 11.198–199 ||

	**uṣṭrayānaṃ samāruhya kharayānaṃ tu kāmataḥ |**

daṇḍāpūpikayā coṣṭrakharayor avyavadhāna etad eva syāt, īṣad adhikaṃ vā |

	**snātvā ca vipro digvāsāḥ prāṇāyāmena śudhyati || 11.200 ||**

**	vinādbhir apsu vānārthaḥ śarīraṃ saṃniṣevya tu |**

**	sacedo jalam āplutya gām ālabhya viśudhyati || 11.201 ||**

jalagrahaṇaṃ ca savidhisnānārtham || 11.200–201 ||

	**vedoditānāṃ nityānāṃ karmaṇāṃ samatikrame |**

**	snātakavratalope ca prāyaścittam abhojanam || 11.202 ||**

**nityānāṃ** pradhānakarmaṇām agnihotrādīnām ativartane **'bhojanam** | śrautaṃ ca nānārthatvāt samuccīyate | guṇakarmaṇāṃ vā | **snātakavratalope** cānirdiṣṭaprāyaścittam idam eva syāt || 11.202 ||

	**huṅkāraṃ brāhmaṇasyoktvā tvaṃkāraṃ ca garīyasaḥ |**

**	snātvānaśnann ahaḥ śeṣam abhivādya prasādayet || 11.203 ||**

viśiṣṭasnānacodaneyaṃ nityādadhikā (?) nimittakīti vijñeyā || 11.203 ||

	**tāḍayitvā tṛṇenāpi kaṇṭhe vābadhya vāsasā |**

**	vivāde vā vinirjitya praṇipatya prasādayet || 11.204 ||**

vivādaś ca laukiko vā kalaho vijñeyaḥ, netaraḥ, tasya vādasaṃjñatvāt || 11.204 ||

	**avagūrya tv abdaśataṃ sahasram abhihatya ca |**

**	jighāṃsayā brāhmaṇasya narakaṃ pratipadyate || 11.205 ||**

na parihāsataḥ || 11.205 ||

	**śoṇitaṃ yāvataḥ pāṃsūn saṃgṛhṇāti mahītale |**

**	tāvanty abdasahasrāṇi tatkartā narake vaset || 11.206 ||**

prāyaścittam idānīṃ tasya karmaṇo vivakṣann idam āha,

	**avagūrya caret kṛcchraṃ atikṛcchraṃ nipātane |**

**	kṛcchrātikṛcchrau kurvīta viprasyotpādya śoṇitam || 11.207 ||**

sarvo brāhmaṇādivarṇaḥ | "brāhmaṇasya rujaḥkṛtyam" iti caitaj jātibhraṃśakaramadha upadiṣṭam | yataḥ tadīyena prāyaścittena kṛcchrātikṛcchrau vikalpitau syātām || 11.207 ||

	**anuktaniṣkṛtīnāṃ tu pāpānām apanuttaye |**

**	śaktiṃ cāvekṣya pāpaṃ ca prāyaścittaṃ prakalpayet || 11.208 ||**

caṇḍālādīnāṃ pratilomānāṃ hiṃsāyām **anuktā niṣkṛtiḥ**, atha vā kāraṇe kṛtānujñāyāṃ ca **noktā niṣkṛtiḥ**, brāhmaṇavadhādiṣu āyudhadānādibhir hantuḥ prītyartham | eteṣu **śaktiṃ cāvekṣya** sādhanavayo'vasthāśarīrasāmarthyakṛtām ca pāpaṃ ca gurulaghutāviśeṣeṇa sapratyayāprtyayaviśeṣeṇa ca | sapratyaye 'pi ca krodhādyanubandhena **prāyaścittaṃ prakalpayed** ity arthaḥ | pariṣad daśāvarā tryavarā vā | atha vā "eko 'pi vedavid dharmam" ity vakṣyati || 11.208 ||

	**yair yair pupāyair enāṃsi mānavo vyapakarṣati |**

**	tān vo hy upāyān vakṣyāmi devarṣipitṛsevitān || 11.209 ||**

**mānava**grahaṇaṃ sarvavarṇārtham | **devādi**grahaṇaṃ cādharmakṣayopāyastutyartham || 11.209 ||

	**tryahaṃ prātas tryahaṃ sāyaṃ tryaham adyād ayācitam |**

**	tryahaṃ paraṃ ca nāśnīyāt prājāpatyaṃ caran dvijaḥ || 11.210 ||**

**	gomūtraṃ gomayaṃ kṣīraṃ dadhi sarpiḥ kuśodakam |**

**	ekarātropavāsaś ca kṛcchraṃ sāntapanaṃ smṛtam || 11.211 ||**

kṛcchrasādhyatvāt kṛcchrapratimo[cana]vacanāt vā kṛcchram || 11.210–211 ||

	**ekaikaṃ grāsam aśnīyāt tryahāṇi trīṇi pūrvavat |**

**	tryahaṃ copavased antyam atikṛcchraṃ caran dvijaḥ || 11.212 ||**

**	taptakṛcchraṃ caran vipro jalakṣīraghṛtānilān |**

**	prati tryahaṃ pibed uṣṇān sakṛtsnāyī samāhitaḥ || 11.213 ||**

**	yatātmano 'pramattasya dvādaśāham abhojanam |**

**	parāko nāma kṛcchro 'yaṃ sarvapāpāpanodanaḥ || 11.214 ||**

sa cāyaṃ kṛcchrātikṛcchro gautamīyo 'bhihitaḥ || 11.212–214 ||

	**ekaikaṃ hrāsayet piṇḍaṃ kṛṣṇe śukle ca vardhayet |**

**	upaspṛśaṃs triṣavaṇam etac cāndrāyaṇaṃ smṛtam || 11.215 ||**

**	etam eva vidhiṃ kṛtsnam ācared yavamadhyame |**

**	śuklapakṣādiniyataś caraṃś cāndrāyaṇaṃ vratam || 11.216 ||**

**	aṣṭāv aṣṭau samaśnīyāt piṇḍān madhyaṃdine sthite |**

**	[niyatātmā haviṣyāśī yaticāndrāyaṇaṃ caran || 11.217 ||**

**	caturaḥ prātar aśnīyāt piṇḍān vipraḥ samāhitaḥ] |**

**	caturo 'stamite sūrye śiśucāndrāyaṇaṃ smṛtam || 11.218 ||**

**	yathā kathaṃcit piṇḍānāṃ tisro 'śītīḥ samāhitaḥ |**

**	māsenāśnan haviṣyasya candrasyaiti salokatām || 11.219 ||**

**	etad rudrās tathādityā vasavaś cācaran vratam |**

**	sarvākuśalamokṣāya marutaś ca maharṣibhiḥ || 11.220 ||**

**	mahāvyāhṛtibhir homaḥ kartavyaḥ svayam anvaham |**

**	ahiṃsā satyam akrodham ārjavaṃ ca samācaret || 11.221 ||**

**	trir ahni trir niśāyāṃ ca savāsā jalam āviśet |**

**	strīśūdrapatitāṃś caiva nābhibhāṣeta karhicit || 11.222 ||**

**	sthānāsanābhyāṃ vihared aśakto 'dhaḥ sayīta vā |**

**	brahmacārī vratī ca syād gurudevadvijārcakaḥ || 11.223 ||**

**	sāvitrīṃ ca japen nityaṃ pavitrāṇi ca śaktitaḥ |**

**	sarveṣv eva vrateṣv evaṃ prāyaścittārtham ādṛtaḥ || 11.224 ||**

**	etair dvijātayaḥ śodhyā vratair āviṣkṛtainasaḥ |**

**	anāviṣkṛtapāpāṃs tu mantrair homair viśodhanaiḥ|| 11.225 ||**

saptadaśaślokāḥ kṛcchrādiśuddhyarthāḥ ṛjvarthatvān na vyākhyātāḥ | **yathā kathaṃcid** iti prakṛtānuvādaḥ, na vidhyantaropadeśaḥ | **anāviṣkṛtapāpān** mantrān homāṃś ca vakṣyati || 11.215–225 ||

	**khyāpanenānutāpena tapasādhyayanena ca |**

**	pāpakṛn mucyate pāpāt tathā dānena cāpadi || 11.226 ||**

khyāpanānutāpanayoḥ prāyaścittayor ayaṃ vidhyarthaḥ ślokaḥ | tathā ca sati tapaḥprabhṛtīnām atra dṛṣṭāntārtham upādānam, na svārtham | tathā **dānena** **cāpadī**ti vṛddhastrībālavyādhitādayo dīrghakālaprāyaścittānuṣṭhāne 'samarthās tapasā dānena śudhyante yathā evaṃ khyāpanānutāpābhyām | tathā ca sati khyāpanaṃ prakāśaprāyaścittena saha samuccīyate sāmarthyāt, na kevalam | anutāpas tūbhābhyām | tatra khyāpanārthavādaḥ || 11.226 ||

	**yathā yathā naro 'dharmaṃ svayaṃ kṛtvānubhāṣate |**

**	tathā tathā tvacevāhis tenādharmeṇa mucyate || 11.227 ||**

śarīrasthaḥ puruṣaḥ śarīraśabdena sthānād upacaryate | mañcavat | yena puṇyapāpayor ātmāśrayaḥ | tathā ca || 11.227 ||

	**kṛtvā pāpaṃ hi saṃtapya tasmāt pāpāt pramucyate |**

**	naitat kuryāt punar iti nivṛttyā śudhyate naraḥ || 11.228 ||**

tathā ca sati nivṛttir api pūrvavat prāyascittam ity etat siddham || 11.228 ||

	**evaṃ saṃcintya manasā pretya karmaphalodayam |**

**	manovāṅmūrtibhir nityaṃ śubhaṃ karma samācaret || 11.229 ||**

ubhayam api nivṛttiṃ prāyaścittaṃ ca, yenaikatrānutpattir eva pāpasya, anyatrotpannasya vināśaḥ | yataś caitad evam ataḥ || 11.229 ||

	**ajñānād yadi vā jñānāt kṛtvā karma vigarhitam |**

**	tasmād vimuktim anvicchan dvitīyaṃ na samācaret || 11.230 ||**

jñānakṛtasyāpy akuśalasya nivṛttyā śuddhiḥ, kiṃ punar ajñānakṛtasyety anena darśayati || 11.230 ||

	**yasmin karmaṇy asya kṛte manasaḥ syād alāghavam |**

**	tasmiṃs tāvat tapaḥ kuryād yāvat tuṣṭikaraṃ bhavet || 11.231 ||**

prāyaścittābhyāsārtho nimittato 'syārambhaḥ | tasyāyam ubhayatra rahasye prakāśe ca vijñeyaḥ | tathā coktaṃ bhāvaprasādasya ku[śa]lakarmahetutvam || 11.231 ||

	**tapomūlam idaṃ sarvaṃ daivamānuṣakaṃ sukham |**

**	tapomadhyaṃ budhaiḥ proktaṃ tapo'ntaṃ vedadarśanāt || 11.232 ||**

devasya tāvat sukhasyāṇimādeḥ, mānuṣasya ca śabdādyupabhogasya, gandharvavidhyādharādisukhasya ca **tapa** evety avasthā kāraṇam || 11.232 ||

	**brāhmaṇasya tapo jñānaṃ tapaḥ kṣatrasya rakṣaṇam |**

**	vaiśyasya tu tapo vārttā tapaḥ śūdrasya sevanam || 11.233 ||**

prāyaścittaprakaraṇe 'syopadeśād vijñāyate dṛṣṭārtheṣv api niyamaḥ śuddhihetuḥ, kiṃ punar vihitaprāyaścittānuṣṭhānānām | tathā coktaṃ jñānasya śuddhihetutvam, "jñānaṃ tapo 'gnir āhāraḥ," "buddhir jñānena śudhyati" iti ca | tasya cārthaprāptasyātra viśuddhyartha upadeśo vijñeyaḥ || 11.233 ||

	**ṛṣayaḥ śaṃsitātmānaḥ phalamūlānilāśanāḥ |**

**	tapasaiva prapaśyanti tryailokyaṃ (?) sacarācaram || 11.234 ||**

prāyaścittānuṣṭhānārthatapasā paśyanti | seyam evaṃ prāyaścittatapaḥ stutiḥ prakaraṇasāmarthyād vijñeyā | evam uttaraślokāḥ || 11.234 ||

	**auṣadhāny agado vidyā daivā ca vividhā sthitiḥ |**

**	tapasaiva prasiddhyanti tapas teṣāṃ hi sādhanam || 11.235 ||**

**	yad dustaraṃ yad durāpaṃ yad durgaṃ yac ca duṣkaram |**

**	sarvaṃ tu tapasā sādhyaṃ tapo hi duratikramam || 11.236 ||**

grahanakṣatravaiṣamyanimittā āpad **dustarā** | **durāpaṃ** cāntardhānāveśākāśagamanādyaiśvaryajīvitaiva | **durgaṃ** ca yad durārchaṃ (?) svargādi | **yac ca duṣkaraṃ** kṛtsnasamudrapānamṛtasaṃjīvanādy agastyajamadagniprabhṛtīnāṃ tat sarvaṃ tapasā śakyam iti | seyam uktasya sāmarthyena prāyaścittatapaḥstutir eva prakaraṇasāmarthyād vijñeyā | yena || 11.235–236 ||

	**mahāpātakinaś caiva śeṣāś cākāryakāriṇaḥ |**

**	tapasaiva sutaptena mucyante kilbiṣāt tataḥ || 11.237 ||**

vinaṣṭakilbiṣāṇāṃ ca pratibandhābhāvād vihitakarmānuṣṭhānatapasā sarvārthena yathoktā siddhiḥ | kiṃ cānyat || 11.237 ||

	**kīṭāś caiva pataṅgāś ca pasavaś ca vayāṃsi ca |**

**	sthāvarāṇi ca bhūtāni divaṃ yānti tapobalāt || 11.238 ||**

kīṭapataṅgā agnipraveśatapasā, paśavo 'patyapoṣaṇasaṃvardhanena vāhakṣīradānādibhiś ca, vayāṃsi cāpatyasaṃvardhanena sādhūnāṃ ca svamāṃsopakāreṇa, sthāvarāṇi ca puṣpamūlaphalachāyādy upakāreṇa, **divaṃ yānti tapobalāt** | tapaḥstutyarthavādo 'yam | atha vā kīṭ[atv]ādiprāptihetukarmasaṃbandhāt prāyaścittena yasmān mucyante | ata evam idam ucyate | seyam apareṇa prakāreṇa prāyaścittastutiḥ | evaṃ ca sati || 11.238 ||

	**yat kiṃcid enaḥ kurvanti manovāṅmūrtibhir janāḥ |**

**	tat sarvaṃ nirdhahanty āśu tapasaiva tapodhanāḥ || 11.239 ||**

yataś ca,

	**tapasaiva viśuddhasya brāhmaṇasya divaukasaḥ |**

**	ijyāś ca pratigṛhṇanti kāmān saṃvardhayanti ca || 11.240 ||**

kāmyakarmasādhyatvāt tad anuṣṭhātṝṇām | ataś caitan nyāyyaṃ kartum | idaṃ cāparaṃ paśya tapaso mahābhāgyam || 11.240 ||

	**prajāpatir idaṃ śāstraṃ tapasaivāsṛjat prabhuḥ |**

**	tathaiva vedān ṛṣayas tapasā pratipedire || 11.241 ||**

prajāpatir api bhūtvā tapaḥśaraṇa iti kartavyeṣu, kiṃ punar manuṣyā ity evam asya stutitvaṃ boddhavyam || 11.241 ||

	**ity evaṃ tapaso devā mahābhāgyaṃ pracakṣate |**

**	sarvasyāsya prapaśyantas tapasaḥ puṇyam uttamam || 11.242 ||**

"tapomūlam idaṃ sarvam" ity etasmāt ślokāt prabhṛti yāvad ayaṃ śloka iyaty atra yā stutiḥ sā prakāśaprāyaścittatapasaḥ | atha vā "anāviṣkṛtapāpas tu" ity ataḥ prabhṛti rahasyaprāyaścittaprakaraṇasāmarthyāt tattapaḥstutiḥ, avirodhād ubhayor vā | atha vā tapaḥsthitānām apratyayākuśalakarmanāśāya tapaḥstutir iti || 11.242 ||

	**vedābhyāso 'nvahaṃ śaktyā mahāyajñakriyā kṣamā |**

**	nāśayanty āśu pāpāni mahāpātakajāny api || 11.243 ||**

prāyaścittaprakaraṇe nityakarmapraśaṃsanā kasmād yujyata iti | yataḥ eteṣām api pāpakṣayahetutvaṃ vijñeyam | na kevalam utkarṣārtham eveti | apare tv āhuḥ: anirdiṣṭaprāyaścittānām enasāṃ pratyayakṛtānām apratyayakṛtānāṃ cetana[bhūtān]ām etat prāyaścittam iti | atra dṛṣṭāntam āha || 11.243 ||

	**yathaidhas tejasā vahniḥ prāptaṃ nirdahati kṣaṇāt |**

**	tathā jñānāgninā pāpaṃ kṛtsnaṃ dahati vedavit || 11.244 ||**

na kevalaṃ vedābhyāsaḥ, kiṃ tarhi tadvijñānam api | śuddhaye vedārthavidām | itarathā hi: prāyaścittaprakaraṇe stutir asyānarthikā syāt | apare tu prāyaścittānuṣṭhānavijñānastutim etāṃ manyante | tad ayuktam, arthagṛhītatvāt prayogavijñānasya | yato 'nyad devatādisatattvavijñānam idaṃ vijñeyam | tathā coktam, **kṛtsnaṃ dahati vedavid** iti | tad idānīṃ rahasyaprāyaścittam upadiśyate || 11.244 ||

	**savyāhṛtikāḥ sapraṇavāḥ prāṇāyāmās tu ṣoṣaśa |**

**	api bhrūṇahaṇaṃ māsāt punanty ahar ahaḥ kṛtāḥ || 11.245 ||**

brahmahatyāyām abhidhāya, rahasyaṃ surāpasyedānīm āha || 11.245 ||

	**kautsaṃ japtvāpa ity etad vāsiṣṭhaṃ ca pratīty ṛcam |**

**	māhendraṃ śuddhavatyaś ca surāpo 'pi viśudhyati || 11.246 ||**

**kautsaṃ** sūktam "apa naḥ śośucad agham" ity aṣṭarcalakṣītam | vāgdaivikaṃ **vāsiṣṭham** "pratistomebhir uṣasaṃ vasiṣṭhāḥ" ity etat | **māhendram** "mahām indro ya ojasā" ity etad aṣṭācatvāriṃśad arcam | anye tu "māhitram" paṭhanti | mantraṃ cemam āhuḥ: "māhitrīṇāmavo 'stu" ity evam | **śuddhavatya** ṛcaḥ prasiddhāḥ || 11.246 ||

	**sakṛj japtvāsyavāmīyaṃ śivasaṃkalpam eva ca |**

**	apahṛtya suvarṇaṃ tu kṣaṇād bhavati nirmalaḥ || 11.247  ||**

"asya vāmasya palitasya hotuḥ" iti dvipañcāśad ṛglakṣitaṃ sūktam **āsyavāmīyam** | **śivasaṃkalpam** api sūktam "yaj jāgrato dūram udaiti daivam" iti ṣaḍṛgupalakṣitam | sakṛd iti ca pratyaham etajjapakarmamāsaṃ jñeyam adhikarād | uktaṃ hi: "api bhrūṇahanaṃ māsāt" iti || 11.247 ||

	**haviṣpāntīyam abhyasya na tam aṃha itīti ca |**

**	japitvā pauruṣaṃ sūktaṃ mucyate gurutalpagaḥ || 11.248 ||**

māsīti vartate sakṛd iti ca | "haviṣpāntam" ity ekonaviṃśarcam | "na tam aṃho na duritam" ity aṣṭarcam | "iti vā itime manaḥ" iti dvādaśarcam "sahasraśīrṣā puruṣaḥ" iti pauruṣaṃ sūktaṃ ṣoḍaśarcam || 11.248 ||

	**enasāṃ sthūlasūkṣmāṇāṃ cikīrṣann apanodanam |**

**	avety ṛcaṃ japed abdaṃ yat kiṃcedam itīti ca || 11.249 ||**

arvāṅ mahāpātakebhyaḥ **enāṃsi sthūlasūkṣmāṇīty** ucyante, upapātakādīni | teṣām **apanodanaṃ cikīrṣan avety ṛcaṃ japed abdam**, "ava dvake ava trikā divaś caranti" iti | apare tu sāvitrīm atra paṭhanti | **yat kiṃ cedam itīti ca** iti yāvat: "yat kiṃ cedaṃ varuṇadaivye jane" ity evamādi || 11.249 ||

	**pratigṛhyāpratigrāhyaṃ bhuktvā cānnaṃ vigarhitam |**

**	japaṃs taratsamandīyaṃ pūyate mānavas tryahāt || 11.250 ||**

taratsamandīyaṃ prasiddham || 11.250 ||

	**somāraudraṃ tu bahvenā māsam abhyasya śudhyati |**

**	sravantyām ācaran snānam aryamṇām iti vā tṛcam || 11.251 ||**

somāraudrau mantrau tatra raudro "mā tvā rudra cukrudhāmā namobhiḥ" iti | saumyaḥ "somaḥ pavate janitā matīnām" iti ca | "aryamṇām" ity eṣu mantraḥ ṛgvedād gamayitavyaḥ || 11.251 ||

	**abdārdham indram ity etad enasvī saptakaṃ japet |**

**	apraśastaṃ tu kṛtvāpsu māsam āsīta bhaikṣabhuk || 11.252 ||**

**abdārdhaṃ** ṣaṇmāsāt "indram idgāthindo bṛhad" ity etat **saptakaṃ japed** aviseṣāt sarvasminn enasi | **apraśastaṃ tu kṛtvāpsu** maithunaṃ māsaṃ nbhaikṣāhāras tiṣṭhet || 11.252 ||

	**mantraiḥ śākalahomīyair abdaṃ hutvā ghṛtaṃ dvijaḥ |**

**	sugurv apy apahanty eno japtvā vā ima ity ṛcam || 11.253 ||**

"devakṛtasyainasaḥ" ity evamādayo 'ṣṭau mantrāḥ **śākalahomīyāḥ** | etair **ghṛtam abdaṃ hutvā suguv apy apahanty enaḥ** sarvamahāpātakāny apīty arthaḥ | **japtvā vā** "imā rudrāya tavase kapardine kṣayadvīrāya" ity etan mantraṃ saṃvatsaram eva | etāṃ japakarma pūrveṇa śākalamantrahomena prāyascittam | anye tu "japtvā vā mana ity ṛcam" [iti paṭhanti]: sā tu śiṣṭebhya āgamayitavyā | "mano nv āhuvāmahe" ity eṣā || 11.253 ||

	**mahāpātakasaṃyukto 'nugacched gāḥ samāhitaḥ |**

**	abbyasyābdaṃ pāvamānīr bhaikṣāhāro viśudhyati || 11.254 ||**

**pāvamānyaḥ** "upāsmai gāyatā nara" ity ārabhya yāvad "yaḥ pāvamānīr adhyeti" ity eṣā ṛk | gavāṃ ca sevanaṃ goghātaprāyaścittam uktam | ihāpi taccheṣaṃ draṣṭavyam || 11.254 ||

	**araṇye vā trir abhyasya prayato vedasaṃhitām |**

**	mucyate pātakais sarvaiḥ parākaiḥ śodhitas tribhiḥ || 11.255 ||**

aviśeṣavacanād yāṃ kāṃcid vedasaṃhitām iti || 11.255 ||

	**tryahaṃ tūpavased yuktas trir ahno 'bhyupayann apaḥ |**

**	mucyate pātakaiḥ sarvais trir japitvāghamarṣaṇam || 11.256 ||**

alpatvāc cāsya prāyaścittasyāśraddadhānānāṃ pravṛttyartham idam āha |

	**yathāśvamedhaḥ kraturāṭ sarvapāpāpanodanaḥ |**

**	tathāghamarṣaṇaṃ sūktaṃ sarvapāpāpanodanam || 11.257 ||**

**	hatvā lokān apīmāṃs trīn aśnann api yatas tataḥ |**

**	ṛgvedaṃ dhārayan vipro nainaḥ prāpnoti kiṃcana || 11.258 ||**

**ṛgveda**grahaṇam itaravedapradarśanārtham api syāt | tathā ca darśayati || 11.257–258 ||

	**ṛksaṃhitāṃ trir abhyasya yajuṣāṃ vā samāhitaḥ |**

**	sāmnāṃ vā sarahasyānāṃ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate || 11.259 ||**

asyeyaṃ stutiḥ pravṛttyarthā || 11.259 ||

	**yathā mahāhradaṃ prāpya kṣiptaṃ loṣṭaṃ vinaśyati |**

**	tathā duścaritaṃ sarvaṃ vede trivṛti majjati || 11.260 ||**

tac ca vedasya trivṛtyartham idaṃ darśayati || 11.260 ||

	**ṛco yajūṃṣi cānyāni sāmāni vividhāni ca |**

**	eṣa jñeyas trivṛd vedo yo vedainaṃ sa vedavit || 11.261 ||**

**ṛcaḥ** prasiddhāḥ | **yajūṃṣ**yādyāni saṃhitāgatāni na tu brāhmaṇamadhe 'dhītāni padakramānvitāni | "yayor ojasā skabhitā rajāṃsi" ity evamādīni **sāmāni** punar **vividhāni** grāmāraṇyārcikastaubhikāni || 11.261 ||

	**ādyaṃ yat tryakṣaraṃ brahma trayī yasmin pratiṣṭhitā |**

**	sa guhyo 'nyas trivṛdvedo yas taṃ veda sa vedavit || 11.262 ||**

yat tryakṣaraṃ brahma varṇatrayasamudāya oṃkāraḥ | yas taṃ veda sa vedavit | tathā ca brāhmaṇam, "[tad] yathā śaṅkunā sarvāṇi parṇāni" ity evamādi | tasya copāsanā purastād ukteti | tathā ca brāhmanam: "om ity etad akṣaram udgītham pāsīta" iti || 11.262 ||

**iti bhāruceḥ kṛtau manuśāstravivaraṇa ekādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ ||**

## 12

**dvādaśo ‘dhyāyaḥ**

	**cāturvarṇyasya kṛtsno 'yam ukto dharmas tvayānagha |**

**	karmaṇāṃ phalanirvṛttiṃ śaṃsa nas tattvataḥ parām || 12.1 ||**

nanu **cāturvarṇasya** vacanād ihāśramadharmavyudāsa iti | na vyudāsaḥ, jāter avināśād anapāyāc cāśramadharmā api varṇadharmā eva | tathā ca kṛtvoktam: "bhagavān sarvavarṇānāṃ yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ" ity evamādi | asya prativacanam "varṇadharmān nibodhata" iti | **kṛtsna**vacanaṃ cātra prāyaścittābhidhānāpekṣam | yenāsmin saty asya dharmaśāstrasya samastapuruṣārthasādhakatvaṃ bhavati | vākyatraye cādṛṣṭpuruṣārthasamāptiḥ | yathā: idaṃ kartavyam, idam akartavyam, mohād akusalakarmanimitte ca kadācit pratiṣedhaśāstravyatikrame satīdaṃ prāyaścittam anuṣṭeyam iti | atra dṛṣṭārthā puruṣārthasamāptiḥ, āyurvedavat | ato yuktam idam āha prāyaścittābhidhānāpekṣaṃ **kṛtsna**grahaṇam, na tu yat pūrvam uktam "eṣa vo 'bhihito dharmo brāhmaṇasya caturvidhaḥ" ity evamādi | "karmaṇāṃ phalanirvṛttim" iti caitat prāyaścitte 'nanuṣṭhite iyam iti prakaraṇasāmarthyāt akuśaladharmāpekṣaṃ pradhānato vijñeyam | evaṃ ca satīdaṃ mahato 'narthalakṣaṇasyādharmavipākasya narakādisthāneṣu yātanāpradarśanaṃ prāyaścittānuṣṭhānaśeṣatayā kalpiṣyate | laghūpāyasādhyatvād dharmakṣayasya prāyaścittopadeśaḥ puruṣārthakārī saṃpadyate | evaṃ ca tadupanyāsapara evāyaṃ śloko veditavyaḥ || 12.1 ||

	**sa tān uvāca dharmātmā maharṣīn mānavo bhṛguḥ |**

**	asya sarvasya śṛṇuta karmayogasya nirṇayam || 12.2 ||**

pratijñāślokaḥ | **karma**śabdaś ca sādhāraṇo 'pi sann ayam adharmārthapradhānaḥ prakaraṇād vijñeyaḥ | tathā coktaṃ purastād iti || 12.2 ||

	**śubhāśubhaphalaṃ karma manovāgdehasaṃbhavam |**

**	karmajā gatayo nṝṇām uttamādhamamadhyamāḥ || 12.3 ||**

**manovāgdeha**kāraṇaṃ ca saṃkalpoktikriyārūpaṃ karmadviprakāraṃ kuśalākuśalatayā bhinnānāṃ gatīnāṃ nimittam | evaṃ ca sati **śubha**grahaṇād atra dharmanirdeśo 'pi prāyaścittaprakaraṇaśeṣa eva praṇāḍikayā vijñeyaḥ || 12.3 ||

	**tasyeha trividhasyāpi tryadhiṣṭhānasya dehinaḥ |**

**	daśalakṣaṇayuktasya mano vidyāt pravartakam || 12.4 ||**

**trividhasyo**ttamamadhyamajaghanyasya, **tryadhiṣṭhānasya** kāyavāṅmanonimittasya, **manaḥ pravartakam** | yena nāsaṃkalpitaṃ manasā puruṣaḥ śaknoti vaktuṃ kartuṃ vā || 12.4 ||

	**paradravyeṣv abhidhyānaṃ manasāniṣṭacintanam |**

**	vitathābhiniveśaś ca trividhaṃ karma mānasam || 12.5 ||**

paradravyāpahārabuddhiḥ | anyas tv āha: mamāpy etat syād ity etat **paradravyābhidhyānam |** tac caitat paripelavan | **manasāniṣṭaṃ** nāma prāṇināṃ jighāṃsā | vitathābhiniveśo dharmādhyastitvādiṣu | tathā ca vyāsaḥ:

	anabhidhyā parasveṣu sarvasattveṣu sauhṛdam |

	karmaṇāṃ phalam astīti trividhaṃ karma saṃsmaret || iti || 12.5 ||

	**pāruṣyam anṛtaṃ caiva paiśunyaṃ cāpi sarvasaḥ |**

**	asaṃbandhapralāpaś ca vāṅmayaṃ syāc caturvidham || 12.6 ||**

satyānṛtaviparītoddeśādi tathākhyaḥ | etadviparītās tu śubhāḥ priyaṃ satyaṃ hitaṃ svādhyāyaś ceti || 12.6 ||

	**adattānām upādānaṃ hiṃsā caivāvidhānataḥ |**

**	paradāropasevā ca śārīraṃ trividhaṃ smṛtam || 12.7 ||**

ayam adharmaḥ yo dharmākhyato (?) viparīt[o dattā]dānaṃ paritrāṇam indriyasaṃyamaś ceti | iyaṃ manogāgdehasādhanā daśavidhā pravṛttiḥ | kuśalākuśalavibhāgena tu viṃśatiprakāraḥ | tathā cobhayathā pradarśiteti || 12.7 ||

	**mānasaṃ manasaivāyam upabhuṅkte śubhāśubham |**

**	vācā vācā kṛtaṃ karma kāyenaiva ca kāyikam || 12.8 ||**

parasya manastāpajanako mānasam eva kuḥkhaṃ prāpnoti | evaṃ vāgapacāre maukyagadgadādinimittaṃ duḥkham | kāye 'pi caiṣaiva yojanā | sādhanānurūpyeṇaivam aniṣṭaphalapradarśanaṃ tannivṛttyartham uttarārthaṃ vā || 12.8 ||

	**śarīrajaiḥ karmadoṣair yāti sthāvaratāṃ naraḥ |**

**	vācikaiḥ pakṣimṛgatāṃ mānasair antyajātitām || 12.9 ||**

śāstranyāyavirodhe nedaṃ hetuphalasaṃbandhapradarśanam, kiṃ tarhi trisādhanasyādharmasyānantaraślokoktasya gurulaghutvapradarśanam | viseṣato guror adharmasya parihārārthaṇṃ jñeyam | prāyascittaśeṣaṃ vā prakaraṇāt | **mṛga**grahaṇaṃ ca sarvatiryagjātipradarśanārtham || 12.9 ||

	**vāgdaṇḍo 'tha manodaṇḍaḥ kāyadaṇḍaś ca te trayaḥ |**

**	yasyaite niyatā buddhau tridaṇḍīti sa ucyate || 12.10 ||**

tryadhiṣṭhānā eva daṇḍās trayaḥ || 12.10 ||

	**tridaṇḍam etaṃ nikṣipya sarvabhūteṣu mānavaḥ |**

**	kāmakrodhau ca saṃyamya tataḥ siddhiṃ nigacchati || 12.11 ||**

**tridaṇḍam etaṃ nikṣipya** svātmany upasaṃhṛtya **sarvabhūteṣv** avasthitam upaghātahetutvena **mānavaḥ siddhiṃ nigacchatīti** vivakṣitam iti | idaṃ tridaṇḍopasaṃharasya karaṇaṃ darsayati | kāmakrodhasaṃyamapūrvakas tridaṇḍōpasaṃhāraḥ krto bhavati | tadupasaṃhārāc ca tato 'nantaraṃ **siddhiṃ nigacchatīty** ayam asya phalanirdesaḥ | **mānava**grahaṇāc ca puruṣadharmatvaṃ tridaṇḍopasaṃhārasya darśayati | idānīṃ kāmakrodhasaṃyamena yasya tridaṇḍopasaṃhārāt siddhiḥ, taṃ sarvadharmādhikārapuruṣaṃ pradarśayitukāma idam āha || 12.11 ||

	**yo 'syātmanaḥ kārayitā taṃ kṣetrajñaṃ pracakṣate |**

**	yaḥ karoti tu karmāṇi sa bhūtātmocyate budhaiḥ || 12.12 ||**

asya śarīrasya kriyāyāṃ pravartayitā **kṣetrajñaḥ** | śarīre cātmaśabdo gauṇaḥ, ātmārthatvāt | śirahpāṇyādilakṣaṇas tu bhūtasaṃghāto 'nnarasamayaḥ śarīrākhyaḥ kartā **bhūtātmā** sa ucyate, bhūtakāryatvāt || 12.12 ||

	**jīvasaṃjño 'ntarātmānyaḥ sahajaḥ sarvadehinām |**

**	yena vedayate sarvaṃ sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ ca janmasu || 12.13 ||**

**yeneti** tṛtīyayā kāraṇopadeśāt mana idaṃ vijñeyam antaḥkaraṇatvāt | jīvaśabdeneti | ātmagrahaṇaṃ cāmokṣaprāpter ā pralayāc ca tadaviyogo yasmāt | evaṃ ca tasya kāraṇanirdeśo yena vedayate kṣetrajñaḥ sukhaduḥkham iti | buddhir ity apare | śrotrādiprāṇādisamūho liṅgākhya ity anye | antaḥkaraṇapakṣe ca kṣetrajñasyopalabdhau kāraṇam idaṃ nirdiśyata ity avipratipattiḥ || 12.13 ||

	**tāv ubhau bhūtasaṃpṛktau mahān kṣetrajña eva ca |**

**	uccāvaceṣu bhūteṣu sthitaṃ taṃ vyāpya tiṣṭhataḥ || 12.14 ||**

**mahac**chabdena tad evāntaḥkaraṇaṃ gṛhyate liṅgādiśabdaparyāyaḥ | **kṣetrajñas** tu kāmādhikārapuruṣaḥ sukhaduḥkhopabhoktā | **uccāvaceṣu bhūteṣv** auttarādharyeṇa vyavasthiteṣv ity arthaḥ | bahulaparyāyo vāyam **uccāvaca**sabdaḥ | bahuṣv ity arthaḥ, sthitaṃ taṃ paramātmānaṃ cetanācetanavyatiriktam upariṣṭād vakṣyamāṇam | vyāpya tiṣṭhataḥ saṃśraya ity arthaḥ | tathā ca vyāsaḥ:

	[dvāv imau puruṣau loke kṣaraś cākṣara eva ca |

	kṣaraḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni kūṭastho 'kṣara ucyate ||

	uttamaḥ puruṣas tv anyaḥ paramātmety udāhṛtaḥ |

	yo lokatrayam āviśya bibharty avyaya īśvaraḥ || iti || 12.14 ||

	**asaṅkhyā mūrtayas tasya niṣpatanti śarīrataḥ |**

**	uccāvacāni bhūtāni satataṃ ceṣṭayanti yāḥ] || 12.15 ||**

**uccāvacāni bhūtāni satataṃ** [yāḥ **asaṅkhyā mūrtīś ceṣṭayanti** tāḥ] tasya paramātmano **niṣpatanti śarīrataḥ** pradhānād ity uktam | **mūrtayaḥ** kāryakāraṇāni kṣetrajñasya bhogasādhanāni | aupaniṣadās tu paramātmānam eva śarīraśabdenāhuḥ || 12.15 ||

	**pañcabhya eva mātrābhyaḥ pretya duṣkṛtīnām nṛṇām |**

**	śarīraṃ yātanārthīyam anyad utpadyate dhruvam || 12.16 ||**

pañcabhyo bhūtamātrābhyaḥ sthūlaṃ yātanākṣamaṃ narakādiṣv anyac charīram upapadyate | kuto 'nyat | sūkṣmāl liṅgāt || 12.16 ||

	**tenānubhūya tā yāmīḥ sarīreṇa tu yātanāḥ |**

**	tāsv eva bhūtamātrāsu pralīyante vibhāgaśaḥ || 12.17 ||**

**	so 'nubhūyāsukhodarkān doṣān viṣayasaṅgajān |**

**	vyapetakalmaṣo 'bhyeti tāv evobhau mahaujasau || 12.18 ||**

mahat paramātmānau || 12.17–18 ||

	**tau dharmaṃ pasyatas tasya pāpaṃ cātandritau saha |**

**	yābhyāṃ prāpnoti saṃpṛktaḥ pretyeha ca śubhāśubham || 12.19 ||**

tau ca tatkṛtāṃ dharmagatiṃ dṛṣṭvā || 12.19 ||

	**yady ācarati dharmaṃ sa prāyaśo 'dharmam alpaśaḥ |**

**	tair eva cāvṛto bhūtaiḥ svarge sukham upāśnute || 12.20 ||**

**	yadi tu prāyaśo 'dharmaṃ sevate dharmam alpaśaḥ |**

**	tair bhūtaiḥ sa parityakto yāmīḥ prāpnoti yātanāḥ || 12.21 ||**

adharmabhūyastvāt |

	**yāmīs tā yātanāḥ prāpya sa jīvo vītakalmaṣaḥ |**

**	tāny eva pañcabhūtāni punar abhyeti bhāgaśaḥ || 12.22 ||**

punar asya karmajasya śarīrasya pratipattyarthaṃ tā eva pañcabhūtamātrā abyeti | yena na tābhir vinā puruṣasyopabhogaḥ saṃbhavati || 12.22 ||

	**etāṃ dṛṣṭvāsya jīvasya gatiṃ svenaiva cetasā |**

śāstrasaṃskṛtenety arthaḥ |

	**dharmato 'dharmataś caiva dharme dadyāt sadā manaḥ || 12.23 ||**

etac ca prakaraṇaṃ prāyaścitta[śeṣatay]ā vijñeyam | atha vā kṛtsnaśāstraśeṣatayaiva vijñeyam | yasmād atreṣṭāniṣṭaphalapradarśanam adharmaparihārāya dharmasvīkaraṇāya cārthāt saṃbhavati || 12.23 ||

	**sattvaṃ rajas tamaś caiva trīn vidyād ātmano guṇān |**

**	yair vyāpyemān sthito bhāvān mahān sarvān aśeṣataḥ || 12.24 ||**

sattvādīnām ātmaguṇatvaṃ vakṣyati | sattvaṃ jñānaṃ tamo 'jñānam ity evamādi | jñānādayas ca puruṣadharmā yataḥ sattvādīnām ātmaguṇatvam ucyate, adhikṛtadharmādharmāpekṣayā | apare tv āhuḥ — sattvādīnām anātmaguṇānām api tad arthatvād ātmaguṇam idam ucyate, pradhānaṃ cehātmaśabdenocyate || 12.24 ||

	**yo yadaiṣāṃ guṇo dehe sākalyenātiricyate |**

**	sa tadā tadguṇaprāyaṃ taṃ karoti śarīriṇam || 12.25 ||**

pūrvakarmāsrayavaśāt kasyacit kadācid atrātireko bhavati || 12.25 ||

	**sattvaṃ jñānaṃ tamo 'jñānaṃ rāgadveṣau rajaḥ smṛtam |**

**	etad vyāptimad eteṣāṃ sarvabhūtāśritaṃ vapuḥ || 12.26 ||**

sattvādīnām idaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ sarvaprāṇiṣu || 12.26 ||

	**tatra yat prītisaṃyuktaṃ kiṃcid ātmani lakṣayet |**

**	praśāntam iva śuddhābhaṃ sattvaṃ tad upadhārayet || 12.27 ||**

karmapravṛttyeyaṃ samāsataḥ sattvavṛttir ātmasaṃvedyocyate || 12.27 ||

	**yat tu duḥkhasamāyuktam aprītikaram ātmanaḥ |**

**	tad rajo 'pratighaṃ vidyāt satataṃ hāri dehinām || 12.28 ||**

atrāpi pūrvavad arthasamāyojanā || 12.28 ||

	**yat tu syān mohasaṃyuktam avyaktaṃ viṣayātmakam |**

**	apratarkyam avijñeyaṃ tamas tad upadhārayet || 12.29 ||**

tamovṛttir api pūrvavad vijñeyā || 12.29 ||

	**trayāṇām api caiteṣāṃ guṇānāṃ yaḥ phalodayaḥ |**

**	agryo madhyo jaghanyaś ca taṃ pravakṣyāmy aśeṣataḥ || 12.30 ||**

pratijñāślokaḥ || 12.30 ||

	**vedābhyāsas tapo jñānaṃ śaucam indriyanigrahaḥ |**

**	dharmakriyātmacintā ca sāttvikaṃ guṇalakṣaṇam || 12.31 ||**

**	ārambharucitādhairyam asatkāryaparigrahaḥ |**

**	viṣayopasevā cājasraṃ rājasam guṇalakṣaṇam || 12 32 ||**

**	lobhaḥ svapno 'dhṛtiḥ krauryaṃ nāstikyaṃ bhinnavṛttitā |**

**	yāciṣṇutā pramādaś ca tāmasaṃ guṇalakṣaṇam || 12.33 ||**

sattvādīnāṃ tribhiḥ ślokaiḥ phalodayo 'yam ucyate || 12.31–33 ||

	**trayāṇām api caiteṣāṃguṇānāṃ triṣu tiṣṭhatām |**

**	idaṃ sāmāsikaṃ jñeyaṃ kramaśo guṇalakṣaṇam || 12.34 ||**

**	yat karma kṛtvā kurvaṃś ca kariṣyaṃś caiva lajjati |**

**	taj jñeyaṃ viduṣā sarvaṃ tāmasaṃ guṇalakṣaṇam || 12.35 ||**

**	yenāsmin karmaṇā loke khyātim icchati puṣkalām |**

**	na ca śocaty asaṃpattau tad vijñeyaṃ tu rājasam || 12.36 ||**

**	yat sarveṇecchati jñātuṃ yan na lajjati cācaran |**

**	yena tuṣyati cātmāsya tat sattvaguṇalakṣaṇam || 12.37 ||**

caturbhiḥ ślokair arthanirmalatvāyāyaṃ guṇalakṣaṇaḥ pūrva[ślokārthaḥ punar] ucyate | tallakṣaṇam evedaṃ cāparam anena prakāreṇānyathocyate || 12.34–37 ||

	**tamaso lakṣaṇaṃ kāmo rajasas tv artha ucyate |**

**	sattvasya lakṣaṇaṃ dharmaḥ śraiṣṭhyam eṣām yathākramam || 12.38 ||**

guṇānā[m eva] |

	**yena yāṃs tu guṇenaiṣāṃ saṃsārān pratipadyate |**

**	tān samāsena vakṣyāmi sarvasyāsya yathākramam || 12.39 ||**

upakṣepo vakṣyamāṇasyāyam | so 'yam ucyate || 12.39 ||

	**devatvaṃ sāttvikā yānti manuṣyatvaṃ tu rājasāḥ |**

**	tiryaktvaṃ tāmasā nityam ity eṣā trividhā gatiḥ || 12.40 ||**

samāsanirdeśo gater guṇanimittāyāḥ || 12.40 ||

	**trividhā trividhaiṣā tu vijñeyā gauṇikī gatiḥ |**

**	adhamā madhyamāgryā ca karmavidyāviśeṣataḥ || 12.41 ||**

trividhā satī punaḥ karmavidyābhiyogāt tridhā bhidyate | etāsv api navasu vṛttiṣu karmavidyayogād eva vṛttaya ānantyena kalpyante || 12.41 ||

	**sthāvaraḥ kṛmikītāś ca matsyāḥ sarpāḥ sarīsṛpāḥ |**

**	paśavaś ca mṛgāś caiva jaghanyā tāmasī gatiḥ || 12.42 ||**

**	hastinaś ca turaṅgāś ca śūdrā mlecchāś ca garhitāḥ |**

**	saṃhā vyāghrā varāhāś ca madhymā tāmasī gatiḥ || 12.43 ||**

**	cāraṇāś ca suparṇāś ca puruṣāś caiva dāṃbhikāḥ |**

**	rakṣāṃsi ca piśācāś ca tāmasīṣūttamā gatiḥ || 12.44 ||**

**	jhallā mallā naṭāś caiva puruṣāś ca kuvṛttayaḥ |**

**	dyūtapānaprasaktāś ca prathamā rājasī gatiḥ || 12.45 ||**

**	rājānaḥ kṣatriyāś caiva rājñāṃ caiva purohitāḥ |**

**	vādayuddhapradhānāś ca madhyamā rājasī gatiḥ || 12.46 ||**

**	gandharvā guhyakā yakṣā vibudhānucarāś ca ye |**

**	tathaivāpsarasaḥ sarvā rājasīṣūttamā gatiḥ || 12.47 ||**

**	tāpasā yatayo viprā ye ca vaimānikā gaṇāḥ |**

**	nakṣatrāṇi ca daityāś ca prathamā sāttvikī gatiḥ || 12.48 ||**

**	yajvāna ṛṣayo devā vedā jyotīṃṣi vatsarāḥ |**

**	pitaraś caiva sādhyāś ca dvitīyā sāttvikī gatiḥ || 12.49 ||**

**	brahmā viśvasṛjo dharmo mahān avyaktam eva ca |**

**	uttamāṃ sāttvikīm etāṃ gatim āhur manīṣiṇaḥ || 12.50 ||**

ekaikasya guṇasya trividhā gatir navabhiḥ ślokaiḥ kīrtitaḥ || 12.42–50 ||

	**eṣa sarvaḥ samuddiṣṭas triprakārasya karmaṇaḥ |**

**	trividhas trividhaḥ kṛtsnaḥ saṃsāraḥ sārvabhautikaḥ || 12.51 ||**

ye 'py atra na kīrtitās te 'py uktasādṛśyās traividhyāntarbhūtā eva veditavyāḥ, ity upasaṃhāraśloko 'yam || 12.51 ||

	**indriyāṇāṃ prasaṅgena dharmasyāsevanena ca |**

**	pāpās saṃyānti saṃsārān avidvāṃso narādhamāḥ || 12.52 ||**

indriyaprasaṅgaḥ pratiṣiddhasevanaṃ dharmasyāsevanaṃ śiṣṭākaraṇam | pratiṣiddhasevanāc chiṣṭākaraṇāc cākṛtaprāyaścittāḥ santaḥ pāpāḥ saṃyānti saṃsārān | kutaḥ punar hetoḥ, yenāvidvāṃsas te, prāyaścittasyākaraṇāt prativyatikramam | ata eva ca **narādhamā** ity uktam | tatra pratiṣiddhasevināṃ tāvad akṛtaprāyaścittānāṃ karmavipākapradarśanārtham idam ārabhyate prakaraṇaṃ prāyaścittānuṣṭhānaśeṣatayā || 12.52 ||

	**yāṃ yāṃ yoniṃ tu jīvo 'yaṃ yena yeneha karmaṇā |**

**	kramaśo yāti loke 'smiṃs tat tat sarvaṃ nibodhata || 12.53 ||**

**	bahūn varṣagaṇān ghorān narakān prāpya tatkṣayāt |**

**	saṃsārān pratipadyante mahāpātakinas tv imān || 12.54 ||**

**	śvasūkarakharoṣṭānāṃ go'jāvimṛgapakṣiṇām |**

**	caṇḍālapulkasānāṃ ca brahmahā yonim ṛcchati || 12.55 ||**

**	kṛmikīṭapataṅgānāṃ viṇbhujāṃ caiva pakṣiṇāṃ |**

**	hiṃsrāṇāṃ caiva sattvānāṃ surāpo brāhmaṇo 'sakṛt || 12.56 ||**

**	lūtāhisaraṭānāṃ ca tiraścāṃ cāmbucāriṇām |**

**	hiṃsrāṇāṃ ca piśācānāṃ steno vipraḥ sahasraśaḥ 12.57 ||**

**	tṛṇagulmalatānāṃ ca kravyādāṃ daṃṣṭriṇām api |**

**	krūrakarmakṛtāṃ caiva śataśo gurutalpagaḥ || 12.58 ||**

**	hiṃsrā bhavanti kravyādāḥ kṛmayo 'bhakṣyabhkṣiṇaḥ |**

**	antyastrīsevinaḥ pretāḥ stenās tv anyonyaghātinaḥ || 12.59 ||**

**	saṃyogaṃ patitair gatvā parasyaiva ca yoṣitam |**

**	apahṛtya ca viprasvaṃ bhavanti brahmarākṣasāḥ || 12.60 ||**

**	maṇimuktāpravālāni hṛtvā lobhena mānavaḥ |**

**	vividhāni ca ratnāni jāyate hemakartṛṣu || 12.61 ||**

**	dhānyaṃ hṛtvā bhavaty ākhuḥ kāṃsyaṃ haṃso jalaṃ plavaḥ |**

**	madhu daṃśaḥ payaḥ kāko rasaṃ svā nakulo ghṛtam || 12.62 ||**

**	māṃsaṃ gṛdhro vapāṃ madgus tailaṃ vai tailapāyikaḥ |**

**	cīrīvākas tu lavaṇaṃ balākā śakunir dadhi || 12.63 ||**

**	kauseyaṃ tittirīr hṛtvā kṣaumaṃ hṛtvā tu darduraḥ |**

**	kārpāsaṃ tāntavaṃ krauñco godhā gāṃ vāggudo guḍam (?) || 12 64 ||**

**	chucchundariḥ śubhān gandhān patraśākaṃ tu barhiṇaḥ |**

**	śvāvit kṛtānnaṃ vividham akṛtānnaṃ tu śalyakaḥ || 12.65 ||**

**	bako bhavati hṛtvāgniṃ gṛhakārī hy upaskaram |**

**	raktāni hṛtvā vāsāṃsi jāyate jīvajīvakaḥ || 12.66 ||**

**	vṛko mṛgebhaṃ vyāghro 'śvaṃ phalamūlaṃ tu markataḥ |**

**	strīm ṛkṣaḥ stokako vāri yānāny uṣṭraḥ paśūn ajaḥ || 12.67 ||**

**stokako** **vāri** peyaṃ **jalaṃ** **plava** ity atra sekartham || 12.53–67 ||

	**yad vā tad vā paradravyam apahṛtya balān naraḥ |**

**	avaśyaṃ yāti tiryaktvaṃ jagdhvā caivāhutaṃ haviḥ || 12.68 ||**

**	striyo 'py etena kalpena coratvaṃ yāḥ prakurvate |**

**	eteṣām eva jantūnāṃ bhāryātvam upayānti tāḥ || 12.69 ||**

**	svebhyaḥ svebhyas tu karmabhyaś cyutā varṇā hy anāpati |**

**	pāpān saṃsṛtya saṃsārān preṣyatāṃ yānti dasyuṣu || 12 70 ||**

"indriyāṇāṃ prasaṅgena dharmasyāsevanena ca" ity etasmāc chlokāt prabhṛti pratiṣiddhasevinām akṛtaprāyaścittānām anarthalakṣaṇaḥ karmaphalavipāka uktaḥ | idānīṃ śiṣṭasyākriyāyāṃ svakarmacyutānām anarthalakṣaṇaḥ karmavipākaḥ pradarśayitavya iti | yata idam ārabhyate || 12.68–70 ||

	**vāntāśyulkāmukhaḥ preto vipro dharmāt svakāc cyutaḥ |**

**	amedhyakuṇapāśī ca kṣatriyaḥ kūṭapūtanaḥ || 12.71 ||**

**	maitrākṣijyotikaḥ preto vaiśyo bhavati pūyabhuk |**

**	cailāṃśakaś ca bhavati śūdro dharmāt svakāc cyutaḥ || 12.72 ||**

cailāṃśako śiṅgurukaḥ | yata etad evaṃ ataś "caritavyam ato nityaṃ prāyaścittaṃ viśuddhaye" ity uktam, mā bhūd akṛtaprāyaścittasyeyān karmaphalavipāko bahukālo 'niṣṭa iti | "bahūn varṣagaṇān ghorān narakān prāpya tatkṣayāt" iti | caitad anuvartate | ninditakarmābhyāsaphalam idānīṃ punaḥ spṛśati || 12.71–72 ||

	**yathā yathā niṣevante viṣayān viṣayātmakāḥ |**

**	tathā tathā kuśalatā teṣāṃ teṣūpajāyate || 12.73 ||**

**	te 'bhyāsāt karmaṇāṃ teṣāṃ pāpānāṃ alpabuddhayaḥ |**

**	saṃprāpnuvanti duḥkhāni tāsu tāsv iha yoniṣu || 12.74 ||**

ninditakarmābhyāsād akṛtaprāyaścittā etad īdṛśam aniṣṭaṃ prāpnuvanti || 12.73–74 ||

	**tāmisrādiṣu cogreṣu narakeṣu vivartanam |**

**	asipatravanādīni bandhanacchedanāni ca || 12.75 ||**

**	vividhāś caiva saṃpīḍāḥ kākolūkaiś ca bhakṣaṇam |**

**	karaṃbhavālukātāpān kumbhīpākāṃś ca duḥsahān || 12.76 ||**

**	saṃbhavāṃś ca viyonīṣu duḥkhaprāyāsu nityaśaḥ |**

**	śītātapābhighātāṃś ca vividhāni bhayāni ca || 12.77 ||**

**	asakṛdgarbhavāseṣu vāsaṃ janma ca dāruṇam |**

**	bandhanāni ca kaṣṭāni parapreṣyatvam eva ca || 12.78 ||**

**	bandhupriyaviyogāṃś ca saṃvāsaṃ caiva durjanaiḥ |**

**	dravyārjanavināśaṃ ca mitrāmitrasya cārjanam || 12.79 ||**

**	jarāṃ caivāpratīkārāṃ vyādhibhiś copapīḍanam |**

**	kleśāṃśca vividhāṃs tāṃs tān mṛtyum eva ca durjayam || 12.80 ||**

**	yādṛśena tu bhāvena yad yat karma niṣevate |**

**	tādṛśena śarīreṇa tat tat phalam upāśnute || 12.81 ||**

saptabhiḥ ślokair aniṣṭaphalaṃ darśayati | sāttvikena rājasena tāmasena vā bhāvena yad yat karma niṣevate, sāttvikaṃ rājasaṃ tāmasaṃ vā tena tena **śarīreṇa** tat sadṛśenety arthaḥ | sattvabahulena rajo bahulena tamobahulena vā **tat tat phalam upāśnute**, sāttvikaṃ rājasaṃ tāmasaṃ vāśnute | yataś caitad evaṃ rajas tamo bahulāt karmaṇo 'kuṣalasaṃkalpahetor aniṣṭaphalaprāptiḥ | atas tatparivarjanena kuśalasaṃkalpakarmaṇā bhavitavyam || 12.75–81 ||

	**eṣa sarvaḥ samuddiṣṭaḥ karmaṇāṃ vaḥ phalodayaḥ |**

kuśalākuśalasaṃkalpamūlānāṃ śāstralakṣaṇānāṃ tadvparītānāṃ cā[na]rthalakṣaṇānām | adhunā |

	**naiḥśreyasakaraṃ karma viprasyedaṃ nibodhata || 12.82 ||**

prāyaścittaprakaraṇasāmarthyād vakṣyamāṇo vedābhyāsādiko vidhiḥ niḥśreyasārtho 'pi sann ātmaśuddhaye saṃpadyata iti vijñeyam | evaṃ hi prakaraṇam anugṛhītaṃ bhavati | atha vāsmiñ chāstre pūrva ābhyudayiko vidhir uktaḥ, adhunā tu **naiḥśreyasakaraṃ karma viprasyedaṃ nibodhata** brahmalokaprāptyarthaṃ mokṣārthaṃ vā | evaṃ ca sati yathā vedasyānti upaniṣado rahasyabrāhmaṇoktā niḥśreyasārtham, evaṃ asminn api dharmaśāstrānte niḥśreyasārthā imā upaniṣado 'bhividhīyante || 12.82 ||

	**vedābhyāsas tapo jñānam indriyāṇāṃ ca saṃyamaḥ |**

**	ahiṃsā gurusevā ca niḥśreyasakaraṃ param || 12.83 ||**

kecit tv atra pūrvapāde **dānaṃ** paṭhanti, apare **dhyānam** | tatra vedābhyāso nāma sāṅgopāṅga[so]sopaniṣatkasya vedasya nityakarmāvirodhenābhyāso gṛhyate | **tapaḥ**śabdena ca nityakarmāṇy abhidhīyante | cāndrāyaṇādīni ca | **jñānaṃ** karmāṅgadevatānicintana **indriyasaṃyamo 'hiṃsā gurusevā** ca yathoktāḥ || 12.83 ||

	**sarveṣām api caiteṣāṃ śubhānām iha karmaṇām |**

**	kiṃcic chreyaskarataraṃ karmoktaṃ puruṣaṃ prati || 12.84 ||**

jñānastutyartho 'yam upanyāsaḥ || 12.84 ||

	**sarveṣām api caiteṣām ātmajñānaṃ paraṃ smṛtam |**

**	tad dhy agryaṃ sarvavidyānāṃ prāpyate hy amṛtaṃ tataḥ || 12.85 ||**

ātmajñānapraśaṃsārthaḥ ślokaḥ | ato [jñāyate] pūrvatra jñānapāṭha eva, na dhyānapāṭhaḥ [nāpi] dānapāṭhaḥ | **ātmajñānaṃ** ca kṣetrajñasya dehendriyamanobuddhyādibhyo 'nyatrādijñānam | tasmin hi saty adhikārapuruṣa upalabdhakṣetrakṣetrajñatattvo madhyastho jitendriyo nirhṛtadoṣo viṣayair anabhimanyamānaḥ śrutiniyatam adhikāraṃ sākalyenānutiṣṭhati | yasmāt ato yuktam abhihitam: **prāpyate hy amṛtaṃ tata** iti | samastasya vyastasya vā paramātmano vedāntopaniṣado vijñānam, karmāṅgadev[vt]ājñānaṃ vā | sarvaṃ caitad ātmajñānagrahaṇena gṛhyate, tasmāt sāmarthyād avirodhāc ca || 12.85 ||

	**ṣaṇṇām eṣāṃ tu pūrveṣāṃ karmaṇāṃ pretya ceha ca |**

**	śreyaskarataraṃ jñeyaṃ sarvadā karma vaidikam || 12.86 ||**

pūrvopadiṣṭānāṃ vaidikānāṃ nityānāṃ karmaṇāṃ praśaṃsā | atra stutau kāraṇaṃ vakti || 12.86 ||

	**vaidike karmayoge tu sarvāṇy etāny aseṣataḥ |**

**	antarbhavanti kramaśas tasmiṃs tasmin kriyāvidhau || 12.87 ||**

vedābhyāsas tāvat karmavidhāv aṅgībhavati śastrastotragrahayājanādau | tapaś copasadvratādi karmāṅgam | jñānam uktaṃ kṣetrajñavijñānādi | indriyasaṃyamaḥ, "na māṃsam aśnīyān na mithunam upeyāt" ity evamādi | **ahiṃsā**: "tasmād etāṃ rātriṃ prāṇabhṛtaḥ prāṇaṃ na vicchindyāt" ity evamādi | **gurusevā** ṛtviganuvṛttiḥ | tac caitad vaidikaṃ karma || 12.87 ||

	**sukhābhyudayikaṃ caiva naiḥśreyasikam eva ca |**

**	pravṛttaṃ ca nivṛttaṃ ca dvividhaṃ karma vaidikam || 12.88 ||**

etac ca kāraṇabhedān karmaṇo dvaividhyaṃ yena atas tatkāraṇād idam ucyate |

	**iha vāmutra vā kāmyaṃ pravṛttaṃ karma kīrtyate |**

jñānapūrvam api saṃkalpopahatam, kiṃ punar ajñānapūrvam |

	**niṣkāmaṃ jñānapūrvaṃ tu nivṛttam upadiśyate || 12.89 ||**

atra ca nivṛtte karmaṇi jñānopadeśāt pravṛtte karmaṇy ajñānasaṃkalpo nimittatvenārthād gamyate | idānīṃ kāraṇabhinnayoḥ phalabhedaṃ śāsti sutarāṃ dvaividhyapradarśakam || 12.89 ||

	**pravṛttaṃ karma saṃsevya devānāṃ eti sārṣṭitām |**

**	nivṛttaṃ sevamānas tu bhūtāny atyeti pañca vai || 12.90 ||**

vāyuśarīra ākāśaśarīro vā sūkṣmo bhavati | tathā coktam: "tad brahmaparam abhyeti vāyubhūtaḥ svasūrtimān" || atha vā mokṣam anyenopāyenemaṃ śāsti pañcabhūtātyayaśabdena | idānīṃ dhyānasya jñānasya vā stuty artham idam ārabhyate |

	**sarvabhūteṣu cātmānaṃ sarvabhūtāni cātmani |**

**	samaṃ paśyan**

samatvena paramātmānaṃ paśyan, ātmavat sarvabhūtāni paśyann ity arthaḥ |

		**ātmayājī**

nivṛttakarmāvasthaḥ paramasaṃyamavān | anena prasaṃkhyānena | tasya phalam āha: evaṃ yuktaḥ |

		**svārājyam adhigacchati || 12.91 ||**

yathoktena śrutyuktenātmayājitvenāpavargāya kalpate | svatantraḥ saṃsāre bhavati na karmakleśavāsagaḥ | etac ca prasaṃkhyānaṃ rāgadveṣagrahaṇārthaviyuktam apavargāya syāt | saṃyamastutyartho vāyaṃ ślokaḥ | ātmajñānam tu pūrvatra saṃskṛtam eva | ubhayārtho vā saṃbhavād ubhayatra || 12.91 ||

	**yathoktāny api karmāṇi parihāya dvijottamaḥ |**

**	ātmajñāne śame ca syād vedābhyāse ca yatnavān || 12.92 ||**

**yathoktāny api karmāṇi parihāyety** ayam arthavādaḥ, ātmajñānaśamavedābhyāsastutaye | na hi nityānāṃ karmaṇāṃ parityāgo 'sty ātmecchayā | śāstratas tu parityāgaḥ pākṣikaḥ puruṣamedhādiṣv anutyāgena | tadabhāvapakṣa anadhikṛtapuruṣaviṣayam etat trayam || 12.92 ||

	**etad dhi janmasāmagryaṃ brāhmaṇasya viśeṣataḥ |**

viśeṣata iti vacanān na tathā kṣatriyavaiśyayoḥ |

	**prāpyaitat kṛtakṛtyo hi dvijo bhavati nānyathā || 12.93 ||**

vedābhyāsādīnāṃ ṣaṇṇāṃ karmaṇāṃ vaidikānām adhikṛtānāṃ stutyupasaṃhāraśloko 'yam || 12.93 ||

	**pitṛdevamanuṣyāṇāṃ vedaś cakṣuḥ sanātanam |**

**	atarkyaṃ cāprameyaṃ ca vedaśāstram iti sthitiḥ || 12.94 ||**

pitṛdevamanuṣyāṇām astitvaprasiddaye karmāṅgatvāyādhikārapuruṣasya **vedaś cakṣuḥ** | cakṣur iva, cakṣuḥ darśanārthatvāt | yena pitaro vedavidhyupahṛtam eva bhuñjate, tena **vedas** teṣāṃ **cakṣur** ity ucyate | **atarkyaṃ** cāpauruṣeyatvāt | **aprameyaṃ** ca phalato **vedaśāstram** | yasmāt ataḥ || 12.94 ||

	**yā vedabāhyāḥ smṛtayo yāś ca kāś ca kudṛṣṭayaḥ |**

**	sarvās tā niṣphalāḥ pretya tamoniṣṭhā hi tāḥ smṛtāḥ || 12.95 ||**

**yā vedabāhyāḥ smṛtaya** āgamā ity arthaḥ | puruṣadṛṣṭiprabhavāḥ | tadīyeṣu śāstreṣu **yāś ca kāś ca** [**kudṛṣṭayaḥ**] **sarvās tā niṣphalāḥ** **pretyā**dhikāravirodhena tatkarmavidhānāt | adhikāramūlo dharmo yataḥ, tadabhāvāt **tamoniṣṭhā hi tāḥ smṛtāḥ** | yataś ca || 12.95 ||

	**utpadyante cyavante ca yāny ato 'nyāni kānicit |**

**	tāny arvāk kālikatayā niṣphalāny anṛtāni ca || 12.96 ||**

ato veda eva svatantro 'nuśāsane 'nyanirapekṣo bhūtvā, bhūyaḥ pramāṇaśāstrānuvidhānāc ca | tanmūlaṃ dharmaśāstram, na tv anyāni tadvidhāni | puruṣakṛtayaḥ kartṛsamākhyātāḥ | yataś caitad evam ataḥ || 12.96 ||

	**cāturvarṇyaṃ taryo lokāś catvāraś cāśramāḥ pṛthak |**

**	bhūtaṃ bhavat bhaviṣyac ca sarvaṃ vedāt prasidhyati || 12.97 ||**

**cāturvarṇyaṃ** tāvad bhūtam atikrāntam | kutaḥ | asmād vartamānāc caturyugād | **bhavad** vartamānaṃ cāturvarṇyam iti prakṛtam | **bhaviṣyac ca** tad eva | yad anāgataṃ caturyuge | atha vā devacaturyugāpekṣayāyaṃ kālatrayanirdeśaḥ cāturvarṇyasya | brahmaṇaḥ kalpāpekṣayā vā | **vedād** eva **prasidhyati**, nānyataḥ, pratyakṣād anumānād vā, tasya śāstralakṣaṇatvāt | tad darśayati | yathā paśutve samāne gomahiṣāśvādīnāṃ vyaktisaṃsthānaviśeopalabdher eva jātibhedānumānam | naivaṃ puruṣatvāviśeṣe brāhmaṇādīnām api jātibhedānumānam asti, yenānumānatas teṣām api jātibhedaḥ pratīyeta | evaṃ ca sati śāstralakṣaṇam eva cāturvarṇyam | "vasante brāhmaṇo 'gnīn ādadhīta" ity evamādi | tathā coktam: "sarvavarṇeṣu tulyāsu" ity evamādi | vedārthānuvāditvaṃ cāśritya smṛter idam udāharaṇam | tathā ca sati yuktam idaṃ yad avocac chāstrakāraḥ **sarvaṃ vedāt prasidhyatīti** | atha vā tadadhikārāpekṣam idaṃ vacanaṃ "cāturvarṇyaṃ . . . vedāt prasidhyati" iti, evaṃ ca trayo lokāḥ tatphalāḥ karmaṇāṃ gatayaḥ catvāraś cāśramāḥ pūrvavad vyākaraṇīyam | bhūtaṃ bhavat bhaviṣyac cetīdaṃ napuṃsakaliṅgaṃ cāturvarṇyanapuṃsakaliṅgāpekṣam | itaratra puṃliṅgatvān nidarśanārtham idaṃ vijñeyam || 12.97 ||

	**śabdaḥ sparsaś ca rūpaṃ ca raso gandhaś ca pañcamaḥ |**

**	vedād eva prasidhyanti prasūtiguṇakarmataḥ || 12.98 ||**

ye hi **śabdā**dayaḥ svargādiṣu śarīralakṣaṇaviṣayalakṣaṇāś cotkṛṣṭābhipretabhogahetavaḥ te **vedād eva prasidhyanti**, nānyadarśanāt buddhādivacanāt | kiṃ sākṣāt | na, kiṃ tarhi **prasūtiguṇakarmataḥ**, prasūtyarthaṃ guṇakarma | **prasūtiguṇakarmataḥ** prasūtyarthaṃ prakṛtānāṃ śabdādīnām | guṇakarma ca puruṣopakārakam | tathā ca lokaprasiddhiḥ: "ko guṇo mama tavopakṛtavataḥ" kaḥ upakāra ity arthaḥ, guṇārtham abhipretapuruṣārthārtham | karma dharmākhyam | yena dharma eva puruṣopakarāya, nādharmaḥ tadviśeṣārtham idaṃ guṇakarmagrahaṇam | evaṃ ca sati na sākṣād vedaḥ śabdādihetuḥ, kiṃ tarhy agnihotrādikarmānuṣṭhānadvāreṇa dharmākhyaṃ guṇakarmaśabdādiprasūtyartham | evaṃ ca na sākṣād vedaḥ śabdādīnāṃ **prasūti**nimittam, kiṃ tarhi dharmapraṇādikayā | saiṣā vedastutir apareṇa prakāreṇa sāmarthyād vijñeyā | atha vā śabdādayo **vedād eva prasidhyanti**, yena **prasūtir** utpattir guṇakarmaṇo dharmasya | vedād dharmaḥ | dharmād api śabdādayaḥ svargādiṣu | ata idam ucyate: dharmād eva prasidhyantīti | atha vāyam asya ślokapādasya caturthasya tṛtīyaḥ pāṭhaḥ: vedād eva prasidhyanti prasūter guṇakarmaṇaḥ | kutaḥ | vedāt | arthas tv anantaropadiṣṭa eva || 12.98 ||

	**bibharti sarvabhūtāni vedaśāstraṃ sanātanam |**

**	tasmād etat paraṃ manye yaj jantor asya sādhanam || 12.99 ||**

tathā ca brāhmaṇam: "havir agnau hūyate | so 'gnir ādityaṃ gamayati | tat sūryo raśmibhir varṣati | tenānnaṃ bhavati | annād bhūtānām utpattiḥ" sthitś ceti vijñāyate | ihāpi coktam: "agnau prāstāhutiḥ samyag ādityam upatiṣṭhate" (MDh 3.66) ity evamādi | **tadmād etat paraṃ manye** puruṣārthakāri **yat** yena kāraṇena **jantor asya** dharmānuśāsanam | etasmāt kāraṇāt || 12.99 ||

	**senāpatyaṃ ca rājyaṃ ca daṇḍanetṛtvam eva ca |**

**	sarvalokādhipatyaṃ ca vedaśāstravid arhati || 12.100 ||**

yathā kathaṃcid vedaṃ prakaraṇāt stauti | atra kāraṇaṃ vakti || 12.100 ||

	**yathā jātabalo vahnir dahaty ārdrān api drumān |**

**	tathā dahati vedajñaḥ karmajaṃ doṣam ātmanaḥ || 12.101 ||**

etasmāt kāraṇāt,

	**vedaśāstrārthatattvajño yatra tatrāśrame vasan |**

**	ihaiva loke tiṣṭhan sa brahmabhūyāya kalpate || 12.102 ||**

**	ajñebhyo granthinaḥ śreṣṭhā granthibhyo dhāriṇo varāḥ |**

**	dhāribhyo jñāninaḥ śreṣṭhā jñānibhyo vyavasāyinaḥ || 12.103 ||**

granthadhāriṇo **dhāriṇaḥ** | pūrvapadalopo 'tra vijñeyaḥ | yathā satyabhāmā bhāmā devadatto datta iti | **dhāribhyo jñāninaḥ**: prayatna[vi]śeṣād adhikataraphalabhājaḥ | **jñānibhyo** 'dhyavasāyinaḥ karmaṇām anuṣṭhātāraḥ | yasmāt || 12.102–103 ||

	**tapo vidyā ca viprasya niḥśreyasakaraṃ param |**

samuccayaprayojanam ācaṣṭe |

	**tapasā kalmaṣaṃ hanti vidyayāmṛtam aśnute || 12.104 ||**

**tapasā kalmaṣaṃ hanti** | tapaḥśabdena nityāni karmāṇi śrautasmārthāny ucyanta ity uktaṃ purastāt | teṣāṃ nityānāṃ karmaṇām anuṣṭhānena kalmaṣaṃ hanti | tathā coktaṃ prāyaścittaprakaraṇe "vedābhyāso 'nvahaṃ śaktyā mahāyajñakriyā kṣamā, śodhayanty āśu pāpāni mahāpātakajāny api" iti | vidyayā paramātmādivijñānenety uktaṃ purastāt prakaraṇāt | **amṛtam aśnute** | sa eva jñānakarmaṇor avirodhāt samuccayaḥ pūrvopadiṣṭa upasaṃhriyate | **amṛtam aśnute** mokṣam brahmatvaṃ vā prāponotīty arthaḥ || 12.104 ||

	**pratyakṣaṃ cānumānaṃ ca śāstraṃ ca vividhāgamam |**

**	trayaṃ suviditaṃ kāryaṃ dharmaśuddhim abhīpsatā || 12.105 ||**

anumānāgamābhyāṃ dharmaśuddhi [na] (?) pratyakṣād, yataḥ tasyopadeśo 'numānaśuddhyarthaḥ | tatpūrvakatvād anumānasyāgamaśeṣatvam | api ca pratyakṣasya kvacid iṣyata eva | yataḥ etasyāṃ kalpanāyām ubhayaśeṣatvād yuktaḥ pratyakṣanirdeśaḥ | anumānasyāpy āgamārthaḥ | evaṃ ca sati pratyakṣānumānatattvaṃ tarkaḥ | śāstraṃ tu vividhāgamam | bahuśākho vedaḥ | "ekaviṃśatidhā bāhvṛcyam ekaśatam adhvaryuśākhāḥ sahasravartmā sāmavedaḥ" | atha vā śāstraṃ vividhāgamam, bahuśākhaṃ dharmaśāstram | avirodhād ubhayaṃ vā śrutismṛtyākhyam | adhunānumānatattvaṃ vijñānaprayojanam ācaṣṭe || 12.105 ||

	**ārṣaṃ dharmopadeśaṃ ca vedaśāstrāvirodhinā |**

**	yas tarkeṇānusaṃdhatte sa dharmaṃ veda netaraḥ || 12.106 ||**

**ārṣam** akṛtakatvāt | **dharmopadeśaḥ** smṛtiḥ | tathā cedam ucyate dharmaśāstram | etad dvayaṃ **vedaśāstrāvirodhinā**, vedagrahaṇāc ca smṛtigrahaṇam api sāmarthyād anuktam apy atra vijñeyam | tadapekṣitatvāc chruteḥ | anabhidhānaṃ tu chandobhaṅgabhayāt | evaṃ ca sati vedasmṛtiśāstrāvirodhinety etad upapannam | prādhānyād vā vedagrahaṇaṃ nidarśanārthaṃ smṛter api | sa ca tarko dviprakāro, yataḥ taṃ viśinaṣṭi **vedaśāstrāvirodhinā** | **yas tarkeṇānusaṃdhatte** sandigha(?)vyāhatapunaruktāśaṅkāyām, **sa dharmaṃ veda na** kevalatārkikaḥ | tathā cetihāsaḥ: "kaccin na lokāyatikān brāhmaṇāṃs tāta sevase, anarthakuśalā hy ete mūrkhāḥ paṇḍitamāninaḥ" iti | kevalāgamo vā | tathā ca vyāsaśloko **bhīmasena**vacanānuvādī:

	śrotriyasyeva te rājan mandakasyālpamedhasaḥ |

	anuvākahatā buddhir naiṣā sūkṣmārthadarśinī || iti |
